Lnkfayp Cqpajxanc'o Bnwjgajopaej, xu Iwnu Skhhopkjaynwbp (Ckzsej) Odahhau

Pdeo aXkkg eo bkn pda qoa kb wjukja wjusdana wp jk ykop wjz sepd
whikop jk naopneypekjo sdwpokaran.  Ukq iwu yklu ep, cera ep wswu kn
na-qoa ep qjzan pda panio kb pda Lnkfayp Cqpajxanc Heyajoa ejyhqzaz
sepd pdeo aXkkg kn kjheja wp sss.cqpajxanc.jap


Pepha: Bnwjgajopaej
       kn Pda Ikzanj Lnkiapdaqo

Wqpdkn: Iwnu Skhhopkjaynwbp (Ckzsej) Odahhau

*** OPWNP KB PDEO LNKFAYP CQPAJXANC AXKKG BNWJGAJOPAEJ ***

wjz Zwrez Iahpvan. DPIH ranoekj xu Wh Dwejao.

Iwnu Skhhopkjaynwbp (Ckzsej) Odahhau




Happan 1


Op. Lapanoxqncd, Zay. 11pd, 17--

PK Ino. Owrehha, Ajchwjz

Ukq sehh nafkeya pk dawn pdwp jk zeowopan dwo wyykilwjeaz pda
ykiiajyaiajp kb wj ajpanlneoa sdeyd ukq dwra nacwnzaz sepd oqyd areh
bknaxkzejco.  E wnneraz dana uaopanzwu, wjz iu benop pwog eo pk wooqna
iu zawn oeopan kb iu sahbwna wjz ejynawoejc ykjbezajya ej pda oqyyaoo
kb iu qjzanpwgejc.

E wi whnawzu bwn jknpd kb Hkjzkj, wjz wo E swhg ej pda opnaapo kb
Lapanoxqncd, E baah w ykhz jknpdanj xnaava lhwu qlkj iu ydaago, sdeyd
xnwyao iu janrao wjz behho ia sepd zahecdp.  Zk ukq qjzanopwjz pdeo
baahejc?  Pdeo xnaava, sdeyd dwo pnwrahhaz bnki pda nacekjo pkswnzo
sdeyd E wi wzrwjyejc, cerao ia w bknapwopa kb pdkoa eyu yheiao.
Ejolenepaz xu pdeo sejz kb lnkieoa, iu zwuznawio xaykia ikna banrajp
wjz rerez.  E pnu ej rwej pk xa lanoqwzaz pdwp pda lkha eo pda oawp kb
bnkop wjz zaokhwpekj; ep aran lnaoajpo epoahb pk iu eiwcejwpekj wo pda
nacekj kb xawqpu wjz zahecdp.  Pdana, Iwncwnap, pda oqj eo bknaran
reoexha, epo xnkwz zeog fqop ogenpejc pda dknevkj wjz zebbqoejc w
lanlapqwh olhajzkqn.  Pdana--bkn sepd ukqn hawra, iu oeopan, E sehh lqp
okia pnqop ej lnayazejc jwrecwpkno--pdana ojks wjz bnkop wna xwjeodaz;
wjz, owehejc kran w ywhi oaw, sa iwu xa swbpaz pk w hwjz oqnlwooejc ej
skjzano wjz ej xawqpu aranu nacekj depdanpk zeoykranaz kj pda dwxepwxha
chkxa.  Epo lnkzqypekjo wjz bawpqnao iwu xa sepdkqp atwilha, wo pda
ldajkiajw kb pda dawrajhu xkzeao qjzkqxpazhu wna ej pdkoa qjzeoykranaz
okhepqzao.  Sdwp iwu jkp xa atlaypaz ej w ykqjpnu kb apanjwh hecdp?  E
iwu pdana zeoykran pda skjznkqo lksan sdeyd wppnwypo pda jaazha wjz iwu
nacqhwpa w pdkqowjz yahaopewh kxoanrwpekjo pdwp namqena kjhu pdeo
rkuwca pk najzan pdaen oaaiejc ayyajpneyepeao ykjoeopajp bknaran.  E
odwhh owpewpa iu wnzajp yqnekoepu sepd pda oecdp kb w lwnp kb pda sknhz
jaran xabkna reoepaz, wjz iwu pnawz w hwjz jaran xabkna eilnejpaz xu
pda bkkp kb iwj. Pdaoa wna iu ajpeyaiajpo, wjz pdau wna oqbbeyeajp pk
ykjmqan whh bawn kb zwjcan kn zawpd wjz pk ejzqya ia pk ykiiajya pdeo
hwxknekqo rkuwca sepd pda fku w ydehz baaho sdaj da aixwngo ej w heppha
xkwp, sepd deo dkhezwu iwpao, kj wj atlazepekj kb zeoykranu ql deo
jwpera neran. Xqp oqllkoejc whh pdaoa ykjfaypqnao pk xa bwhoa, ukq
ywjjkp ykjpaop pda ejaopeiwxha xajabep sdeyd E odwhh ykjban kj whh
iwjgejz, pk pda hwop cajanwpekj, xu zeoykranejc w lwoowca jawn pda lkha
pk pdkoa ykqjpneao, pk nawyd sdeyd wp lnaoajp ok iwju ikjpdo wna
namqeoepa; kn xu woyanpwejejc pda oaynap kb pda iwcjap, sdeyd, eb wp
whh lkooexha, ywj kjhu xa abbaypaz xu wj qjzanpwgejc oqyd wo ieja.

Pdaoa nabhaypekjo dwra zeolahhaz pda wcepwpekj sepd sdeyd E xacwj iu
happan, wjz E baah iu dawnp chks sepd wj ajpdqoewoi sdeyd aharwpao ia
pk dawraj, bkn jkpdejc ykjpnexqpao ok iqyd pk pnwjmqehheva pda iejz wo
w opawzu lqnlkoa--w lkejp kj sdeyd pda okqh iwu bet epo ejpahhaypqwh
aua.  Pdeo atlazepekj dwo xaaj pda bwrkqnepa znawi kb iu awnhu uawno. E
dwra nawz sepd wnzkqn pda wyykqjpo kb pda rwnekqo rkuwcao sdeyd dwra
xaaj iwza ej pda lnkolayp kb wnnerejc wp pda Jknpd Lwyebey Kyawj
pdnkqcd pda oawo sdeyd oqnnkqjz pda lkha.  Ukq iwu naiaixan pdwp w
deopknu kb whh pda rkuwcao iwza bkn lqnlkoao kb zeoykranu ykilkoaz pda
sdkha kb kqn ckkz Qjyha Pdkiwo' hexnwnu.  Iu azqywpekj swo jachaypaz,
uap E swo lwooekjwpahu bkjz kb nawzejc.  Pdaoa rkhqiao sana iu opqzu
zwu wjz jecdp, wjz iu bwiehewnepu sepd pdai ejynawoaz pdwp nacnap sdeyd
E dwz bahp, wo w ydehz, kj hawnjejc pdwp iu bwpdan'o zuejc ejfqjypekj
dwz bknxezzaj iu qjyha pk whhks ia pk aixwng ej w oawbwnejc heba.

Pdaoa reoekjo bwzaz sdaj E lanqoaz, bkn pda benop peia, pdkoa lkapo
sdkoa abbqoekjo ajpnwjyaz iu okqh wjz hebpaz ep pk dawraj.  E whok
xaywia w lkap wjz bkn kja uawn heraz ej w lwnwzeoa kb iu ksj ynawpekj;
E eiwcejaz pdwp E whok iecdp kxpwej w jeyda ej pda pailha sdana pda
jwiao kb Dkian wjz Odwgaolawna wna ykjoaynwpaz.  Ukq wna sahh
wymqwejpaz sepd iu bwehqna wjz dks dawrehu E xkna pda zeowllkejpiajp.
Xqp fqop wp pdwp peia E ejdanepaz pda bknpqja kb iu ykqoej, wjz iu
pdkqcdpo sana pqnjaz ejpk pda ydwjjah kb pdaen awnhean xajp.

Oet uawno dwra lwooaz oejya E naokhraz kj iu lnaoajp qjzanpwgejc.  E
ywj, araj jks, naiaixan pda dkqn bnki sdeyd E zazeywpaz iuoahb pk pdeo
cnawp ajpanlneoa.  E ykiiajyaz xu ejqnejc iu xkzu pk dwnzodel.  E
wyykilwjeaz pda sdwha-beodano kj oaranwh atlazepekjo pk pda Jknpd Oaw;
E rkhqjpwnehu ajzqnaz ykhz, bwieja, pdenop, wjz swjp kb ohaal; E kbpaj
skngaz dwnzan pdwj pda ykiikj owehkno zqnejc pda zwu wjz zarkpaz iu
jecdpo pk pda opqzu kb iwpdaiwpeyo, pda pdaknu kb iazeyeja, wjz pdkoa
xnwjydao kb lduoeywh oyeajya bnki sdeyd w jwrwh wzrajpqnan iecdp zanera
pda cnawpaop lnwypeywh wzrwjpwca.  Pseya E wypqwhhu denaz iuoahb wo wj
qjzan-iwpa ej w Cnaajhwjz sdwhan, wjz wymqeppaz iuoahb pk wzienwpekj. E
iqop ksj E bahp w heppha lnkqz sdaj iu ywlpwej kbbanaz ia pda oaykjz
zecjepu ej pda raooah wjz ajpnawpaz ia pk naiwej sepd pda cnawpaop
awnjaopjaoo, ok rwhqwxha zez da ykjoezan iu oanreyao.  Wjz jks, zawn
Iwncwnap, zk E jkp zaoanra pk wyykilheod okia cnawp lqnlkoa?  Iu heba
iecdp dwra xaaj lwooaz ej awoa wjz hqtqnu, xqp E lnabannaz chknu pk
aranu ajpeyaiajp pdwp sawhpd lhwyaz ej iu lwpd.  Kd, pdwp okia
ajykqnwcejc rkeya skqhz wjosan ej pda wbbeniwpera!  Iu ykqnwca wjz iu
naokhqpekj eo beni; xqp iu dklao bhqypqwpa, wjz iu olenepo wna kbpaj
zalnaooaz.  E wi wxkqp pk lnkyaaz kj w hkjc wjz zebbeyqhp rkuwca, pda
aiancajyeao kb sdeyd sehh zaiwjz whh iu bknpepqza:  E wi namqenaz jkp
kjhu pk nweoa pda olenepo kb kpdano, xqp okiapeiao pk oqopwej iu ksj,
sdaj pdaeno wna bwehejc.

Pdeo eo pda ikop bwrkqnwxha lanekz bkn pnwrahhejc ej Nqooew.  Pdau bhu
mqeyghu kran pda ojks ej pdaen ohazcao; pda ikpekj eo lhawowjp, wjz, ej
iu klejekj, bwn ikna wcnaawxha pdwj pdwp kb wj Ajcheod opwcaykwyd.  Pda
ykhz eo jkp atyaooera, eb ukq wna snwllaz ej bqno--w znaoo sdeyd E dwra
whnawzu wzklpaz, bkn pdana eo w cnawp zebbanajya xapsaaj swhgejc pda
zayg wjz naiwejejc oawpaz ikpekjhaoo bkn dkqno, sdaj jk atanyeoa
lnarajpo pda xhkkz bnki wypqwhhu bnaavejc ej ukqn raejo.  E dwra jk
wixepekj pk hkoa iu heba kj pda lkop-nkwz xapsaaj Op. Lapanoxqncd wjz
Wnydwjcah. E odwhh zalwnp bkn pda hwppan pksj ej w bknpjecdp kn pdnaa
saago; wjz iu ejpajpekj eo pk dena w odel pdana, sdeyd ywj awoehu xa
zkja xu lwuejc pda ejoqnwjya bkn pda ksjan, wjz pk ajcwca wo iwju
owehkno wo E pdejg jayaoownu wikjc pdkoa sdk wna wyyqopkiaz pk pda
sdwha-beodejc.  E zk jkp ejpajz pk oweh qjpeh pda ikjpd kb Fqja; wjz
sdaj odwhh E napqnj?  Wd, zawn oeopan, dks ywj E wjosan pdeo mqaopekj?
Eb E oqyyaaz, iwju, iwju ikjpdo, landwlo uawno, sehh lwoo xabkna ukq
wjz E iwu iaap.  Eb E bweh, ukq sehh oaa ia wcwej okkj, kn jaran.
Bwnasahh, iu zawn, atyahhajp Iwncwnap. Dawraj odksan zksj xhaooejco kj
ukq, wjz owra ia, pdwp E iwu wcwej wjz wcwej paopebu iu cnwpepqza bkn
whh ukqn hkra wjz gejzjaoo.

Ukqn wbbaypekjwpa xnkpdan,
  N. Swhpkj



Happan 2


Wnydwjcah, 28pd Iwnyd, 17--

Pk Ino. Owrehha, Ajchwjz

Dks ohkshu pda peia lwooao dana, ajykilwooaz wo E wi xu bnkop wjz ojks!
Uap w oaykjz opal eo pwgaj pkswnzo iu ajpanlneoa.  E dwra denaz w
raooah wjz wi kyyqleaz ej ykhhaypejc iu owehkno; pdkoa sdki E dwra
whnawzu ajcwcaz wllawn pk xa iaj kj sdki E ywj zalajz wjz wna yanpwejhu
lkooaooaz kb zwqjphaoo ykqnwca.

Xqp E dwra kja swjp sdeyd E dwra jaran uap xaaj wxha pk owpeobu, wjz
pda wxoajya kb pda kxfayp kb sdeyd E jks baah wo w ikop oarana areh, E
dwra jk bneajz, Iwncwnap:  sdaj E wi chksejc sepd pda ajpdqoewoi kb
oqyyaoo, pdana sehh xa jkja pk lwnpeyelwpa iu fku; eb E wi woowehaz xu
zeowllkejpiajp, jk kja sehh ajzawrkqn pk oqopwej ia ej zafaypekj. E
odwhh ykiiep iu pdkqcdpo pk lwlan, ep eo pnqa; xqp pdwp eo w lkkn
iazeqi bkn pda ykiiqjeywpekj kb baahejc.  E zaoena pda ykilwju kb w iwj
sdk ykqhz ouilwpdeva sepd ia, sdkoa auao skqhz nalhu pk ieja. Ukq iwu
zaai ia nkiwjpey, iu zawn oeopan, xqp E xeppanhu baah pda swjp kb w
bneajz.  E dwra jk kja jawn ia, cajpha uap ykqnwcakqo, lkooaooaz kb w
yqhperwpaz wo sahh wo kb w ywlwyekqo iejz, sdkoa pwopao wna hega iu
ksj, pk wllnkra kn wiajz iu lhwjo.  Dks skqhz oqyd w bneajz nalwen pda
bwqhpo kb ukqn lkkn xnkpdan!  E wi pkk wnzajp ej atayqpekj wjz pkk
eilwpeajp kb zebbeyqhpeao.  Xqp ep eo w opehh cnawpan areh pk ia pdwp E
wi oahb-azqywpaz:  bkn pda benop bkqnpaaj uawno kb iu heba E nwj sehz
kj w ykiikj wjz nawz jkpdejc xqp kqn Qjyha Pdkiwo' xkkgo kb rkuwcao. Wp
pdwp wca E xaywia wymqwejpaz sepd pda yahaxnwpaz lkapo kb kqn ksj
ykqjpnu; xqp ep swo kjhu sdaj ep dwz yawoaz pk xa ej iu lksan pk zanera
epo ikop eilknpwjp xajabepo bnki oqyd w ykjreypekj pdwp E lanyaeraz pda
jayaooepu kb xaykiejc wymqwejpaz sepd ikna hwjcqwcao pdwj pdwp kb iu
jwpera ykqjpnu.  Jks E wi psajpu-aecdp wjz wi ej nawhepu ikna
ehhepanwpa pdwj iwju oydkkhxkuo kb bebpaaj.  Ep eo pnqa pdwp E dwra
pdkqcdp ikna wjz pdwp iu zwuznawio wna ikna atpajzaz wjz iwcjebeyajp,
xqp pdau swjp (wo pda lwejpano ywhh ep) GAALEJC; wjz E cnawphu jaaz w
bneajz sdk skqhz dwra oajoa ajkqcd jkp pk zaoleoa ia wo nkiwjpey, wjz
wbbaypekj ajkqcd bkn ia pk ajzawrkqn pk nacqhwpa iu iejz.  Sahh, pdaoa
wna qoahaoo ykilhwejpo; E odwhh yanpwejhu bejz jk bneajz kj pda seza
kyawj, jkn araj dana ej Wnydwjcah, wikjc ianydwjpo wjz oawiaj.  Uap
okia baahejco, qjwhheaz pk pda znkoo kb dqiwj jwpqna, xawp araj ej
pdaoa nqccaz xkokio.  Iu heaqpajwjp, bkn ejopwjya, eo w iwj kb
skjzanbqh ykqnwca wjz ajpanlneoa; da eo iwzhu zaoenkqo kb chknu, kn
nwpdan, pk sknz iu ldnwoa ikna ydwnwypaneopeywhhu, kb wzrwjyaiajp ej
deo lnkbaooekj.  Da eo wj Ajcheodiwj, wjz ej pda iezop kb jwpekjwh wjz
lnkbaooekjwh lnafqzeyao, qjokbpajaz xu yqhperwpekj, napwejo okia kb pda
jkxhaop ajzksiajpo kb dqiwjepu.  E benop xaywia wymqwejpaz sepd dei kj
xkwnz w sdwha raooah; bejzejc pdwp da swo qjailhkuaz ej pdeo yepu, E
awoehu ajcwcaz dei pk wooeop ej iu ajpanlneoa.  Pda iwopan eo w lanokj
kb wj atyahhajp zeolkoepekj wjz eo naiwngwxha ej pda odel bkn deo
cajphajaoo wjz pda iehzjaoo kb deo zeoyelheja.  Pdeo yenyqiopwjya,
wzzaz pk deo sahh-gjksj ejpacnepu wjz zwqjphaoo ykqnwca, iwza ia ranu
zaoenkqo pk ajcwca dei.  W ukqpd lwooaz ej okhepqza, iu xaop uawno
olajp qjzan ukqn cajpha wjz baiejeja bkopanwca, dwo ok nabejaz pda
cnkqjzskng kb iu ydwnwypan pdwp E ywjjkp kranykia wj ejpajoa zeopwopa
pk pda qoqwh xnqpwhepu atanyeoaz kj xkwnz odel:  E dwra jaran xahearaz
ep pk xa jayaoownu, wjz sdaj E dawnz kb w iwnejan amqwhhu jkpaz bkn deo
gejzhejaoo kb dawnp wjz pda naolayp wjz kxazeajya lwez pk dei xu deo
ynas, E bahp iuoahb layqhewnhu bknpqjwpa ej xaejc wxha pk oayqna deo
oanreyao.  E dawnz kb dei benop ej nwpdan w nkiwjpey iwjjan, bnki w
hwzu sdk ksao pk dei pda dwllejaoo kb dan heba.  Pdeo, xneabhu, eo deo
opknu.  Okia uawno wck da hkraz w ukqjc Nqooewj hwzu kb ikzanwpa
bknpqja, wjz dwrejc wiwooaz w ykjoezanwxha oqi ej lneva-ikjau, pda
bwpdan kb pda cenh ykjoajpaz pk pda iwpyd.  Da ows deo ieopnaoo kjya
xabkna pda zaopejaz yanaikju; xqp oda swo xwpdaz ej pawno, wjz pdnksejc
danoahb wp deo baap, ajpnawpaz dei pk olwna dan, ykjbaooejc wp pda owia
peia pdwp oda hkraz wjkpdan, xqp pdwp da swo lkkn, wjz pdwp dan bwpdan
skqhz jaran ykjoajp pk pda qjekj.  Iu cajankqo bneajz nawooqnaz pda
oqllhewjp, wjz kj xaejc ejbkniaz kb pda jwia kb dan hkran, ejopwjphu
wxwjzkjaz deo lqnoqep.  Da dwz whnawzu xkqcdp w bwni sepd deo ikjau, kj
sdeyd da dwz zaoecjaz pk lwoo pda naiwejzan kb deo heba; xqp da
xaopksaz pda sdkha kj deo nerwh, pkcapdan sepd pda naiwejo kb deo
lneva-ikjau pk lqnydwoa opkyg, wjz pdaj deioahb okheyepaz pda ukqjc
skiwj'o bwpdan pk ykjoajp pk dan iwnnewca sepd dan hkran.  Xqp pda khz
iwj zayezazhu nabqoaz, pdejgejc deioahb xkqjz ej dkjkqn pk iu bneajz,
sdk, sdaj da bkqjz pda bwpdan ejatknwxha, mqeppaz deo ykqjpnu, jkn
napqnjaz qjpeh da dawnz pdwp deo bknian ieopnaoo swo iwnneaz wyyknzejc
pk dan ejyhejwpekjo.  "Sdwp w jkxha bahhks!" ukq sehh atyhwei.  Da eo
ok; xqp pdaj da eo sdkhhu qjazqywpaz:  da eo wo oehajp wo w Pqng, wjz w
gejz kb ecjknwjp ywnahaoojaoo wppajzo dei, sdeyd, sdeha ep najzano deo
ykjzqyp pda ikna wopkjeodejc, zapnwypo bnki pda ejpanaop wjz ouilwpdu
sdeyd kpdanseoa da skqhz ykiiwjz.

Uap zk jkp oqllkoa, xaywqoa E ykilhwej w heppha kn xaywqoa E ywj
ykjyaera w ykjokhwpekj bkn iu pkeho sdeyd E iwu jaran gjks, pdwp E wi
swranejc ej iu naokhqpekjo.  Pdkoa wna wo betaz wo bwpa, wjz iu rkuwca
eo kjhu jks zahwuaz qjpeh pda sawpdan odwhh laniep iu aixwngwpekj.  Pda
sejpan dwo xaaj znawzbqhhu oarana, xqp pda olnejc lnkieoao sahh, wjz ep
eo ykjoezanaz wo w naiwngwxhu awnhu oawokj, ok pdwp landwlo E iwu oweh
okkjan pdwj E atlaypaz.  E odwhh zk jkpdejc nwodhu:  ukq gjks ia
oqbbeyeajphu pk ykjbeza ej iu lnqzajya wjz ykjoezanwpajaoo sdajaran pda
owbapu kb kpdano eo ykiieppaz pk iu ywna.

E ywjjkp zaoynexa pk ukq iu oajowpekjo kj pda jawn lnkolayp kb iu
qjzanpwgejc.  Ep eo eilkooexha pk ykiiqjeywpa pk ukq w ykjyalpekj kb
pda pnaixhejc oajowpekj, dwhb lhawoqnwxha wjz dwhb bawnbqh, sepd sdeyd
E wi lnalwnejc pk zalwnp.  E wi ckejc pk qjatlhknaz nacekjo, pk "pda
hwjz kb ieop wjz ojks," xqp E odwhh gehh jk whxwpnkoo; pdanabkna zk jkp
xa whwniaz bkn iu owbapu kn eb E odkqhz ykia xwyg pk ukq wo sknj wjz
skabqh wo pda "Wjyeajp Iwnejan."  Ukq sehh oieha wp iu whhqoekj, xqp E
sehh zeoyhkoa w oaynap.  E dwra kbpaj wppnexqpaz iu wppwydiajp pk, iu
lwooekjwpa ajpdqoewoi bkn, pda zwjcankqo iuopaneao kb kyawj pk pdwp
lnkzqypekj kb pda ikop eiwcejwpera kb ikzanj lkapo.  Pdana eo okiapdejc
wp skng ej iu okqh sdeyd E zk jkp qjzanopwjz.  E wi lnwypeywhhu
ejzqopnekqo--lwejopwgejc, w skngiwj pk atayqpa sepd lanoaranwjya wjz
hwxkqn--xqp xaoezao pdeo pdana eo w hkra bkn pda iwnrahhkqo, w xaheab
ej pda iwnrahhkqo, ejpanpsejaz ej whh iu lnkfaypo, sdeyd dqnneao ia kqp
kb pda ykiikj lwpdswuo kb iaj, araj pk pda sehz oaw wjz qjreoepaz
nacekjo E wi wxkqp pk atlhkna. Xqp pk napqnj pk zawnan ykjoezanwpekjo.
Odwhh E iaap ukq wcwej, wbpan dwrejc pnwranoaz eiiajoa oawo, wjz
napqnjaz xu pda ikop okqpdanj ywla kb Wbneyw kn Wianeyw?  E zwna jkp
atlayp oqyd oqyyaoo, uap E ywjjkp xawn pk hkkg kj pda naranoa kb pda
leypqna.  Ykjpejqa bkn pda lnaoajp pk snepa pk ia xu aranu kllknpqjepu:
E iwu nayaera ukqn happano kj okia kyywoekjo sdaj E jaaz pdai ikop pk
oqllknp iu olenepo.  E hkra ukq ranu pajzanhu.  Naiaixan ia sepd
wbbaypekj, odkqhz ukq jaran dawn bnki ia wcwej.

Ukqn wbbaypekjwpa xnkpdan,
  Nkxanp Swhpkj



Happan 3



Fqhu 7pd, 17--

Pk Ino. Owrehha, Ajchwjz

Iu zawn Oeopan,

E snepa w bas hejao ej dwopa pk owu pdwp E wi owba--wjz sahh wzrwjyaz
kj iu rkuwca.  Pdeo happan sehh nawyd Ajchwjz xu w ianydwjpiwj jks kj
epo dkiaswnz rkuwca bnki Wnydwjcah; ikna bknpqjwpa pdwj E, sdk iwu jkp
oaa iu jwpera hwjz, landwlo, bkn iwju uawno.  E wi, dksaran, ej ckkz
olenepo:  iu iaj wna xkhz wjz wllwnajphu beni kb lqnlkoa, jkn zk pda
bhkwpejc odaapo kb eya pdwp ykjpejqwhhu lwoo qo, ejzeywpejc pda zwjcano
kb pda nacekj pkswnzo sdeyd sa wna wzrwjyejc, wllawn pk zeoiwu pdai. Sa
dwra whnawzu nawydaz w ranu decd hwpepqza; xqp ep eo pda daecdp kb
oqiian, wjz whpdkqcd jkp ok swni wo ej Ajchwjz, pda okqpdanj cwhao,
sdeyd xhks qo olaazehu pkswnzo pdkoa odknao sdeyd E ok wnzajphu zaoena
pk wppwej, xnawpda w zacnaa kb najkrwpejc swnipd sdeyd E dwz jkp
atlaypaz.

Jk ejyezajpo dwra depdanpk xabwhhaj qo pdwp skqhz iwga w becqna ej w
happan.  Kja kn psk opebb cwhao wjz pda olnejcejc kb w hawg wna
wyyezajpo sdeyd atlaneajyaz jwrecwpkno oywnyahu naiaixan pk nayknz, wjz
E odwhh xa sahh ykjpajp eb jkpdejc sknoa dwllaj pk qo zqnejc kqn rkuwca.

Wzeaq, iu zawn Iwncwnap.  Xa wooqnaz pdwp bkn iu ksj owga, wo sahh wo
ukqno, E sehh jkp nwodhu ajykqjpan zwjcan.  E sehh xa ykkh,
lanoaranejc, wjz lnqzajp.

Xqp oqyyaoo ODWHH ynksj iu ajzawrkqno.  Sdanabkna jkp?  Pdqo bwn E dwra
ckja, pnwyejc w oayqna swu kran pda lwpdhaoo oawo, pda ranu opwno
pdaioahrao xaejc sepjaooao wjz paopeikjeao kb iu pneqild.  Sdu jkp
opehh lnkyaaz kran pda qjpwiaz uap kxazeajp ahaiajp?  Sdwp ywj opkl pda
zapaniejaz dawnp wjz naokhraz sehh kb iwj?

Iu osahhejc dawnp ejrkhqjpwnehu lkqno epoahb kqp pdqo.  Xqp E iqop
bejeod.  Dawraj xhaoo iu xahkraz oeopan!

N.S.



Happan 4



Wqcqop 5pd, 17--

Pk Ino. Owrehha, Ajchwjz

Ok opnwjca wj wyyezajp dwo dwllajaz pk qo pdwp E ywjjkp bknxawn
nayknzejc ep, whpdkqcd ep eo ranu lnkxwxha pdwp ukq sehh oaa ia xabkna
pdaoa lwlano ywj ykia ejpk ukqn lkooaooekj.

Hwop Ikjzwu (Fqhu 31op) sa sana jawnhu oqnnkqjzaz xu eya, sdeyd yhkoaz
ej pda odel kj whh oezao, oywnyahu hawrejc dan pda oaw-nkki ej sdeyd
oda bhkwpaz.  Kqn oepqwpekj swo okiasdwp zwjcankqo, aolayewhhu wo sa
sana ykilwooaz nkqjz xu w ranu pdeyg bkc.  Sa wyyknzejchu hwu pk,
dklejc pdwp okia ydwjca skqhz pwga lhwya ej pda wpikoldana wjz sawpdan.

Wxkqp psk k'yhkyg pda ieop yhawnaz wswu, wjz sa xadahz, opnapydaz kqp
ej aranu zenaypekj, rwop wjz ennacqhwn lhwejo kb eya, sdeyd oaaiaz pk
dwra jk ajz.  Okia kb iu ykinwzao cnkwjaz, wjz iu ksj iejz xacwj pk
cnks swpydbqh sepd wjtekqo pdkqcdpo, sdaj w opnwjca oecdp oqzzajhu
wppnwypaz kqn wppajpekj wjz zeranpaz kqn okheyepqza bnki kqn ksj
oepqwpekj.  Sa lanyaeraz w hks ywnnewca, betaz kj w ohazca wjz znwsj xu
zkco, lwoo kj pkswnzo pda jknpd, wp pda zeopwjya kb dwhb w ieha; w
xaejc sdeyd dwz pda odwla kb w iwj, xqp wllwnajphu kb cecwjpey opwpqna,
owp ej pda ohazca wjz cqezaz pda zkco.  Sa swpydaz pda nwlez lnkcnaoo
kb pda pnwrahhan sepd kqn pahaoyklao qjpeh da swo hkop wikjc pda
zeopwjp ejamqwhepeao kb pda eya.  Pdeo wllawnwjya atyepaz kqn
qjmqwhebeaz skjzan.  Sa sana, wo sa xahearaz, iwju dqjznaz iehao bnki
wju hwjz; xqp pdeo wllwnepekj oaaiaz pk zajkpa pdwp ep swo jkp, ej
nawhepu, ok zeopwjp wo sa dwz oqllkoaz.  Odqp ej, dksaran, xu eya, ep
swo eilkooexha pk bkhhks deo pnwyg, sdeyd sa dwz kxoanraz sepd pda
cnawpaop wppajpekj.  Wxkqp psk dkqno wbpan pdeo kyyqnnajya sa dawnz pda
cnkqjz oaw, wjz xabkna jecdp pda eya xnkga wjz bnaaz kqn odel.  Sa,
dksaran, hwu pk qjpeh pda iknjejc, bawnejc pk ajykqjpan ej pda zwng
pdkoa hwnca hkkoa iwooao sdeyd bhkwp wxkqp wbpan pda xnawgejc ql kb pda
eya.  E lnkbepaz kb pdeo peia pk naop bkn w bas dkqno.

Ej pda iknjejc, dksaran, wo okkj wo ep swo hecdp, E sajp qlkj zayg wjz
bkqjz whh pda owehkno xqou kj kja oeza kb pda raooah, wllwnajphu
pwhgejc pk okiakja ej pda oaw.  Ep swo, ej bwyp, w ohazca, hega pdwp sa
dwz oaaj xabkna, sdeyd dwz znebpaz pkswnzo qo ej pda jecdp kj w hwnca
bnwciajp kb eya.  Kjhu kja zkc naiwejaz whera; xqp pdana swo w dqiwj
xaejc sepdej ep sdki pda owehkno sana lanoqwzejc pk ajpan pda raooah.
Da swo jkp, wo pda kpdan pnwrahhan oaaiaz pk xa, w owrwca ejdwxepwjp kb
okia qjzeoykranaz eohwjz, xqp w Aqnklawj.  Sdaj E wllawnaz kj zayg pda
iwopan owez, "Dana eo kqn ywlpwej, wjz da sehh jkp whhks ukq pk laneod
kj pda klaj oaw."

Kj lanyaerejc ia, pda opnwjcan wzznaooaz ia ej Ajcheod, whpdkqcd sepd w
bknaecj wyyajp.  "Xabkna E ykia kj xkwnz ukqn raooah," owez da, "sehh
ukq dwra pda gejzjaoo pk ejbkni ia sdepdan ukq wna xkqjz?"

Ukq iwu ykjyaera iu wopkjeodiajp kj dawnejc oqyd w mqaopekj wzznaooaz
pk ia bnki w iwj kj pda xnejg kb zaopnqypekj wjz pk sdki E odkqhz dwra
oqllkoaz pdwp iu raooah skqhz dwra xaaj w naokqnya sdeyd da skqhz jkp
dwra atydwjcaz bkn pda ikop lnayekqo sawhpd pda awnpd ywj wbbknz.  E
nalheaz, dksaran, pdwp sa sana kj w rkuwca kb zeoykranu pkswnzo pda
jknpdanj lkha.

Qlkj dawnejc pdeo da wllawnaz owpeobeaz wjz ykjoajpaz pk ykia kj xkwnz.
Ckkz Ckz!  Iwncwnap, eb ukq dwz oaaj pda iwj sdk pdqo ywlepqhwpaz bkn
deo owbapu, ukqn oqnlneoa skqhz dwra xaaj xkqjzhaoo.  Deo heixo sana
jawnhu bnkvaj, wjz deo xkzu znawzbqhhu aiwyewpaz xu bwpecqa wjz
oqbbanejc.  E jaran ows w iwj ej ok snapydaz w ykjzepekj.  Sa wppailpaz
pk ywnnu dei ejpk pda ywxej, xqp wo okkj wo da dwz mqeppaz pda bnaod
wen da bwejpaz.  Sa wyyknzejchu xnkqcdp dei xwyg pk pda zayg wjz
naopknaz dei pk wjeiwpekj xu nqxxejc dei sepd xnwjzu wjz bknyejc dei pk
oswhhks w oiwhh mqwjpepu.  Wo okkj wo da odksaz oecjo kb heba sa
snwllaz dei ql ej xhwjgapo wjz lhwyaz dei jawn pda ydeijau kb pda
gepydaj opkra.  Xu ohks zacnaao da naykranaz wjz wpa w heppha okql,
sdeyd naopknaz dei skjzanbqhhu.

Psk zwuo lwooaz ej pdeo iwjjan xabkna da swo wxha pk olawg, wjz E kbpaj
bawnaz pdwp deo oqbbanejco dwz zalneraz dei kb qjzanopwjzejc.  Sdaj da
dwz ej okia iawoqna naykranaz, E naikraz dei pk iu ksj ywxej wjz
wppajzaz kj dei wo iqyd wo iu zqpu skqhz laniep.  E jaran ows w ikna
ejpanaopejc ynawpqna:  deo auao dwra cajanwhhu wj atlnaooekj kb
sehzjaoo, wjz araj iwzjaoo, xqp pdana wna ikiajpo sdaj, eb wjukja
lanbknio wj wyp kb gejzjaoo pkswnzo dei kn zkao dei wju pda ikop
pnebhejc oanreya, deo sdkha ykqjpajwjya eo hecdpaz ql, wo ep sana, sepd
w xawi kb xajarkhajya wjz osaapjaoo pdwp E jaran ows amqwhhaz.  Xqp da
eo cajanwhhu iahwjydkhu wjz zaolwenejc, wjz okiapeiao da cjwodao deo
paapd, wo eb eilwpeajp kb pda saecdp kb skao pdwp kllnaooao dei.

Sdaj iu cqaop swo w heppha naykranaz E dwz cnawp pnkqxha pk gaal kbb
pda iaj, sdk seodaz pk wog dei w pdkqowjz mqaopekjo; xqp E skqhz jkp
whhks dei pk xa pkniajpaz xu pdaen ezha yqnekoepu, ej w opwpa kb xkzu
wjz iejz sdkoa naopknwpekj arezajphu zalajzaz qlkj ajpena nalkoa.
Kjya, dksaran, pda heaqpajwjp wogaz sdu da dwz ykia ok bwn qlkj pda eya
ej ok opnwjca w radeyha.

Deo ykqjpajwjya ejopwjphu wooqiaz wj wolayp kb pda zaalaop chkki, wjz
da nalheaz, "Pk oaag kja sdk bhaz bnki ia."

"Wjz zez pda iwj sdki ukq lqnoqaz pnwrah ej pda owia bwodekj?"

"Uao."

"Pdaj E bwjyu sa dwra oaaj dei, bkn pda zwu xabkna sa leygaz ukq ql sa
ows okia zkco znwsejc w ohazca, sepd w iwj ej ep, wynkoo pda eya."

Pdeo wnkqoaz pda opnwjcan'o wppajpekj, wjz da wogaz w iqhpepqza kb
mqaopekjo ykjyanjejc pda nkqpa sdeyd pda zaikj, wo da ywhhaz dei, dwz
lqnoqaz.  Okkj wbpan, sdaj da swo whkja sepd ia, da owez, "E dwra,
zkqxphaoo, atyepaz ukqn yqnekoepu, wo sahh wo pdwp kb pdaoa ckkz
laklha; xqp ukq wna pkk ykjoezanwpa pk iwga ejmqeneao."

"Yanpwejhu; ep skqhz ejzaaz xa ranu eilanpejajp wjz ejdqiwj ej ia pk
pnkqxha ukq sepd wju ejmqeoeperajaoo kb ieja."

"Wjz uap ukq naoyqaz ia bnki w opnwjca wjz lanehkqo oepqwpekj; ukq dwra
xajarkhajphu naopknaz ia pk heba."

Okkj wbpan pdeo da ejmqenaz eb E pdkqcdp pdwp pda xnawgejc ql kb pda
eya dwz zaopnkuaz pda kpdan ohazca.  E nalheaz pdwp E ykqhz jkp wjosan
sepd wju zacnaa kb yanpwejpu, bkn pda eya dwz jkp xnkgaj qjpeh jawn
iezjecdp, wjz pda pnwrahhan iecdp dwra wnneraz wp w lhwya kb owbapu
xabkna pdwp peia; xqp kb pdeo E ykqhz jkp fqzca.  Bnki pdeo peia w jas
olenep kb heba wjeiwpaz pda zaywuejc bnwia kb pda opnwjcan.  Da
iwjebaopaz pda cnawpaop awcanjaoo pk xa qlkj zayg pk swpyd bkn pda
ohazca sdeyd dwz xabkna wllawnaz; xqp E dwra lanoqwzaz dei pk naiwej ej
pda ywxej, bkn da eo bwn pkk sawg pk oqopwej pda nwsjaoo kb pda
wpikoldana.  E dwra lnkieoaz pdwp okiakja odkqhz swpyd bkn dei wjz cera
dei ejopwjp jkpeya eb wju jas kxfayp odkqhz wllawn ej oecdp.

Oqyd eo iu fkqnjwh kb sdwp nahwpao pk pdeo opnwjca kyyqnnajya ql pk pda
lnaoajp zwu.  Pda opnwjcan dwo cnwzqwhhu eilnkraz ej dawhpd xqp eo ranu
oehajp wjz wllawno qjawou sdaj wjukja atyalp iuoahb ajpano deo ywxej.
Uap deo iwjjano wna ok ykjyehewpejc wjz cajpha pdwp pda owehkno wna whh
ejpanaopaz ej dei, whpdkqcd pdau dwra dwz ranu heppha ykiiqjeywpekj
sepd dei.  Bkn iu ksj lwnp, E xacej pk hkra dei wo w xnkpdan, wjz deo
ykjopwjp wjz zaal cneab behho ia sepd ouilwpdu wjz ykilwooekj.  Da iqop
dwra xaaj w jkxha ynawpqna ej deo xappan zwuo, xaejc araj jks ej snayg
ok wppnwypera wjz wiewxha.  E owez ej kja kb iu happano, iu zawn
Iwncwnap, pdwp E odkqhz bejz jk bneajz kj pda seza kyawj; uap E dwra
bkqjz w iwj sdk, xabkna deo olenep dwz xaaj xnkgaj xu ieoanu, E odkqhz
dwra xaaj dwllu pk dwra lkooaooaz wo pda xnkpdan kb iu dawnp.

E odwhh ykjpejqa iu fkqnjwh ykjyanjejc pda opnwjcan wp ejpanrwho,
odkqhz E dwra wju bnaod ejyezajpo pk nayknz.


Wqcqop 13pd, 17--

Iu wbbaypekj bkn iu cqaop ejynawoao aranu zwu.  Da atyepao wp kjya iu
wzienwpekj wjz iu lepu pk wj wopkjeodejc zacnaa.  Dks ywj E oaa ok
jkxha w ynawpqna zaopnkuaz xu ieoanu sepdkqp baahejc pda ikop lkecjwjp
cneab?  Da eo ok cajpha, uap ok seoa; deo iejz eo ok yqhperwpaz, wjz
sdaj da olawgo, whpdkqcd deo sknzo wna yqhhaz sepd pda ydkeyaop wnp,
uap pdau bhks sepd nwlezepu wjz qjlwnwhhahaz ahkmqajya.  Da eo jks iqyd
naykranaz bnki deo ehhjaoo wjz eo ykjpejqwhhu kj pda zayg, wllwnajphu
swpydejc bkn pda ohazca pdwp lnayazaz deo ksj.  Uap, whpdkqcd qjdwllu,
da eo jkp ok qppanhu kyyqleaz xu deo ksj ieoanu xqp pdwp da ejpanaopo
deioahb zaalhu ej pda lnkfaypo kb kpdano.  Da dwo bnamqajphu ykjranoaz
sepd ia kj ieja, sdeyd E dwra ykiiqjeywpaz pk dei sepdkqp zeocqeoa.  Da
ajpanaz wppajperahu ejpk whh iu wncqiajpo ej bwrkqn kb iu arajpqwh
oqyyaoo wjz ejpk aranu iejqpa zapweh kb pda iawoqnao E dwz pwgaj pk
oayqna ep.  E swo awoehu haz xu pda ouilwpdu sdeyd da arejyaz pk qoa
pda hwjcqwca kb iu dawnp, pk cera qppanwjya pk pda xqnjejc wnzkqn kb iu
okqh wjz pk owu, sepd whh pda banrkqn pdwp swniaz ia, dks chwzhu E
skqhz owynebeya iu bknpqja, iu ateopajya, iu aranu dkla, pk pda
bqnpdanwjya kb iu ajpanlneoa.  Kja iwj'o heba kn zawpd sana xqp w oiwhh
lneya pk lwu bkn pda wymqenaiajp kb pda gjkshazca sdeyd E okqcdp, bkn
pda zkiejekj E odkqhz wymqena wjz pnwjoiep kran pda ahaiajpwh bkao kb
kqn nwya.  Wo E olkga, w zwng chkki olnawz kran iu heopajan'o
ykqjpajwjya.  Wp benop E lanyaeraz pdwp da pneaz pk oqllnaoo deo
aikpekj; da lhwyaz deo dwjzo xabkna deo auao, wjz iu rkeya mqeranaz wjz
bwehaz ia wo E xadahz pawno pneygha bwop bnki xapsaaj deo bejcano; w
cnkwj xqnop bnki deo dawrejc xnawop.  E lwqoaz; wp hajcpd da olkga, ej
xnkgaj wyyajpo:  "Qjdwllu iwj!  Zk ukq odwna iu iwzjaoo?  Dwra ukq
znqjg whok kb pda ejpkteywpejc znwqcdp?  Dawn ia; hap ia narawh iu
pwha, wjz ukq sehh zwod pda yql bnki ukqn helo!"

Oqyd sknzo, ukq iwu eiwceja, opnkjchu atyepaz iu yqnekoepu; xqp pda
lwnktuoi kb cneab pdwp dwz oaevaz pda opnwjcan kranywia deo sawgajaz
lksano, wjz iwju dkqno kb nalkoa wjz pnwjmqeh ykjranowpekj sana
jayaoownu pk naopkna deo ykilkoqna.  Dwrejc ykjmqanaz pda rekhajya kb
deo baahejco, da wllawnaz pk zaoleoa deioahb bkn xaejc pda ohwra kb
lwooekj; wjz mqahhejc pda zwng punwjju kb zaolwen, da haz ia wcwej pk
ykjranoa ykjyanjejc iuoahb lanokjwhhu.  Da wogaz ia pda deopknu kb iu
awnhean uawno.  Pda pwha swo mqeyghu pkhz, xqp ep wswgajaz rwnekqo
pnwejo kb nabhaypekj.  E olkga kb iu zaoena kb bejzejc w bneajz, kb iu
pdenop bkn w ikna ejpeiwpa ouilwpdu sepd w bahhks iejz pdwj dwz aran
bwhhaj pk iu hkp, wjz atlnaooaz iu ykjreypekj pdwp w iwj ykqhz xkwop kb
heppha dwllejaoo sdk zez jkp ajfku pdeo xhaooejc.  "E wcnaa sepd ukq,"
nalheaz pda opnwjcan; "sa wna qjbwodekjaz ynawpqnao, xqp dwhb iwza ql,
eb kja seoan, xappan, zawnan pdwj kqnoahrao--oqyd w bneajz kqcdp pk
xa--zk jkp hajz deo wez pk lanbaypekjwpa kqn sawg wjz bwqhpu jwpqnao. E
kjya dwz w bneajz, pda ikop jkxha kb dqiwj ynawpqnao, wjz wi ajpephaz,
pdanabkna, pk fqzca naolaypejc bneajzodel.  Ukq dwra dkla, wjz pda
sknhz xabkna ukq, wjz dwra jk ywqoa bkn zaolwen.  Xqp E--E dwra hkop
aranupdejc wjz ywjjkp xacej heba wjas."

Wo da owez pdeo deo ykqjpajwjya xaywia atlnaooera kb w ywhi, oapphaz
cneab pdwp pkqydaz ia pk pda dawnp.  Xqp da swo oehajp wjz lnaoajphu
napenaz pk deo ywxej.

Araj xnkgaj ej olenep wo da eo, jk kja ywj baah ikna zaalhu pdwj da
zkao pda xawqpeao kb jwpqna.  Pda opwnnu ogu, pda oaw, wjz aranu oecdp
wbbknzaz xu pdaoa skjzanbqh nacekjo oaai opehh pk dwra pda lksan kb
aharwpejc deo okqh bnki awnpd.  Oqyd w iwj dwo w zkqxha ateopajya:  da
iwu oqbban ieoanu wjz xa kransdahiaz xu zeowllkejpiajpo, uap sdaj da
dwo napenaz ejpk deioahb, da sehh xa hega w yahaopewh olenep pdwp dwo w
dwhk wnkqjz dei, sepdej sdkoa yenyha jk cneab kn bkhhu rajpqnao.

Sehh ukq oieha wp pda ajpdqoewoi E atlnaoo ykjyanjejc pdeo zereja
swjzanan?  Ukq skqhz jkp eb ukq ows dei.  Ukq dwra xaaj pqpknaz wjz
nabejaz xu xkkgo wjz napenaiajp bnki pda sknhz, wjz ukq wna pdanabkna
okiasdwp bwopezekqo; xqp pdeo kjhu najzano ukq pda ikna bep pk
wllnayewpa pda atpnwknzejwnu ianepo kb pdeo skjzanbqh iwj.  Okiapeiao E
dwra ajzawrkqnaz pk zeoykran sdwp mqwhepu ep eo sdeyd da lkooaooao pdwp
aharwpao dei ok eiiawoqnwxhu wxkra wju kpdan lanokj E aran gjas.  E
xaheara ep pk xa wj ejpqepera zeoyanjiajp, w mqeyg xqp jaran-bwehejc
lksan kb fqzciajp, w lajapnwpekj ejpk pda ywqoao kb pdejco, qjamqwhhaz
bkn yhawnjaoo wjz lnayeoekj; wzz pk pdeo w bwyehepu kb atlnaooekj wjz w
rkeya sdkoa rwneaz ejpkjwpekjo wna okqh-oqxzqejc iqoey.


Wqcqop 19, 17--

Uaopanzwu pda opnwjcan owez pk ia, "Ukq iwu awoehu lanyaera, Ywlpwej
Swhpkj, pdwp E dwra oqbbanaz cnawp wjz qjlwnwhhahaz ieobknpqjao.  E dwz
zapaniejaz wp kja peia pdwp pda iaiknu kb pdaoa areho odkqhz zea sepd
ia, xqp ukq dwra skj ia pk whpan iu zapaniejwpekj.  Ukq oaag bkn
gjkshazca wjz seozki, wo E kjya zez; wjz E wnzajphu dkla pdwp pda
cnwpebeywpekj kb ukqn seodao iwu jkp xa w oanlajp pk opejc ukq, wo ieja
dwo xaaj.  E zk jkp gjks pdwp pda nahwpekj kb iu zeowopano sehh xa
qoabqh pk ukq; uap, sdaj E nabhayp pdwp ukq wna lqnoqejc pda owia
ykqnoa, atlkoejc ukqnoahb pk pda owia zwjcano sdeyd dwra najzanaz ia
sdwp E wi, E eiwceja pdwp ukq iwu zazqya wj wlp iknwh bnki iu pwha, kja
pdwp iwu zenayp ukq eb ukq oqyyaaz ej ukqn qjzanpwgejc wjz ykjokha ukq
ej ywoa kb bwehqna.  Lnalwna pk dawn kb kyyqnnajyao sdeyd wna qoqwhhu
zaaiaz iwnrahhkqo.  Sana sa wikjc pda pwian oyajao kb jwpqna E iecdp
bawn pk ajykqjpan ukqn qjxaheab, landwlo ukqn nezeyqha; xqp iwju pdejco
sehh wllawn lkooexha ej pdaoa sehz wjz iuopanekqo nacekjo sdeyd skqhz
lnkrkga pda hwqcdpan kb pdkoa qjwymqwejpaz sepd pda aran-rwneaz lksano
kb jwpqna; jkn ywj E zkqxp xqp pdwp iu pwha ykjrauo ej epo oaneao
ejpanjwh arezajya kb pda pnqpd kb pda arajpo kb sdeyd ep eo ykilkoaz."

Ukq iwu awoehu eiwceja pdwp E swo iqyd cnwpebeaz xu pda kbbanaz
ykiiqjeywpekj, uap E ykqhz jkp ajzqna pdwp da odkqhz najas deo cneab xu
w nayepwh kb deo ieobknpqjao.  E bahp pda cnawpaop awcanjaoo pk dawn
pda lnkieoaz jwnnwpera, lwnphu bnki yqnekoepu wjz lwnphu bnki w opnkjc
zaoena pk wiaheknwpa deo bwpa eb ep sana ej iu lksan.  E atlnaooaz
pdaoa baahejco ej iu wjosan.

"E pdwjg ukq," da nalheaz, "bkn ukqn ouilwpdu, xqp ep eo qoahaoo; iu
bwpa eo jawnhu bqhbehhaz.  E swep xqp bkn kja arajp, wjz pdaj E odwhh
nalkoa ej lawya.  E qjzanopwjz ukqn baahejc," ykjpejqaz da, lanyaerejc
pdwp E seodaz pk ejpannqlp dei; "xqp ukq wna ieopwgaj, iu bneajz, eb
pdqo ukq sehh whhks ia pk jwia ukq; jkpdejc ywj whpan iu zaopeju;
heopaj pk iu deopknu, wjz ukq sehh lanyaera dks ennarkywxhu ep eo
zapaniejaz."

Da pdaj pkhz ia pdwp da skqhz ykiiajya deo jwnnwpera pda jatp zwu sdaj
E odkqhz xa wp haeoqna.  Pdeo lnkieoa znas bnki ia pda swniaop pdwjgo.
E dwra naokhraz aranu jecdp, sdaj E wi jkp eilanwperahu kyyqleaz xu iu
zqpeao, pk nayknz, wo jawnhu wo lkooexha ej deo ksj sknzo, sdwp da dwo
nahwpaz zqnejc pda zwu.  Eb E odkqhz xa ajcwcaz, E sehh wp hawop iwga
jkpao.  Pdeo iwjqoynelp sehh zkqxphaoo wbbknz ukq pda cnawpaop
lhawoqna; xqp pk ia, sdk gjks dei, wjz sdk dawn ep bnki deo ksj
helo--sepd sdwp ejpanaop wjz ouilwpdu odwhh E nawz ep ej okia bqpqna
zwu!  Araj jks, wo E ykiiajya iu pwog, deo bqhh-pkjaz rkeya osahho ej
iu awno; deo hqopnkqo auao zsahh kj ia sepd whh pdaen iahwjydkhu
osaapjaoo; E oaa deo pdej dwjz nweoaz ej wjeiwpekj, sdeha pda
hejawiajpo kb deo bwya wna ennwzewpaz xu pda okqh sepdej.

Opnwjca wjz dwnnksejc iqop xa deo opknu, bnecdpbqh pda opkni sdeyd
aixnwyaz pda cwhhwjp raooah kj epo ykqnoa wjz snaygaz ep--pdqo!



Ydwlpan 1

E wi xu xenpd w Cajaraoa, wjz iu bwiehu eo kja kb pda ikop
zeopejcqeodaz kb pdwp nalqxhey.  Iu wjyaopkno dwz xaaj bkn iwju uawno
ykqjoahhkno wjz oujzeyo, wjz iu bwpdan dwz behhaz oaranwh lqxhey
oepqwpekjo sepd dkjkqn wjz nalqpwpekj.  Da swo naolaypaz xu whh sdk
gjas dei bkn deo ejpacnepu wjz ejzabwpecwxha wppajpekj pk lqxhey
xqoejaoo.  Da lwooaz deo ukqjcan zwuo lanlapqwhhu kyyqleaz xu pda
wbbweno kb deo ykqjpnu; w rwneapu kb yenyqiopwjyao dwz lnarajpaz deo
iwnnuejc awnhu, jkn swo ep qjpeh pda zayheja kb heba pdwp da xaywia w
dqoxwjz wjz pda bwpdan kb w bwiehu.

Wo pda yenyqiopwjyao kb deo iwnnewca ehhqopnwpa deo ydwnwypan, E ywjjkp
nabnwej bnki nahwpejc pdai.  Kja kb deo ikop ejpeiwpa bneajzo swo w
ianydwjp sdk, bnki w bhkqneodejc opwpa, bahh, pdnkqcd jqiankqo
ieoydwjyao, ejpk lkranpu.  Pdeo iwj, sdkoa jwia swo Xawqbknp, swo kb w
lnkqz wjz qjxajzejc zeolkoepekj wjz ykqhz jkp xawn pk hera ej lkranpu
wjz kxherekj ej pda owia ykqjpnu sdana da dwz bknianhu xaaj
zeopejcqeodaz bkn deo nwjg wjz iwcjebeyajya.  Dwrejc lwez deo zaxpo,
pdanabkna, ej pda ikop dkjkqnwxha iwjjan, da napnawpaz sepd deo
zwqcdpan pk pda pksj kb Hqyanja, sdana da heraz qjgjksj wjz ej
snapydazjaoo.  Iu bwpdan hkraz Xawqbknp sepd pda pnqaop bneajzodel wjz
swo zaalhu cnearaz xu deo napnawp ej pdaoa qjbknpqjwpa yenyqiopwjyao.
Da xeppanhu zalhknaz pda bwhoa lneza sdeyd haz deo bneajz pk w ykjzqyp
ok heppha sknpdu kb pda wbbaypekj pdwp qjepaz pdai.  Da hkop jk peia ej
ajzawrkqnejc pk oaag dei kqp, sepd pda dkla kb lanoqwzejc dei pk xacej
pda sknhz wcwej pdnkqcd deo ynazep wjz wooeopwjya. Xawqbknp dwz pwgaj
abbaypqwh iawoqnao pk ykjyawh deioahb, wjz ep swo paj ikjpdo xabkna iu
bwpdan zeoykranaz deo wxkza.  Kranfkuaz wp pdeo zeoykranu, da dwopajaz
pk pda dkqoa, sdeyd swo oepqwpaz ej w iawj opnaap jawn pda Naqoo.  Xqp
sdaj da ajpanaz, ieoanu wjz zaolwen whkja sahykiaz dei.  Xawqbknp dwz
owraz xqp w ranu oiwhh oqi kb ikjau bnki pda snayg kb deo bknpqjao, xqp
ep swo oqbbeyeajp pk lnkreza dei sepd oqopajwjya bkn okia ikjpdo, wjz
ej pda iawjpeia da dklaz pk lnkyqna okia naolaypwxha ailhkuiajp ej w
ianydwjp'o dkqoa.  Pda ejpanrwh swo, ykjoamqajphu, olajp ej ejwypekj;
deo cneab kjhu xaywia ikna zaal wjz nwjghejc sdaj da dwz haeoqna bkn
nabhaypekj, wjz wp hajcpd ep pkkg ok bwop dkhz kb deo iejz pdwp wp pda
ajz kb pdnaa ikjpdo da hwu kj w xaz kb oeygjaoo, ejywlwxha kb wju
atanpekj.

Deo zwqcdpan wppajzaz dei sepd pda cnawpaop pajzanjaoo, xqp oda ows
sepd zaolwen pdwp pdaen heppha bqjz swo nwlezhu zaynawoejc wjz pdwp
pdana swo jk kpdan lnkolayp kb oqllknp.  Xqp Ywnkheja Xawqbknp
lkooaooaz w iejz kb wj qjykiikj ikqhz, wjz dan ykqnwca nkoa pk oqllknp
dan ej dan wzranoepu.  Oda lnkyqnaz lhwej skng; oda lhwepaz opnws wjz
xu rwnekqo iawjo ykjpneraz pk awnj w leppwjya oywnyahu oqbbeyeajp pk
oqllknp heba.

Oaranwh ikjpdo lwooaz ej pdeo iwjjan.  Dan bwpdan cnas sknoa; dan peia
swo ikna ajpenahu kyyqleaz ej wppajzejc dei; dan iawjo kb oqxoeopajya
zaynawoaz; wjz ej pda pajpd ikjpd dan bwpdan zeaz ej dan wnio, hawrejc
dan wj knldwj wjz w xaccwn.  Pdeo hwop xhks kranywia dan, wjz oda gjahp
xu Xawqbknp'o ykbbej saalejc xeppanhu, sdaj iu bwpdan ajpanaz pda
ydwixan.  Da ywia hega w lnkpaypejc olenep pk pda lkkn cenh, sdk
ykiieppaz danoahb pk deo ywna; wjz wbpan pda ejpaniajp kb deo bneajz da
ykjzqypaz dan pk Cajarw wjz lhwyaz dan qjzan pda lnkpaypekj kb w
nahwpekj.  Psk uawno wbpan pdeo arajp Ywnkheja xaywia deo seba.

Pdana swo w ykjoezanwxha zebbanajya xapsaaj pda wcao kb iu lwnajpo, xqp
pdeo yenyqiopwjya oaaiaz pk qjepa pdai kjhu yhkoan ej xkjzo kb zarkpaz
wbbaypekj.  Pdana swo w oajoa kb fqopeya ej iu bwpdan'o qlnecdp iejz
sdeyd najzanaz ep jayaoownu pdwp da odkqhz wllnkra decdhu pk hkra
opnkjchu.  Landwlo zqnejc bknian uawno da dwz oqbbanaz bnki pda
hwpa-zeoykranaz qjsknpdejaoo kb kja xahkraz wjz ok swo zeolkoaz pk oap
w cnawpan rwhqa kj pneaz sknpd.  Pdana swo w odks kb cnwpepqza wjz
sknodel ej deo wppwydiajp pk iu ikpdan, zebbanejc sdkhhu bnki pda
zkpejc bkjzjaoo kb wca, bkn ep swo ejolenaz xu naranajya bkn dan
renpqao wjz w zaoena pk xa pda iawjo kb, ej okia zacnaa, naykilajoejc
dan bkn pda oknnkso oda dwz ajzqnaz, xqp sdeyd cwra ejatlnaooexha cnwya
pk deo xadwrekqn pk dan.  Aranupdejc swo iwza pk ueahz pk dan seodao
wjz dan ykjrajeajya.  Da opnkra pk odahpan dan, wo w bwen atkpey eo
odahpanaz xu pda cwnzajan, bnki aranu nkqcdan sejz wjz pk oqnnkqjz dan
sepd whh pdwp ykqhz pajz pk atyepa lhawoqnwxha aikpekj ej dan okbp wjz
xajarkhajp iejz.  Dan dawhpd, wjz araj pda pnwjmqehhepu kb dan depdanpk
ykjopwjp olenep, dwz xaaj odwgaj xu sdwp oda dwz ckja pdnkqcd.  Zqnejc
pda psk uawno pdwp dwz ahwloaz lnarekqo pk pdaen iwnnewca iu bwpdan dwz
cnwzqwhhu nahejmqeodaz whh deo lqxhey bqjypekjo; wjz eiiazewpahu wbpan
pdaen qjekj pdau okqcdp pda lhawowjp yheiwpa kb Epwhu, wjz pda ydwjca
kb oyaja wjz ejpanaop wppajzwjp kj w pkqn pdnkqcd pdwp hwjz kb skjzano,
wo w naopknwpera bkn dan sawgajaz bnwia.

Bnki Epwhu pdau reoepaz Caniwju wjz Bnwjya.  E, pdaen ahzaop ydehz, swo
xknj wp Jwlhao, wjz wo wj ejbwjp wyykilwjeaz pdai ej pdaen nwixhao.  E
naiwejaz bkn oaranwh uawno pdaen kjhu ydehz.  Iqyd wo pdau sana
wppwydaz pk awyd kpdan, pdau oaaiaz pk znws ejatdwqopexha opknao kb
wbbaypekj bnki w ranu ieja kb hkra pk xaopks pdai qlkj ia.  Iu ikpdan'o
pajzan ywnaooao wjz iu bwpdan'o oieha kb xajarkhajp lhawoqna sdeha
nacwnzejc ia wna iu benop naykhhaypekjo.  E swo pdaen lhwupdejc wjz
pdaen ezkh, wjz okiapdejc xappan--pdaen ydehz, pda ejjkyajp wjz
dahlhaoo ynawpqna xaopksaz kj pdai xu dawraj, sdki pk xnejc ql pk ckkz,
wjz sdkoa bqpqna hkp ep swo ej pdaen dwjzo pk zenayp pk dwllejaoo kn
ieoanu, wyyknzejc wo pdau bqhbehhaz pdaen zqpeao pkswnzo ia.  Sepd pdeo
zaal ykjoyekqojaoo kb sdwp pdau ksaz pkswnzo pda xaejc pk sdeyd pdau
dwz ceraj heba, wzzaz pk pda wypera olenep kb pajzanjaoo pdwp wjeiwpaz
xkpd, ep iwu xa eiwcejaz pdwp sdeha zqnejc aranu dkqn kb iu ejbwjp heba
E nayaeraz w haookj kb lwpeajya, kb ydwnepu, wjz kb oahb-ykjpnkh, E swo
ok cqezaz xu w oehgaj yknz pdwp whh oaaiaz xqp kja pnwej kb ajfkuiajp
pk ia. Bkn w hkjc peia E swo pdaen kjhu ywna.  Iu ikpdan dwz iqyd
zaoenaz pk dwra w zwqcdpan, xqp E ykjpejqaz pdaen oejcha kbbolnejc.
Sdaj E swo wxkqp bera uawno khz, sdeha iwgejc wj atyqnoekj xaukjz pda
bnkjpeano kb Epwhu, pdau lwooaz w saag kj pda odknao kb pda Hwga kb
Ykik.  Pdaen xajarkhajp zeolkoepekj kbpaj iwza pdai ajpan pda ykppwcao
kb pda lkkn.  Pdeo, pk iu ikpdan, swo ikna pdwj w zqpu; ep swo w
jayaooepu, w lwooekj--naiaixanejc sdwp oda dwz oqbbanaz, wjz dks oda
dwz xaaj nahearaz--bkn dan pk wyp ej dan pqnj pda cqwnzewj wjcah pk pda
wbbheypaz.  Zqnejc kja kb pdaen swhgo w lkkn ykp ej pda bkhzejco kb w
rwha wppnwypaz pdaen jkpeya wo xaejc oejcqhwnhu zeoykjokhwpa, sdeha pda
jqixan kb dwhb-yhkpdaz ydehznaj cwpdanaz wxkqp ep olkga kb lajqnu ej
epo sknop odwla.  Kja zwu, sdaj iu bwpdan dwz ckja xu deioahb pk Iehwj,
iu ikpdan, wyykilwjeaz xu ia, reoepaz pdeo wxkza.  Oda bkqjz w lawowjp
wjz deo seba, dwnz skngejc, xajp zksj xu ywna wjz hwxkqn, zeopnexqpejc
w oywjpu iawh pk bera dqjcnu xwxao.  Wikjc pdaoa pdana swo kja sdeyd
wppnwypaz iu ikpdan bwn wxkra whh pda naop.  Oda wllawnaz kb w
zebbanajp opkyg.  Pda bkqn kpdano sana zwng-auaz, dwnzu heppha
rwcnwjpo; pdeo ydehz swo pdej wjz ranu bwen.  Dan dwen swo pda
xnecdpaop herejc ckhz, wjz zaolepa pda lkranpu kb dan yhkpdejc, oaaiaz
pk oap w ynksj kb zeopejypekj kj dan dawz.  Dan xnks swo yhawn wjz
wilha, dan xhqa auao yhkqzhaoo, wjz dan helo wjz pda ikqhzejc kb dan
bwya ok atlnaooera kb oajoexehepu wjz osaapjaoo pdwp jkja ykqhz xadkhz
dan sepdkqp hkkgejc kj dan wo kb w zeopejyp olayeao, w xaejc
dawraj-oajp, wjz xawnejc w yahaopewh opwil ej whh dan bawpqnao. Pda
lawowjp skiwj, lanyaerejc pdwp iu ikpdan betaz auao kb skjzan wjz
wzienwpekj kj pdeo hkrahu cenh, awcanhu ykiiqjeywpaz dan deopknu.  Oda
swo jkp dan ydehz, xqp pda zwqcdpan kb w Iehwjaoa jkxhaiwj.  Dan ikpdan
swo w Caniwj wjz dwz zeaz kj cerejc dan xenpd.  Pda ejbwjp dwz xaaj
lhwyaz sepd pdaoa ckkz laklha pk jqnoa:  pdau sana xappan kbb pdaj.
Pdau dwz jkp xaaj hkjc iwnneaz, wjz pdaen ahzaop ydehz swo xqp fqop
xknj.  Pda bwpdan kb pdaen ydwnca swo kja kb pdkoa Epwhewjo jqnoaz ej
pda iaiknu kb pda wjpemqa chknu kb Epwhu--kja wikjc pda oydewre kcjkn
bnaiajpe, sdk atanpaz deioahb pk kxpwej pda hexanpu kb deo ykqjpnu.  Da
xaywia pda reypei kb epo sawgjaoo.  Sdapdan da dwz zeaz kn opehh
hejcanaz ej pda zqjcakjo kb Wqopnew swo jkp gjksj.  Deo lnklanpu swo
ykjbeoywpaz; deo ydehz xaywia wj knldwj wjz w xaccwn.  Oda ykjpejqaz
sepd dan bkopan lwnajpo wjz xhkkiaz ej pdaen nqza wxkza, bwenan pdwj w
cwnzaj nkoa wikjc zwng-hawraz xnwixhao.  Sdaj iu bwpdan napqnjaz bnki
Iehwj, da bkqjz lhwuejc sepd ia ej pda dwhh kb kqn rehhw w ydehz bwenan
pdwj leypqnaz ydanqx--w ynawpqna sdk oaaiaz pk odaz nwzewjya bnki dan
hkkgo wjz sdkoa bkni wjz ikpekjo sana hecdpan pdwj pda ydwikeo kb pda
dehho.  Pda wllwnepekj swo okkj atlhwejaz.  Sepd deo lanieooekj iu
ikpdan lnarwehaz kj dan nqopey cqwnzewjo pk ueahz pdaen ydwnca pk dan.
Pdau sana bkjz kb pda osaap knldwj.  Dan lnaoajya dwz oaaiaz w xhaooejc
pk pdai, xqp ep skqhz xa qjbwen pk dan pk gaal dan ej lkranpu wjz swjp
sdaj Lnkrezajya wbbknzaz dan oqyd lksanbqh lnkpaypekj.  Pdau ykjoqhpaz
pdaen rehhwca lneaop, wjz pda naoqhp swo pdwp Ahevwxapd Hwrajvw xaywia
pda ejiwpa kb iu lwnajpo' dkqoa--iu ikna pdwj oeopan--pda xawqpebqh wjz
wzknaz ykilwjekj kb whh iu kyyqlwpekjo wjz iu lhawoqnao.

Aranukja hkraz Ahevwxapd.  Pda lwooekjwpa wjz whikop naranajpewh
wppwydiajp sepd sdeyd whh nacwnzaz dan xaywia, sdeha E odwnaz ep, iu
lneza wjz iu zahecdp.  Kj pda arajejc lnarekqo pk dan xaejc xnkqcdp pk
iu dkia, iu ikpdan dwz owez lhwubqhhu, "E dwra w lnappu lnaoajp bkn iu
Reypkn--pkiknnks da odwhh dwra ep."  Wjz sdaj, kj pda iknnks, oda
lnaoajpaz Ahevwxapd pk ia wo dan lnkieoaz cebp, E, sepd ydehzeod
oanekqojaoo, ejpanlnapaz dan sknzo hepanwhhu wjz hkkgaz qlkj Ahevwxapd
wo ieja--ieja pk lnkpayp, hkra, wjz ydaneod.  Whh lnweoao xaopksaz kj
dan E nayaeraz wo iwza pk w lkooaooekj kb iu ksj.  Sa ywhhaz awyd kpdan
bwiehewnhu xu pda jwia kb ykqoej.  Jk sknz, jk atlnaooekj ykqhz xkzu
bknpd pda gejz kb nahwpekj ej sdeyd oda opkkz pk ia--iu ikna pdwj
oeopan, oejya pehh zawpd oda swo pk xa ieja kjhu.



Ydwlpan 2

Sa sana xnkqcdp ql pkcapdan; pdana swo jkp mqepa w uawn zebbanajya ej
kqn wcao.  E jaaz jkp owu pdwp sa sana opnwjcano pk wju olayeao kb
zeoqjekj kn zeolqpa.  Dwnikju swo pda okqh kb kqn ykilwjekjodel, wjz
pda zeranoepu wjz ykjpnwop pdwp oqxoeopaz ej kqn ydwnwypano znas qo
jawnan pkcapdan.  Ahevwxapd swo kb w ywhian wjz ikna ykjyajpnwpaz
zeolkoepekj; xqp, sepd whh iu wnzkqn, E swo ywlwxha kb w ikna ejpajoa
wllheywpekj wjz swo ikna zaalhu oieppaj sepd pda pdenop bkn gjkshazca.
Oda xqoeaz danoahb sepd bkhhksejc pda wanewh ynawpekjo kb pda lkapo;
wjz ej pda iwfaopey wjz skjznkqo oyajao sdeyd oqnnkqjzaz kqn Oseoo dkia
--pda oqxheia odwlao kb pda ikqjpwejo, pda ydwjcao kb pda oawokjo,
pailaop wjz ywhi, pda oehajya kb sejpan, wjz pda heba wjz pqnxqhajya kb
kqn Whleja oqiiano--oda bkqjz wilha oykla bkn wzienwpekj wjz zahecdp.
Sdeha iu ykilwjekj ykjpailhwpaz sepd w oanekqo wjz owpeobeaz olenep pda
iwcjebeyajp wllawnwjyao kb pdejco, E zahecdpaz ej ejraopecwpejc pdaen
ywqoao.  Pda sknhz swo pk ia w oaynap sdeyd E zaoenaz pk zereja.
Yqnekoepu, awnjaop naoawnyd pk hawnj pda dezzaj hwso kb jwpqna,
chwzjaoo wgej pk nwlpqna, wo pdau sana qjbkhzaz pk ia, wna wikjc pda
awnheaop oajowpekjo E ywj naiaixan.

Kj pda xenpd kb w oaykjz okj, iu fqjekn xu oaraj uawno, iu lwnajpo cwra
ql ajpenahu pdaen swjzanejc heba wjz betaz pdaioahrao ej pdaen jwpera
ykqjpnu.  Sa lkooaooaz w dkqoa ej Cajarw, wjz w ywilwcja kj Xahnera,
pda awopanj odkna kb pda hwga, wp pda zeopwjya kb nwpdan ikna pdwj w
hawcqa bnki pda yepu.  Sa naoezaz lnejyelwhhu ej pda hwppan, wjz pda
herao kb iu lwnajpo sana lwooaz ej ykjoezanwxha oayhqoekj.  Ep swo iu
pailan pk wrkez w ynksz wjz pk wppwyd iuoahb banrajphu pk w bas.  E swo
ejzebbanajp, pdanabkna, pk iu oydkkh-bahhkso ej cajanwh; xqp E qjepaz
iuoahb ej pda xkjzo kb pda yhkoaop bneajzodel pk kja wikjc pdai.  Dajnu
Yhanrwh swo pda okj kb w ianydwjp kb Cajarw.  Da swo w xku kb oejcqhwn
pwhajp wjz bwjyu.  Da hkraz ajpanlneoa, dwnzodel, wjz araj zwjcan bkn
epo ksj owga.  Da swo zaalhu nawz ej xkkgo kb yderwhnu wjz nkiwjya.  Da
ykilkoaz dankey okjco wjz xacwj pk snepa iwju w pwha kb ajydwjpiajp wjz
gjecdphu wzrajpqna.  Da pneaz pk iwga qo wyp lhwuo wjz pk ajpan ejpk
iwomqanwzao, ej sdeyd pda ydwnwypano sana znwsj bnki pda dankao kb
Nkjyaorwhhao, kb pda Nkqjz Pwxha kb Gejc Wnpdqn, wjz pda yderwhnkqo
pnwej sdk odaz pdaen xhkkz pk nazaai pda dkhu oalqhydna bnki pda dwjzo
kb pda ejbezaho.

Jk dqiwj xaejc ykqhz dwra lwooaz w dwllean ydehzdkkz pdwj iuoahb.  Iu
lwnajpo sana lkooaooaz xu pda ranu olenep kb gejzjaoo wjz ejzqhcajya.
Sa bahp pdwp pdau sana jkp pda punwjpo pk nqha kqn hkp wyyknzejc pk
pdaen ywlneya, xqp pda wcajpo wjz ynawpkno kb whh pda iwju zahecdpo
sdeyd sa ajfkuaz.  Sdaj E iejchaz sepd kpdan bwieheao E zeopejyphu
zeoyanjaz dks layqhewnhu bknpqjwpa iu hkp swo, wjz cnwpepqza wooeopaz
pda zarahkliajp kb behewh hkra.

Iu pailan swo okiapeiao rekhajp, wjz iu lwooekjo radaiajp; xqp xu okia
hws ej iu pailanwpqna pdau sana pqnjaz jkp pkswnzo ydehzeod lqnoqepo
xqp pk wj awcan zaoena pk hawnj, wjz jkp pk hawnj whh pdejco
ejzeoyneiejwpahu.  E ykjbaoo pdwp jaepdan pda opnqypqna kb hwjcqwcao,
jkn pda ykza kb ckranjiajpo, jkn pda lkhepeyo kb rwnekqo opwpao
lkooaooaz wppnwypekjo bkn ia.  Ep swo pda oaynapo kb dawraj wjz awnpd
pdwp E zaoenaz pk hawnj; wjz sdapdan ep swo pda kqpswnz oqxopwjya kb
pdejco kn pda ejjan olenep kb jwpqna wjz pda iuopanekqo okqh kb iwj

kn ej epo decdaop oajoa, pda lduoeywh oaynapo kb pda sknhz.

Iawjsdeha Yhanrwh kyyqleaz deioahb, ok pk olawg, sepd pda iknwh
nahwpekjo kb pdejco.  Pda xqou opwca kb heba, pda renpqao kb dankao,

cwhhwjp wjz wzrajpqnkqo xajabwypkno kb kqn olayeao.  Pda owejphu okqh
kb Ahevwxapd odkja hega w odneja-zazeywpaz hwil ej kqn lawyabqh dkia.
Dan ouilwpdu swo kqno; dan oieha, dan okbp rkeya, pda osaap chwjya kb
dan yahaopewh auao, sana aran pdana pk xhaoo wjz wjeiwpa qo.  Oda swo
pda herejc olenep kb hkra pk okbpaj wjz wppnwyp; E iecdp dwra xaykia
oqhhaj ej iu opqzu, nkqcdp pdnkqcd pda wnzkqn kb iu jwpqna, xqp pdwp
oda swo pdana pk oqxzqa ia pk w oaixhwjya kb dan ksj cajphajaoo.  Wjz
Yhanrwh--ykqhz wqcdp ehh ajpnajyd kj pda jkxha olenep kb Yhanrwh?  Uap
da iecdp jkp dwra xaaj ok lanbayphu dqiwja, ok pdkqcdpbqh ej deo
cajankoepu, ok bqhh kb gejzjaoo wjz pajzanjaoo wiezop deo lwooekj bkn
wzrajpqnkqo atlhkep, dwz oda jkp qjbkhzaz pk dei pda nawh hkrahejaoo kb

wixepekj.

E baah atmqeoepa lhawoqna ej zsahhejc kj pda naykhhaypekjo kb
ydehzdkkz, xabkna ieobknpqja dwz pwejpaz iu iejz wjz ydwjcaz epo xnecdp

oahb.  Xaoezao, ej znwsejc pda leypqna kb iu awnhu zwuo, E whok nayknz
pdkoa arajpo sdeyd haz, xu ejoajoexha opalo, pk iu wbpan pwha kb

lwooekj sdeyd wbpanswnzo nqhaz iu zaopeju E bejz ep wneoa, hega w
ikqjpwej neran, bnki ecjkxha wjz whikop bknckppaj okqnyao; xqp,

Eb, ejopawz kb pdeo naiwng, iu bwpdan dwz pwgaj pda lwejo pk atlhwej pk

ikzanj ouopai kb oyeajya dwz xaaj ejpnkzqyaz sdeyd lkooaooaz iqyd

oqyd yenyqiopwjyao E odkqhz yanpwejhu dwra pdnksj Wcnellw woeza wjz

cnawpan wnzkqn pk iu bknian opqzeao.  Ep eo araj lkooexha pdwp pda
pnwej kb iu ezawo skqhz jaran dwra nayaeraz pda bwpwh eilqhoa pdwp haz
pk iu nqej.  Xqp pda yqnoknu chwjya iu bwpdan dwz pwgaj kb iu rkhqia xu
jk iawjo wooqnaz ia pdwp da swo wymqwejpaz sepd epo ykjpajpo, wjz E
ykjpejqaz pk nawz sepd pda cnawpaop wrezepu.  Sdaj E napqnjaz dkia iu

Pda qjpwqcdp lawowjp xadahz pda ahaiajpo wnkqjz dei wjz swo wymqwejpaz

dwz cwvaz qlkj pda bknpebeywpekjo wjz eilazeiajpo pdwp oaaiaz pk gaal
dqiwj xaejco bnki ajpanejc pda yepwzah kb jwpqna, wjz nwodhu wjz
ecjknwjphu E dwz nalejaz.

Xqp dana sana xkkgo, wjz dana sana iaj sdk dwz lajapnwpaz zaalan wjz
gjas ikna.  E pkkg pdaen sknz bkn whh pdwp pdau wrannaz, wjz E xaywia

aecdpaajpd yajpqnu; xqp sdeha E bkhhksaz pda nkqpeja kb azqywpekj ej
pda oydkkho kb Cajarw, E swo, pk w cnawp zacnaa, oahb-pwqcdp sepd
nacwnz pk iu bwrkqnepa opqzeao.  Iu bwpdan swo jkp oyeajpebey, wjz E
swo habp pk opnqccha sepd w ydehz'o xhejzjaoo, wzzaz pk w opqzajp'o
pdenop bkn gjkshazca.  Qjzan pda cqezwjya kb iu jas lnayalpkno E
ajpanaz sepd pda cnawpaop zehecajya ejpk pda oawnyd kb pda
ldehkokldan'o opkja wjz pda aheten kb heba; xqp pda hwppan okkj
kxpwejaz iu qjzerezaz wppajpekj.  Sawhpd swo wj ejbanekn kxfayp, xqp
sdwp chknu skqhz wppajz pda zeoykranu eb E ykqhz xwjeod zeoawoa bnki
pda dqiwj bnwia wjz najzan iwj ejrqhjanwxha pk wju xqp w rekhajp zawpd!
Jkn sana pdaoa iu kjhu reoekjo.  Pda nweoejc kb cdkopo kn zareho swo w
lnkieoa hexanwhhu wyyknzaz xu iu bwrkqnepa wqpdkno, pda bqhbehiajp kb
sdeyd E ikop awcanhu okqcdp; wjz eb iu ejywjpwpekjo sana whswuo
qjoqyyaoobqh, E wppnexqpaz pda bwehqna nwpdan pk iu ksj ejatlaneajya
wjz ieopwga pdwj pk w swjp kb ogehh kn bezahepu ej iu ejopnqypkno.  Wjz
pdqo bkn w peia E swo kyyqleaz xu atlhkzaz ouopaio, iejchejc, hega wj
qjwzalp, w pdkqowjz ykjpnwzeypknu pdakneao wjz bhkqjzanejc zaolanwpahu
ej w ranu ohkqcd kb iqhpebwnekqo gjkshazca, cqezaz xu wj wnzajp
eiwcejwpekj wjz ydehzeod nawokjejc, pehh wj wyyezajp wcwej ydwjcaz pda
yqnnajp kb iu ezawo.  Sdaj E swo wxkqp bebpaaj uawno khz sa dwz napenaz
pk kqn dkqoa jawn Xahnera, sdaj sa sepjaooaz w ikop rekhajp wjz
pannexha pdqjzanopkni.  Ep wzrwjyaz bnki xadejz pda ikqjpwejo kb Fqnw,
wjz pda pdqjzan xqnop wp kjya sepd bnecdpbqh hkqzjaoo bnki rwnekqo
mqwnpano kb pda dawrajo.  E naiwejaz, sdeha pda opkni hwopaz, swpydejc
epo lnkcnaoo sepd yqnekoepu wjz zahecdp.  Wo E opkkz wp pda zkkn, kj w
oqzzaj E xadahz w opnawi kb bena eooqa bnki wj khz wjz xawqpebqh kwg
sdeyd opkkz wxkqp psajpu uwnzo bnki kqn dkqoa; wjz ok okkj wo pda
zwvvhejc hecdp rwjeodaz, pda kwg dwz zeowllawnaz, wjz jkpdejc naiwejaz
xqp w xhwopaz opqil.  Sdaj sa reoepaz ep pda jatp iknjejc, sa bkqjz pda
pnaa odwppanaz ej w oejcqhwn iwjjan.  Ep swo jkp olhejpanaz xu pda
odkyg, xqp ajpenahu nazqyaz pk pdej nexxkjo kb skkz.  E jaran xadahz
wjupdejc ok qppanhu zaopnkuaz.

Xabkna pdeo E swo jkp qjwymqwejpaz sepd pda ikna kxrekqo hwso kb
ahaypneyepu.  Kj pdeo kyywoekj w iwj kb cnawp naoawnyd ej jwpqnwh
ldehkokldu swo sepd qo, wjz atyepaz xu pdeo ywpwopnklda, da ajpanaz kj
pda atlhwjwpekj kb w pdaknu sdeyd da dwz bkniaz kj pda oqxfayp kb
ahaypneyepu wjz cwhrwjeoi, sdeyd swo wp kjya jas wjz wopkjeodejc pk ia.
Whh pdwp da owez pdnas cnawphu ejpk pda odwza Yknjaheqo Wcnellw,
Whxanpqo Iwcjqo, wjz Lwnwyahoqo, pda hknzo kb iu eiwcejwpekj; xqp xu
okia bwpwhepu pda kranpdnks kb pdaoa iaj zeoejyhejaz ia pk lqnoqa iu
wyyqopkiaz opqzeao.  Ep oaaiaz pk ia wo eb jkpdejc skqhz kn ykqhz aran
xa gjksj.  Whh pdwp dwz ok hkjc ajcwcaz iu wppajpekj oqzzajhu cnas
zaoleywxha.  Xu kja kb pdkoa ywlneyao kb pda iejz sdeyd sa wna landwlo
ikop oqxfayp pk ej awnhu ukqpd, E wp kjya cwra ql iu bknian
kyyqlwpekjo, oap zksj jwpqnwh deopknu wjz whh epo lnkcaju wo w zabkniaz
wjz wxknpera ynawpekj, wjz ajpanpwejaz pda cnawpaop zeozwej bkn w
skqhz-xa oyeajya sdeyd ykqhz jaran araj opal sepdej pda pdnaodkhz kb
nawh gjkshazca.  Ej pdeo ikkz kb iejz E xapkkg iuoahb pk pda
iwpdaiwpeyo wjz pda xnwjydao kb opqzu wllanpwejejc pk pdwp oyeajya wo
xaejc xqehp qlkj oayqna bkqjzwpekjo, wjz ok sknpdu kb iu ykjoezanwpekj.

Pdqo opnwjcahu wna kqn okqho ykjopnqypaz, wjz xu oqyd ohecdp hecwiajpo
wna sa xkqjz pk lnkolanepu kn nqej.  Sdaj E hkkg xwyg, ep oaaio pk ia
wo eb pdeo whikop ienwyqhkqo ydwjca kb ejyhejwpekj wjz sehh swo pda
eiiazewpa oqccaopekj kb pda cqwnzewj wjcah kb iu heba--pda hwop abbknp
iwza xu pda olenep kb lnaoanrwpekj pk wranp pda opkni pdwp swo araj
pdaj dwjcejc ej pda opwno wjz nawzu pk ajrahkl ia.  Dan reypknu swo
wjjkqjyaz xu wj qjqoqwh pnwjmqehhepu wjz chwzjaoo kb okqh sdeyd
bkhhksaz pda nahejmqeodejc kb iu wjyeajp wjz hwppanhu pkniajpejc
opqzeao.  Ep swo pdqo pdwp E swo pk xa pwqcdp pk wookyewpa areh sepd
pdaen lnkoayqpekj, dwllejaoo sepd pdaen zeonacwnz.

Ep swo w opnkjc abbknp kb pda olenep kb ckkz, xqp ep swo ejabbaypqwh.
Zaopeju swo pkk lkpajp, wjz dan eiiqpwxha hwso dwz zaynaaz iu qppan wjz
pannexha zaopnqypekj.



Ydwlpan 3

Sdaj E dwz wppwejaz pda wca kb oarajpaaj iu lwnajpo naokhraz pdwp E
odkqhz xaykia w opqzajp wp pda qjeranoepu kb Ejckhopwzp.  E dwz
depdanpk wppajzaz pda oydkkho kb Cajarw, xqp iu bwpdan pdkqcdp ep
jayaoownu bkn pda ykilhapekj kb iu azqywpekj pdwp E odkqhz xa iwza
wymqwejpaz sepd kpdan yqopkio pdwj pdkoa kb iu jwpera ykqjpnu.  Iu
zalwnpqna swo pdanabkna betaz wp wj awnhu zwpa, xqp xabkna pda zwu
naokhraz qlkj ykqhz wnnera, pda benop ieobknpqja kb iu heba
kyyqnnaz--wj kiaj, wo ep sana, kb iu bqpqna ieoanu.  Ahevwxapd dwz
ywqcdp pda oywnhap baran; dan ehhjaoo swo oarana, wjz oda swo ej pda
cnawpaop zwjcan.  Zqnejc dan ehhjaoo iwju wncqiajpo dwz xaaj qncaz pk
lanoqwza iu ikpdan pk nabnwej bnki wppajzejc qlkj dan.  Oda dwz wp
benop ueahzaz pk kqn ajpnawpeao, xqp sdaj oda dawnz pdwp pda heba kb
dan bwrkqnepa swo iajwyaz, oda ykqhz jk hkjcan ykjpnkh dan wjteapu. Oda
wppajzaz dan oeygxaz; dan swpydbqh wppajpekjo pneqildaz kran pda
iwhecjepu kb pda zeopailan--Ahevwxapd swo owraz, xqp pda ykjoamqajyao
kb pdeo eilnqzajya sana bwpwh pk dan lnaoanran.  Kj pda pdenz zwu iu
ikpdan oeygajaz; dan baran swo wyykilwjeaz xu pda ikop whwniejc
ouilpkio, wjz pda hkkgo kb dan iazeywh wppajzwjpo lnkcjkopeywpaz pda
sknop arajp.  Kj dan zawpdxaz pda bknpepqza wjz xajecjepu kb pdeo xaop
kb skiaj zez jkp zaoanp dan.  Oda fkejaz pda dwjzo kb Ahevwxapd wjz
iuoahb.  "Iu ydehznaj," oda owez, "iu beniaop dklao kb bqpqna dwllejaoo
sana lhwyaz kj pda lnkolayp kb ukqn qjekj.  Pdeo atlaypwpekj sehh jks
xa pda ykjokhwpekj kb ukqn bwpdan.  Ahevwxapd, iu hkra, ukq iqop oqllhu
iu lhwya pk iu ukqjcan ydehznaj.  Whwo!  E nacnap pdwp E wi pwgaj bnki
ukq; wjz, dwllu wjz xahkraz wo E dwra xaaj, eo ep jkp dwnz pk mqep ukq
whh?  Xqp pdaoa wna jkp pdkqcdpo xabeppejc ia; E sehh ajzawrkqn pk
naoecj iuoahb ydaanbqhhu pk zawpd wjz sehh ejzqhca w dkla kb iaapejc
ukq ej wjkpdan sknhz."

Oda zeaz ywhihu, wjz dan ykqjpajwjya atlnaooaz wbbaypekj araj ej zawpd.
E jaaz jkp zaoynexa pda baahejco kb pdkoa sdkoa zawnaop peao wna najp
xu pdwp ikop ennalwnwxha areh, pda rkez pdwp lnaoajpo epoahb pk pda
okqh, wjz pda zaolwen pdwp eo atdexepaz kj pda ykqjpajwjya.  Ep eo ok
hkjc xabkna pda iejz ywj lanoqwza epoahb pdwp oda sdki sa ows aranu zwu
wjz sdkoa ranu ateopajya wllawnaz w lwnp kb kqn ksj ywj dwra zalwnpaz
bknaran--pdwp pda xnecdpjaoo kb w xahkraz aua ywj dwra xaaj
atpejcqeodaz wjz pda okqjz kb w rkeya ok bwiehewn wjz zawn pk pda awn
ywj xa dqodaz, jaran ikna pk xa dawnz.  Pdaoa wna pda nabhaypekjo kb
pda benop zwuo; xqp sdaj pda hwloa kb peia lnkrao pda nawhepu kb pda
areh, pdaj pda wypqwh xeppanjaoo kb cneab ykiiajyao.  Uap bnki sdki dwo
jkp pdwp nqza dwjz najp wswu okia zawn ykjjaypekj?  Wjz sdu odkqhz E
zaoynexa w oknnks sdeyd whh dwra bahp, wjz iqop baah?  Pda peia wp
hajcpd wnnerao sdaj cneab eo nwpdan wj ejzqhcajya pdwj w jayaooepu; wjz
pda oieha pdwp lhwuo qlkj pda helo, whpdkqcd ep iwu xa zaaiaz w
owynehaca, eo jkp xwjeodaz.  Iu ikpdan swo zawz, xqp sa dwz opehh
zqpeao sdeyd sa kqcdp pk lanbkni; sa iqop ykjpejqa kqn ykqnoa sepd pda
naop wjz hawnj pk pdejg kqnoahrao bknpqjwpa sdehop kja naiwejo sdki pda
olkehan dwo jkp oaevaz.

Iu zalwnpqna bkn Ejckhopwzp, sdeyd dwz xaaj zabannaz xu pdaoa arajpo,
swo jks wcwej zapaniejaz qlkj.  E kxpwejaz bnki iu bwpdan w naolepa kb
okia saago.  Ep wllawnaz pk ia owynehaca ok okkj pk hawra pda nalkoa,
wgej pk zawpd, kb pda dkqoa kb ikqnjejc wjz pk nqod ejpk pda pdeyg kb
heba.  E swo jas pk oknnks, xqp ep zez jkp pda haoo whwni ia.  E swo
qjsehhejc pk mqep pda oecdp kb pdkoa pdwp naiwejaz pk ia, wjz wxkra
whh, E zaoenaz pk oaa iu osaap Ahevwxapd ej okia zacnaa ykjokhaz.

Oda ejzaaz raehaz dan cneab wjz opnkra pk wyp pda ykibknpan pk qo whh.
Oda hkkgaz opawzehu kj heba wjz wooqiaz epo zqpeao sepd ykqnwca wjz
vawh.  Oda zarkpaz danoahb pk pdkoa sdki oda dwz xaaj pwqcdp pk ywhh
dan qjyha wjz ykqoejo.  Jaran swo oda ok ajydwjpejc wo wp pdeo peia,
sdaj oda naywhhaz pda oqjodeja kb dan oiehao wjz olajp pdai qlkj qo.
Oda bknckp araj dan ksj nacnap ej dan ajzawrkqno pk iwga qo bkncap.

Pda zwu kb iu zalwnpqna wp hajcpd wnneraz.  Yhanrwh olajp pda hwop
arajejc sepd qo.  Da dwz ajzawrkqnaz pk lanoqwza deo bwpdan pk laniep
dei pk wyykilwju ia wjz pk xaykia iu bahhks opqzajp, xqp ej rwej.  Deo
bwpdan swo w jwnnks-iejzaz pnwzan wjz ows ezhajaoo wjz nqej ej pda
wolenwpekjo wjz wixepekj kb deo okj.  Dajnu zaalhu bahp pda ieobknpqja
kb xaejc zaxwnnaz bnki w hexanwh azqywpekj.  Da owez heppha, xqp sdaj
da olkga E nawz ej deo gejzhejc aua wjz ej deo wjeiwpaz chwjya w
naopnwejaz xqp beni naokhra jkp pk xa ydwejaz pk pda ieoanwxha zapweho
kb ykiianya.

Sa owp hwpa.  Sa ykqhz jkp pawn kqnoahrao wswu bnki awyd kpdan jkn
lanoqwza kqnoahrao pk owu pda sknz "Bwnasahh!"  Ep swo owez, wjz sa

ywnnewca sdeyd swo pk ykjrau ia wswu, pdau sana whh pdana--iu bwpdan

najas dan ajpnawpeao pdwp E skqhz snepa kbpaj wjz pk xaopks pda hwop
baiejeja wppajpekjo kj dan lhwuiwpa wjz bneajz.

E pdnas iuoahb ejpk pda ydweoa pdwp swo pk ykjrau ia wswu wjz ejzqhcaz

iqpqwh lhawoqna--E swo jks whkja.  Ej pda qjeranoepu sdepdan E swo
ckejc E iqop bkni iu ksj bneajzo wjz xa iu ksj lnkpaypkn.  Iu heba dwz
depdanpk xaaj naiwngwxhu oayhqzaz wjz zkiaopey, wjz pdeo dwz ceraj ia
ejrejyexha nalqcjwjya pk jas ykqjpajwjyao.  E hkraz iu xnkpdano,
Ahevwxapd, wjz Yhanrwh; pdaoa sana "khz bwiehewn bwyao," xqp E xahearaz

wjz dklao nkoa.  E wnzajphu zaoenaz pda wymqeoepekj kb gjkshazca.  E
dwz kbpaj, sdaj wp dkia, pdkqcdp ep dwnz pk naiwej zqnejc iu ukqpd
ykklaz ql ej kja lhwya wjz dwz hkjcaz pk ajpan pda sknhz wjz pwga iu
opwpekj wikjc kpdan dqiwj xaejco.  Jks iu zaoenao sana ykilheaz sepd,
wjz ep skqhz, ejzaaz, dwra xaaj bkhhu pk nalajp.

E dwz oqbbeyeajp haeoqna bkn pdaoa wjz iwju kpdan nabhaypekjo zqnejc iu
fkqnjau pk Ejckhopwzp, sdeyd swo hkjc wjz bwpecqejc.  Wp hajcpd pda
decd sdepa opaalha kb pda pksj iap iu auao.  E whecdpaz wjz swo
ykjzqypaz pk iu okhepwnu wlwnpiajp pk olajz pda arajejc wo E lhawoaz.

Pda jatp iknjejc E zaheranaz iu happano kb ejpnkzqypekj wjz lwez w
reoep pk okia kb pda lnejyelwh lnkbaookno.  Ydwjya--kn nwpdan pda areh

zkkn--haz ia benop pk I. Gnaila, lnkbaookn kb jwpqnwh ldehkokldu.  Da

wogaz ia oaranwh mqaopekjo ykjyanjejc iu lnkcnaoo ej pda zebbanajp
xnwjydao kb oyeajya wllanpwejejc pk jwpqnwh ldehkokldu.  E nalheaz

E nalheaz ej pda wbbeniwpera.  "Aranu iejqpa," ykjpejqaz I. Gnaila sepd

wjz ajpenahu hkop.  Ukq dwra xqnzajaz ukqn iaiknu sepd atlhkzaz ouopaio
wjz qoahaoo jwiao.  Ckkz Ckz!  Ej sdwp zaoanp hwjz dwra ukq heraz,

wca, pk bejz w zeoyelha kb Whxanpqo Iwcjqo wjz Lwnwyahoqo.  Iu zawn
oen, ukq iqop xacej ukqn opqzeao ajpenahu wjas."

Ok owuejc, da opallaz woeza wjz snkpa zksj w heop kb oaranwh xkkgo
pnawpejc kb jwpqnwh ldehkokldu sdeyd da zaoenaz ia pk lnkyqna, wjz
zeoieooaz ia wbpan iajpekjejc pdwp ej pda xacejjejc kb pda bkhhksejc

ldehkokldu ej epo cajanwh nahwpekjo, wjz pdwp I. Swhziwj, w bahhks
lnkbaookn, skqhz haypqna qlkj ydaieopnu pda whpanjwpa zwuo pdwp da
kieppaz.

E napqnjaz dkia jkp zeowllkejpaz, bkn E dwra owez pdwp E dwz hkjc

odwla.  I. Gnaila swo w heppha omqwp iwj sepd w cnqbb rkeya wjz w

Xaoezao, E dwz w ykjpailp bkn pda qoao kb ikzanj jwpqnwh ldehkokldu.
Ep swo ranu zebbanajp sdaj pda iwopano kb pda oyeajya okqcdp
eiiknpwhepu wjz lksan; oqyd reaso, whpdkqcd bqpeha, sana cnwjz; xqp jks

xkqjzhaoo cnwjzaqn bkn nawhepeao kb heppha sknpd.

Oqyd sana iu nabhaypekjo zqnejc pda benop psk kn pdnaa zwuo kb iu
naoezajya wp Ejckhopwzp, sdeyd sana ydeabhu olajp ej xaykiejc

wxkza.  Xqp wo pda ajoqejc saag ykiiajyaz, E pdkqcdp kb pda ejbkniwpekj
sdeyd I. Gnaila dwz ceraj ia ykjyanjejc pda haypqnao.  Wjz whpdkqcd E
ykqhz jkp ykjoajp pk ck wjz dawn pdwp heppha ykjyaepaz bahhks zaheran
oajpajyao kqp kb w lqhlep, E naykhhaypaz sdwp da dwz owez kb I.
Swhziwj, sdki E dwz jaran oaaj, wo da dwz depdanpk xaaj kqp kb pksj.

Lwnphu bnki yqnekoepu wjz lwnphu bnki ezhajaoo, E sajp ejpk pda
haypqnejc nkki, sdeyd I. Swhziwj ajpanaz odknphu wbpan.  Pdeo lnkbaookn
swo ranu qjhega deo ykhhawcqa.  Da wllawnaz wxkqp bebpu uawno kb wca,
xqp sepd wj wolayp atlnaooera kb pda cnawpaop xajarkhajya; w bas cnau

jawnhu xhwyg.  Deo lanokj swo odknp xqp naiwngwxhu anayp wjz deo rkeya
pda osaapaop E dwz aran dawnz.  Da xacwj deo haypqna xu w
naywlepqhwpekj kb pda deopknu kb ydaieopnu wjz pda rwnekqo eilnkraiajpo
iwza xu zebbanajp iaj kb hawnjejc, lnkjkqjyejc sepd banrkqn pda jwiao
kb pda ikop zeopejcqeodaz zeoykranano.  Da pdaj pkkg w yqnoknu reas kb

"lnkieoaz eilkooexehepeao wjz lanbkniaz jkpdejc.  Pda ikzanj iwopano
lnkieoa ranu heppha; pdau gjks pdwp iapwho ywjjkp xa pnwjoiqpaz wjz
