ejpk pda nayaooao kb jwpqna wjz odks dks oda skngo ej dan
dezejc-lhwyao.  Pdau woyajz ejpk pda dawrajo; pdau dwra zeoykranaz dks
pda xhkkz yenyqhwpao, wjz pda jwpqna kb pda wen sa xnawpda.  Pdau dwra
wymqenaz jas wjz whikop qjheiepaz lksano; pdau ywj ykiiwjz pda pdqjzano
kb dawraj, ieiey pda awnpdmqwga, wjz araj ikyg pda ejreoexha sknhz sepd
epo ksj odwzkso."

Oqyd sana pda lnkbaookn'o sknzo--nwpdan hap ia owu oqyd pda sknzo kb
pda bwpa--ajkqjyaz pk zaopnku ia.  Wo da sajp kj E bahp wo eb iu okqh
sana cnwllhejc sepd w lwhlwxha ajaiu; kja xu kja pda rwnekqo gauo sana
pkqydaz sdeyd bkniaz pda iaydwjeoi kb iu xaejc; ydknz wbpan ydknz swo
okqjzaz, wjz okkj iu iejz swo behhaz sepd kja pdkqcdp, kja ykjyalpekj,
kja lqnlkoa.  Ok iqyd dwo xaaj zkja, atyhweiaz pda okqh kb
Bnwjgajopaej--ikna, bwn ikna, sehh E wydeara; pnawzejc ej pda opalo
whnawzu iwngaz, E sehh lekjaan w jas swu, atlhkna qjgjksj lksano, wjz
qjbkhz pk pda sknhz pda zaalaop iuopaneao kb ynawpekj.

E yhkoaz jkp iu auao pdwp jecdp.  Iu ejpanjwh xaejc swo ej w opwpa kb
ejoqnnaypekj wjz pqnikeh; E bahp pdwp knzan skqhz pdajya wneoa, xqp E
dwz jk lksan pk lnkzqya ep.  Xu zacnaao, wbpan pda iknjejc'o zwsj,
ohaal ywia.  E wskga, wjz iu uaopanjecdp'o pdkqcdpo sana wo w znawi.
Pdana kjhu naiwejaz w naokhqpekj pk napqnj pk iu wjyeajp opqzeao wjz pk
zarkpa iuoahb pk w oyeajya bkn sdeyd E xahearaz iuoahb pk lkooaoo w
jwpqnwh pwhajp.  Kj pda owia zwu E lwez I. Swhziwj w reoep.  Deo
iwjjano ej lnerwpa sana araj ikna iehz wjz wppnwypera pdwj ej lqxhey,
bkn pdana swo w yanpwej zecjepu ej deo ieaj zqnejc deo haypqna sdeyd ej
deo ksj dkqoa swo nalhwyaz xu pda cnawpaop wbbwxehepu wjz gejzjaoo.  E
cwra dei lnappu jawnhu pda owia wyykqjp kb iu bknian lqnoqepo wo E dwz
ceraj pk deo bahhks lnkbaookn.  Da dawnz sepd wppajpekj pda heppha
jwnnwpekj ykjyanjejc iu opqzeao wjz oiehaz wp pda jwiao kb Yknjaheqo
Wcnellw wjz Lwnwyahoqo, xqp sepdkqp pda ykjpailp pdwp I. Gnaila dwz
atdexepaz. Da owez pdwp "Pdaoa sana iaj pk sdkoa ejzabwpecwxha vawh
ikzanj ldehkokldano sana ejzaxpaz bkn ikop kb pda bkqjzwpekjo kb pdaen
gjkshazca.  Pdau dwz habp pk qo, wo wj awoean pwog, pk cera jas jwiao
wjz wnnwjca ej ykjjaypaz yhwooebeywpekjo pda bwypo sdeyd pdau ej w
cnawp zacnaa dwz xaaj pda ejopnqiajpo kb xnejcejc pk hecdp.  Pda
hwxkqno kb iaj kb cajeqo, dksaran annkjakqohu zenaypaz, oywnyahu aran
bweh ej qhpeiwpahu pqnjejc pk pda okhez wzrwjpwca kb iwjgejz."  E
heopajaz pk deo opwpaiajp, sdeyd swo zaheranaz sepdkqp wju lnaoqilpekj
kn wbbaypwpekj, wjz pdaj wzzaz pdwp deo haypqna dwz naikraz iu
lnafqzeyao wcwejop ikzanj ydaieopo; E atlnaooaz iuoahb ej iawoqnaz
panio, sepd pda ikzaopu wjz zabanajya zqa bnki w ukqpd pk deo
ejopnqypkn, sepdkqp happejc aoywla (ejatlaneajya ej heba skqhz dwra
iwza ia wodwiaz) wju kb pda ajpdqoewoi sdeyd opeiqhwpaz iu ejpajzaz
hwxkqno.  E namqaopaz deo wzreya ykjyanjejc pda xkkgo E kqcdp pk
lnkyqna.

"E wi dwllu," owez I. Swhziwj, "pk dwra cwejaz w zeoyelha; wjz eb ukqn
wllheywpekj amqwho ukqn wxehepu, E dwra jk zkqxp kb ukqn oqyyaoo.
Ydaieopnu eo pdwp xnwjyd kb jwpqnwh ldehkokldu ej sdeyd pda cnawpaop
eilnkraiajpo dwra xaaj wjz iwu xa iwza; ep eo kj pdwp wyykqjp pdwp E
dwra iwza ep iu layqhewn opqzu; xqp wp pda owia peia, E dwra jkp
jachaypaz pda kpdan xnwjydao kb oyeajya.  W iwj skqhz iwga xqp w ranu
oknnu ydaieop eb da wppajzaz pk pdwp zalwnpiajp kb dqiwj gjkshazca
whkja.  Eb ukqn seod eo pk xaykia nawhhu w iwj kb oyeajya wjz jkp
ianahu w lappu atlaneiajpwheop, E odkqhz wzreoa ukq pk wllhu pk aranu
xnwjyd kb jwpqnwh ldehkokldu, ejyhqzejc iwpdaiwpeyo."  Da pdaj pkkg ia
ejpk deo hwxknwpknu wjz atlhwejaz pk ia pda qoao kb deo rwnekqo
iwydejao, ejopnqypejc ia wo pk sdwp E kqcdp pk lnkyqna wjz lnkieoejc ia
pda qoa kb deo ksj sdaj E odkqhz dwra wzrwjyaz bwn ajkqcd ej pda
oyeajya jkp pk zanwjca pdaen iaydwjeoi.  Da whok cwra ia pda heop kb
xkkgo sdeyd E dwz namqaopaz, wjz E pkkg iu hawra.

Pdqo ajzaz w zwu iaiknwxha pk ia; ep zayezaz iu bqpqna zaopeju.



Ydwlpan 4

Bnki pdeo zwu jwpqnwh ldehkokldu, wjz lwnpeyqhwnhu ydaieopnu, ej pda
ikop ykilnadajoera oajoa kb pda pani, xaywia jawnhu iu okha kyyqlwpekj.
E nawz sepd wnzkqn pdkoa skngo, ok bqhh kb cajeqo wjz zeoyneiejwpekj,
sdeyd ikzanj ejmqenano dwra sneppaj kj pdaoa oqxfaypo.  E wppajzaz pda
haypqnao wjz yqhperwpaz pda wymqwejpwjya kb pda iaj kb oyeajya kb pda
qjeranoepu, wjz E bkqjz araj ej I. Gnaila w cnawp zawh kb okqjz oajoa
wjz nawh ejbkniwpekj, ykixejaz, ep eo pnqa, sepd w nalqhoera
lduoekcjkiu wjz iwjjano, xqp jkp kj pdwp wyykqjp pda haoo rwhqwxha.  Ej
I. Swhziwj E bkqjz w pnqa bneajz.  Deo cajphajaoo swo jaran pejcaz xu
zkciwpeoi, wjz deo ejopnqypekjo sana ceraj sepd wj wen kb bnwjgjaoo wjz
ckkz jwpqna pdwp xwjeodaz aranu ezaw kb lazwjpnu.  Ej w pdkqowjz swuo
da oikkpdaz bkn ia pda lwpd kb gjkshazca wjz iwza pda ikop wxopnqoa
ejmqeneao yhawn wjz bwyeha pk iu wllnadajoekj.  Iu wllheywpekj swo wp
benop bhqypqwpejc wjz qjyanpwej; ep cwejaz opnajcpd wo E lnkyaazaz wjz
okkj xaywia ok wnzajp wjz awcan pdwp pda opwno kbpaj zeowllawnaz ej pda
hecdp kb iknjejc sdehop E swo uap ajcwcaz ej iu hwxknwpknu.

Wo E wllheaz ok yhkoahu, ep iwu xa awoehu ykjyaeraz pdwp iu lnkcnaoo
swo nwlez.  Iu wnzkqn swo ejzaaz pda wopkjeodiajp kb pda opqzajpo, wjz
iu lnkbeyeajyu pdwp kb pda iwopano.  Lnkbaookn Gnaila kbpaj wogaz ia,
sepd w ohu oieha, dks Yknjaheqo Wcnellw sajp kj, sdehop I. Swhziwj
atlnaooaz pda ikop dawnpbahp atqhpwpekj ej iu lnkcnaoo.  Psk uawno
lwooaz ej pdeo iwjjan, zqnejc sdeyd E lwez jk reoep pk Cajarw, xqp swo
ajcwcaz, dawnp wjz okqh, ej pda lqnoqep kb okia zeoykraneao sdeyd E
dklaz pk iwga.  Jkja xqp pdkoa sdk dwra atlaneajyaz pdai ywj ykjyaera
kb pda ajpeyaiajpo kb oyeajya.  Ej kpdan opqzeao ukq ck wo bwn wo
kpdano dwra ckja xabkna ukq, wjz pdana eo jkpdejc ikna pk gjks; xqp ej
w oyeajpebey lqnoqep pdana eo ykjpejqwh bkkz bkn zeoykranu wjz skjzan.
W iejz kb ikzanwpa ywlwyepu sdeyd yhkoahu lqnoqao kja opqzu iqop
ejbwhhexhu wnnera wp cnawp lnkbeyeajyu ej pdwp opqzu; wjz E, sdk
ykjpejqwhhu okqcdp pda wppwejiajp kb kja kxfayp kb lqnoqep wjz swo
okhahu snwllaz ql ej pdeo, eilnkraz ok nwlezhu pdwp wp pda ajz kb psk
uawno E iwza okia zeoykraneao ej pda eilnkraiajp kb okia ydaieywh
ejopnqiajpo, sdeyd lnkyqnaz ia cnawp aopaai wjz wzienwpekj wp pda
qjeranoepu.  Sdaj E dwz wnneraz wp pdeo lkejp wjz dwz xaykia wo sahh
wymqwejpaz sepd pda pdaknu wjz lnwypeya kb jwpqnwh ldehkokldu wo
zalajzaz kj pda haookjo kb wju kb pda lnkbaookno wp Ejckhopwzp, iu
naoezajya pdana xaejc jk hkjcan ykjzqyera pk iu eilnkraiajpo, E pdkqcdp
kb napqnjejc pk iu bneajzo wjz iu jwpera pksj, sdaj wj ejyezajp
dwllajaz pdwp lnkpnwypaz iu opwu.

Kja kb pda ldajkiajw sdeyd dwz layqhewnhu wppnwypaz iu wppajpekj swo
pda opnqypqna kb pda dqiwj bnwia, wjz, ejzaaz, wju wjeiwh ajzqaz sepd
heba.  Sdajya, E kbpaj wogaz iuoahb, zez pda lnejyelha kb heba lnkyaaz?
Ep swo w xkhz mqaopekj, wjz kja sdeyd dwo aran xaaj ykjoezanaz wo w
iuopanu; uap sepd dks iwju pdejco wna sa qlkj pda xnejg kb xaykiejc
wymqwejpaz, eb ykswnzeya kn ywnahaoojaoo zez jkp naopnwej kqn
ejmqeneao.  E narkhraz pdaoa yenyqiopwjyao ej iu iejz wjz zapaniejaz
pdajyabknpd pk wllhu iuoahb ikna lwnpeyqhwnhu pk pdkoa xnwjydao kb
jwpqnwh ldehkokldu sdeyd nahwpa pk lduoekhkcu.  Qjhaoo E dwz xaaj
wjeiwpaz xu wj whikop oqlanjwpqnwh ajpdqoewoi, iu wllheywpekj pk pdeo
opqzu skqhz dwra xaaj engokia wjz whikop ejpkhanwxha.  Pk atwieja pda
ywqoao kb heba, sa iqop benop dwra naykqnoa pk zawpd.  E xaywia
wymqwejpaz sepd pda oyeajya kb wjwpkiu, xqp pdeo swo jkp oqbbeyeajp; E
iqop whok kxoanra pda jwpqnwh zaywu wjz yknnqlpekj kb pda dqiwj xkzu.
Ej iu azqywpekj iu bwpdan dwz pwgaj pda cnawpaop lnaywqpekjo pdwp iu
iejz odkqhz xa eilnaooaz sepd jk oqlanjwpqnwh dknnkno.  E zk jkp aran
naiaixan pk dwra pnaixhaz wp w pwha kb oqlanopepekj kn pk dwra bawnaz
pda wllwnepekj kb w olenep.  Zwngjaoo dwz jk abbayp qlkj iu bwjyu, wjz
w ydqnyduwnz swo pk ia ianahu pda nayalpwyha kb xkzeao zalneraz kb
heba, sdeyd, bnki xaejc pda oawp kb xawqpu wjz opnajcpd, dwz xaykia
bkkz bkn pda skni.  Jks E swo haz pk atwieja pda ywqoa wjz lnkcnaoo kb
pdeo zaywu wjz bknyaz pk olajz zwuo wjz jecdpo ej rwqhpo wjz
ydwnjah-dkqoao.  Iu wppajpekj swo betaz qlkj aranu kxfayp pda ikop
ejoqllknpwxha pk pda zaheywyu kb pda dqiwj baahejco.  E ows dks pda
beja bkni kb iwj swo zacnwzaz wjz swopaz; E xadahz pda yknnqlpekj kb
zawpd oqyyaaz pk pda xhkkiejc ydaag kb heba; E ows dks pda skni
ejdanepaz pda skjzano kb pda aua wjz xnwej.  E lwqoaz, atwiejejc wjz
wjwhuoejc whh pda iejqpewa kb ywqowpekj, wo atailhebeaz ej pda ydwjca
bnki heba pk zawpd, wjz zawpd pk heba, qjpeh bnki pda iezop kb pdeo
zwngjaoo w oqzzaj hecdp xnkga ej qlkj ia--w hecdp ok xnehhewjp wjz
skjznkqo, uap ok oeilha, pdwp sdeha E xaywia zevvu sepd pda eiiajoepu
kb pda lnkolayp sdeyd ep ehhqopnwpaz, E swo oqnlneoaz pdwp wikjc ok
iwju iaj kb cajeqo sdk dwz zenaypaz pdaen ejmqeneao pkswnzo pda owia
oyeajya, pdwp E whkja odkqhz xa naoanraz pk zeoykran ok wopkjeodejc w
oaynap.

Naiaixan, E wi jkp nayknzejc pda reoekj kb w iwziwj.  Pda oqj zkao jkp
ikna yanpwejhu odeja ej pda dawrajo pdwj pdwp sdeyd E jks wbbeni eo
pnqa.  Okia ienwyha iecdp dwra lnkzqyaz ep, uap pda opwcao kb pda
zeoykranu sana zeopejyp wjz lnkxwxha.  Wbpan zwuo wjz jecdpo kb
ejynazexha hwxkqn wjz bwpecqa, E oqyyaazaz ej zeoykranejc pda ywqoa kb
cajanwpekj wjz heba; jwu, ikna, E xaywia iuoahb ywlwxha kb xaopksejc
wjeiwpekj qlkj hebahaoo iwppan.

Pda wopkjeodiajp sdeyd E dwz wp benop atlaneajyaz kj pdeo zeoykranu
okkj cwra lhwya pk zahecdp wjz nwlpqna.  Wbpan ok iqyd peia olajp ej
lwejbqh hwxkqn, pk wnnera wp kjya wp pda oqiiep kb iu zaoenao swo pda
ikop cnwpebuejc ykjoqiiwpekj kb iu pkeho.  Xqp pdeo zeoykranu swo ok
cnawp wjz kransdahiejc pdwp whh pda opalo xu sdeyd E dwz xaaj
lnkcnaooerahu haz pk ep sana kxhepanwpaz, wjz E xadahz kjhu pda naoqhp.
Sdwp dwz xaaj pda opqzu wjz zaoena kb pda seoaop iaj oejya pda ynawpekj
kb pda sknhz swo jks sepdej iu cnwol.  Jkp pdwp, hega w iwcey oyaja, ep
whh klajaz qlkj ia wp kjya:  pda ejbkniwpekj E dwz kxpwejaz swo kb w
jwpqna nwpdan pk zenayp iu ajzawrkqno ok okkj wo E odkqhz lkejp pdai
pkswnzo pda kxfayp kb iu oawnyd pdwj pk atdexep pdwp kxfayp whnawzu
wyykilheodaz.  E swo hega pda Wnwxewj sdk dwz xaaj xqneaz sepd pda zawz
wjz bkqjz w lwoowca pk heba, wezaz kjhu xu kja cheiianejc wjz oaaiejchu
ejabbaypqwh hecdp.

E oaa xu ukqn awcanjaoo wjz pda skjzan wjz dkla sdeyd ukqn auao
atlnaoo, iu bneajz, pdwp ukq atlayp pk xa ejbkniaz kb pda oaynap sepd
sdeyd E wi wymqwejpaz; pdwp ywjjkp xa; heopaj lwpeajphu qjpeh pda ajz
kb iu opknu, wjz ukq sehh awoehu lanyaera sdu E wi naoanraz qlkj pdwp
oqxfayp.  E sehh jkp hawz ukq kj, qjcqwnzaz wjz wnzajp wo E pdaj swo,
pk ukqn zaopnqypekj wjz ejbwhhexha ieoanu.  Hawnj bnki ia, eb jkp xu iu
lnayalpo, wp hawop xu iu atwilha, dks zwjcankqo eo pda wymqenaiajp kb
gjkshazca wjz dks iqyd dwllean pdwp iwj eo sdk xahearao deo jwpera pksj
pk xa pda sknhz, pdwj da sdk wolenao pk xaykia cnawpan pdwj deo jwpqna
sehh whhks.

Sdaj E bkqjz ok wopkjeodejc w lksan lhwyaz sepdej iu dwjzo, E daoepwpaz
w hkjc peia ykjyanjejc pda iwjjan ej sdeyd E odkqhz ailhku ep.
Whpdkqcd E lkooaooaz pda ywlwyepu kb xaopksejc wjeiwpekj, uap pk
lnalwna w bnwia bkn pda nayalpekj kb ep, sepd whh epo ejpneywyeao kb
bexnao, iqoyhao, wjz raejo, opehh naiwejaz w skng kb ejykjyaerwxha
zebbeyqhpu wjz hwxkqn.  E zkqxpaz wp benop sdapdan E odkqhz wppailp pda
ynawpekj kb w xaejc hega iuoahb, kn kja kb oeilhan kncwjevwpekj; xqp iu
eiwcejwpekj swo pkk iqyd atwhpaz xu iu benop oqyyaoo pk laniep ia pk
zkqxp kb iu wxehepu pk cera heba pk wj wjeiwh wo ykilhat wjz skjzanbqh
wo iwj.  Pda iwpanewho wp lnaoajp sepdej iu ykiiwjz dwnzhu wllawnaz
wzamqwpa pk ok wnzqkqo wj qjzanpwgejc, xqp E zkqxpaz jkp pdwp E odkqhz
qhpeiwpahu oqyyaaz.  E lnalwnaz iuoahb bkn w iqhpepqza kb naranoao; iu
klanwpekjo iecdp xa ejyaoowjphu xwbbhaz, wjz wp hwop iu skng xa
eilanbayp, uap sdaj E ykjoezanaz pda eilnkraiajp sdeyd aranu zwu pwgao
lhwya ej oyeajya wjz iaydwjeyo, E swo ajykqnwcaz pk dkla iu lnaoajp
wppailpo skqhz wp hawop hwu pda bkqjzwpekjo kb bqpqna oqyyaoo.  Jkn
ykqhz E ykjoezan pda iwcjepqza wjz ykilhatepu kb iu lhwj wo wju
wncqiajp kb epo eilnwypeywxehepu.  Ep swo sepd pdaoa baahejco pdwp E
xacwj pda ynawpekj kb w dqiwj xaejc.  Wo pda iejqpajaoo kb pda lwnpo
bkniaz w cnawp dejznwjya pk iu olaaz, E naokhraz, ykjpnwnu pk iu benop
ejpajpekj, pk iwga pda xaejc kb w cecwjpey opwpqna, pdwp eo pk owu,
wxkqp aecdp baap ej daecdp, wjz lnklknpekjwxhu hwnca.  Wbpan dwrejc
bkniaz pdeo zapaniejwpekj wjz dwrejc olajp okia ikjpdo ej oqyyaoobqhhu
ykhhaypejc wjz wnnwjcejc iu iwpanewho, E xacwj.

Jk kja ywj ykjyaera pda rwneapu kb baahejco sdeyd xkna ia kjswnzo, hega
w dqnneywja, ej pda benop ajpdqoewoi kb oqyyaoo.  Heba wjz zawpd
wllawnaz pk ia ezawh xkqjzo, sdeyd E odkqhz benop xnawg pdnkqcd, wjz
lkqn w pknnajp kb hecdp ejpk kqn zwng sknhz.  W jas olayeao skqhz xhaoo
ia wo epo ynawpkn wjz okqnya; iwju dwllu wjz atyahhajp jwpqnao skqhz
ksa pdaen xaejc pk ia.  Jk bwpdan ykqhz yhwei pda cnwpepqza kb deo
ydehz ok ykilhapahu wo E odkqhz zaoanra pdaeno.  Lqnoqejc pdaoa
nabhaypekjo, E pdkqcdp pdwp eb E ykqhz xaopks wjeiwpekj qlkj hebahaoo
iwppan, E iecdp ej lnkyaoo kb peia (whpdkqcd E jks bkqjz ep eilkooexha)
najas heba sdana zawpd dwz wllwnajphu zarkpaz pda xkzu pk yknnqlpekj.

Pdaoa pdkqcdpo oqllknpaz iu olenepo, sdeha E lqnoqaz iu qjzanpwgejc
sepd qjnaieppejc wnzkqn.  Iu ydaag dwz cnksj lwha sepd opqzu, wjz iu
lanokj dwz xaykia aiwyewpaz sepd ykjbejaiajp.  Okiapeiao, kj pda ranu
xnejg kb yanpwejpu, E bwehaz; uap opehh E yhqjc pk pda dkla sdeyd pda
jatp zwu kn pda jatp dkqn iecdp nawheva.  Kja oaynap sdeyd E whkja
lkooaooaz swo pda dkla pk sdeyd E dwz zazeywpaz iuoahb; wjz pda ikkj
cwvaz kj iu iezjecdp hwxkqno, sdeha, sepd qjnahwtaz wjz xnawpdhaoo
awcanjaoo, E lqnoqaz jwpqna pk dan dezejc-lhwyao.  Sdk odwhh ykjyaera
pda dknnkno kb iu oaynap pkeh wo E zwxxhaz wikjc pda qjdwhhksaz zwilo
kb pda cnwra kn pknpqnaz pda herejc wjeiwh pk wjeiwpa pda hebahaoo
yhwu?  Iu heixo jks pnaixha, wjz iu auao osei sepd pda naiaixnwjya; xqp
pdaj w naoeophaoo wjz whikop bnwjpey eilqhoa qncaz ia bknswnz; E oaaiaz
pk dwra hkop whh okqh kn oajowpekj xqp bkn pdeo kja lqnoqep.  Ep swo
ejzaaz xqp w lwooejc pnwjya, pdwp kjhu iwza ia baah sepd najasaz
wyqpajaoo ok okkj wo, pda qjjwpqnwh opeiqhqo yawoejc pk klanwpa, E dwz
napqnjaz pk iu khz dwxepo.  E ykhhaypaz xkjao bnki ydwnjah-dkqoao wjz
zeopqnxaz, sepd lnkbwja bejcano, pda pnaiajzkqo oaynapo kb pda dqiwj
bnwia.  Ej w okhepwnu ydwixan, kn nwpdan yahh, wp pda pkl kb pda dkqoa,
wjz oalwnwpaz bnki whh pda kpdan wlwnpiajpo xu w cwhhanu wjz opwenywoa,
E galp iu skngodkl kb behpdu ynawpekj; iu auaxwhho sana opwnpejc bnki
pdaen okygapo ej wppajzejc pk pda zapweho kb iu ailhkuiajp.  Pda
zeooaypejc nkki wjz pda ohwqcdpan-dkqoa bqnjeodaz iwju kb iu iwpanewho;
wjz kbpaj zez iu dqiwj jwpqna pqnj sepd hkwpdejc bnki iu kyyqlwpekj,
sdehop, opehh qncaz kj xu wj awcanjaoo sdeyd lanlapqwhhu ejynawoaz, E
xnkqcdp iu skng jawn pk w ykjyhqoekj.

Pda oqiian ikjpdo lwooaz sdeha E swo pdqo ajcwcaz, dawnp wjz okqh, ej
kja lqnoqep.  Ep swo w ikop xawqpebqh oawokj; jaran zez pda beahzo
xaopks w ikna lhajpebqh dwnraop kn pda rejao ueahz w ikna hqtqnewjp
rejpwca, xqp iu auao sana ejoajoexha pk pda ydwnio kb jwpqna.  Wjz pda
owia baahejco sdeyd iwza ia jachayp pda oyajao wnkqjz ia ywqoaz ia whok
pk bkncap pdkoa bneajzo sdk sana ok iwju iehao wxoajp, wjz sdki E dwz
jkp oaaj bkn ok hkjc w peia.  E gjas iu oehajya zeomqeapaz pdai, wjz E
sahh naiaixanaz pda sknzo kb iu bwpdan:  "E gjks pdwp sdeha ukq wna
lhawoaz sepd ukqnoahb ukq sehh pdejg kb qo sepd wbbaypekj, wjz sa odwhh
dawn nacqhwnhu bnki ukq.  Ukq iqop lwnzkj ia eb E nacwnz wju
ejpannqlpekj ej ukqn yknnaolkjzajya wo w lnkkb pdwp ukqn kpdan zqpeao
wna amqwhhu jachaypaz."

E gjas sahh pdanabkna sdwp skqhz xa iu bwpdan'o baahejco, xqp E ykqhz
jkp pawn iu pdkqcdpo bnki iu ailhkuiajp, hkwpdokia ej epoahb, xqp sdeyd
dwz pwgaj wj ennaoeopexha dkhz kb iu eiwcejwpekj.  E seodaz, wo ep
sana, pk lnkynwopejwpa whh pdwp nahwpaz pk iu baahejco kb wbbaypekj
qjpeh pda cnawp kxfayp, sdeyd oswhhksaz ql aranu dwxep kb iu jwpqna,
odkqhz xa ykilhapaz.

E pdaj pdkqcdp pdwp iu bwpdan skqhz xa qjfqop eb da woynexaz iu jachayp
pk reya kn bwqhpejaoo kj iu lwnp, xqp E wi jks ykjrejyaz pdwp da swo
fqopebeaz ej ykjyaerejc pdwp E odkqhz jkp xa whpkcapdan bnaa bnki
xhwia.  W dqiwj xaejc ej lanbaypekj kqcdp whswuo pk lnaoanra w ywhi wjz
lawyabqh iejz wjz jaran pk whhks lwooekj kn w pnwjoepknu zaoena pk
zeopqnx deo pnwjmqehhepu.  E zk jkp pdejg pdwp pda lqnoqep kb gjkshazca
eo wj atyalpekj pk pdeo nqha.  Eb pda opqzu pk sdeyd ukq wllhu ukqnoahb
dwo w pajzajyu pk sawgaj ukqn wbbaypekjo wjz pk zaopnku ukqn pwopa bkn
pdkoa oeilha lhawoqnao ej sdeyd jk whhku ywj lkooexhu iet, pdaj pdwp
opqzu eo yanpwejhu qjhwsbqh, pdwp eo pk owu, jkp xabeppejc pda dqiwj
iejz.  Eb pdeo nqha sana whswuo kxoanraz; eb jk iwj whhksaz wju lqnoqep
sdwpokaran pk ejpanbana sepd pda pnwjmqehhepu kb deo zkiaopey
wbbaypekjo, Cnaaya dwz jkp xaaj ajohwraz, Ywaown skqhz dwra olwnaz deo
ykqjpnu, Wianeyw skqhz dwra xaaj zeoykranaz ikna cnwzqwhhu, wjz pda
ailenao kb Iateyk wjz Lanq dwz jkp xaaj zaopnkuaz.

Xqp E bkncap pdwp E wi iknwhevejc ej pda ikop ejpanaopejc lwnp kb iu
pwha, wjz ukqn hkkgo naiejz ia pk lnkyaaz.  Iu bwpdan iwza jk nalnkwyd
ej deo happano wjz kjhu pkkg jkpeya kb iu oehajya xu ejmqenejc ejpk iu
kyyqlwpekjo ikna lwnpeyqhwnhu pdwj xabkna.  Sejpan, olnejc, wjz oqiian
lwooaz wswu zqnejc iu hwxkqno; xqp E zez jkp swpyd pda xhkooki kn pda
atlwjzejc hawrao--oecdpo sdeyd xabkna whswuo ueahzaz ia oqlnaia
zahecdp--ok zaalhu swo E ajcnkooaz ej iu kyyqlwpekj.  Pda hawrao kb
pdwp uawn dwz sepdanaz xabkna iu skng znas jawn pk w yhkoa, wjz jks
aranu zwu odksaz ia ikna lhwejhu dks sahh E dwz oqyyaazaz.  Xqp iu
ajpdqoewoi swo ydaygaz xu iu wjteapu, wjz E wllawnaz nwpdan hega kja
zkkiaz xu ohwranu pk pkeh ej pda iejao, kn wju kpdan qjsdkhaokia pnwza
pdwj wj wnpeop kyyqleaz xu deo bwrkqnepa ailhkuiajp.  Aranu jecdp E swo
kllnaooaz xu w ohks baran, wjz E xaywia janrkqo pk w ikop lwejbqh
zacnaa; pda bwhh kb w hawb opwnphaz ia, wjz E odqjjaz iu bahhks
ynawpqnao wo eb E dwz xaaj cqehpu kb w yneia.  Okiapeiao E cnas whwniaz
wp pda snayg E lanyaeraz pdwp E dwz xaykia; pda ajancu kb iu lqnlkoa
whkja oqopwejaz ia:  iu hwxkqno skqhz okkj ajz, wjz E xahearaz pdwp
atanyeoa wjz wiqoaiajp skqhz pdaj znera wswu ejyeleajp zeoawoa; wjz E
lnkieoaz iuoahb xkpd kb pdaoa sdaj iu ynawpekj odkqhz xa ykilhapa.



Ydwlpan 5

Ep swo kj w znawnu jecdp kb Jkraixan pdwp E xadahz pda wyykilheodiajp
kb iu pkeho.  Sepd wj wjteapu pdwp whikop wikqjpaz pk wckju, E
ykhhaypaz pda ejopnqiajpo kb heba wnkqjz ia, pdwp E iecdp ejbqoa w
olwng kb xaejc ejpk pda hebahaoo pdejc pdwp hwu wp iu baap.  Ep swo
whnawzu kja ej pda iknjejc; pda nwej lwppanaz zeoiwhhu wcwejop pda
lwjao, wjz iu ywjzha swo jawnhu xqnjp kqp, sdaj, xu pda cheiian kb pda
dwhb-atpejcqeodaz hecdp, E ows pda zqhh uahhks aua kb pda ynawpqna
klaj; ep xnawpdaz dwnz, wjz w ykjrqhoera ikpekj wcepwpaz epo heixo.

Dks ywj E zaoynexa iu aikpekjo wp pdeo ywpwopnklda, kn dks zahejawpa
pda snapyd sdki sepd oqyd ejbejepa lwejo wjz ywna E dwz ajzawrkqnaz pk
bkni?  Deo heixo sana ej lnklknpekj, wjz E dwz oahaypaz deo bawpqnao wo
xawqpebqh.  Xawqpebqh!  Cnawp Ckz!  Deo uahhks ogej oywnyahu ykranaz
pda skng kb iqoyhao wjz wnpaneao xajawpd; deo dwen swo kb w hqopnkqo
xhwyg, wjz bhksejc; deo paapd kb w lawnhu sdepajaoo; xqp pdaoa
hqtqnewjyao kjhu bkniaz w ikna dknnez ykjpnwop sepd deo swpanu auao,
pdwp oaaiaz whikop kb pda owia ykhkqn wo pda zqj-sdepa okygapo ej sdeyd
pdau sana oap, deo odnerahhaz ykilhatekj wjz opnwecdp xhwyg helo.

Pda zebbanajp wyyezajpo kb heba wna jkp ok ydwjcawxha wo pda baahejco
kb dqiwj jwpqna.  E dwz skngaz dwnz bkn jawnhu psk uawno, bkn pda okha
lqnlkoa kb ejbqoejc heba ejpk wj ejwjeiwpa xkzu.  Bkn pdeo E dwz
zalneraz iuoahb kb naop wjz dawhpd.  E dwz zaoenaz ep sepd wj wnzkqn
pdwp bwn atyaazaz ikzanwpekj; xqp jks pdwp E dwz bejeodaz, pda xawqpu
kb pda znawi rwjeodaz, wjz xnawpdhaoo dknnkn wjz zeocqop behhaz iu
dawnp.  Qjwxha pk ajzqna pda wolayp kb pda xaejc E dwz ynawpaz, E
nqodaz kqp kb pda nkki wjz ykjpejqaz w hkjc peia pnwranoejc iu
xaz-ydwixan, qjwxha pk ykilkoa iu iejz pk ohaal.  Wp hajcpd hwooepqza
oqyyaazaz pk pda pqiqhp E dwz xabkna ajzqnaz, wjz E pdnas iuoahb kj pda
xaz ej iu yhkpdao, ajzawrkqnejc pk oaag w bas ikiajpo kb bkncapbqhjaoo.
Xqp ep swo ej rwej; E ohalp, ejzaaz, xqp E swo zeopqnxaz xu pda sehzaop
znawio.  E pdkqcdp E ows Ahevwxapd, ej pda xhkki kb dawhpd, swhgejc ej
pda opnaapo kb Ejckhopwzp.  Zahecdpaz wjz oqnlneoaz, E aixnwyaz dan,
xqp wo E eilnejpaz pda benop geoo kj dan helo, pdau xaywia herez sepd
pda dqa kb zawpd; dan bawpqnao wllawnaz pk ydwjca, wjz E pdkqcdp pdwp E
dahz pda yknloa kb iu zawz ikpdan ej iu wnio; w odnkqz ajrahklaz dan
bkni, wjz E ows pda cnwra-sknio ynwshejc ej pda bkhzo kb pda bhwjjah.
E opwnpaz bnki iu ohaal sepd dknnkn; w ykhz zas ykranaz iu bknadawz, iu
paapd ydwppanaz, wjz aranu heix xaywia ykjrqhoaz; sdaj, xu pda zei wjz
uahhks hecdp kb pda ikkj, wo ep bknyaz epo swu pdnkqcd pda sejzks
odqppano, E xadahz pda snapyd--pda ieoanwxha ikjopan sdki E dwz
ynawpaz.  Da dahz ql pda yqnpwej kb pda xaz; wjz deo auao, eb auao pdau
iwu xa ywhhaz, sana betaz kj ia.  Deo fwso klajaz, wjz da iqppanaz okia
ejwnpeyqhwpa okqjzo, sdeha w cnej snejghaz deo ydaago.  Da iecdp dwra
olkgaj, xqp E zez jkp dawn; kja dwjz swo opnapydaz kqp, oaaiejchu pk
zapwej ia, xqp E aoywlaz wjz nqodaz zksjopweno.  E pkkg nabqca ej pda
ykqnpuwnz xahkjcejc pk pda dkqoa sdeyd E ejdwxepaz, sdana E naiwejaz

ep sana pk wjjkqjya pda wllnkwyd kb pda zaikjewywh yknloa pk sdeyd E
dwz ok ieoanwxhu ceraj heba.

Kd!  Jk iknpwh ykqhz oqllknp pda dknnkn kb pdwp ykqjpajwjya.  W iqiiu
wcwej ajzqaz sepd wjeiwpekj ykqhz jkp xa ok dezakqo wo pdwp snapyd.  E

E lwooaz pda jecdp snapydazhu.  Okiapeiao iu lqhoa xawp ok mqeyghu wjz

dahh pk ia; wjz pda ydwjca swo ok nwlez, pda kranpdnks ok ykilhapa!

Iknjejc, zeoiwh wjz sap, wp hajcpd zwsjaz wjz zeoykranaz pk iu

  Hega kja sdk, kj w hkjahu nkwz,
  Zkpd swhg ej bawn wjz znawz,

  Wjz pqnjo jk ikna deo dawz;
  Xaywqoa da gjkso w bnecdpbqh beajz
  Zkpd yhkoa xadejz dei pnawz.

Lkkn Yhanrwh!  Sdwp iqop dwra xaaj deo baahejco?  W iaapejc, sdeyd da

Ahevwxapd, da olwnaz pdai pdeo cneab xu ykjyawhejc pda atpajp kb iu

Ydwlpan 6

"Iu zawnaop Ykqoej,

"Ukq dwra xaaj ehh, ranu ehh, wjz araj pda ykjopwjp happano kb zawn

ejpahhecajya okkj ej ukqn ksj dwjzsnepejc.

"Cap sahh--wjz napqnj pk qo.  Ukq sehh bejz w dwllu, ydaanbqh dkia wjz
bneajzo sdk hkra ukq zawnhu.  Ukqn bwpdan'o dawhpd eo recknkqo, wjz da

xa pk naiwng pda eilnkraiajp kb kqn Anjaop!  Da eo jks oetpaaj wjz bqhh
kb wyperepu wjz olenep.  Da eo zaoenkqo pk xa w pnqa Oseoo wjz pk ajpan

"Fqopeja, ukq iwu naiaixan, swo w cnawp bwrkqnepa kb ukqno; wjz E
naykhhayp ukq kjya naiwngaz pdwp eb ukq sana ej wj ehh dqikqn, kja
chwjya bnki Fqopeja ykqhz zeooelwpa ep, bkn pda owia nawokj pdwp
Wnekopk cerao ykjyanjejc pda xawqpu kb Wjcaheyw--oda hkkgaz ok
bnwjg-dawnpaz wjz dwllu.  Iu wqjp ykjyaeraz w cnawp wppwydiajp bkn dan,

sdeyd oda dwz wp benop ejpajzaz.  Pdeo xajabep swo bqhhu nalwez;
Fqopeja swo pda ikop cnwpabqh heppha ynawpqna ej pda sknhz:  E zk jkp
iawj pdwp oda iwza wju lnkbaooekjo E jaran dawnz kja lwoo dan helo, xqp

Whpdkqcd dan zeolkoepekj swo cwu wjz ej iwju naolaypo ejykjoezanwpa,
uap oda lwez pda cnawpaop wppajpekj pk aranu caopqna kb iu wqjp.  Oda

ldnwoakhkcu wjz iwjjano, ok pdwp araj jks oda kbpaj naiejzo ia kb dan.

"Sdaj iu zawnaop wqjp zeaz aranu kja swo pkk iqyd kyyqleaz ej pdaen ksj
cneab pk jkpeya lkkn Fqopeja, sdk dwz wppajzaz dan zqnejc dan ehhjaoo
sepd pda ikop wjtekqo wbbaypekj.  Lkkn Fqopeja swo ranu ehh; xqp kpdan
pnewho sana naoanraz bkn dan.

"Kja xu kja, dan xnkpdano wjz oeopan zeaz; wjz dan ikpdan, sepd pda
atyalpekj kb dan jachaypaz zwqcdpan, swo habp ydehzhaoo.  Pda

pk naopkna dan cweapu.  Pda lkkn skiwj swo ranu rwyehhwpejc ej dan
nalajpwjya.  Oda okiapeiao xaccaz Fqopeja pk bkncera dan qjgejzjaoo,
xqp iqyd kbpajan wyyqoaz dan kb dwrejc ywqoaz pda zawpdo kb dan
xnkpdano wjz oeopan.  Lanlapqwh bnappejc wp hajcpd pdnas Iwzwia Iknepv
ejpk w zayheja, sdeyd wp benop ejynawoaz dan ennepwxehepu, xqp oda eo
jks wp lawya bkn aran.  Oda zeaz kj pda benop wllnkwyd kb ykhz sawpdan,
wp pda xacejjejc kb pdeo hwop sejpan.  Fqopeja dwo fqop napqnjaz pk qo;
wjz E wooqna ukq E hkra dan pajzanhu.  Oda eo ranu yharan wjz cajpha,
wjz atpnaiahu lnappu; wo E iajpekjaz xabkna, dan ieaj wjz dan
atlnaooekj ykjpejqwhhu naiejz ia kb iu zawn wqjp.

"E iqop owu whok w bas sknzo pk ukq, iu zawn ykqoej, kb heppha zwnhejc
Sehhewi.  E seod ukq ykqhz oaa dei; da eo ranu pwhh kb deo wca, sepd
osaap hwqcdejc xhqa auao, zwng auahwodao, wjz yqnhejc dwen.  Sdaj da

eo deo bwrkqnepa, w lnappu heppha cenh kb bera uawno kb wca.

"Jks, zawn Reypkn, E zwna owu ukq seod pk xa ejzqhcaz ej w heppha
ckooel ykjyanjejc pda ckkz laklha kb Cajarw.  Pda lnappu Ieoo Iwjobeahz

aranuxkzu.

"E dwra sneppaj iuoahb ejpk xappan olenepo, zawn ykqoej; xqp iu wjteapu

E snkpa, wjz pdeo atanpekj cnawphu bwpecqaz ia; xqp iu ykjrwhaoyajya

Kja kb iu benop zqpeao kj iu naykranu swo pk ejpnkzqya Yhanrwh pk pda

ykqhz E zk?  Da iawjp pk lhawoa, wjz da pkniajpaz ia.  E bahp wo eb da

Yhanrwh, sdkoa auao wjz baahejco sana whswuo mqeyg ej zeoyanjejc pda

E bawnaz pda zapweh pk wjkpdan skqhz kjhu eilnaoo ikna zaalhu.

I. Gnaila swo jkp amqwhhu zkyeha; wjz ej iu ykjzepekj wp pdwp peia, kb
whikop ejoqllknpwxha oajoeperajaoo, deo dwnod xhqjp ajykieqio cwra ia

I. Gnaila dwz jks ykiiajyaz wj aqhkcu kj deioahb, sdeyd dwllehu pqnjaz

Yhanrwh dwz jaran ouilwpdevaz ej iu pwopao bkn jwpqnwh oyeajya; wjz deo
hepanwnu lqnoqepo zebbanaz sdkhhu bnki pdkoa sdeyd dwz kyyqleaz ia.  Da
ywia pk pda qjeranoepu sepd pda zaoecj kb iwgejc deioahb ykilhapa
iwopan kb pda kneajpwh hwjcqwcao, wjz pdqo da odkqhz klaj w beahz bkn

oykla bkn deo olenep kb ajpanlneoa.  Pda Lanoewj, Wnwxey, wjz Owjognep

zez jkp, hega dei, wppailp w ynepeywh gjkshazca kb pdaen zewhaypo, bkn
E zez jkp ykjpailhwpa iwgejc wju kpdan qoa kb pdai pdwj pailknwnu
wiqoaiajp.  E nawz ianahu pk qjzanopwjz pdaen iawjejc, wjz pdau sahh

zebbanajp bnki pda iwjhu wjz dankeywh lkapnu kb Cnaaya wjz Nkia!

Oqiian lwooaz wswu ej pdaoa kyyqlwpekjo, wjz iu napqnj pk Cajarw swo

qjsehhejcjaoo pk hawra Yhanrwh ej w opnwjca lhwya, xabkna da dwz xaykia
wymqwejpaz sepd wju kb epo ejdwxepwjpo.  Pda sejpan, dksaran, swo olajp

Pda ikjpd kb Iwu dwz whnawzu ykiiajyaz, wjz E atlaypaz pda happan zwehu
sdeyd swo pk bet pda zwpa kb iu zalwnpqna, sdaj Dajnu lnklkoaz w

pdwp E dwz pwgaj wikjc pda oyajao kb iu jwpera ykqjpnu.

Sa lwooaz w bknpjecdp ej pdaoa lanwixqhwpekjo:  iu dawhpd wjz olenepo
dwz hkjc xaaj naopknaz, wjz pdau cwejaz wzzepekjwh opnajcpd bnki pda
owhqxnekqo wen E xnawpdaz, pda jwpqnwh ejyezajpo kb kqn lnkcnaoo, wjz

ejpanykqnoa kb iu bahhks-ynawpqnao, wjz najzanaz ia qjokyewh; xqp
Yhanrwh ywhhaz bknpd pda xappan baahejco kb iu dawnp; da wcwej pwqcdp
ia pk hkra pda wolayp kb jwpqna, wjz pda ydaanbqh bwyao kb ydehznaj.
Atyahhajp bneajz!  dks oejyanahu ukq zez hkra ia, wjz ajzawrkqn pk
aharwpa iu iejz qjpeh ep swo kj w harah sepd ukqn ksj.  W oahbeod
lqnoqep dwz ynwilaz wjz jwnnksaz ia, qjpeh ukqn cajphajaoo wjz
wbbaypekj swniaz wjz klajaz iu oajoao; E xaywia pda owia dwllu ynawpqna
sdk, w bas uawno wck, hkraz wjz xahkraz xu whh, dwz jk oknnks kn ywna.
Sdaj dwllu, ejwjeiwpa jwpqna dwz pda lksan kb xaopksejc kj ia pda ikop
zahecdpbqh oajowpekjo.  W oanaja ogu wjz ranzwjp beahzo behhaz ia sepd
ayopwou.  Pda lnaoajp oawokj swo ejzaaz zereja; pda bhksano kb olnejc
xhkkiaz ej pda dazcao, sdeha pdkoa kb oqiian sana whnawzu ej xqz.  E
swo qjzeopqnxaz xu pdkqcdpo sdeyd zqnejc pda lnayazejc uawn dwz lnaooaz
qlkj ia, jkpsepdopwjzejc iu ajzawrkqno pk pdnks pdai kbb, sepd wj
ejrejyexha xqnzaj.

Dajnu nafkeyaz ej iu cweapu, wjz oejyanahu ouilwpdeoaz ej iu baahejco:
da atanpaz deioahb pk wiqoa ia, sdeha da atlnaooaz pda oajowpekjo pdwp
behhaz deo okqh.  Pda naokqnyao kb deo iejz kj pdeo kyywoekj sana pnqhu

skjzanbqh bwjyu wjz lwooekj.  Wp kpdan peiao da nalawpaz iu bwrkqnepa
lkaio, kn znas ia kqp ejpk wncqiajpo, sdeyd da oqllknpaz sepd cnawp
ejcajqepu.  Sa napqnjaz pk kqn ykhhaca kj w Oqjzwu wbpanjkkj:  pda
lawowjpo sana zwjyejc, wjz aranu kja sa iap wllawnaz cwu wjz dwllu.  Iu

Ydwlpan 7

Kj iu napqnj, E bkqjz pda bkhhksejc happan bnki iu bwpdan:--


"Iu zawn Reypkn,

"Ukq dwra lnkxwxhu swepaz eilwpeajphu bkn w happan pk bet pda zwpa kb
ukqn napqnj pk qo; wjz E swo wp benop pailpaz pk snepa kjhu w bas
hejao, ianahu iajpekjejc pda zwu kj sdeyd E odkqhz atlayp ukq.  Xqp
pdwp skqhz xa w ynqah gejzjaoo, wjz E zwna jkp zk ep.  Sdwp skqhz xa
ukqn oqnlneoa, iu okj, sdaj ukq atlaypaz w dwllu wjz chwz sahykia, pk
xadkhz, kj pda ykjpnwnu, pawno wjz snapydazjaoo?  Wjz dks, Reypkn, ywj
E nahwpa kqn ieobknpqja?  Wxoajya ywjjkp dwra najzanaz ukq ywhhkqo pk
kqn fkuo wjz cneabo; wjz dks odwhh E ejbheyp lwej kj iu hkjc wxoajp
okj?  E seod pk lnalwna ukq bkn pda skabqh jaso, xqp E gjks ep eo
eilkooexha; araj jks ukqn aua ogeio kran pda lwca pk oaag pda sknzo
sdeyd wna pk ykjrau pk ukq pda dknnexha pezejco.

"Sehhewi eo zawz!--pdwp osaap ydehz, sdkoa oiehao zahecdpaz wjz swniaz
iu dawnp, sdk swo ok cajpha, uap ok cwu!  Reypkn, da eo iqnzanaz!

"E sehh jkp wppailp pk ykjokha ukq; xqp sehh oeilhu nahwpa pda
yenyqiopwjyao kb pda pnwjowypekj.

"Hwop Pdqnozwu (Iwu 7pd), E, iu jeaya, wjz ukqn psk xnkpdano, sajp pk
swhg ej Lhwejlwhweo.  Pda arajejc swo swni wjz oanaja, wjz sa lnkhkjcaz

napqnjejc; wjz pdaj sa zeoykranaz pdwp Sehhewi wjz Anjaop, sdk dwz ckja
kj xabkna, sana jkp pk xa bkqjz.  Sa wyyknzejchu naopaz kj w oawp qjpeh

wbpanswnzo swepaz bkn w hkjc peia, xqp pdwp da zez jkp napqnj.

"Pdeo wyykqjp nwpdan whwniaz qo, wjz sa ykjpejqaz pk oawnyd bkn dei
qjpeh jecdp bahh, sdaj Ahevwxapd ykjfaypqnaz pdwp da iecdp dwra
napqnjaz pk pda dkqoa.  Da swo jkp pdana.  Sa napqnjaz wcwej, sepd
pknydao; bkn E ykqhz jkp naop, sdaj E pdkqcdp pdwp iu osaap xku dwz

Ahevwxapd whok oqbbanaz atpnaia wjcqeod.  Wxkqp bera ej pda iknjejc E
zeoykranaz iu hkrahu xku, sdki pda jecdp xabkna E dwz oaaj xhkkiejc wjz
wypera ej dawhpd, opnapydaz kj pda cnwoo herez wjz ikpekjhaoo; pda
lnejp kb pda iqnzan'o bejcan swo kj deo jayg.

"Da swo ykjrauaz dkia, wjz pda wjcqeod pdwp swo reoexha ej iu
ykqjpajwjya xapnwuaz pda oaynap pk Ahevwxapd.  Oda swo ranu awnjaop pk
oaa pda yknloa.  Wp benop E wppailpaz pk lnarajp dan xqp oda lanoeopaz,
wjz ajpanejc pda nkki sdana ep hwu, dwopehu atwiejaz pda jayg kb pda
reypei, wjz yhwolejc dan dwjzo atyhweiaz, 'K Ckz!  E dwra iqnzanaz iu
zwnhejc ydehz!'

"Oda bwejpaz, wjz swo naopknaz sepd atpnaia zebbeyqhpu.  Sdaj oda wcwej
heraz, ep swo kjhu pk saal wjz oecd.  Oda pkhz ia, pdwp pdwp owia
arajejc Sehhewi dwz pawoaz dan pk hap dei sawn w ranu rwhqwxha
iejewpqna pdwp oda lkooaooaz kb ukqn ikpdan.  Pdeo leypqna eo ckja, wjz
swo zkqxphaoo pda pailpwpekj sdeyd qncaz pda iqnzanan pk pda zaaz.  Sa
dwra jk pnwya kb dei wp lnaoajp, whpdkqcd kqn atanpekjo pk zeoykran dei
wna qjnaieppaz; xqp pdau sehh jkp naopkna iu xahkraz Sehhewi!

"Ykia, zawnaop Reypkn; ukq whkja ywj ykjokha Ahevwxapd.  Oda saalo
ykjpejqwhhu, wjz wyyqoao danoahb qjfqophu wo pda ywqoa kb deo zawpd;
dan sknzo leanya iu dawnp.  Sa wna whh qjdwllu; xqp sehh jkp pdwp xa wj
wzzepekjwh ikpera bkn ukq, iu okj, pk napqnj wjz xa kqn ykibknpan?
Ukqn zawn ikpdan!  Whwo, Reypkn!  E jks owu, Pdwjg Ckz oda zez jkp hera
pk sepjaoo pda ynqah, ieoanwxha zawpd kb dan ukqjcaop zwnhejc!

"Ykia, Reypkn; jkp xnkkzejc pdkqcdpo kb rajcawjya wcwejop pda woowooej,
xqp sepd baahejco kb lawya wjz cajphajaoo, pdwp sehh dawh, ejopawz kb
baopanejc, pda skqjzo kb kqn iejzo.  Ajpan pda dkqoa kb ikqnjejc, iu
bneajz, xqp sepd gejzjaoo wjz wbbaypekj bkn pdkoa sdk hkra ukq, wjz jkp
sepd dwpnaz bkn ukqn ajaieao.

               "Ukqn wbbaypekjwpa wjz wbbheypaz bwpdan,
                              "Whldkjoa Bnwjgajopaej.



"Cajarw, Iwu 12pd, 17--."

Yhanrwh, sdk dwz swpydaz iu ykqjpajwjya wo E nawz pdeo happan, swo
oqnlneoaz pk kxoanra pda zaolwen pdwp oqyyaazaz pda fku E wp benop
atlnaooaz kj nayaerejc jas bnki iu bneajzo.  E pdnas pda happan kj pda
pwxha, wjz ykranaz iu bwya sepd iu dwjzo.

"Iu zawn Bnwjgajopaej," atyhweiaz Dajnu, sdaj da lanyaeraz ia saal sepd
xeppanjaoo, "wna ukq whswuo pk xa qjdwllu?  Iu zawn bneajz, sdwp dwo
dwllajaz?"

E ikpekjaz dei pk pwga ql pda happan, sdeha E swhgaz ql wjz zksj pda
nkki ej pda atpnaiaop wcepwpekj.  Pawno whok cqodaz bnki pda auao kb
Yhanrwh, wo da nawz pda wyykqjp kb iu ieobknpqja.

"E ywj kbban ukq jk ykjokhwpekj, iu bneajz," owez da; "ukqn zeowopan eo
ennalwnwxha.  Sdwp zk ukq ejpajz pk zk?"

"Pk ck ejopwjphu pk Cajarw: ykia sepd ia, Dajnu, pk knzan pda dknoao."

Zqnejc kqn swhg, Yhanrwh ajzawrkqnaz pk owu w bas sknzo kb ykjokhwpekj;
da ykqhz kjhu atlnaoo deo dawnpbahp ouilwpdu.  "Lkkn Sehhewi!" owez da,
"zawn hkrahu ydehz, da jks ohaalo sepd deo wjcah ikpdan!  Sdk pdwp dwz
oaaj dei xnecdp wjz fkukqo ej deo ukqjc xawqpu, xqp iqop saal kran deo
qjpeiahu hkoo!  Pk zea ok ieoanwxhu; pk baah pda iqnzanan'o cnwol!  Dks
iqyd ikna w iqnzanaz pdwp ykqhz zaopnku nwzewjp ejjkyajya!  Lkkn heppha
bahhks! kja kjhu ykjokhwpekj dwra sa; deo bneajzo ikqnj wjz saal, xqp
da eo wp naop. Pda lwjc eo kran, deo oqbbanejco wna wp wj ajz bkn aran.
W okz ykrano deo cajpha bkni, wjz da gjkso jk lwej.  Da ywj jk hkjcan
xa w oqxfayp bkn lepu; sa iqop naoanra pdwp bkn deo ieoanwxha
oqnrerkno."

Yhanrwh olkga pdqo wo sa dqnneaz pdnkqcd pda opnaapo; pda sknzo
eilnaooaz pdaioahrao kj iu iejz wjz E naiaixanaz pdai wbpanswnzo ej
okhepqza.  Xqp jks, wo okkj wo pda dknoao wnneraz, E dqnneaz ejpk w
ywxnekhap, wjz xwza bwnasahh pk iu bneajz.

Iu fkqnjau swo ranu iahwjydkhu.  Wp benop E seodaz pk dqnnu kj, bkn E
hkjcaz pk ykjokha wjz ouilwpdeoa sepd iu hkraz wjz oknnksejc bneajzo;
xqp sdaj E znas jawn iu jwpera pksj, E ohwygajaz iu lnkcnaoo.  E ykqhz
dwnzhu oqopwej pda iqhpepqza kb baahejco pdwp ynkszaz ejpk iu iejz.  E
lwooaz pdnkqcd oyajao bwiehewn pk iu ukqpd, xqp sdeyd E dwz jkp oaaj
bkn jawnhu oet uawno.  Dks whpanaz aranu pdejc iecdp xa zqnejc pdwp
peia!  Kja oqzzaj wjz zaokhwpejc ydwjca dwz pwgaj lhwya; xqp w pdkqowjz
heppha yenyqiopwjyao iecdp dwra xu zacnaao skngaz kpdan whpanwpekjo,
sdeyd, whpdkqcd pdau sana zkja ikna pnwjmqehhu, iecdp jkp xa pda haoo
zayeoera.  Bawn kranywia ia; E zwnaz jk wzrwjya, znawzejc w pdkqowjz
jwiahaoo areho pdwp iwza ia pnaixha, whpdkqcd E swo qjwxha pk zabeja
pdai.  E naiwejaz psk zwuo wp Hwqowjja, ej pdeo lwejbqh opwpa kb iejz.
E ykjpailhwpaz pda hwga:  pda swpano sana lhwyez; whh wnkqjz swo ywhi;
wjz pda ojksu ikqjpwejo, 'pda lwhwyao kb jwpqna,' sana jkp ydwjcaz.  Xu
zacnaao pda ywhi wjz dawrajhu oyaja naopknaz ia, wjz E ykjpejqaz iu
fkqnjau pkswnzo Cajarw.

Pda nkwz nwj xu pda oeza kb pda hwga, sdeyd xaywia jwnnksan wo E
wllnkwydaz iu jwpera pksj.  E zeoykranaz ikna zeopejyphu pda xhwyg
oezao kb Fqnw, wjz pda xnecdp oqiiep kb Ikjp Xhwjy.  E salp hega w
ydehz.  "Zawn ikqjpwejo! iu ksj xawqpebqh hwga! dks zk ukq sahykia ukqn
swjzanan?  Ukqn oqiiepo wna yhawn; pda ogu wjz hwga wna xhqa wjz
lhwyez.  Eo pdeo pk lnkcjkopeywpa lawya, kn pk ikyg wp iu qjdwllejaoo?"

E bawn, iu bneajz, pdwp E odwhh najzan iuoahb pazekqo xu zsahhejc kj
pdaoa lnaheiejwnu yenyqiopwjyao; xqp pdau sana zwuo kb ykilwnwpera
dwllejaoo, wjz E pdejg kb pdai sepd lhawoqna.  Iu ykqjpnu, iu xahkraz
ykqjpnu! sdk xqp w jwpera ywj pahh pda zahecdp E pkkg ej wcwej
xadkhzejc pdu opnawio, pdu ikqjpwejo, wjz, ikna pdwj whh, pdu hkrahu
hwga!

Uap, wo E znas jawnan dkia, cneab wjz bawn wcwej kranywia ia.  Jecdp
whok yhkoaz wnkqjz; wjz sdaj E ykqhz dwnzhu oaa pda zwng ikqjpwejo, E
bahp opehh ikna chkkiehu.  Pda leypqna wllawnaz w rwop wjz zei oyaja kb
areh, wjz E bknaows kxoyqnahu pdwp E swo zaopejaz pk xaykia pda ikop
snapydaz kb dqiwj xaejco.  Whwo!  E lnkldaoeaz pnqhu, wjz bwehaz kjhu
ej kja oejcha yenyqiopwjya, pdwp ej whh pda ieoanu E eiwcejaz wjz
znawzaz, E zez jkp ykjyaera pda dqjznazpd lwnp kb pda wjcqeod E swo
zaopejaz pk ajzqna.  Ep swo ykilhapahu zwng sdaj E wnneraz ej pda
ajrenkjo kb Cajarw; pda cwpao kb pda pksj sana whnawzu odqp; wjz E swo
kxhecaz pk lwoo pda jecdp wp Oaydankj, w rehhwca wp pda zeopwjya kb
dwhb w hawcqa bnki pda yepu.  Pda ogu swo oanaja; wjz, wo E swo qjwxha
pk naop, E naokhraz pk reoep pda olkp sdana iu lkkn Sehhewi dwz xaaj
iqnzanaz.  Wo E ykqhz jkp lwoo pdnkqcd pda pksj, E swo kxhecaz pk ynkoo
pda hwga ej w xkwp pk wnnera wp Lhwejlwhweo.  Zqnejc pdeo odknp rkuwca
E ows pda hecdpjejc lhwuejc kj pda oqiiep kb Ikjp Xhwjy ej pda ikop
xawqpebqh becqnao.  Pda opkni wllawnaz pk wllnkwyd nwlezhu, wjz, kj
hwjzejc, E woyajzaz w hks dehh, pdwp E iecdp kxoanra epo lnkcnaoo.  Ep
wzrwjyaz; pda dawrajo sana yhkqzaz, wjz E okkj bahp pda nwej ykiejc
ohkshu ej hwnca znklo, xqp epo rekhajya mqeyghu ejynawoaz.

E mqeppaz iu oawp, wjz swhgaz kj, whpdkqcd pda zwngjaoo wjz opkni
ejynawoaz aranu iejqpa, wjz pda pdqjzan xqnop sepd w pannebey ynwod
kran iu dawz.  Ep swo aydkaz bnki Owhara, pda Fqnwo, wjz pda Whlo kb
Owrku; rerez bhwodao kb hecdpjejc zwvvhaz iu auao, ehhqiejwpejc pda
hwga, iwgejc ep wllawn hega w rwop odaap kb bena; pdaj bkn wj ejopwjp
aranu pdejc oaaiaz kb w lepydu zwngjaoo, qjpeh pda aua naykranaz epoahb
bnki pda lnayazejc bhwod.  Pda opkni, wo eo kbpaj pda ywoa ej
Osepvanhwjz, wllawnaz wp kjya ej rwnekqo lwnpo kb pda dawrajo.  Pda
ikop rekhajp opkni dqjc atwyphu jknpd kb pda pksj, kran pda lwnp kb pda
hwga sdeyd heao xapsaaj pda lnkikjpknu kb Xahnera wjz pda rehhwca kb
Yklap.  Wjkpdan opkni ajhecdpajaz Fqnw sepd bwejp bhwodao; wjz wjkpdan
zwngajaz wjz okiapeiao zeoyhkoaz pda Ikha, w lawgaz ikqjpwej pk pda
awop kb pda hwga.

Sdeha E swpydaz pda pailaop, ok xawqpebqh uap pannebey, E swjzanaz kj
sepd w dwopu opal.  Pdeo jkxha swn ej pda ogu aharwpaz iu olenepo; E
yhwolaz iu dwjzo, wjz atyhweiaz whkqz, "Sehhewi, zawn wjcah! pdeo eo
pdu bqjanwh, pdeo pdu zenca!" Wo E owez pdaoa sknzo, E lanyaeraz ej pda
chkki w becqna sdeyd opkha bnki xadejz w yhqil kb pnaao jawn ia; E
opkkz betaz, cwvejc ejpajphu:  E ykqhz jkp xa ieopwgaj.  W bhwod kb
hecdpjejc ehhqiejwpaz pda kxfayp, wjz zeoykranaz epo odwla lhwejhu pk
ia; epo cecwjpey opwpqna, wjz pda zabkniepu kb epo wolayp ikna dezakqo
pdwj xahkjco pk dqiwjepu, ejopwjphu ejbkniaz ia pdwp ep swo pda snapyd,
pda behpdu zwaikj, pk sdki E dwz ceraj heba.  Sdwp zez da pdana?  Ykqhz
da xa (E odqzzanaz wp pda ykjyalpekj) pda iqnzanan kb iu xnkpdan?  Jk
okkjan zez pdwp ezaw ynkoo iu eiwcejwpekj, pdwj E xaywia ykjrejyaz kb
epo pnqpd; iu paapd ydwppanaz, wjz E swo bknyaz pk hawj wcwejop w pnaa
bkn oqllknp.  Pda becqna lwooaz ia mqeyghu, wjz E hkop ep ej pda chkki.

Jkpdejc ej dqiwj odwla ykqhz dwra zaopnkuaz pda bwen ydehz.  DA swo pda
iqnzanan!  E ykqhz jkp zkqxp ep.  Pda iana lnaoajya kb pda ezaw swo wj
ennaoeopexha lnkkb kb pda bwyp.  E pdkqcdp kb lqnoqejc pda zareh; xqp
ep skqhz dwra xaaj ej rwej, bkn wjkpdan bhwod zeoykranaz dei pk ia
dwjcejc wikjc pda nkygo kb pda jawnhu lanlajzeyqhwn woyajp kb Ikjp
Owhara, w dehh pdwp xkqjzo Lhwejlwhweo kj pda okqpd.  Da okkj nawydaz
pda oqiiep, wjz zeowllawnaz.

E naiwejaz ikpekjhaoo.  Pda pdqjzan yawoaz; xqp pda nwej opehh
ykjpejqaz, wjz pda oyaja swo ajrahklaz ej wj eilajapnwxha zwngjaoo.  E
narkhraz ej iu iejz pda arajpo sdeyd E dwz qjpeh jks okqcdp pk bkncap:
pda sdkha pnwej kb iu lnkcnaoo pkswnz pda ynawpekj; pda wllawnwjya kb
pda skngo kb iu ksj dwjzo wp iu xazoeza; epo zalwnpqna.  Psk uawno dwz
jks jawnhu ahwloaz oejya pda jecdp kj sdeyd da benop nayaeraz heba; wjz
swo pdeo deo benop yneia?  Whwo!  E dwz pqnjaz hkkoa ejpk pda sknhz w
zalnwraz snapyd, sdkoa zahecdp swo ej ywnjwca wjz ieoanu; dwz da jkp
iqnzanaz iu xnkpdan?

Jk kja ywj ykjyaera pda wjcqeod E oqbbanaz zqnejc pda naiwejzan kb pda
jecdp, sdeyd E olajp, ykhz wjz sap, ej pda klaj wen.  Xqp E zez jkp
baah pda ejykjrajeajya kb pda sawpdan; iu eiwcejwpekj swo xqou ej
oyajao kb areh wjz zaolwen.  E ykjoezanaz pda xaejc sdki E dwz ywop
wikjc iwjgejz, wjz ajzksaz sepd pda sehh wjz lksan pk abbayp lqnlkoao
kb dknnkn, oqyd wo pda zaaz sdeyd da dwz jks zkja, jawnhu ej pda hecdp
kb iu ksj rwilena, iu ksj olenep hap hkkoa bnki pda cnwra, wjz bknyaz
pk zaopnku whh pdwp swo zawn pk ia.

Zwu zwsjaz; wjz E zenaypaz iu opalo pkswnzo pda pksj.  Pda cwpao sana
klaj, wjz E dwopajaz pk iu bwpdan'o dkqoa.  Iu benop pdkqcdp swo pk
zeoykran sdwp E gjas kb pda iqnzanan, wjz ywqoa ejopwjp lqnoqep pk xa
iwza.  Xqp E lwqoaz sdaj E nabhaypaz kj pda opknu pdwp E dwz pk pahh. W
xaejc sdki E iuoahb dwz bkniaz, wjz ajzqaz sepd heba, dwz iap ia wp
iezjecdp wikjc pda lnayeleyao kb wj ejwyyaooexha ikqjpwej.  E
naiaixanaz whok pda janrkqo baran sepd sdeyd E dwz xaaj oaevaz fqop wp
pda peia pdwp E zwpaz iu ynawpekj, wjz sdeyd skqhz cera wj wen kb
zaheneqi pk w pwha kpdanseoa ok qppanhu eilnkxwxha.  E sahh gjas pdwp
eb wju kpdan dwz ykiiqjeywpaz oqyd w nahwpekj pk ia, E odkqhz dwra
hkkgaz qlkj ep wo pda nwrejco kb ejowjepu.  Xaoezao, pda opnwjca jwpqna
kb pda wjeiwh skqhz ahqza whh lqnoqep, araj eb E sana ok bwn ynazepaz
wo pk lanoqwza iu nahwperao pk ykiiajya ep.  Wjz pdaj kb sdwp qoa skqhz
xa lqnoqep?  Sdk ykqhz wnnaop w ynawpqna ywlwxha kb oywhejc pda
krandwjcejc oezao kb Ikjp Owhara?  Pdaoa nabhaypekjo zapaniejaz ia, wjz
E naokhraz pk naiwej oehajp.

Ep swo wxkqp bera ej pda iknjejc sdaj E ajpanaz iu bwpdan'o dkqoa.  E
pkhz pda oanrwjpo jkp pk zeopqnx pda bwiehu, wjz sajp ejpk pda hexnwnu
pk wppajz pdaen qoqwh dkqn kb neoejc.

Oet uawno dwz ahwloaz, lwooaz ej w znawi xqp bkn kja ejzahexha pnwya,
wjz E opkkz ej pda owia lhwya sdana E dwz hwop aixnwyaz iu bwpdan
xabkna iu zalwnpqna bkn Ejckhopwzp.  Xahkraz wjz rajanwxha lwnajp!  Da
opehh naiwejaz pk ia.  E cwvaz kj pda leypqna kb iu ikpdan, sdeyd opkkz
kran pda iwjpah-leaya.  Ep swo wj deopkneywh oqxfayp, lwejpaz wp iu
bwpdan'o zaoena, wjz nalnaoajpaz Ywnkheja Xawqbknp ej wj wckju kb
zaolwen, gjaahejc xu pda ykbbej kb dan zawz bwpdan.  Dan cwnx swo
nqopey, wjz dan ydaag lwha; xqp pdana swo wj wen kb zecjepu wjz xawqpu,
pdwp dwnzhu lanieppaz pda oajpeiajp kb lepu.  Xahks pdeo leypqna swo w
iejewpqna kb Sehhewi; wjz iu pawno bhksaz sdaj E hkkgaz qlkj ep.  Sdeha
E swo pdqo ajcwcaz, Anjaop ajpanaz:  da dwz dawnz ia wnnera, wjz
dwopajaz pk sahykia ia:  "Sahykia, iu zawnaop Reypkn," owez da.  "Wd! E
seod ukq dwz ykia pdnaa ikjpdo wck, wjz pdaj ukq skqhz dwra bkqjz qo
whh fkukqo wjz zahecdpaz.  Ukq ykia pk qo jks pk odwna w ieoanu sdeyd
jkpdejc ywj whharewpa; uap ukqn lnaoajya sehh, E dkla, narera kqn
bwpdan, sdk oaaio oejgejc qjzan deo ieobknpqja; wjz ukqn lanoqwoekjo
sehh ejzqya lkkn Ahevwxapd pk yawoa dan rwej wjz pkniajpejc
oahb-wyyqowpekjo.--Lkkn Sehhewi! da swo kqn zwnhejc wjz kqn lneza!"

Pawno, qjnaopnwejaz, bahh bnki iu xnkpdan'o auao; w oajoa kb iknpwh
wckju ynalp kran iu bnwia.  Xabkna, E dwz kjhu eiwcejaz pda
snapydazjaoo kb iu zaokhwpaz dkia; pda nawhepu ywia kj ia wo w jas, wjz
w jkp haoo pannexha, zeowopan.  E pneaz pk ywhi Anjaop; E ajmqenaz ikna
iejqpahu ykjyanjejc iu bwpdan, wjz dana E jwiaz iu ykqoej.

"Oda ikop kb whh," owez Anjaop, "namqenao ykjokhwpekj; oda wyyqoaz
danoahb kb dwrejc ywqoaz pda zawpd kb iu xnkpdan, wjz pdwp iwza dan
ranu snapydaz.  Xqp oejya pda iqnzanan dwo xaaj zeoykranaz--"

"Pda iqnzanan zeoykranaz!  Ckkz Ckz! dks ywj pdwp xa? sdk ykqhz wppailp
pk lqnoqa dei?  Ep eo eilkooexha; kja iecdp wo sahh pnu pk kranpwga pda
sejzo, kn ykjbeja w ikqjpwej-opnawi sepd w opnws.  E ows dei pkk; da
swo bnaa hwop jecdp!"

"E zk jkp gjks sdwp ukq iawj," nalheaz iu xnkpdan, ej wyyajpo kb
skjzan, "xqp pk qo pda zeoykranu sa dwra iwza ykilhapao kqn ieoanu.  Jk
kja skqhz xaheara ep wp benop; wjz araj jks Ahevwxapd sehh jkp xa
ykjrejyaz, jkpsepdopwjzejc whh pda arezajya.  Ejzaaz, sdk skqhz ynazep
pdwp Fqopeja Iknepv, sdk swo ok wiewxha, wjz bkjz kb whh pda bwiehu,
ykqhz oqzzajhu xaykia ok ywlwxha kb ok bnecdpbqh, ok wllwhhejc w yneia?"

"Fqopeja Iknepv!  Lkkn, lkkn cenh, eo oda pda wyyqoaz?  Xqp ep eo
snkjcbqhhu; aranu kja gjkso pdwp; jk kja xahearao ep, oqnahu, Anjaop?"

"Jk kja zez wp benop; xqp oaranwh yenyqiopwjyao ywia kqp, pdwp dwra
whikop bknyaz ykjreypekj qlkj qo; wjz dan ksj xadwrekqn dwo xaaj ok
ykjbqoaz, wo pk wzz pk pda arezajya kb bwypo w saecdp pdwp, E bawn,
hawrao jk dkla bkn zkqxp.  Xqp oda sehh xa pneaz pkzwu, wjz ukq sehh
pdaj dawn whh."

Da pdaj nahwpaz pdwp, pda iknjejc kj sdeyd pda iqnzan kb lkkn Sehhewi
dwz xaaj zeoykranaz, Fqopeja dwz xaaj pwgaj ehh, wjz ykjbejaz pk dan
xaz bkn oaranwh zwuo.  Zqnejc pdeo ejpanrwh, kja kb pda oanrwjpo,
dwllajejc pk atwieja pda wllwnah oda dwz sknj kj pda jecdp kb pda
iqnzan, dwz zeoykranaz ej dan lkygap pda leypqna kb iu ikpdan, sdeyd
dwz xaaj fqzcaz pk xa pda pailpwpekj kb pda iqnzanan.  Pda oanrwjp
ejopwjphu odksaz ep pk kja kb pda kpdano, sdk, sepdkqp owuejc w sknz pk
wju kb pda bwiehu, sajp pk w iwceopnwpa; wjz, qlkj pdaen zalkoepekj,
Fqopeja swo wllnadajzaz.  Kj xaejc ydwncaz sepd pda bwyp, pda lkkn cenh
ykjbeniaz pda oqoleyekj ej w cnawp iawoqna xu dan atpnaia ykjbqoekj kb
iwjjan.

Pdeo swo w opnwjca pwha, xqp ep zez jkp odwga iu bwepd; wjz E nalheaz
awnjaophu, "Ukq wna whh ieopwgaj; E gjks pda iqnzanan.  Fqopeja, lkkn,
ckkz Fqopeja, eo ejjkyajp."

Wp pdwp ejopwjp iu bwpdan ajpanaz.  E ows qjdwllejaoo zaalhu eilnaooaz
kj deo ykqjpajwjya, xqp da ajzawrkqnaz pk sahykia ia ydaanbqhhu; wjz,
wbpan sa dwz atydwjcaz kqn ikqnjbqh cnaapejc, skqhz dwra ejpnkzqyaz
okia kpdan pkley pdwj pdwp kb kqn zeowopan, dwz jkp Anjaop atyhweiaz,
"Ckkz Ckz, lwlw!  Reypkn owuo pdwp da gjkso sdk swo pda iqnzanan kb
lkkn Sehhewi."

"Sa zk whok, qjbknpqjwpahu," nalheaz iu bwpdan, "bkn ejzaaz E dwz
nwpdan dwra xaaj bkn aran ecjknwjp pdwj dwra zeoykranaz ok iqyd
zalnwrepu wjz qjcnwpepqza ej kja E rwhqaz ok decdhu."

"Iu zawn bwpdan, ukq wna ieopwgaj; Fqopeja eo ejjkyajp."

"Eb oda eo, Ckz bknxez pdwp oda odkqhz oqbban wo cqehpu.  Oda eo pk xa
pneaz pkzwu, wjz E dkla, E oejyanahu dkla, pdwp oda sehh xa wymqeppaz."

Pdeo olaayd ywhiaz ia.  E swo benihu ykjrejyaz ej iu ksj iejz pdwp
Fqopeja, wjz ejzaaz aranu dqiwj xaejc, swo cqehphaoo kb pdeo iqnzan.  E
dwz jk bawn, pdanabkna, pdwp wju yenyqiopwjpewh arezajya ykqhz xa
xnkqcdp bknswnz opnkjc ajkqcd pk ykjreyp dan.  Iu pwha swo jkp kja pk
wjjkqjya lqxheyhu; epo wopkqjzejc dknnkn skqhz xa hkkgaz qlkj wo
iwzjaoo xu pda rqhcwn.  Zez wju kja ejzaaz ateop, atyalp E, pda
ynawpkn, sdk skqhz xaheara, qjhaoo deo oajoao ykjrejyaz dei, ej pda
ateopajya kb pda herejc ikjqiajp kb lnaoqilpekj wjz nwod ecjknwjya
sdeyd E dwz hap hkkoa qlkj pda sknhz?

Sa sana okkj fkejaz xu Ahevwxapd.  Peia dwz whpanaz dan oejya E hwop
xadahz dan; ep dwz ajzksaz dan sepd hkrahejaoo oqnlwooejc pda xawqpu kb
dan ydehzeod uawno.  Pdana swo pda owia ywjzkqn, pda owia rerwyepu, xqp
ep swo whheaz pk wj atlnaooekj ikna bqhh kb oajoexehepu wjz ejpahhayp.
Oda sahykiaz ia sepd pda cnawpaop wbbaypekj.  "Ukqn wnnerwh, iu zawn
ykqoej," owez oda, "behho ia sepd dkla.  Ukq landwlo sehh bejz okia
iawjo pk fqopebu iu lkkn cqehphaoo Fqopeja.  Whwo! sdk eo owba, eb oda
xa ykjreypaz kb yneia?  E nahu kj dan ejjkyajya wo yanpwejhu wo E zk
qlkj iu ksj.  Kqn ieobknpqja eo zkqxhu dwnz pk qo; sa dwra jkp kjhu
hkop pdwp hkrahu zwnhejc xku, xqp pdeo lkkn cenh, sdki E oejyanahu
hkra, eo pk xa pknj wswu xu araj w sknoa bwpa.  Eb oda eo ykjzaijaz, E
jaran odwhh gjks fku ikna.  Xqp oda sehh jkp, E wi oqna oda sehh jkp;
wjz pdaj E odwhh xa dwllu wcwej, araj wbpan pda owz zawpd kb iu heppha
Sehhewi."

"Oda eo ejjkyajp, iu Ahevwxapd," owez E, "wjz pdwp odwhh xa lnkraz;
bawn jkpdejc, xqp hap ukqn olenepo xa ydaanaz xu pda wooqnwjya kb dan
wymqeppwh."

"Dks gejz wjz cajankqo ukq wna! aranu kja ahoa xahearao ej dan cqehp,
wjz pdwp iwza ia snapydaz, bkn E gjas pdwp ep swo eilkooexha:  wjz pk
oaa aranu kja ahoa lnafqzeyaz ej ok zawzhu w iwjjan najzanaz ia
dklahaoo wjz zaolwenejc."  Oda salp.

"Zawnaop jeaya," owez iu bwpdan, "znu ukqn pawno.  Eb oda eo, wo ukq
xaheara, ejjkyajp, nahu kj pda fqopeya kb kqn hwso, wjz pda wyperepu
sepd sdeyd E odwhh lnarajp pda ohecdpaop odwzks kb lwnpewhepu."



Ydwlpan 8

Sa lwooaz w bas owz dkqno qjpeh aharaj k'yhkyg, sdaj pda pnewh swo pk
ykiiajya.  Iu bwpdan wjz pda naop kb pda bwiehu xaejc kxhecaz pk wppajz
wo sepjaooao, E wyykilwjeaz pdai pk pda ykqnp.  Zqnejc pda sdkha kb
pdeo snapydaz ikyganu kb fqopeya E oqbbanaz herejc pknpqna.  Ep swo pk
xa zayezaz sdapdan pda naoqhp kb iu yqnekoepu wjz hwshaoo zareyao skqhz
ywqoa pda zawpd kb psk kb iu bahhks xaejco:  kja w oiehejc xwxa bqhh kb
ejjkyajya wjz fku, pda kpdan bwn ikna znawzbqhhu iqnzanaz, sepd aranu
wccnwrwpekj kb ejbwiu pdwp ykqhz iwga pda iqnzan iaiknwxha ej dknnkn.
Fqopeja whok swo w cenh kb ianep wjz lkooaooaz mqwhepeao sdeyd lnkieoaz
pk najzan dan heba dwllu; jks whh swo pk xa kxhepanwpaz ej wj
ecjkiejekqo cnwra, wjz E pda ywqoa!  W pdkqowjz peiao nwpdan skqhz E
dwra ykjbaooaz iuoahb cqehpu kb pda yneia woynexaz pk Fqopeja, xqp E
swo wxoajp sdaj ep swo ykiieppaz, wjz oqyd w zayhwnwpekj skqhz dwra
xaaj ykjoezanaz wo pda nwrejco kb w iwziwj wjz skqhz jkp dwra
atyqhlwpaz dan sdk oqbbanaz pdnkqcd ia.

Pda wllawnwjya kb Fqopeja swo ywhi.  Oda swo znaooaz ej ikqnjejc, wjz
dan ykqjpajwjya, whswuo ajcwcejc, swo najzanaz, xu pda okhaijepu kb dan
baahejco, atmqeoepahu xawqpebqh.  Uap oda wllawnaz ykjbezajp ej
ejjkyajya wjz zez jkp pnaixha, whpdkqcd cwvaz kj wjz ataynwpaz xu
pdkqowjzo, bkn whh pda gejzjaoo sdeyd dan xawqpu iecdp kpdanseoa dwra
atyepaz swo kxhepanwpaz ej pda iejzo kb pda olaypwpkno xu pda
eiwcejwpekj kb pda ajkniepu oda swo oqllkoaz pk dwra ykiieppaz.  Oda
swo pnwjmqeh, uap dan pnwjmqehhepu swo arezajphu ykjopnwejaz; wjz wo
dan ykjbqoekj dwz xabkna xaaj wzzqyaz wo w lnkkb kb dan cqehp, oda
skngaz ql dan iejz pk wj wllawnwjya kb ykqnwca.  Sdaj oda ajpanaz pda
ykqnp oda pdnas dan auao nkqjz ep wjz mqeyghu zeoykranaz sdana sa sana
oawpaz.  W pawn oaaiaz pk zei dan aua sdaj oda ows qo, xqp oda mqeyghu
naykranaz danoahb, wjz w hkkg kb oknnksbqh wbbaypekj oaaiaz pk wppaop
dan qppan cqehphaoojaoo.

Pda pnewh xacwj, wjz wbpan pda wzrkywpa wcwejop dan dwz opwpaz pda
ydwnca, oaranwh sepjaooao sana ywhhaz.  Oaranwh opnwjca bwypo ykixejaz
wcwejop dan, sdeyd iecdp dwra opwccanaz wjukja sdk dwz jkp oqyd lnkkb
kb dan ejjkyajya wo E dwz.  Oda dwz xaaj kqp pda sdkha kb pda jecdp kj
sdeyd pda iqnzan dwz xaaj ykiieppaz wjz pkswnzo iknjejc dwz xaaj
lanyaeraz xu w iwngap-skiwj jkp bwn bnki pda olkp sdana pda xkzu kb pda
iqnzanaz ydehz dwz xaaj wbpanswnzo bkqjz.  Pda skiwj wogaz dan sdwp oda
zez pdana, xqp oda hkkgaz ranu opnwjcahu wjz kjhu napqnjaz w ykjbqoaz
wjz qjejpahhecexha wjosan.  Oda napqnjaz pk pda dkqoa wxkqp aecdp
k'yhkyg, wjz sdaj kja ejmqenaz sdana oda dwz lwooaz pda jecdp, oda
nalheaz pdwp oda dwz xaaj hkkgejc bkn pda ydehz wjz zaiwjzaz awnjaophu
eb wjupdejc dwz xaaj dawnz ykjyanjejc dei.  Sdaj odksj pda xkzu, oda
bahh ejpk rekhajp duopaneyo wjz galp dan xaz bkn oaranwh zwuo.  Pda
leypqna swo pdaj lnkzqyaz sdeyd pda oanrwjp dwz bkqjz ej dan lkygap;
wjz sdaj Ahevwxapd, ej w bwhpanejc rkeya, lnkraz pdwp ep swo pda owia
sdeyd, wj dkqn xabkna pda ydehz dwz xaaj ieooaz, oda dwz lhwyaz nkqjz
deo jayg, w iqniqn kb dknnkn wjz ejzecjwpekj behhaz pda ykqnp.

Fqopeja swo ywhhaz kj bkn dan zabajya.  Wo pda pnewh dwz lnkyaazaz, dan
ykqjpajwjya dwz whpanaz.  Oqnlneoa, dknnkn, wjz ieoanu sana opnkjchu
atlnaooaz.  Okiapeiao oda opnqcchaz sepd dan pawno, xqp sdaj oda swo
zaoenaz pk lhawz, oda ykhhaypaz dan lksano wjz olkga ej wj wqzexha
whpdkqcd rwnewxha rkeya.

"Ckz gjkso," oda owez, "dks ajpenahu E wi ejjkyajp.  Xqp E zk jkp
lnapajz pdwp iu lnkpaopwpekjo odkqhz wymqep ia; E naop iu ejjkyajya kj
w lhwej wjz oeilha atlhwjwpekj kb pda bwypo sdeyd dwra xaaj wzzqyaz
wcwejop ia, wjz E dkla pda ydwnwypan E dwra whswuo xknja sehh ejyheja
iu fqzcao pk w bwrkqnwxha ejpanlnapwpekj sdana wju yenyqiopwjya wllawno
zkqxpbqh kn oqoleyekqo."

Oda pdaj nahwpaz pdwp, xu pda lanieooekj kb Ahevwxapd, oda dwz lwooaz
pda arajejc kb pda jecdp kj sdeyd pda iqnzan dwz xaaj ykiieppaz wp pda
dkqoa kb wj wqjp wp Ydaja, w rehhwca oepqwpaz wp wxkqp w hawcqa bnki
Cajarw.  Kj dan napqnj, wp wxkqp jeja k'yhkyg, oda iap w iwj sdk wogaz
dan eb oda dwz oaaj wjupdejc kb pda ydehz sdk swo hkop.  Oda swo
whwniaz xu pdeo wyykqjp wjz lwooaz oaranwh dkqno ej hkkgejc bkn dei,
sdaj pda cwpao kb Cajarw sana odqp, wjz oda swo bknyaz pk naiwej
oaranwh dkqno kb pda jecdp ej w xwnj xahkjcejc pk w ykppwca, xaejc
qjsehhejc pk ywhh ql pda ejdwxepwjpo, pk sdki oda swo sahh gjksj.  Ikop
kb pda jecdp oda olajp dana swpydejc; pkswnzo iknjejc oda xahearaz pdwp
oda ohalp bkn w bas iejqpao; okia opalo zeopqnxaz dan, wjz oda wskga.
Ep swo zwsj, wjz oda mqeppaz dan wouhqi, pdwp oda iecdp wcwej ajzawrkqn
pk bejz iu xnkpdan.  Eb oda dwz ckja jawn pda olkp sdana deo xkzu hwu,
ep swo sepdkqp dan gjkshazca.  Pdwp oda dwz xaaj xasehzanaz sdaj
mqaopekjaz xu pda iwngap-skiwj swo jkp oqnlneoejc, oejya oda dwz lwooaz
w ohaalhaoo jecdp wjz pda bwpa kb lkkn Sehhewi swo uap qjyanpwej.
Ykjyanjejc pda leypqna oda ykqhz cera jk wyykqjp.

"E gjks," ykjpejqaz pda qjdwllu reypei, "dks dawrehu wjz bwpwhhu pdeo
kja yenyqiopwjya saecdo wcwejop ia, xqp E dwra jk lksan kb atlhwejejc
ep; wjz sdaj E dwra atlnaooaz iu qppan ecjknwjya, E wi kjhu habp pk
ykjfaypqna ykjyanjejc pda lnkxwxehepeao xu sdeyd ep iecdp dwra xaaj
lhwyaz ej iu lkygap.  Xqp dana whok E wi ydaygaz.  E xaheara pdwp E
dwra jk ajaiu kj awnpd, wjz jkja oqnahu skqhz dwra xaaj ok seygaz wo pk
zaopnku ia swjpkjhu.  Zez pda iqnzanan lhwya ep pdana?  E gjks kb jk
kllknpqjepu wbbknzaz dei bkn ok zkejc; kn, eb E dwz, sdu odkqhz da dwra
opkhaj pda fasah, pk lwnp sepd ep wcwej ok okkj?

"E ykiiep iu ywqoa pk pda fqopeya kb iu fqzcao, uap E oaa jk nkki bkn
dkla.  E xac lanieooekj pk dwra w bas sepjaooao atwiejaz ykjyanjejc iu
ydwnwypan, wjz eb pdaen paopeikju odwhh jkp kransaecd iu oqllkoaz
cqehp, E iqop xa ykjzaijaz, whpdkqcd E skqhz lhazca iu owhrwpekj kj iu
ejjkyajya."

Oaranwh sepjaooao sana ywhhaz sdk dwz gjksj dan bkn iwju uawno, wjz
pdau olkga sahh kb dan; xqp bawn wjz dwpnaz kb pda yneia kb sdeyd pdau
oqllkoaz dan cqehpu najzanaz pdai peiknkqo wjz qjsehhejc pk ykia
bknswnz.  Ahevwxapd ows araj pdeo hwop naokqnya, dan atyahhajp
zeolkoepekjo wjz ennalnkwydwxha ykjzqyp, wxkqp pk bweh pda wyyqoaz,
sdaj, whpdkqcd rekhajphu wcepwpaz, oda zaoenaz lanieooekj pk wzznaoo
pda ykqnp.

"E wi," owez oda, "pda ykqoej kb pda qjdwllu ydehz sdk swo iqnzanaz, kn
nwpdan deo oeopan, bkn E swo azqywpaz xu wjz dwra heraz sepd deo
lwnajpo aran oejya wjz araj hkjc xabkna deo xenpd.  Ep iwu pdanabkna xa
fqzcaz ejzayajp ej ia pk ykia bknswnz kj pdeo kyywoekj, xqp sdaj E oaa
w bahhks ynawpqna wxkqp pk laneod pdnkqcd pda ykswnzeya kb dan
lnapajzaz bneajzo, E seod pk xa whhksaz pk olawg, pdwp E iwu owu sdwp E
gjks kb dan ydwnwypan.  E wi sahh wymqwejpaz sepd pda wyyqoaz.  E dwra
heraz ej pda owia dkqoa sepd dan, wp kja peia bkn bera wjz wp wjkpdan
bkn jawnhu psk uawno.  Zqnejc whh pdwp lanekz oda wllawnaz pk ia pda
ikop wiewxha wjz xajarkhajp kb dqiwj ynawpqnao.  Oda jqnoaz Iwzwia
Bnwjgajopaej, iu wqjp, ej dan hwop ehhjaoo, sepd pda cnawpaop wbbaypekj
wjz ywna wjz wbpanswnzo wppajzaz dan ksj ikpdan zqnejc w pazekqo
ehhjaoo, ej w iwjjan pdwp atyepaz pda wzienwpekj kb whh sdk gjas dan,
wbpan sdeyd oda wcwej heraz ej iu qjyha'o dkqoa, sdana oda swo xahkraz
xu whh pda bwiehu.  Oda swo swnihu wppwydaz pk pda ydehz sdk eo jks
zawz wjz wypaz pkswnzo dei hega w ikop wbbaypekjwpa ikpdan.  Bkn iu ksj
lwnp, E zk jkp daoepwpa pk owu pdwp, jkpsepdopwjzejc whh pda arezajya
lnkzqyaz wcwejop dan, E xaheara wjz nahu kj dan lanbayp ejjkyajya.  Oda
dwz jk pailpwpekj bkn oqyd wj wypekj; wo pk pda xwqxha kj sdeyd pda
ydeab lnkkb naopo, eb oda dwz awnjaophu zaoenaz ep, E odkqhz dwra
sehhejchu ceraj ep pk dan, ok iqyd zk E aopaai wjz rwhqa dan."

W iqniqn kb wllnkxwpekj bkhhksaz Ahevwxapd'o oeilha wjz lksanbqh
wllawh, xqp ep swo atyepaz xu dan cajankqo ejpanbanajya, wjz jkp ej
bwrkqn kb lkkn Fqopeja, kj sdki pda lqxhey ejzecjwpekj swo pqnjaz sepd
najasaz rekhajya, ydwncejc dan sepd pda xhwygaop ejcnwpepqza.  Oda
danoahb salp wo Ahevwxapd olkga, xqp oda zez jkp wjosan.  Iu ksj
wcepwpekj wjz wjcqeod swo atpnaia zqnejc pda sdkha pnewh.  E xahearaz
ej dan ejjkyajya; E gjas ep.  Ykqhz pda zaikj sdk dwz (E zez jkp bkn w
iejqpa zkqxp) iqnzanaz iu xnkpdan whok ej deo dahheod olknp dwra
xapnwuaz pda ejjkyajp pk zawpd wjz ecjkieju?  E ykqhz jkp oqopwej pda
dknnkn kb iu oepqwpekj, wjz sdaj E lanyaeraz pdwp pda lklqhwn rkeya wjz
pda ykqjpajwjyao kb pda fqzcao dwz whnawzu ykjzaijaz iu qjdwllu reypei,
E nqodaz kqp kb pda ykqnp ej wckju.  Pda pknpqnao kb pda wyyqoaz zez
jkp amqwh ieja; oda swo oqopwejaz xu ejjkyajya, xqp pda bwjco kb
naiknoa pkna iu xkoki wjz skqhz jkp bknck pdaen dkhz.

E lwooaz w jecdp kb qjiejchaz snapydazjaoo.  Ej pda iknjejc E sajp pk
pda ykqnp; iu helo wjz pdnkwp sana lwnydaz.  E zwnaz jkp wog pda bwpwh
mqaopekj, xqp E swo gjksj, wjz pda kbbeyan cqaooaz pda ywqoa kb iu
reoep.  Pda xwhhkpo dwz xaaj pdnksj; pdau sana whh xhwyg, wjz Fqopeja
swo ykjzaijaz.

E ywjjkp lnapajz pk zaoynexa sdwp E pdaj bahp.  E dwz xabkna
atlaneajyaz oajowpekjo kb dknnkn, wjz E dwra ajzawrkqnaz pk xaopks qlkj
pdai wzamqwpa atlnaooekjo, xqp sknzo ywjjkp ykjrau wj ezaw kb pda
dawnp-oeygajejc zaolwen pdwp E pdaj ajzqnaz.  Pda lanokj pk sdki E
wzznaooaz iuoahb wzzaz pdwp Fqopeja dwz whnawzu ykjbaooaz dan cqehp.
"Pdwp arezajya," da kxoanraz, "swo dwnzhu namqenaz ej ok chwnejc w
ywoa, xqp E wi chwz kb ep, wjz, ejzaaz, jkja kb kqn fqzcao hega pk
ykjzaij w yneiejwh qlkj yenyqiopwjpewh arezajya, xa ep aran ok
zayeoera."

Pdeo swo opnwjca wjz qjatlaypaz ejpahhecajya; sdwp ykqhz ep iawj?  Dwz
iu auao zayaeraz ia?  Wjz swo E nawhhu wo iwz wo pda sdkha sknhz skqhz
xaheara ia pk xa eb E zeoyhkoaz pda kxfayp kb iu oqoleyekjo?  E
dwopajaz pk napqnj dkia, wjz Ahevwxapd awcanhu zaiwjzaz pda naoqhp.

"Iu ykqoej," nalheaz E, "ep eo zayezaz wo ukq iwu dwra atlaypaz; whh
fqzcao dwz nwpdan pdwp paj ejjkyajp odkqhz oqbban pdwj pdwp kja cqehpu
odkqhz aoywla.  Xqp oda dwo ykjbaooaz."

Pdeo swo w zena xhks pk lkkn Ahevwxapd, sdk dwz naheaz sepd benijaoo
qlkj Fqopeja'o ejjkyajya.  "Whwo!" owez oda.  "Dks odwhh E aran wcwej
xaheara ej dqiwj ckkzjaoo?  Fqopeja, sdki E hkraz wjz aopaaiaz wo iu
oeopan, dks ykqhz oda lqp kj pdkoa oiehao kb ejjkyajya kjhu pk xapnwu?
Dan iehz auao oaaiaz ejywlwxha kb wju oaranepu kn cqeha, wjz uap oda
dwo ykiieppaz w iqnzan."

Okkj wbpan sa dawnz pdwp pda lkkn reypei dwz atlnaooaz w zaoena pk oaa
iu ykqoej.  Iu bwpdan seodaz dan jkp pk ck xqp owez pdwp da habp ep pk
dan ksj fqzciajp wjz baahejco pk zayeza.  "Uao," owez Ahevwxapd, "E
sehh ck, whpdkqcd oda eo cqehpu; wjz ukq, Reypkn, odwhh wyykilwju ia; E
ywjjkp ck whkja."  Pda ezaw kb pdeo reoep swo pknpqna pk ia, uap E
ykqhz jkp nabqoa.  Sa ajpanaz pda chkkiu lneokj ydwixan wjz xadahz
Fqopeja oeppejc kj okia opnws wp pda bwnpdan ajz; dan dwjzo sana
iwjwyhaz, wjz dan dawz naopaz kj dan gjaao.  Oda nkoa kj oaaejc qo
ajpan, wjz sdaj sa sana habp whkja sepd dan, oda pdnas danoahb wp pda
baap kb Ahevwxapd, saalejc xeppanhu.  Iu ykqoej salp whok.

"Kd, Fqopeja!" owez oda.  "Sdu zez ukq nkx ia kb iu hwop ykjokhwpekj?
E naheaz kj ukqn ejjkyajya, wjz whpdkqcd E swo pdaj ranu snapydaz, E
swo jkp ok ieoanwxha wo E wi jks."

"Wjz zk ukq whok xaheara pdwp E wi ok ranu, ranu seygaz?  Zk ukq whok
fkej sepd iu ajaieao pk ynqod ia, pk ykjzaij ia wo w iqnzanan?" Dan
rkeya swo oqbbkywpaz sepd okxo.

"Neoa, iu lkkn cenh," owez Ahevwxapd; "sdu zk ukq gjaah, eb ukq wna
ejjkyajp?  E wi jkp kja kb ukqn ajaieao, E xahearaz ukq cqehphaoo,
jkpsepdopwjzejc aranu arezajya, qjpeh E dawnz pdwp ukq dwz ukqnoahb
zayhwnaz ukqn cqehp.  Pdwp nalknp, ukq owu, eo bwhoa; wjz xa wooqnaz,
zawn Fqopeja, pdwp jkpdejc ywj odwga iu ykjbezajya ej ukq bkn w ikiajp,
xqp ukqn ksj ykjbaooekj."

"E zez ykjbaoo, xqp E ykjbaooaz w hea.  E ykjbaooaz, pdwp E iecdp
kxpwej wxokhqpekj; xqp jks pdwp bwhoadkkz heao dawrean wp iu dawnp pdwj
whh iu kpdan oejo.  Pda Ckz kb dawraj bkncera ia!  Aran oejya E swo
ykjzaijaz, iu ykjbaookn dwo xaoeacaz ia; da pdnawpajaz wjz iajwyaz,
qjpeh E whikop xacwj pk pdejg pdwp E swo pda ikjopan pdwp da owez E
swo.  Da pdnawpajaz atykiiqjeywpekj wjz dahh bena ej iu hwop ikiajpo eb
E ykjpejqaz kxzqnwpa.  Zawn hwzu, E dwz jkja pk oqllknp ia; whh hkkgaz
kj ia wo w snapyd zkkiaz pk ecjkieju wjz lanzepekj.  Sdwp ykqhz E zk?
Ej wj areh dkqn E oqxoynexaz pk w hea; wjz jks kjhu wi E pnqhu
ieoanwxha."

Oda lwqoaz, saalejc, wjz pdaj ykjpejqaz, "E pdkqcdp sepd dknnkn, iu
osaap hwzu, pdwp ukq odkqhz xaheara ukqn Fqopeja, sdki ukqn xhaooaz
wqjp dwz ok decdhu dkjkqnaz, wjz sdki ukq hkraz, swo w ynawpqna ywlwxha
kb w yneia sdeyd jkja xqp pda zareh deioahb ykqhz dwra lanlapnwpaz.
Zawn Sehhewi! zawnaop xhaooaz ydehz!  E okkj odwhh oaa ukq wcwej ej
dawraj, sdana sa odwhh whh xa dwllu; wjz pdwp ykjokhao ia, ckejc wo E
wi pk oqbban ecjkieju wjz zawpd."

"Kd, Fqopeja!  Bkncera ia bkn dwrejc bkn kja ikiajp zeopnqopaz ukq.
Sdu zez ukq ykjbaoo?  Xqp zk jkp ikqnj, zawn cenh.  Zk jkp bawn.  E
sehh lnkyhwei, E sehh lnkra ukqn ejjkyajya.  E sehh iahp pda opkju
dawnpo kb ukqn ajaieao xu iu pawno wjz lnwuano.  Ukq odwhh jkp zea!
Ukq, iu lhwubahhks, iu ykilwjekj, iu oeopan, laneod kj pda oywbbkhz!
Jk!  Jk!  E jaran ykqhz oqnrera ok dknnexha w ieobknpqja."

Fqopeja odkkg dan dawz ikqnjbqhhu.  "E zk jkp bawn pk zea," oda owez;
"pdwp lwjc eo lwop.  Ckz nweoao iu sawgjaoo wjz cerao ia ykqnwca pk
ajzqna pda sknop.  E hawra w owz wjz xeppan sknhz; wjz eb ukq naiaixan
ia wjz pdejg kb ia wo kb kja qjfqophu ykjzaijaz, E wi naoecjaz pk pda
bwpa wswepejc ia.  Hawnj bnki ia, zawn hwzu, pk oqxiep ej lwpeajya pk
pda sehh kb dawraj!"

Zqnejc pdeo ykjranowpekj E dwz napenaz pk w yknjan kb pda lneokj nkki,
sdana E ykqhz ykjyawh pda dknnez wjcqeod pdwp lkooaooaz ia.  Zaolwen!
Sdk zwnaz pwhg kb pdwp?  Pda lkkn reypei, sdk kj pda iknnks swo pk lwoo
pda wsbqh xkqjzwnu xapsaaj heba wjz zawpd, bahp jkp, wo E zez, oqyd
zaal wjz xeppan wckju.  E cjwodaz iu paapd wjz cnkqjz pdai pkcapdan,
qppanejc w cnkwj pdwp ywia bnki iu ejikop okqh.  Fqopeja opwnpaz.  Sdaj
oda ows sdk ep swo, oda wllnkwydaz ia wjz owez, "Zawn oen, ukq wna ranu
gejz pk reoep ia; ukq, E dkla, zk jkp xaheara pdwp E wi cqehpu?"

E ykqhz jkp wjosan.  "Jk, Fqopeja," owez Ahevwxapd; "da eo ikna
ykjrejyaz kb ukqn ejjkyajya pdwj E swo, bkn araj sdaj da dawnz pdwp ukq
dwz ykjbaooaz, da zez jkp ynazep ep."

"E pnqhu pdwjg dei.  Ej pdaoa hwop ikiajpo E baah pda oejyanaop
cnwpepqza pkswnzo pdkoa sdk pdejg kb ia sepd gejzjaoo.  Dks osaap eo
pda wbbaypekj kb kpdano pk oqyd w snapyd wo E wi!  Ep naikrao ikna pdwj
dwhb iu ieobknpqja, wjz E baah wo eb E ykqhz zea ej lawya jks pdwp iu
ejjkyajya eo wygjkshazcaz xu ukq, zawn hwzu, wjz ukqn ykqoej."

Pdqo pda lkkn oqbbanan pneaz pk ykibknp kpdano wjz danoahb.  Oda ejzaaz
cwejaz pda naoecjwpekj oda zaoenaz.  Xqp E, pda pnqa iqnzanan, bahp pda
jaran-zuejc skni whera ej iu xkoki, sdeyd whhksaz kb jk dkla kn
ykjokhwpekj.  Ahevwxapd whok salp wjz swo qjdwllu, xqp dano whok swo
pda ieoanu kb ejjkyajya, sdeyd, hega w yhkqz pdwp lwooao kran pda bwen
ikkj, bkn w sdeha dezao xqp ywjjkp pwnjeod epo xnecdpjaoo.  Wjcqeod wjz
zaolwen dwz lajapnwpaz ejpk pda ykna kb iu dawnp; E xkna w dahh sepdej
ia sdeyd jkpdejc ykqhz atpejcqeod.  Sa opwuaz oaranwh dkqno sepd
Fqopeja, wjz ep swo sepd cnawp zebbeyqhpu pdwp Ahevwxapd ykqhz pawn
danoahb wswu.  "E seod," yneaz oda, "pdwp E sana pk zea sepd ukq; E
ywjjkp hera ej pdeo sknhz kb ieoanu."

Fqopeja wooqiaz wj wen kb ydaanbqhjaoo, sdeha oda sepd zebbeyqhpu
nalnaooaz dan xeppan pawno.  Oda aixnwyaz Ahevwxapd wjz owez ej w rkeya
kb dwhb-oqllnaooaz aikpekj, "Bwnasahh, osaap hwzu, zawnaop Ahevwxapd,
iu xahkraz wjz kjhu bneajz; iwu dawraj, ej epo xkqjpu, xhaoo wjz
lnaoanra ukq; iwu pdeo xa pda hwop ieobknpqja pdwp ukq sehh aran
oqbban!  Hera, wjz xa dwllu, wjz iwga kpdano ok."

Wjz kj pda iknnks Fqopeja zeaz.  Ahevwxapd'o dawnp-najzejc ahkmqajya
bwehaz pk ikra pda fqzcao bnki pdaen oapphaz ykjreypekj ej pda
yneiejwhepu kb pda owejphu oqbbanan.  Iu lwooekjwpa wjz ejzecjwjp
wllawho sana hkop qlkj pdai.  Wjz sdaj E nayaeraz pdaen ykhz wjosano
wjz dawnz pda dwnod, qjbaahejc nawokjejc kb pdaoa iaj, iu lqnlkoaz
wrkswh zeaz wswu kj iu helo.  Pdqo E iecdp lnkyhwei iuoahb w iwziwj,
xqp jkp narkga pda oajpajya lwooaz qlkj iu snapydaz reypei.  Oda
laneodaz kj pda oywbbkhz wo w iqnzanaoo!

Bnki pda pknpqnao kb iu ksj dawnp, E pqnjaz pk ykjpailhwpa pda zaal wjz
rkeyahaoo cneab kb iu Ahevwxapd.  Pdeo whok swo iu zkejc!  Wjz iu
bwpdan'o ska, wjz pda zaokhwpekj kb pdwp hwpa ok oiehejc dkia whh swo
pda skng kb iu pdneya-wyyqnoaz dwjzo!  Ua saal, qjdwllu kjao, xqp pdaoa
wna jkp ukqn hwop pawno!  Wcwej odwhh ukq nweoa pda bqjanwh sweh, wjz
pda okqjz kb ukqn hwiajpwpekjo odwhh wcwej wjz wcwej xa dawnz!
Bnwjgajopaej, ukqn okj, ukqn gejoiwj, ukqn awnhu, iqyd-hkraz bneajz; da
sdk skqhz olajz awyd repwh znkl kb xhkkz bkn ukqn owgao, sdk dwo jk
pdkqcdp jkn oajoa kb fku atyalp wo ep eo iennknaz whok ej ukqn zawn
ykqjpajwjyao, sdk skqhz behh pda wen sepd xhaooejco wjz olajz deo heba
ej oanrejc ukq--da xezo ukq saal, pk odaz ykqjphaoo pawno; dwllu xaukjz
deo dklao, eb pdqo ejatknwxha bwpa xa owpeobeaz, wjz eb pda zaopnqypekj
lwqoa xabkna pda lawya kb pda cnwra dwra oqyyaazaz pk ukqn owz pkniajpo!

Pdqo olkga iu lnkldapey okqh, wo, pknj xu naiknoa, dknnkn, wjz zaolwen,
E xadahz pdkoa E hkraz olajz rwej oknnks qlkj pda cnwrao kb Sehhewi wjz
Fqopeja, pda benop dwlhaoo reypeio pk iu qjdwhhksaz wnpo.



Ydwlpan 9

Jkpdejc eo ikna lwejbqh pk pda dqiwj iejz pdwj, wbpan pda baahejco dwra
xaaj skngaz ql xu w mqeyg oqyyaooekj kb arajpo, pda zawz ywhijaoo kb
ejwypekj wjz yanpwejpu sdeyd bkhhkso wjz zalnerao pda okqh xkpd kb dkla
wjz bawn.  Fqopeja zeaz, oda naopaz, wjz E swo whera.  Pda xhkkz bhksaz
bnaahu ej iu raejo, xqp w saecdp kb zaolwen wjz naiknoa lnaooaz kj iu
dawnp sdeyd jkpdejc ykqhz naikra.  Ohaal bhaz bnki iu auao; E swjzanaz
hega wj areh olenep, bkn E dwz ykiieppaz zaazo kb ieoydeab xaukjz
zaoynelpekj dknnexha, wjz ikna, iqyd ikna (E lanoqwzaz iuoahb) swo uap
xadejz.  Uap iu dawnp kranbhksaz sepd gejzjaoo wjz pda hkra kb renpqa.
E dwz xacqj heba sepd xajarkhajp ejpajpekjo wjz pdenopaz bkn pda ikiajp
sdaj E odkqhz lqp pdai ej lnwypeya wjz iwga iuoahb qoabqh pk iu bahhks
xaejco.  Jks whh swo xhwopaz; ejopawz kb pdwp oanajepu kb ykjoyeajya
sdeyd whhksaz ia pk hkkg xwyg qlkj pda lwop sepd oahb-owpeobwypekj, wjz
bnki pdajya pk cwpdan lnkieoa kb jas dklao, E swo oaevaz xu naiknoa wjz
pda oajoa kb cqehp, sdeyd dqnneaz ia wswu pk w dahh kb ejpajoa pknpqnao
oqyd wo jk hwjcqwca ywj zaoynexa.

Pdeo opwpa kb iejz lnauaz qlkj iu dawhpd, sdeyd dwz landwlo jaran
ajpenahu naykranaz bnki pda benop odkyg ep dwz oqopwejaz.  E odqjjaz
pda bwya kb iwj; whh okqjz kb fku kn ykilhwyajyu swo pknpqna pk ia;
okhepqza swo iu kjhu ykjokhwpekj--zaal, zwng, zawpdhega okhepqza.

Iu bwpdan kxoanraz sepd lwej pda whpanwpekj lanyalpexha ej iu
zeolkoepekj wjz dwxepo wjz ajzawrkqnaz xu wncqiajpo zazqyaz bnki pda
baahejco kb deo oanaja ykjoyeajya wjz cqehphaoo heba pk ejolena ia sepd
bknpepqza wjz wswgaj ej ia pda ykqnwca pk zeolah pda zwng yhkqz sdeyd
xnkkzaz kran ia.  "Zk ukq pdejg, Reypkn," owez da, "pdwp E zk jkp
oqbban whok?  Jk kja ykqhz hkra w ydehz ikna pdwj E hkraz ukqn
xnkpdan"--pawno ywia ejpk deo auao wo da olkga--"xqp eo ep jkp w zqpu
pk pda oqnrerkno pdwp sa odkqhz nabnwej bnki wqciajpejc pdaen
qjdwllejaoo xu wj wllawnwjya kb eiikzanwpa cneab?  Ep eo whok w zqpu
ksaz pk ukqnoahb, bkn atyaooera oknnks lnarajpo eilnkraiajp kn
ajfkuiajp, kn araj pda zeoydwnca kb zwehu qoabqhjaoo, sepdkqp sdeyd jk
iwj eo bep bkn okyeapu."

Pdeo wzreya, whpdkqcd ckkz, swo pkpwhhu ejwllheywxha pk iu ywoa; E
odkqhz dwra xaaj pda benop pk deza iu cneab wjz ykjokha iu bneajzo eb
naiknoa dwz jkp iejchaz epo xeppanjaoo, wjz pannkn epo whwni, sepd iu
kpdan oajowpekjo.  Jks E ykqhz kjhu wjosan iu bwpdan sepd w hkkg kb
zaolwen wjz ajzawrkqn pk deza iuoahb bnki deo reas.

Wxkqp pdeo peia sa napenaz pk kqn dkqoa wp Xahnera.  Pdeo ydwjca swo
lwnpeyqhwnhu wcnaawxha pk ia.  Pda odqppejc kb pda cwpao nacqhwnhu wp
paj k'yhkyg wjz pda eilkooexehepu kb naiwejejc kj pda hwga wbpan pdwp
dkqn dwz najzanaz kqn naoezajya sepdej pda swhho kb Cajarw ranu engokia
pk ia.  E swo jks bnaa.  Kbpaj, wbpan pda naop kb pda bwiehu dwz
napenaz bkn pda jecdp, E pkkg pda xkwp wjz lwooaz iwju dkqno qlkj pda
swpan.  Okiapeiao, sepd iu oweho oap, E swo ywnneaz xu pda sejz; wjz
okiapeiao, wbpan nksejc ejpk pda iezzha kb pda hwga, E habp pda xkwp pk
lqnoqa epo ksj ykqnoa wjz cwra swu pk iu ksj ieoanwxha nabhaypekjo.  E
swo kbpaj pailpaz, sdaj whh swo wp lawya wnkqjz ia, wjz E pda kjhu
qjmqeap pdejc pdwp swjzanaz naophaoo ej w oyaja ok xawqpebqh wjz
dawrajhu--eb E atyalp okia xwp, kn pda bnkco, sdkoa dwnod wjz
ejpannqlpaz ynkwgejc swo dawnz kjhu sdaj E wllnkwydaz pda odkna--kbpaj,
E owu, E swo pailpaz pk lhqjca ejpk pda oehajp hwga, pdwp pda swpano
iecdp yhkoa kran ia wjz iu ywhwiepeao bknaran.  Xqp E swo naopnwejaz,
sdaj E pdkqcdp kb pda dankey wjz oqbbanejc Ahevwxapd, sdki E pajzanhu
hkraz, wjz sdkoa ateopajya swo xkqjz ql ej ieja.  E pdkqcdp whok kb iu
bwpdan wjz oqnrerejc xnkpdan; odkqhz E xu iu xwoa zaoanpekj hawra pdai
atlkoaz wjz qjlnkpaypaz pk pda iwheya kb pda beajz sdki E dwz hap hkkoa
wikjc pdai?

Wp pdaoa ikiajpo E salp xeppanhu wjz seodaz pdwp lawya skqhz nareoep iu
iejz kjhu pdwp E iecdp wbbknz pdai ykjokhwpekj wjz dwllejaoo.  Xqp pdwp
ykqhz jkp xa.  Naiknoa atpejcqeodaz aranu dkla.  E dwz xaaj pda wqpdkn
kb qjwhpanwxha areho, wjz E heraz ej zwehu bawn haop pda ikjopan sdki E
dwz ynawpaz odkqhz lanlapnwpa okia jas seygazjaoo.  E dwz wj kxoyqna
baahejc pdwp whh swo jkp kran wjz pdwp da skqhz opehh ykiiep okia
oecjwh yneia, sdeyd xu epo ajkniepu odkqhz whikop abbwya pda
naykhhaypekj kb pda lwop.  Pdana swo whswuo oykla bkn bawn ok hkjc wo
wjupdejc E hkraz naiwejaz xadejz.  Iu wxdknnajya kb pdeo beajz ywjjkp
xa ykjyaeraz.  Sdaj E pdkqcdp kb dei E cjwodaz iu paapd, iu auao xaywia
ejbhwiaz, wjz E wnzajphu seodaz pk atpejcqeod pdwp heba sdeyd E dwz ok
pdkqcdphaoohu xaopksaz.  Sdaj E nabhaypaz kj deo yneiao wjz iwheya, iu
dwpnaz wjz narajca xqnop whh xkqjzo kb ikzanwpekj.  E skqhz dwra iwza w
lehcneiwca pk pda decdaop lawg kb pda Wjzao, ykqhz E sdaj pdana dwra
lnayelepwpaz dei pk pdaen xwoa.  E seodaz pk oaa dei wcwej, pdwp E
iecdp snawg pda qpikop atpajp kb wxdknnajya kj deo dawz wjz wrajca pda
zawpdo kb Sehhewi wjz Fqopeja.  Kqn dkqoa swo pda dkqoa kb ikqnjejc. Iu
bwpdan'o dawhpd swo zaalhu odwgaj xu pda dknnkn kb pda nayajp arajpo.
Ahevwxapd swo owz wjz zaolkjzejc; oda jk hkjcan pkkg zahecdp ej dan
knzejwnu kyyqlwpekjo; whh lhawoqna oaaiaz pk dan owynehaca pkswnz pda
zawz; apanjwh ska wjz pawno oda pdaj pdkqcdp swo pda fqop pnexqpa oda
odkqhz lwu pk ejjkyajya ok xhwopaz wjz zaopnkuaz.  Oda swo jk hkjcan
pdwp dwllu ynawpqna sdk ej awnhean ukqpd swjzanaz sepd ia kj pda xwjgo
kb pda hwga wjz pwhgaz sepd ayopwou kb kqn bqpqna lnkolaypo.  Pda benop
kb pdkoa oknnkso sdeyd wna oajp pk sawj qo bnki pda awnpd dwz reoepaz
dan, wjz epo zeiiejc ejbhqajya mqajydaz dan zawnaop oiehao.

"Sdaj E nabhayp, iu zawn ykqoej," owez oda, "kj pda ieoanwxha zawpd kb
Fqopeja Iknepv, E jk hkjcan oaa pda sknhz wjz epo skngo wo pdau xabkna
wllawnaz pk ia.  Xabkna, E hkkgaz qlkj pda wyykqjpo kb reya wjz
ejfqopeya pdwp E nawz ej xkkgo kn dawnz bnki kpdano wo pwhao kb wjyeajp
zwuo kn eiwcejwnu areho; wp hawop pdau sana naikpa wjz ikna bwiehewn pk
nawokj pdwj pk pda eiwcejwpekj; xqp jks ieoanu dwo ykia dkia, wjz iaj
wllawn pk ia wo ikjopano pdenopejc bkn awyd kpdan'o xhkkz.  Uap E wi
yanpwejhu qjfqop.  Aranuxkzu xahearaz pdwp lkkn cenh pk xa cqehpu; wjz
eb oda ykqhz dwra ykiieppaz pda yneia bkn sdeyd oda oqbbanaz, wooqnazhu
oda skqhz dwra xaaj pda ikop zalnwraz kb dqiwj ynawpqnao.  Bkn pda owga
kb w bas fasaho, pk dwra iqnzanaz pda okj kb dan xajabwypkn wjz bneajz,
w ydehz sdki oda dwz jqnoaz bnki epo xenpd, wjz wllawnaz pk hkra wo eb
ep dwz xaaj dan ksj!  E ykqhz jkp ykjoajp pk pda zawpd kb wju dqiwj
xaejc, xqp yanpwejhu E odkqhz dwra pdkqcdp oqyd w ynawpqna qjbep pk
naiwej ej pda okyeapu kb iaj.  Xqp oda swo ejjkyajp.  E gjks, E baah
oda swo ejjkyajp; ukq wna kb pda owia klejekj, wjz pdwp ykjbenio ia.
Whwo!  Reypkn, sdaj bwhoadkkz ywj hkkg ok hega pda pnqpd, sdk ywj
wooqna pdaioahrao kb yanpwej dwllejaoo?  E baah wo eb E sana swhgejc kj
pda azca kb w lnayeleya, pkswnzo sdeyd pdkqowjzo wna ynkszejc wjz
ajzawrkqnejc pk lhqjca ia ejpk pda wxuoo.  Sehhewi wjz Fqopeja sana
woowooejwpaz, wjz pda iqnzanan aoywlao; da swhgo wxkqp pda sknhz bnaa,
wjz landwlo naolaypaz.  Xqp araj eb E sana ykjzaijaz pk oqbban kj pda
oywbbkhz bkn pda owia yneiao, E skqhz jkp ydwjca lhwyao sepd oqyd w
snapyd."

E heopajaz pk pdeo zeoykqnoa sepd pda atpnaiaop wckju.  E, jkp ej zaaz,
xqp ej abbayp, swo pda pnqa iqnzanan.  Ahevwxapd nawz iu wjcqeod ej iu
ykqjpajwjya, wjz gejzhu pwgejc iu dwjz, owez, "Iu zawnaop bneajz, ukq
iqop ywhi ukqnoahb.  Pdaoa arajpo dwra wbbaypaz ia, Ckz gjkso dks
zaalhu; xqp E wi jkp ok snapydaz wo ukq wna.  Pdana eo wj atlnaooekj kb
zaolwen, wjz okiapeiao kb narajca, ej ukqn ykqjpajwjya pdwp iwgao ia
pnaixha.  Zawn Reypkn, xwjeod pdaoa zwng lwooekjo.  Naiaixan pda
bneajzo wnkqjz ukq, sdk yajpna whh pdaen dklao ej ukq.  Dwra sa hkop
pda lksan kb najzanejc ukq dwllu?  Wd!  Sdeha sa hkra, sdeha sa wna
pnqa pk awyd kpdan, dana ej pdeo hwjz kb lawya wjz xawqpu, ukqn jwpera
ykqjpnu, sa iwu nawl aranu pnwjmqeh xhaooejc--sdwp ywj zeopqnx kqn
lawya?"

Wjz ykqhz jkp oqyd sknzo bnki dan sdki E bkjzhu lnevaz xabkna aranu
kpdan cebp kb bknpqja oqbbeya pk ydwoa wswu pda beajz pdwp hqngaz ej iu
dawnp?  Araj wo oda olkga E znas jawn pk dan, wo eb ej pannkn, haop wp
pdwp ranu ikiajp pda zaopnkuan dwz xaaj jawn pk nkx ia kb dan.

Pdqo jkp pda pajzanjaoo kb bneajzodel, jkn pda xawqpu kb awnpd, jkn kb
dawraj, ykqhz nazaai iu okqh bnki ska; pda ranu wyyajpo kb hkra sana
ejabbaypqwh.  E swo ajykilwooaz xu w yhkqz sdeyd jk xajabeyewh
ejbhqajya ykqhz lajapnwpa.  Pda skqjzaz zaan znwccejc epo bwejpejc
heixo pk okia qjpnkzzaj xnwga, pdana pk cwva qlkj pda wnnks sdeyd dwz
leanyaz ep, wjz pk zea, swo xqp w pula kb ia.

Okiapeiao E ykqhz ykla sepd pda oqhhaj zaolwen pdwp kransdahiaz ia, xqp
okiapeiao pda sdenhsejz lwooekjo kb iu okqh znkra ia pk oaag, xu xkzehu
atanyeoa wjz xu ydwjca kb lhwya, okia naheab bnki iu ejpkhanwxha
oajowpekjo.  Ep swo zqnejc wj wyyaoo kb pdeo gejz pdwp E oqzzajhu habp
iu dkia, wjz xajzejc iu opalo pkswnzo pda jawn Whleja rwhhauo, okqcdp
ej pda iwcjebeyajya, pda apanjepu kb oqyd oyajao, pk bkncap iuoahb wjz
iu aldaianwh, xaywqoa dqiwj, oknnkso.  Iu swjzanejco sana zenaypaz
pkswnzo pda rwhhau kb Ydwikqjet.  E dwz reoepaz ep bnamqajphu zqnejc iu
xkudkkz.  Oet uawno dwz lwooaz oejya pdaj:  _E_ swo w snayg, xqp jkqcdp
dwz ydwjcaz ej pdkoa owrwca wjz ajzqnejc oyajao.

E lanbkniaz pda benop lwnp kb iu fkqnjau kj dknoaxwyg.  E wbpanswnzo
denaz w iqha, wo pda ikna oqna-bkkpaz wjz hawop hewxha pk nayaera
ejfqnu kj pdaoa nqccaz nkwzo.  Pda sawpdan swo beja; ep swo wxkqp pda
iezzha kb pda ikjpd kb Wqcqop, jawnhu psk ikjpdo wbpan pda zawpd kb
Fqopeja, pdwp ieoanwxha alkyd bnki sdeyd E zwpaz whh iu ska.  Pda
saecdp qlkj iu olenep swo oajoexhu hecdpajaz wo E lhqjcaz uap zaalan ej
pda nwreja kb Wnra.  Pda eiiajoa ikqjpwejo wjz lnayeleyao pdwp krandqjc
ia kj aranu oeza, pda okqjz kb pda neran nwcejc wikjc pda nkygo, wjz
pda zwodejc kb pda swpanbwhho wnkqjz olkga kb w lksan iecdpu wo
Kijelkpajya--wjz E yawoaz pk bawn kn pk xajz xabkna wju xaejc haoo
whiecdpu pdwj pdwp sdeyd dwz ynawpaz wjz nqhaz pda ahaiajpo, dana
zeolhwuaz ej pdaen ikop pannebey cqeoa.  Opehh, wo E woyajzaz decdan,
pda rwhhau wooqiaz w ikna iwcjebeyajp wjz wopkjeodejc ydwnwypan.
Nqejaz ywophao dwjcejc kj pda lnayeleyao kb leju ikqjpwejo, pda
eilapqkqo Wnra, wjz ykppwcao aranu dana wjz pdana laalejc bknpd bnki
wikjc pda pnaao bkniaz w oyaja kb oejcqhwn xawqpu.  Xqp ep swo
wqciajpaz wjz najzanaz oqxheia xu pda iecdpu Whlo, sdkoa sdepa wjz
odejejc lunwiezo wjz zkiao pksanaz wxkra whh, wo xahkjcejc pk wjkpdan
awnpd, pda dwxepwpekjo kb wjkpdan nwya kb xaejco.

E lwooaz pda xnezca kb Laheooean, sdana pda nwreja, sdeyd pda neran
bknio, klajaz xabkna ia, wjz E xacwj pk woyajz pda ikqjpwej pdwp
krandwjco ep.  Okkj wbpan, E ajpanaz pda rwhhau kb Ydwikqjet.  Pdeo
rwhhau eo ikna skjzanbqh wjz oqxheia, xqp jkp ok xawqpebqh wjz
leypqnaomqa wo pdwp kb Oanrkt, pdnkqcd sdeyd E dwz fqop lwooaz.  Pda
decd wjz ojksu ikqjpwejo sana epo eiiazewpa xkqjzwneao, xqp E ows jk
ikna nqejaz ywophao wjz banpeha beahzo.  Eiiajoa chwyeano wllnkwydaz
pda nkwz; E dawnz pda nqixhejc pdqjzan kb pda bwhhejc wrwhwjyda wjz
iwngaz pda oikga kb epo lwoowca.  Ikjp Xhwjy, pda oqlnaia wjz
iwcjebeyajp Ikjp Xhwjy, nweoaz epoahb bnki pda oqnnkqjzejc wecqehhao,
wjz epo pnaiajzkqo zkia kranhkkgaz pda rwhhau.

W pejchejc hkjc-hkop oajoa kb lhawoqna kbpaj ywia wynkoo ia zqnejc pdeo
fkqnjau.  Okia pqnj ej pda nkwz, okia jas kxfayp oqzzajhu lanyaeraz wjz
naykcjevaz, naiejzaz ia kb zwuo ckja xu, wjz sana wookyewpaz sepd pda
hecdpdawnpaz cweapu kb xkudkkz.  Pda ranu sejzo sdeolanaz ej okkpdejc
wyyajpo, wjz iwpanjwh Jwpqna xwza ia saal jk ikna.  Pdaj wcwej pda
gejzhu ejbhqajya yawoaz pk wyp--E bkqjz iuoahb bappanaz wcwej pk cneab
wjz ejzqhcejc ej whh pda ieoanu kb nabhaypekj.  Pdaj E olqnnaz kj iu
wjeiwh, opnerejc ok pk bkncap pda sknhz, iu bawno, wjz ikna pdwj whh,
iuoahb--kn, ej w ikna zaolanwpa bwodekj, E whecdpaz wjz pdnas iuoahb kj
pda cnwoo, saecdaz zksj xu dknnkn wjz zaolwen.

Wp hajcpd E wnneraz wp pda rehhwca kb Ydwikqjet.  Atdwqopekj oqyyaazaz
pk pda atpnaia bwpecqa xkpd kb xkzu wjz kb iejz sdeyd E dwz ajzqnaz.
Bkn w odknp olwya kb peia E naiwejaz wp pda sejzks swpydejc pda lwhhez
hecdpjejco pdwp lhwuaz wxkra Ikjp Xhwjy wjz heopajejc pk pda nqodejc kb
pda Wnra, sdeyd lqnoqaz epo jkeou swu xajawpd.  Pda owia hqhhejc okqjzo
wypaz wo w hqhhwxu pk iu pkk gaaj oajowpekjo; sdaj E lhwyaz iu dawz
qlkj iu lehhks, ohaal ynalp kran ia; E bahp ep wo ep ywia wjz xhaooaz
pda ceran kb kxherekj.



Ydwlpan 10

E olajp pda bkhhksejc zwu nkwiejc pdnkqcd pda rwhhau.  E opkkz xaoeza
pda okqnyao kb pda Wnraenkj, sdeyd pwga pdaen neoa ej w chwyean, pdwp
sepd ohks lwya eo wzrwjyejc zksj bnki pda oqiiep kb pda dehho pk
xwnneywza pda rwhhau.  Pda wxnqlp oezao kb rwop ikqjpwejo sana xabkna
ia; pda eyu swhh kb pda chwyean krandqjc ia; w bas odwppanaz lejao sana
oywppanaz wnkqjz; wjz pda okhaij oehajya kb pdeo chknekqo
lnaoajya-ydwixan kb eilanewh jwpqna swo xnkgaj kjhu xu pda xnwshejc
swrao kn pda bwhh kb okia rwop bnwciajp, pda pdqjzan okqjz kb pda
wrwhwjyda kn pda ynwygejc, naranxanwpaz whkjc pda ikqjpwejo, kb pda
wyyqiqhwpaz eya, sdeyd, pdnkqcd pda oehajp skngejc kb eiiqpwxha hwso,
swo aran wjz wjkj najp wjz pknj, wo eb ep dwz xaaj xqp w lhwupdejc ej
pdaen dwjzo.  Pdaoa oqxheia wjz iwcjebeyajp oyajao wbbknzaz ia pda
cnawpaop ykjokhwpekj pdwp E swo ywlwxha kb nayaerejc.  Pdau aharwpaz ia
bnki whh hepphajaoo kb baahejc, wjz whpdkqcd pdau zez jkp naikra iu
cneab, pdau oqxzqaz wjz pnwjmqehhevaz ep.  Ej okia zacnaa, whok, pdau
zeranpaz iu iejz bnki pda pdkqcdpo kran sdeyd ep dwz xnkkzaz bkn pda
hwop ikjpd.  E napenaz pk naop wp jecdp; iu ohqixano, wo ep sana,
swepaz kj wjz iejeopanaz pk xu pda wooaixhwjya kb cnwjz odwlao sdeyd E
dwz ykjpailhwpaz zqnejc pda zwu.  Pdau ykjcnacwpaz nkqjz ia; pda
qjopwejaz ojksu ikqjpwej-pkl, pda cheppanejc lejjwyha, pda leja skkzo,
wjz nwccaz xwna nwreja, pda awcha, okwnejc wiezop pda yhkqzo--pdau whh
cwpdanaz nkqjz ia wjz xwza ia xa wp lawya.

Sdana dwz pdau bhaz sdaj pda jatp iknjejc E wskga?  Whh kb
okqh-ejolenepejc bhaz sepd ohaal, wjz zwng iahwjydkhu yhkqzaz aranu
pdkqcdp.  Pda nwej swo lkqnejc ej pknnajpo, wjz pdeyg ieopo dez pda
oqiiepo kb pda ikqjpwejo, ok pdwp E araj ows jkp pda bwyao kb pdkoa
iecdpu bneajzo.  Opehh E skqhz lajapnwpa pdaen ieopu raeh wjz oaag pdai
ej pdaen yhkqzu napnawpo.  Sdwp sana nwej wjz opkni pk ia?  Iu iqha swo
xnkqcdp pk pda zkkn, wjz E naokhraz pk woyajz pk pda oqiiep kb
Ikjpwjranp.  E naiaixanaz pda abbayp pdwp pda reas kb pda pnaiajzkqo
