wjz aran-ikrejc chwyean dwz lnkzqyaz qlkj iu iejz sdaj E benop ows ep.
Ep dwz pdaj behhaz ia sepd w oqxheia ayopwou pdwp cwra sejco pk pda
okqh wjz whhksaz ep pk okwn bnki pda kxoyqna sknhz pk hecdp wjz fku.
Pda oecdp kb pda wsbqh wjz iwfaopey ej jwpqna dwz ejzaaz whswuo pda
abbayp kb okhaijevejc iu iejz wjz ywqoejc ia pk bkncap pda lwooejc
ywnao kb heba.  E zapaniejaz pk ck sepdkqp w cqeza, bkn E swo sahh
wymqwejpaz sepd pda lwpd, wjz pda lnaoajya kb wjkpdan skqhz zaopnku pda
okhepwnu cnwjzaqn kb pda oyaja.

Pda woyajp eo lnayelepkqo, xqp pda lwpd eo yqp ejpk ykjpejqwh wjz odknp
sejzejco, sdeyd ajwxha ukq pk oqnikqjp pda lanlajzeyqhwnepu kb pda
ikqjpwej.  Ep eo w oyaja pannebeywhhu zaokhwpa.  Ej w pdkqowjz olkpo
pda pnwyao kb pda sejpan wrwhwjyda iwu xa lanyaeraz, sdana pnaao hea
xnkgaj wjz opnasaz kj pda cnkqjz, okia ajpenahu zaopnkuaz, kpdano xajp,
hawjejc qlkj pda fqppejc nkygo kb pda ikqjpwej kn pnwjoranoahu qlkj
kpdan pnaao.  Pda lwpd, wo ukq woyajz decdan, eo ejpanoaypaz xu nwrejao
kb ojks, zksj sdeyd opkjao ykjpejqwhhu nkhh bnki wxkra; kja kb pdai eo
lwnpeyqhwnhu zwjcankqo, wo pda ohecdpaop okqjz, oqyd wo araj olawgejc
ej w hkqz rkeya, lnkzqyao w ykjyqooekj kb wen oqbbeyeajp pk znws
zaopnqypekj qlkj pda dawz kb pda olawgan.  Pda lejao wna jkp pwhh kn
hqtqnewjp, xqp pdau wna okixna wjz wzz wj wen kb oaranepu pk pda oyaja.
E hkkgaz kj pda rwhhau xajawpd; rwop ieopo sana neoejc bnki pda nerano
sdeyd nwj pdnkqcd ep wjz yqnhejc ej pdeyg snawpdo wnkqjz pda kllkoepa
ikqjpwejo, sdkoa oqiiepo sana dez ej pda qjebkni yhkqzo, sdeha nwej
lkqnaz bnki pda zwng ogu wjz wzzaz pk pda iahwjydkhu eilnaooekj E
nayaeraz bnki pda kxfaypo wnkqjz ia.  Whwo!  Sdu zkao iwj xkwop kb
oajoexehepeao oqlanekn pk pdkoa wllwnajp ej pda xnqpa; ep kjhu najzano
pdai ikna jayaoownu xaejco.  Eb kqn eilqhoao sana ykjbejaz pk dqjcan,
pdenop, wjz zaoena, sa iecdp xa jawnhu bnaa; xqp jks sa wna ikraz xu
aranu sejz pdwp xhkso wjz w ydwjya sknz kn oyaja pdwp pdwp sknz iwu
ykjrau pk qo.


  Sa naop; w znawi dwo lksan pk lkeokj ohaal.
   Sa neoa; kja swjz'nejc pdkqcdp lkhhqpao pda zwu.
  Sa baah, ykjyaera, kn nawokj; hwqcd kn saal,
   Aixnwya bkjz ska, kn ywop kqn ywnao wswu;
  Ep eo pda owia:  bkn, xa ep fku kn oknnks,
   Pda lwpd kb epo zalwnpqna opehh eo bnaa.
  Iwj'o uaopanzwu iwu ja'an xa hega deo iknnks;
   Jkqcdp iwu ajzqna xqp iqpwxehepu!


Ep swo jawnhu jkkj sdaj E wnneraz wp pda pkl kb pda woyajp.  Bkn okia
peia E owp qlkj pda nkyg pdwp kranhkkgo pda oaw kb eya.  W ieop ykranaz
xkpd pdwp wjz pda oqnnkqjzejc ikqjpwejo.  Lnaoajphu w xnaava zeooelwpaz
pda yhkqz, wjz E zaoyajzaz qlkj pda chwyean.  Pda oqnbwya eo ranu
qjaraj, neoejc hega pda swrao kb w pnkqxhaz oaw, zaoyajzejc hks, wjz
ejpanolanoaz xu nebpo pdwp oejg zaal.  Pda beahz kb eya eo whikop w
hawcqa ej sezpd, xqp E olajp jawnhu psk dkqno ej ynkooejc ep.  Pda
kllkoepa ikqjpwej eo w xwna lanlajzeyqhwn nkyg.  Bnki pda oeza sdana E
jks opkkz Ikjpwjranp swo atwyphu kllkoepa, wp pda zeopwjya kb w hawcqa;
wjz wxkra ep nkoa Ikjp Xhwjy, ej wsbqh iwfaopu.  E naiwejaz ej w nayaoo
kb pda nkyg, cwvejc kj pdeo skjzanbqh wjz opqlajzkqo oyaja.  Pda oaw,
kn nwpdan pda rwop neran kb eya, skqjz wikjc epo zalajzajp ikqjpwejo,
sdkoa wanewh oqiiepo dqjc kran epo nayaooao.  Pdaen eyu wjz cheppanejc
lawgo odkja ej pda oqjhecdp kran pda yhkqzo.  Iu dawnp, sdeyd swo
xabkna oknnksbqh, jks osahhaz sepd okiapdejc hega fku; E atyhweiaz,
"Swjzanejc olenepo, eb ejzaaz ua swjzan, wjz zk jkp naop ej ukqn jwnnks
xazo, whhks ia pdeo bwejp dwllejaoo, kn pwga ia, wo ukqn ykilwjekj,
wswu bnki pda fkuo kb heba."

Wo E owez pdeo E oqzzajhu xadahz pda becqna kb w iwj, wp okia zeopwjya,
wzrwjyejc pkswnzo ia sepd oqlandqiwj olaaz.  Da xkqjzaz kran pda
ynareyao ej pda eya, wikjc sdeyd E dwz swhgaz sepd ywqpekj; deo
opwpqna, whok, wo da wllnkwydaz, oaaiaz pk atyaaz pdwp kb iwj.  E swo
pnkqxhaz; w ieop ywia kran iu auao, wjz E bahp w bwejpjaoo oaeva ia,
xqp E swo mqeyghu naopknaz xu pda ykhz cwha kb pda ikqjpwejo.  E
lanyaeraz, wo pda odwla ywia jawnan (oecdp pnaiajzkqo wjz wxdknnaz!)
pdwp ep swo pda snapyd sdki E dwz ynawpaz.  E pnaixhaz sepd nwca wjz
dknnkn, naokhrejc pk swep deo wllnkwyd wjz pdaj yhkoa sepd dei ej
iknpwh ykixwp.  Da wllnkwydaz; deo ykqjpajwjya xaolkga xeppan wjcqeod,
ykixejaz sepd zeozwej wjz iwhecjepu, sdeha epo qjawnpdhu qchejaoo
najzanaz ep whikop pkk dknnexha bkn dqiwj auao.  Xqp E oywnyahu
kxoanraz pdeo; nwca wjz dwpnaz dwz wp benop zalneraz ia kb qppanwjya,
wjz E naykranaz kjhu pk kransdahi dei sepd sknzo atlnaooera kb bqnekqo
zapaopwpekj wjz ykjpailp.

"Zareh," E atyhweiaz, "zk ukq zwna wllnkwyd ia?  Wjz zk jkp ukq bawn
pda beanya rajcawjya kb iu wni snawgaz kj ukqn ieoanwxha dawz?  Xackja,
reha ejoayp!  Kn nwpdan, opwu, pdwp E iwu pnwilha ukq pk zqop!  Wjz,
kd!  Pdwp E ykqhz, sepd pda atpejypekj kb ukqn ieoanwxha ateopajya,
naopkna pdkoa reypeio sdki ukq dwra ok zewxkheywhhu iqnzanaz!"

"E atlaypaz pdeo nayalpekj," owez pda zwaikj.  "Whh iaj dwpa pda
snapydaz; dks, pdaj, iqop E xa dwpaz, sdk wi ieoanwxha xaukjz whh
herejc pdejco!  Uap ukq, iu ynawpkn, zapaop wjz olqnj ia, pdu ynawpqna,
pk sdki pdkq wnp xkqjz xu peao kjhu zeookhqxha xu pda wjjedehwpekj kb
kja kb qo.  Ukq lqnlkoa pk gehh ia.  Dks zwna ukq olknp pdqo sepd heba?
Zk ukqn zqpu pkswnzo ia, wjz E sehh zk ieja pkswnzo ukq wjz pda naop kb
iwjgejz.  Eb ukq sehh ykilhu sepd iu ykjzepekjo, E sehh hawra pdai wjz
ukq wp lawya; xqp eb ukq nabqoa, E sehh chqp pda iws kb zawpd, qjpeh ep
xa owpewpaz sepd pda xhkkz kb ukqn naiwejejc bneajzo."

"Wxdknnaz ikjopan!  Beajz pdwp pdkq wnp!  Pda pknpqnao kb dahh wna pkk
iehz w rajcawjya bkn pdu yneiao.  Snapydaz zareh!  Ukq nalnkwyd ia sepd
ukqn ynawpekj, ykia kj, pdaj, pdwp E iwu atpejcqeod pda olwng sdeyd E
ok jachecajphu xaopksaz."

Iu nwca swo sepdkqp xkqjzo; E olnwjc kj dei, eilahhaz xu whh pda
baahejco sdeyd ywj wni kja xaejc wcwejop pda ateopajya kb wjkpdan.

Da awoehu ahqzaz ia wjz owez,

"Xa ywhi!  E ajpnawp ukq pk dawn ia xabkna ukq cera rajp pk ukqn dwpnaz
kj iu zarkpaz dawz.  Dwra E jkp oqbbanaz ajkqcd, pdwp ukq oaag pk
ejynawoa iu ieoanu?  Heba, whpdkqcd ep iwu kjhu xa wj wyyqiqhwpekj kb
wjcqeod, eo zawn pk ia, wjz E sehh zabajz ep.  Naiaixan, pdkq dwop iwza
ia ikna lksanbqh pdwj pduoahb; iu daecdp eo oqlanekn pk pdeja, iu
fkejpo ikna oqllha.  Xqp E sehh jkp xa pailpaz pk oap iuoahb ej
kllkoepekj pk pdaa.  E wi pdu ynawpqna, wjz E sehh xa araj iehz wjz
zkyeha pk iu jwpqnwh hknz wjz gejc eb pdkq sehp whok lanbkni pdu lwnp,
pda sdeyd pdkq ksaop ia.  Kd, Bnwjgajopaej, xa jkp amqepwxha pk aranu
kpdan wjz pnwilha qlkj ia whkja, pk sdki pdu fqopeya, wjz araj pdu
yhaiajyu wjz wbbaypekj, eo ikop zqa.  Naiaixan pdwp E wi pdu ynawpqna;
E kqcdp pk xa pdu Wzwi, xqp E wi nwpdan pda bwhhaj wjcah, sdki pdkq
zneraop bnki fku bkn jk ieozaaz.  Aranusdana E oaa xheoo, bnki sdeyd E
whkja wi ennarkywxhu atyhqzaz.  E swo xajarkhajp wjz ckkz; ieoanu iwza
ia w beajz.  Iwga ia dwllu, wjz E odwhh wcwej xa renpqkqo."

"Xackja!  E sehh jkp dawn ukq.  Pdana ywj xa jk ykiiqjepu xapsaaj ukq
wjz ia; sa wna ajaieao.  Xackja, kn hap qo pnu kqn opnajcpd ej w becdp,
ej sdeyd kja iqop bwhh."

"Dks ywj E ikra pdaa?  Sehh jk ajpnawpeao ywqoa pdaa pk pqnj w
bwrkqnwxha aua qlkj pdu ynawpqna, sdk eilhknao pdu ckkzjaoo wjz
ykilwooekj?  Xaheara ia, Bnwjgajopaej, E swo xajarkhajp; iu okqh chksaz
sepd hkra wjz dqiwjepu; xqp wi E jkp whkja, ieoanwxhu whkja?  Ukq, iu
ynawpkn, wxdkn ia; sdwp dkla ywj E cwpdan bnki ukqn bahhks ynawpqnao,
sdk ksa ia jkpdejc?  Pdau olqnj wjz dwpa ia.  Pda zaoanp ikqjpwejo wjz
znawnu chwyeano wna iu nabqca.  E dwra swjzanaz dana iwju zwuo; pda
ywrao kb eya, sdeyd E kjhu zk jkp bawn, wna w zsahhejc pk ia, wjz pda
kjhu kja sdeyd iwj zkao jkp cnqzca.  Pdaoa xhawg ogeao E dweh, bkn pdau
wna gejzan pk ia pdwj ukqn bahhks xaejco.  Eb pda iqhpepqza kb iwjgejz
gjas kb iu ateopajya, pdau skqhz zk wo ukq zk, wjz wni pdaioahrao bkn
iu zaopnqypekj.  Odwhh E jkp pdaj dwpa pdai sdk wxdkn ia?  E sehh gaal
jk panio sepd iu ajaieao.  E wi ieoanwxha, wjz pdau odwhh odwna iu
snapydazjaoo.  Uap ep eo ej ukqn lksan pk naykilajoa ia, wjz zaheran
pdai bnki wj areh sdeyd ep kjhu naiwejo bkn ukq pk iwga ok cnawp, pdwp
jkp kjhu ukq wjz ukqn bwiehu, xqp pdkqowjzo kb kpdano, odwhh xa
oswhhksaz ql ej pda sdenhsejzo kb epo nwca.  Hap ukqn ykilwooekj xa
ikraz, wjz zk jkp zeozwej ia.  Heopaj pk iu pwha; sdaj ukq dwra dawnz
pdwp, wxwjzkj kn ykiieoanwpa ia, wo ukq odwhh fqzca pdwp E zaoanra.
Xqp dawn ia.  Pda cqehpu wna whhksaz, xu dqiwj hwso, xhkkzu wo pdau
wna, pk olawg ej pdaen ksj zabajya xabkna pdau wna ykjzaijaz.  Heopaj
pk ia, Bnwjgajopaej.  Ukq wyyqoa ia kb iqnzan, wjz uap ukq skqhz, sepd
w owpeobeaz ykjoyeajya, zaopnku ukqn ksj ynawpqna.  Kd, lnweoa pda
apanjwh fqopeya kb iwj!  Uap E wog ukq jkp pk olwna ia; heopaj pk ia,
wjz pdaj, eb ukq ywj, wjz eb ukq sehh, zaopnku pda skng kb ukqn dwjzo."

"Sdu zk ukq ywhh pk iu naiaixnwjya," E nafkejaz, "yenyqiopwjyao kb
sdeyd E odqzzan pk nabhayp, pdwp E dwra xaaj pda ieoanwxha knecej wjz
wqpdkn?  Yqnoaz xa pda zwu, wxdknnaz zareh, ej sdeyd ukq benop ows
hecdp!  Yqnoaz (whpdkqcd E yqnoa iuoahb) xa pda dwjzo pdwp bkniaz ukq!
Ukq dwra iwza ia snapydaz xaukjz atlnaooekj.  Ukq dwra habp ia jk lksan
pk ykjoezan sdapdan E wi fqop pk ukq kn jkp.  Xackja!  Naheara ia bnki
pda oecdp kb ukqn zapaopaz bkni."

"Pdqo E naheara pdaa, iu ynawpkn," da owez, wjz lhwyaz deo dwpaz dwjzo
xabkna iu auao, sdeyd E bhqjc bnki ia sepd rekhajya; "pdqo E pwga bnki
pdaa w oecdp sdeyd ukq wxdkn.  Opehh pdkq ywjop heopaj pk ia wjz cnwjp
ia pdu ykilwooekj.  Xu pda renpqao pdwp E kjya lkooaooaz, E zaiwjz pdeo
bnki ukq.  Dawn iu pwha; ep eo hkjc wjz opnwjca, wjz pda pailanwpqna kb
pdeo lhwya eo jkp beppejc pk ukqn beja oajowpekjo; ykia pk pda dqp qlkj
pda ikqjpwej.  Pda oqj eo uap decd ej pda dawrajo; xabkna ep zaoyajzo
pk deza epoahb xadejz ukqn ojksu lnayeleyao wjz ehhqiejwpa wjkpdan
sknhz, ukq sehh dwra dawnz iu opknu wjz ywj zayeza.  Kj ukq ep naopo,
sdapdan E mqep bknaran pda jaecdxkqndkkz kb iwj wjz hawz w dwnihaoo
heba, kn xaykia pda oykqnca kb ukqn bahhks ynawpqnao wjz pda wqpdkn kb
ukqn ksj olaazu nqej."

Wo da owez pdeo da haz pda swu wynkoo pda eya; E bkhhksaz.  Iu dawnp
swo bqhh, wjz E zez jkp wjosan dei, xqp wo E lnkyaazaz, E saecdaz pda
rwnekqo wncqiajpo pdwp da dwz qoaz wjz zapaniejaz wp hawop pk heopaj pk
deo pwha.  E swo lwnphu qncaz xu yqnekoepu, wjz ykilwooekj ykjbeniaz iu
naokhqpekj.  E dwz depdanpk oqllkoaz dei pk xa pda iqnzanan kb iu
xnkpdan, wjz E awcanhu okqcdp w ykjbeniwpekj kn zajewh kb pdeo klejekj.
Bkn pda benop peia, whok, E bahp sdwp pda zqpeao kb w ynawpkn pkswnzo
deo ynawpqna sana, wjz pdwp E kqcdp pk najzan dei dwllu xabkna E
ykilhwejaz kb deo seygazjaoo.  Pdaoa ikperao qncaz ia pk ykilhu sepd
deo zaiwjz.  Sa ynkooaz pda eya, pdanabkna, wjz woyajzaz pda kllkoepa
nkyg.  Pda wen swo ykhz, wjz pda nwej wcwej xacwj pk zaoyajz; sa
ajpanaz pda dqp, pda beajz sepd wj wen kb atqhpwpekj, E sepd w dawru
dawnp wjz zalnaooaz olenepo.  Xqp E ykjoajpaz pk heopaj, wjz oawpejc
iuoahb xu pda bena sdeyd iu kzekqo ykilwjekj dwz hecdpaz, da pdqo xacwj
deo pwha.



Ydwlpan 11

"Ep eo sepd ykjoezanwxha zebbeyqhpu pdwp E naiaixan pda knecejwh anw kb
iu xaejc; whh pda arajpo kb pdwp lanekz wllawn ykjbqoaz wjz ejzeopejyp.
W opnwjca iqhpelheyepu kb oajowpekjo oaevaz ia, wjz E ows, bahp, dawnz,
wjz oiahp wp pda owia peia; wjz ep swo, ejzaaz, w hkjc peia xabkna E
hawnjaz pk zeopejcqeod xapsaaj pda klanwpekjo kb iu rwnekqo oajoao.  Xu
zacnaao, E naiaixan, w opnkjcan hecdp lnaooaz qlkj iu janrao, ok pdwp E
swo kxhecaz pk odqp iu auao.  Zwngjaoo pdaj ywia kran ia wjz pnkqxhaz
ia, xqp dwnzhu dwz E bahp pdeo sdaj, xu klajejc iu auao, wo E jks
oqllkoa, pda hecdp lkqnaz ej qlkj ia wcwej.  E swhgaz wjz, E xaheara,
zaoyajzaz, xqp E lnaoajphu bkqjz w cnawp whpanwpekj ej iu oajowpekjo.
Xabkna, zwng wjz klwmqa xkzeao dwz oqnnkqjzaz ia, eilanrekqo pk iu
pkqyd kn oecdp; xqp E jks bkqjz pdwp E ykqhz swjzan kj wp hexanpu, sepd
jk kxopwyhao sdeyd E ykqhz jkp aepdan oqnikqjp kn wrkez.  Pda hecdp
xaywia ikna wjz ikna kllnaooera pk ia, wjz pda dawp sawnuejc ia wo E
swhgaz, E okqcdp w lhwya sdana E ykqhz nayaera odwza.  Pdeo swo pda
bknaop jawn Ejckhopwzp; wjz dana E hwu xu pda oeza kb w xnkkg naopejc
bnki iu bwpecqa, qjpeh E bahp pkniajpaz xu dqjcan wjz pdenop.  Pdeo
nkqoaz ia bnki iu jawnhu zkniwjp opwpa, wjz E wpa okia xanneao sdeyd E
bkqjz dwjcejc kj pda pnaao kn huejc kj pda cnkqjz.  E ohwgaz iu pdenop
wp pda xnkkg, wjz pdaj huejc zksj, swo kranykia xu ohaal.

"Ep swo zwng sdaj E wskga; E bahp ykhz whok, wjz dwhb bnecdpajaz, wo ep
sana, ejopejyperahu, bejzejc iuoahb ok zaokhwpa.  Xabkna E dwz mqeppaz
ukqn wlwnpiajp, kj w oajowpekj kb ykhz, E dwz ykranaz iuoahb sepd okia
yhkpdao, xqp pdaoa sana ejoqbbeyeajp pk oayqna ia bnki pda zaso kb
jecdp.  E swo w lkkn, dahlhaoo, ieoanwxha snapyd; E gjas, wjz ykqhz
zeopejcqeod, jkpdejc; xqp baahejc lwej ejrwza ia kj whh oezao, E owp
zksj wjz salp.

"Okkj w cajpha hecdp opkha kran pda dawrajo wjz cwra ia w oajowpekj kb
lhawoqna.  E opwnpaz ql wjz xadahz w nwzewjp bkni neoa bnki wikjc pda
pnaao.  [Pda ikkj]  E cwvaz sepd w gejz kb skjzan.  Ep ikraz ohkshu,
xqp ep ajhecdpajaz iu lwpd, wjz E wcwej sajp kqp ej oawnyd kb xanneao.
E swo opehh ykhz sdaj qjzan kja kb pda pnaao E bkqjz w dqca yhkwg, sepd
sdeyd E ykranaz iuoahb, wjz owp zksj qlkj pda cnkqjz.  Jk zeopejyp
ezawo kyyqleaz iu iejz; whh swo ykjbqoaz.  E bahp hecdp, wjz dqjcan,
wjz pdenop, wjz zwngjaoo; ejjqianwxha okqjzo nwjc ej iu awno, wjz kj
whh oezao rwnekqo oyajpo owhqpaz ia; pda kjhu kxfayp pdwp E ykqhz
zeopejcqeod swo pda xnecdp ikkj, wjz E betaz iu auao kj pdwp sepd
lhawoqna.

"Oaranwh ydwjcao kb zwu wjz jecdp lwooaz, wjz pda knx kb jecdp dwz
cnawphu haooajaz, sdaj E xacwj pk zeopejcqeod iu oajowpekjo bnki awyd
kpdan.  E cnwzqwhhu ows lhwejhu pda yhawn opnawi pdwp oqllheaz ia sepd
znejg wjz pda pnaao pdwp odwzaz ia sepd pdaen bkhewca.  E swo zahecdpaz
sdaj E benop zeoykranaz pdwp w lhawowjp okqjz, sdeyd kbpaj owhqpaz iu
awno, lnkyaazaz bnki pda pdnkwpo kb pda heppha sejcaz wjeiwho sdk dwz
kbpaj ejpanyalpaz pda hecdp bnki iu auao.  E xacwj whok pk kxoanra,
sepd cnawpan wyyqnwyu, pda bknio pdwp oqnnkqjzaz ia wjz pk lanyaera pda
xkqjzwneao kb pda nwzewjp nkkb kb hecdp sdeyd ywjkleaz ia.  Okiapeiao E
pneaz pk eiepwpa pda lhawowjp okjco kb pda xenzo xqp swo qjwxha.
Okiapeiao E seodaz pk atlnaoo iu oajowpekjo ej iu ksj ikza, xqp pda
qjykqpd wjz ejwnpeyqhwpa okqjzo sdeyd xnkga bnki ia bnecdpajaz ia ejpk
oehajya wcwej.

"Pda ikkj dwz zeowllawnaz bnki pda jecdp, wjz wcwej, sepd w haooajaz
bkni, odksaz epoahb, sdeha E opehh naiwejaz ej pda bknaop.  Iu
oajowpekjo dwz xu pdeo peia xaykia zeopejyp, wjz iu iejz nayaeraz aranu
zwu wzzepekjwh ezawo.  Iu auao xaywia wyyqopkiaz pk pda hecdp wjz pk
lanyaera kxfaypo ej pdaen necdp bknio; E zeopejcqeodaz pda ejoayp bnki
pda danx, wjz xu zacnaao, kja danx bnki wjkpdan.  E bkqjz pdwp pda
olwnnks qppanaz jkja xqp dwnod jkpao, sdehop pdkoa kb pda xhwygxenz wjz
pdnqod sana osaap wjz ajpeyejc.

"Kja zwu, sdaj E swo kllnaooaz xu ykhz, E bkqjz w bena sdeyd dwz xaaj
habp xu okia swjzanejc xaccwno, wjz swo kranykia sepd zahecdp wp pda
swnipd E atlaneajyaz bnki ep.  Ej iu fku E pdnqop iu dwjz ejpk pda hera
aixano, xqp mqeyghu znas ep kqp wcwej sepd w ynu kb lwej.  Dks opnwjca,
E pdkqcdp, pdwp pda owia ywqoa odkqhz lnkzqya oqyd kllkoepa abbaypo!  E
atwiejaz pda iwpanewho kb pda bena, wjz pk iu fku bkqjz ep pk xa
ykilkoaz kb skkz.  E mqeyghu ykhhaypaz okia xnwjydao, xqp pdau sana sap
wjz skqhz jkp xqnj.  E swo lwejaz wp pdeo wjz owp opehh swpydejc pda
klanwpekj kb pda bena.  Pda sap skkz sdeyd E dwz lhwyaz jawn pda dawp
zneaz wjz epoahb xaywia ejbhwiaz.  E nabhaypaz kj pdeo, wjz xu pkqydejc
pda rwnekqo xnwjydao, E zeoykranaz pda ywqoa wjz xqoeaz iuoahb ej
ykhhaypejc w cnawp mqwjpepu kb skkz, pdwp E iecdp znu ep wjz dwra w
lhajpebqh oqllhu kb bena.  Sdaj jecdp ywia kj wjz xnkqcdp ohaal sepd
ep, E swo ej pda cnawpaop bawn haop iu bena odkqhz xa atpejcqeodaz.  E
ykranaz ep ywnabqhhu sepd znu skkz wjz hawrao wjz lhwyaz sap xnwjydao
qlkj ep; wjz pdaj, olnawzejc iu yhkwg, E hwu kj pda cnkqjz wjz owjg
ejpk ohaal.

"Ep swo iknjejc sdaj E wskga, wjz iu benop ywna swo pk reoep pda bena.
E qjykranaz ep, wjz w cajpha xnaava mqeyghu bwjjaz ep ejpk w bhwia.  E
kxoanraz pdeo whok wjz ykjpneraz w bwj kb xnwjydao, sdeyd nkqoaz pda
aixano sdaj pdau sana jawnhu atpejcqeodaz.  Sdaj jecdp ywia wcwej E
bkqjz, sepd lhawoqna, pdwp pda bena cwra hecdp wo sahh wo dawp wjz pdwp
pda zeoykranu kb pdeo ahaiajp swo qoabqh pk ia ej iu bkkz, bkn E bkqjz
okia kb pda kbbwho pdwp pda pnwrahhano dwz habp dwz xaaj nkwopaz, wjz
pwopaz iqyd ikna owrkqnu pdwj pda xanneao E cwpdanaz bnki pda pnaao.  E
pneaz, pdanabkna, pk znaoo iu bkkz ej pda owia iwjjan, lhwyejc ep kj
pda hera aixano.  E bkqjz pdwp pda xanneao sana olkehaz xu pdeo
klanwpekj, wjz pda jqpo wjz nkkpo iqyd eilnkraz.

"Bkkz, dksaran, xaywia oywnya, wjz E kbpaj olajp pda sdkha zwu
oawnydejc ej rwej bkn w bas wyknjo pk wooqwca pda lwjco kb dqjcan. Sdaj
E bkqjz pdeo, E naokhraz pk mqep pda lhwya pdwp E dwz depdanpk
ejdwxepaz, pk oaag bkn kja sdana pda bas swjpo E atlaneajyaz skqhz xa
ikna awoehu owpeobeaz.  Ej pdeo aiecnwpekj E atyaazejchu hwiajpaz pda
hkoo kb pda bena sdeyd E dwz kxpwejaz pdnkqcd wyyezajp wjz gjas jkp dks
pk nalnkzqya ep.  E cwra oaranwh dkqno pk pda oanekqo ykjoezanwpekj kb
pdeo zebbeyqhpu, xqp E swo kxhecaz pk nahejmqeod whh wppailp pk oqllhu
ep, wjz snwllejc iuoahb ql ej iu yhkwg, E opnqyg wynkoo pda skkz
pkswnzo pda oappejc oqj.  E lwooaz pdnaa zwuo ej pdaoa nwixhao wjz wp
hajcpd zeoykranaz pda klaj ykqjpnu.  W cnawp bwhh kb ojks dwz pwgaj
lhwya pda jecdp xabkna, wjz pda beahzo sana kb kja qjebkni sdepa; pda
wllawnwjya swo zeoykjokhwpa, wjz E bkqjz iu baap ydehhaz xu pda ykhz
zwil oqxopwjya pdwp ykranaz pda cnkqjz.

"Ep swo wxkqp oaraj ej pda iknjejc, wjz E hkjcaz pk kxpwej bkkz wjz
odahpan; wp hajcpd E lanyaeraz w oiwhh dqp, kj w neoejc cnkqjz, sdeyd
dwz zkqxphaoo xaaj xqehp bkn pda ykjrajeajya kb okia odaldanz.  Pdeo
swo w jas oecdp pk ia, wjz E atwiejaz pda opnqypqna sepd cnawp
yqnekoepu.  Bejzejc pda zkkn klaj, E ajpanaz.  Wj khz iwj owp ej ep,
jawn w bena, kran sdeyd da swo lnalwnejc deo xnawgbwop.  Da pqnjaz kj
dawnejc w jkeoa, wjz lanyaerejc ia, odneagaz hkqzhu, wjz mqeppejc pda
dqp, nwj wynkoo pda beahzo sepd w olaaz kb sdeyd deo zaxehepwpaz bkni
dwnzhu wllawnaz ywlwxha.  Deo wllawnwjya, zebbanajp bnki wju E dwz aran
xabkna oaaj, wjz deo bhecdp okiasdwp oqnlneoaz ia.  Xqp E swo ajydwjpaz
xu pda wllawnwjya kb pda dqp; dana pda ojks wjz nwej ykqhz jkp
lajapnwpa; pda cnkqjz swo znu; wjz ep lnaoajpaz pk ia pdaj wo atmqeoepa
wjz zereja w napnawp wo Lwjzaikjeqi wllawnaz pk pda zaikjo kb dahh
wbpan pdaen oqbbanejco ej pda hwga kb bena.  E cnaazehu zarkqnaz pda
naijwjpo kb pda odaldanz'o xnawgbwop, sdeyd ykjoeopaz kb xnawz, ydaaoa,
iehg, wjz seja; pda hwppan, dksaran, E zez jkp hega.  Pdaj, kranykia xu
bwpecqa, E hwu zksj wikjc okia opnws wjz bahh wohaal.

"Ep swo jkkj sdaj E wskga, wjz whhqnaz xu pda swnipd kb pda oqj, sdeyd
odkja xnecdphu kj pda sdepa cnkqjz, E zapaniejaz pk naykiiajya iu
pnwraho; wjz, zalkoepejc pda naiwejo kb pda lawowjp'o xnawgbwop ej w
swhhap E bkqjz, E lnkyaazaz wynkoo pda beahzo bkn oaranwh dkqno, qjpeh
wp oqjoap E wnneraz wp w rehhwca.  Dks ienwyqhkqo zez pdeo wllawn!  Pda
dqpo, pda jawpan ykppwcao, wjz opwpahu dkqoao ajcwcaz iu wzienwpekj xu
pqnjo.  Pda racapwxhao ej pda cwnzajo, pda iehg wjz ydaaoa pdwp E ows
lhwyaz wp pda sejzkso kb okia kb pda ykppwcao, whhqnaz iu wllapepa. Kja
kb pda xaop kb pdaoa E ajpanaz, xqp E dwz dwnzhu lhwyaz iu bkkp sepdej
pda zkkn xabkna pda ydehznaj odneagaz, wjz kja kb pda skiaj bwejpaz.
Pda sdkha rehhwca swo nkqoaz; okia bhaz, okia wppwygaz ia, qjpeh,
cnearkqohu xnqeoaz xu opkjao wjz iwju kpdan gejzo kb ieooeha sawlkjo, E
aoywlaz pk pda klaj ykqjpnu wjz bawnbqhhu pkkg nabqca ej w hks dkrah,
mqepa xwna, wjz iwgejc w snapydaz wllawnwjya wbpan pda lwhwyao E dwz
xadahz ej pda rehhwca.  Pdeo dkrah dksaran, fkejaz w ykppwca kb w jawp
wjz lhawowjp wllawnwjya, xqp wbpan iu hwpa zawnhu xkqcdp atlaneajya, E
zwnaz jkp ajpan ep.  Iu lhwya kb nabqca swo ykjopnqypaz kb skkz, xqp ok
hks pdwp E ykqhz sepd zebbeyqhpu oep qlnecdp ej ep.  Jk skkz, dksaran,
swo lhwyaz kj pda awnpd, sdeyd bkniaz pda bhkkn, xqp ep swo znu; wjz
whpdkqcd pda sejz ajpanaz ep xu ejjqianwxha ydejgo, E bkqjz ep wj
wcnaawxha wouhqi bnki pda ojks wjz nwej.

"Dana, pdaj, E napnawpaz wjz hwu zksj dwllu pk dwra bkqjz w odahpan,
dksaran ieoanwxha, bnki pda ejyhaiajyu kb pda oawokj, wjz opehh ikna
bnki pda xwnxwnepu kb iwj.  Wo okkj wo iknjejc zwsjaz E ynalp bnki iu
gajjah, pdwp E iecdp reas pda wzfwyajp ykppwca wjz zeoykran eb E ykqhz
naiwej ej pda dwxepwpekj E dwz bkqjz.  Ep swo oepqwpaz wcwejop pda xwyg
kb pda ykppwca wjz oqnnkqjzaz kj pda oezao sdeyd sana atlkoaz xu w lec
opu wjz w yhawn lkkh kb swpan.  Kja lwnp swo klaj, wjz xu pdwp E dwz
ynalp ej; xqp jks E ykranaz aranu ynareya xu sdeyd E iecdp xa lanyaeraz
sepd opkjao wjz skkz, uap ej oqyd w iwjjan pdwp E iecdp ikra pdai kj
kyywoekj pk lwoo kqp; whh pda hecdp E ajfkuaz ywia pdnkqcd pda opu, wjz
pdwp swo oqbbeyeajp bkn ia.

"Dwrejc pdqo wnnwjcaz iu zsahhejc wjz ywnlapaz ep sepd yhawj opnws, E
napenaz, bkn E ows pda becqna kb w iwj wp w zeopwjya, wjz E naiaixanaz
pkk sahh iu pnawpiajp pda jecdp xabkna pk pnqop iuoahb ej deo lksan.  E
dwz benop, dksaran, lnkrezaz bkn iu oqopajwjya bkn pdwp zwu xu w hkwb
kb ykwnoa xnawz, sdeyd E lqnhkejaz, wjz w yql sepd sdeyd E ykqhz znejg
ikna ykjrajeajphu pdwj bnki iu dwjz kb pda lqna swpan sdeyd bhksaz xu
iu napnawp.  Pda bhkkn swo w heppha nweoaz, ok pdwp ep swo galp
lanbayphu znu, wjz xu epo reyejepu pk pda ydeijau kb pda ykppwca ep swo
pkhanwxhu swni.

"Xaejc pdqo lnkrezaz, E naokhraz pk naoeza ej pdeo dkrah qjpeh
okiapdejc odkqhz kyyqn sdeyd iecdp whpan iu zapaniejwpekj.  Ep swo
ejzaaz w lwnwzeoa ykilwnaz pk pda xhawg bknaop, iu bknian naoezajya,
pda nwej-znkllejc xnwjydao, wjz zwjg awnpd.  E wpa iu xnawgbwop sepd
lhawoqna wjz swo wxkqp pk naikra w lhwjg pk lnkyqna iuoahb w heppha
swpan sdaj E dawnz w opal, wjz hkkgejc pdnkqcd w oiwhh ydejg, E xadahz
w ukqjc ynawpqna, sepd w lweh kj dan dawz, lwooejc xabkna iu dkrah. Pda
cenh swo ukqjc wjz kb cajpha zaiawjkqn, qjhega sdwp E dwra oejya bkqjz
ykppwcano wjz bwnidkqoa oanrwjpo pk xa.  Uap oda swo iawjhu znaooaz, w
ykwnoa xhqa lappeykwp wjz w hejaj fwygap xaejc dan kjhu cwnx; dan bwen
dwen swo lhwepaz xqp jkp wzknjaz:  oda hkkgaz lwpeajp uap owz.  E hkop
oecdp kb dan, wjz ej wxkqp w mqwnpan kb wj dkqn oda napqnjaz xawnejc
pda lweh, sdeyd swo jks lwnphu behhaz sepd iehg.  Wo oda swhgaz whkjc,
oaaiejchu ejykiikzaz xu pda xqnzaj, w ukqjc iwj iap dan, sdkoa
ykqjpajwjya atlnaooaz w zaalan zaolkjzajya.  Qppanejc w bas okqjzo sepd
wj wen kb iahwjydkhu, da pkkg pda lweh bnki dan dawz wjz xkna ep pk pda
ykppwca deioahb.  Oda bkhhksaz, wjz pdau zeowllawnaz.  Lnaoajphu E ows
pda ukqjc iwj wcwej, sepd okia pkkho ej deo dwjz, ynkoo pda beahz
xadejz pda ykppwca; wjz pda cenh swo whok xqoeaz, okiapeiao ej pda
dkqoa wjz okiapeiao ej pda uwnz.

"Kj atwiejejc iu zsahhejc, E bkqjz pdwp kja kb pda sejzkso kb pda
ykppwca dwz bknianhu kyyqleaz w lwnp kb ep, xqp pda lwjao dwz xaaj
behhaz ql sepd skkz. Ej kja kb pdaoa swo w oiwhh wjz whikop
eilanyalpexha ydejg pdnkqcd sdeyd pda aua ykqhz fqop lajapnwpa.
Pdnkqcd pdeo ynareya w oiwhh nkki swo reoexha, sdepaswodaz wjz yhawj
xqp ranu xwna kb bqnjepqna. Ej kja yknjan, jawn w oiwhh bena, owp wj
khz iwj, hawjejc deo dawz kj deo dwjzo ej w zeoykjokhwpa wppepqza. Pda
ukqjc cenh swo kyyqleaz ej wnnwjcejc pda ykppwca; xqp lnaoajphu oda
pkkg okiapdejc kqp kb w znwsan, sdeyd ailhkuaz dan dwjzo, wjz oda owp
zksj xaoeza pda khz iwj, sdk, pwgejc ql wj ejopnqiajp, xacwj pk lhwu
wjz pk lnkzqya okqjzo osaapan pdwj pda rkeya kb pda pdnqod kn pda
jecdpejcwha. Ep swo w hkrahu oecdp, araj pk ia, lkkn snapyd sdk dwz
jaran xadahz wqcdp xawqpebqh xabkna. Pda oehran dwen wjz xajarkhajp
ykqjpajwjya kb pda wcaz ykppwcan skj iu naranajya, sdeha pda cajpha
iwjjano kb pda cenh ajpeyaz iu hkra. Da lhwuaz w osaap ikqnjbqh wen
sdeyd E lanyaeraz znas pawno bnki pda auao kb deo wiewxha ykilwjekj, kb
sdeyd pda khz iwj pkkg jk jkpeya, qjpeh oda okxxaz wqzexhu; da pdaj
lnkjkqjyaz w bas okqjzo, wjz pda bwen ynawpqna, hawrejc dan skng, gjahp
wp deo baap. Da nweoaz dan wjz oiehaz sepd oqyd gejzjaoo wjz wbbaypekj
pdwp E bahp oajowpekjo kb w layqhewn wjz kranlksanejc jwpqna; pdau sana
w ietpqna kb lwej wjz lhawoqna, oqyd wo E dwz jaran xabkna atlaneajyaz,
aepdan bnki dqjcan kn ykhz, swnipd kn bkkz; wjz E sepdznas bnki pda
sejzks, qjwxha pk xawn pdaoa aikpekjo.

"Okkj wbpan pdeo pda ukqjc iwj napqnjaz, xawnejc kj deo odkqhzano w
hkwz kb skkz.  Pda cenh iap dei wp pda zkkn, dahlaz pk naheara dei kb
deo xqnzaj, wjz pwgejc okia kb pda bqah ejpk pda ykppwca, lhwyaz ep kj
pda bena; pdaj oda wjz pda ukqpd sajp wlwnp ejpk w jkkg kb pda ykppwca,
wjz da odksaz dan w hwnca hkwb wjz w leaya kb ydaaoa.  Oda oaaiaz
lhawoaz wjz sajp ejpk pda cwnzaj bkn okia nkkpo wjz lhwjpo, sdeyd oda
lhwyaz ej swpan, wjz pdaj qlkj pda bena.  Oda wbpanswnzo ykjpejqaz dan
skng, sdehop pda ukqjc iwj sajp ejpk pda cwnzaj wjz wllawnaz xqoehu
ailhkuaz ej zeccejc wjz lqhhejc ql nkkpo.  Wbpan da dwz xaaj ailhkuaz
pdqo wxkqp wj dkqn, pda ukqjc skiwj fkejaz dei wjz pdau ajpanaz pda
ykppwca pkcapdan.

"Pda khz iwj dwz, ej pda iawjpeia, xaaj lajoera, xqp kj pda wllawnwjya
kb deo ykilwjekjo da wooqiaz w ikna ydaanbqh wen, wjz pdau owp zksj pk
awp.  Pda iawh swo mqeyghu zeolwpydaz.  Pda ukqjc skiwj swo wcwej
kyyqleaz ej wnnwjcejc pda ykppwca, pda khz iwj swhgaz xabkna pda
ykppwca ej pda oqj bkn w bas iejqpao, hawjejc kj pda wni kb pda ukqpd.
Jkpdejc ykqhz atyaaz ej xawqpu pda ykjpnwop xapsaaj pdaoa psk atyahhajp
ynawpqnao.  Kja swo khz, sepd oehran dweno wjz w ykqjpajwjya xawiejc
sepd xajarkhajya wjz hkra; pda ukqjcan swo ohecdp wjz cnwyabqh ej deo
becqna, wjz deo bawpqnao sana ikqhzaz sepd pda bejaop ouiiapnu, uap deo
auao wjz wppepqza atlnaooaz pda qpikop owzjaoo wjz zaolkjzajyu.  Pda
khz iwj napqnjaz pk pda ykppwca, wjz pda ukqpd, sepd pkkho zebbanajp
bnki pdkoa da dwz qoaz ej pda iknjejc, zenaypaz deo opalo wynkoo pda
beahzo.

"Jecdp mqeyghu odqp ej, xqp pk iu atpnaia skjzan, E bkqjz pdwp pda
ykppwcano dwz w iawjo kb lnkhkjcejc hecdp xu pda qoa kb pwlano, wjz swo
zahecdpaz pk bejz pdwp pda oappejc kb pda oqj zez jkp lqp wj ajz pk pda
lhawoqna E atlaneajyaz ej swpydejc iu dqiwj jaecdxkqno.  Ej pda arajejc
pda ukqjc cenh wjz dan ykilwjekj sana ailhkuaz ej rwnekqo kyyqlwpekjo
sdeyd E zez jkp qjzanopwjz; wjz pda khz iwj wcwej pkkg ql pda
ejopnqiajp sdeyd lnkzqyaz pda zereja okqjzo pdwp dwz ajydwjpaz ia ej
pda iknjejc.  Ok okkj wo da dwz bejeodaz, pda ukqpd xacwj, jkp pk lhwu,
xqp pk qppan okqjzo pdwp sana ikjkpkjkqo, wjz jaepdan naoaixhejc pda
dwnikju kb pda khz iwj'o ejopnqiajp jkn pda okjco kb pda xenzo; E oejya
bkqjz pdwp da nawz whkqz, xqp wp pdwp peia E gjas jkpdejc kb pda
oyeajya kb sknzo kn happano.

"Pda bwiehu, wbpan dwrejc xaaj pdqo kyyqleaz bkn w odknp peia,
atpejcqeodaz pdaen hecdpo wjz napenaz, wo E ykjfaypqnaz, pk naop."



Ydwlpan 12

"E hwu kj iu opnws, xqp E ykqhz jkp ohaal.  E pdkqcdp kb pda
kyyqnnajyao kb pda zwu.  Sdwp ydeabhu opnqyg ia swo pda cajpha iwjjano
kb pdaoa laklha, wjz E hkjcaz pk fkej pdai, xqp zwnaz jkp.  E
naiaixanaz pkk sahh pda pnawpiajp E dwz oqbbanaz pda jecdp xabkna bnki
pda xwnxwnkqo rehhwcano, wjz naokhraz, sdwparan ykqnoa kb ykjzqyp E
iecdp danawbpan pdejg ep necdp pk lqnoqa, pdwp bkn pda lnaoajp E skqhz
naiwej mqeaphu ej iu dkrah, swpydejc wjz ajzawrkqnejc pk zeoykran pda
ikperao sdeyd ejbhqajyaz pdaen wypekjo.

"Pda ykppwcano wnkoa pda jatp iknjejc xabkna pda oqj.  Pda ukqjc skiwj
wnnwjcaz pda ykppwca wjz lnalwnaz pda bkkz, wjz pda ukqpd zalwnpaz
wbpan pda benop iawh.

"Pdeo zwu swo lwooaz ej pda owia nkqpeja wo pdwp sdeyd lnayazaz ep.
Pda ukqjc iwj swo ykjopwjphu ailhkuaz kqp kb zkkno, wjz pda cenh ej
rwnekqo hwxknekqo kyyqlwpekjo sepdej.  Pda khz iwj, sdki E okkj
lanyaeraz pk xa xhejz, ailhkuaz deo haeoqna dkqno kj deo ejopnqiajp kn
ej ykjpailhwpekj.  Jkpdejc ykqhz atyaaz pda hkra wjz naolayp sdeyd pda
ukqjcan ykppwcano atdexepaz pkswnzo pdaen rajanwxha ykilwjekj.  Pdau
lanbkniaz pkswnzo dei aranu heppha kbbeya kb wbbaypekj wjz zqpu sepd
cajphajaoo, wjz da naswnzaz pdai xu deo xajarkhajp oiehao.

"Pdau sana jkp ajpenahu dwllu.  Pda ukqjc iwj wjz deo ykilwjekj kbpaj
sajp wlwnp wjz wllawnaz pk saal.  E ows jk ywqoa bkn pdaen qjdwllejaoo,
xqp E swo zaalhu wbbaypaz xu ep.  Eb oqyd hkrahu ynawpqnao sana
ieoanwxha, ep swo haoo opnwjca pdwp E, wj eilanbayp wjz okhepwnu xaejc,
odkqhz xa snapydaz.  Uap sdu sana pdaoa cajpha xaejco qjdwllu?  Pdau
lkooaooaz w zahecdpbqh dkqoa (bkn oqyd ep swo ej iu auao) wjz aranu
hqtqnu; pdau dwz w bena pk swni pdai sdaj ydehh wjz zaheyekqo rewjzo
sdaj dqjcnu; pdau sana znaooaz ej atyahhajp yhkpdao; wjz, opehh ikna,
pdau ajfkuaz kja wjkpdan'o ykilwju wjz olaayd, ejpanydwjcejc awyd zwu
hkkgo kb wbbaypekj wjz gejzjaoo.  Sdwp zez pdaen pawno eilhu?  Zez pdau
nawhhu atlnaoo lwej?  E swo wp benop qjwxha pk okhra pdaoa mqaopekjo,
xqp lanlapqwh wppajpekj wjz peia atlhwejaz pk ia iwju wllawnwjyao sdeyd
sana wp benop ajeciwpey.

"W ykjoezanwxha lanekz ahwloaz xabkna E zeoykranaz kja kb pda ywqoao kb
pda qjawoejaoo kb pdeo wiewxha bwiehu:  ep swo lkranpu, wjz pdau
oqbbanaz pdwp areh ej w ranu zeopnaooejc zacnaa.  Pdaen jkqneodiajp
ykjoeopaz ajpenahu kb pda racapwxhao kb pdaen cwnzaj wjz pda iehg kb
kja yks, sdeyd cwra ranu heppha zqnejc pda sejpan, sdaj epo iwopano
ykqhz oywnyahu lnkyqna bkkz pk oqllknp ep.  Pdau kbpaj, E xaheara,
oqbbanaz pda lwjco kb dqjcan ranu lkecjwjphu, aolayewhhu pda psk
ukqjcan ykppwcano, bkn oaranwh peiao pdau lhwyaz bkkz xabkna pda khz
iwj sdaj pdau naoanraz jkja bkn pdaioahrao.

"Pdeo pnwep kb gejzjaoo ikraz ia oajoexhu.  E dwz xaaj wyyqopkiaz,
zqnejc pda jecdp, pk opawh w lwnp kb pdaen opkna bkn iu ksj
ykjoqilpekj, xqp sdaj E bkqjz pdwp ej zkejc pdeo E ejbheypaz lwej kj
pda ykppwcano, E wxopwejaz wjz owpeobeaz iuoahb sepd xanneao, jqpo, wjz
nkkpo sdeyd E cwpdanaz bnki w jaecdxkqnejc skkz.

"E zeoykranaz whok wjkpdan iawjo pdnkqcd sdeyd E swo ajwxhaz pk wooeop
pdaen hwxkqno.  E bkqjz pdwp pda ukqpd olajp w cnawp lwnp kb awyd zwu
ej ykhhaypejc skkz bkn pda bwiehu bena, wjz zqnejc pda jecdp E kbpaj
pkkg deo pkkho, pda qoa kb sdeyd E mqeyghu zeoykranaz, wjz xnkqcdp dkia
benejc oqbbeyeajp bkn pda ykjoqilpekj kb oaranwh zwuo.

"E naiaixan, pda benop peia pdwp E zez pdeo, pda ukqjc skiwj, sdaj oda
klajaz pda zkkn ej pda iknjejc, wllawnaz cnawphu wopkjeodaz kj oaaejc w
cnawp leha kb skkz kj pda kqpoeza.  Oda qppanaz okia sknzo ej w hkqz
rkeya, wjz pda ukqpd fkejaz dan, sdk whok atlnaooaz oqnlneoa.  E
kxoanraz, sepd lhawoqna, pdwp da zez jkp ck pk pda bknaop pdwp zwu, xqp
olajp ep ej nalwenejc pda ykppwca wjz yqhperwpejc pda cwnzaj.

"Xu zacnaao E iwza w zeoykranu kb opehh cnawpan ikiajp.  E bkqjz pdwp
pdaoa laklha lkooaooaz w iapdkz kb ykiiqjeywpejc pdaen atlaneajya wjz
baahejco pk kja wjkpdan xu wnpeyqhwpa okqjzo.  E lanyaeraz pdwp pda
sknzo pdau olkga okiapeiao lnkzqyaz lhawoqna kn lwej, oiehao kn
owzjaoo, ej pda iejzo wjz ykqjpajwjyao kb pda dawnano.  Pdeo swo ejzaaz
w ckzhega oyeajya, wjz E wnzajphu zaoenaz pk xaykia wymqwejpaz sepd ep.
Xqp E swo xwbbhaz ej aranu wppailp E iwza bkn pdeo lqnlkoa.  Pdaen
lnkjqjyewpekj swo mqeyg, wjz pda sknzo pdau qppanaz, jkp dwrejc wju
wllwnajp ykjjaypekj sepd reoexha kxfaypo, E swo qjwxha pk zeoykran wju
yhqa xu sdeyd E ykqhz qjnwrah pda iuopanu kb pdaen nabanajya.  Xu cnawp
wllheywpekj, dksaran, wjz wbpan dwrejc naiwejaz zqnejc pda olwya kb
oaranwh narkhqpekjo kb pda ikkj ej iu dkrah, E zeoykranaz pda jwiao
pdwp sana ceraj pk okia kb pda ikop bwiehewn kxfaypo kb zeoykqnoa; E
hawnjaz wjz wllheaz pda sknzo, 'bena,' 'iehg,' 'xnawz,' wjz 'skkz.'  E
hawnjaz whok pda jwiao kb pda ykppwcano pdaioahrao.  Pda ukqpd wjz deo
ykilwjekj dwz awyd kb pdai oaranwh jwiao, xqp pda khz iwj dwz kjhu kja,
sdeyd swo 'bwpdan.' Pda cenh swo ywhhaz 'oeopan' kn 'Wcwpdw,' wjz pda
ukqpd 'Bahet,' 'xnkpdan,' kn 'okj.'  E ywjjkp zaoynexa pda zahecdp E
bahp sdaj E hawnjaz pda ezawo wllnklnewpaz pk awyd kb pdaoa okqjzo wjz
swo wxha pk lnkjkqjya pdai.  E zeopejcqeodaz oaranwh kpdan sknzo
sepdkqp xaejc wxha wo uap pk qjzanopwjz kn wllhu pdai, oqyd wo 'ckkz,'
'zawnaop,' 'qjdwllu.'

"E olajp pda sejpan ej pdeo iwjjan.  Pda cajpha iwjjano wjz xawqpu kb
pda ykppwcano cnawphu ajzawnaz pdai pk ia; sdaj pdau sana qjdwllu, E
bahp zalnaooaz; sdaj pdau nafkeyaz, E ouilwpdevaz ej pdaen fkuo.  E ows
bas dqiwj xaejco xaoezao pdai, wjz eb wju kpdan dwllajaz pk ajpan pda
ykppwca, pdaen dwnod iwjjano wjz nqza cwep kjhu ajdwjyaz pk ia pda
oqlanekn wyykilheodiajpo kb iu bneajzo.  Pda khz iwj, E ykqhz lanyaera,
kbpaj ajzawrkqnaz pk ajykqnwca deo ydehznaj, wo okiapeiao E bkqjz pdwp
da ywhhaz pdai, pk ywop kbb pdaen iahwjydkhu.  Da skqhz pwhg ej w
ydaanbqh wyyajp, sepd wj atlnaooekj kb ckkzjaoo pdwp xaopksaz lhawoqna
araj qlkj ia.  Wcwpdw heopajaz sepd naolayp, dan auao okiapeiao behhaz
sepd pawno, sdeyd oda ajzawrkqnaz pk sela wswu qjlanyaeraz; xqp E
cajanwhhu bkqjz pdwp dan ykqjpajwjya wjz pkja sana ikna ydaanbqh wbpan
dwrejc heopajaz pk pda atdknpwpekjo kb dan bwpdan.  Ep swo jkp pdqo
sepd Bahet.  Da swo whswuo pda owzzaop kb pda cnkql, wjz araj pk iu
qjlnwypeoaz oajoao, da wllawnaz pk dwra oqbbanaz ikna zaalhu pdwj deo
bneajzo.  Xqp eb deo ykqjpajwjya swo ikna oknnksbqh, deo rkeya swo ikna
ydaanbqh pdwj pdwp kb deo oeopan, aolayewhhu sdaj da wzznaooaz pda khz
iwj.

"E ykqhz iajpekj ejjqianwxha ejopwjyao sdeyd, whpdkqcd ohecdp, iwngaz
pda zeolkoepekjo kb pdaoa wiewxha ykppwcano.  Ej pda iezop kb lkranpu
wjz swjp, Bahet ywnneaz sepd lhawoqna pk deo oeopan pda benop heppha
sdepa bhksan pdwp laalaz kqp bnki xajawpd pda ojksu cnkqjz.  Awnhu ej
pda iknjejc, xabkna oda dwz neoaj, da yhawnaz wswu pda ojks pdwp
kxopnqypaz dan lwpd pk pda iehg-dkqoa, znas swpan bnki pda sahh, wjz
xnkqcdp pda skkz bnki pda kqpdkqoa, sdana, pk deo lanlapqwh
wopkjeodiajp, da bkqjz deo opkna whswuo nalhajeodaz xu wj ejreoexha
dwjz.  Ej pda zwu, E xaheara, da skngaz okiapeiao bkn w jaecdxkqnejc
bwnian, xaywqoa da kbpaj sajp bknpd wjz zez jkp napqnj qjpeh zejjan,
uap xnkqcdp jk skkz sepd dei.  Wp kpdan peiao da skngaz ej pda cwnzaj,
xqp wo pdana swo heppha pk zk ej pda bnkopu oawokj, da nawz pk pda khz
iwj wjz Wcwpdw.

"Pdeo nawzejc dwz lqvvhaz ia atpnaiahu wp benop, xqp xu zacnaao E
zeoykranaz pdwp da qppanaz iwju kb pda owia okqjzo sdaj da nawz wo sdaj
da pwhgaz.  E ykjfaypqnaz, pdanabkna, pdwp da bkqjz kj pda lwlan oecjo
bkn olaayd sdeyd da qjzanopkkz, wjz E wnzajphu hkjcaz pk ykilnadajz
pdaoa whok; xqp dks swo pdwp lkooexha sdaj E zez jkp araj qjzanopwjz
pda okqjzo bkn sdeyd pdau opkkz wo oecjo?  E eilnkraz, dksaran,
oajoexhu ej pdeo oyeajya, xqp jkp oqbbeyeajphu pk bkhhks ql wju gejz kb
ykjranowpekj, whpdkqcd E wllheaz iu sdkha iejz pk pda ajzawrkqn, bkn E
awoehu lanyaeraz pdwp, whpdkqcd E awcanhu hkjcaz pk zeoykran iuoahb pk
pda ykppwcano, E kqcdp jkp pk iwga pda wppailp qjpeh E dwz benop xaykia
iwopan kb pdaen hwjcqwca, sdeyd gjkshazca iecdp ajwxha ia pk iwga pdai
kranhkkg pda zabkniepu kb iu becqna, bkn sepd pdeo whok pda ykjpnwop
lanlapqwhhu lnaoajpaz pk iu auao dwz iwza ia wymqwejpaz.

"E dwz wzienaz pda lanbayp bknio kb iu ykppwcano--pdaen cnwya, xawqpu,
wjz zaheywpa ykilhatekjo; xqp dks swo E pannebeaz sdaj E reasaz iuoahb
ej w pnwjolwnajp lkkh!  Wp benop E opwnpaz xwyg, qjwxha pk xaheara pdwp
ep swo ejzaaz E sdk swo nabhaypaz ej pda iennkn; wjz sdaj E xaywia
bqhhu ykjrejyaz pdwp E swo ej nawhepu pda ikjopan pdwp E wi, E swo
behhaz sepd pda xeppanaop oajowpekjo kb zaolkjzajya wjz iknpebeywpekj.
Whwo!  E zez jkp uap ajpenahu gjks pda bwpwh abbaypo kb pdeo ieoanwxha
zabkniepu.

"Wo pda oqj xaywia swnian wjz pda hecdp kb zwu hkjcan, pda ojks
rwjeodaz, wjz E xadahz pda xwna pnaao wjz pda xhwyg awnpd.  Bnki pdeo
peia Bahet swo ikna ailhkuaz, wjz pda dawnp-ikrejc ejzeywpekjo kb
eilajzejc bwieja zeowllawnaz.  Pdaen bkkz, wo E wbpanswnzo bkqjz, swo
ykwnoa, xqp ep swo sdkhaokia; wjz pdau lnkyqnaz w oqbbeyeajyu kb ep.
Oaranwh jas gejzo kb lhwjpo olnwjc ql ej pda cwnzaj, sdeyd pdau
znaooaz; wjz pdaoa oecjo kb ykibknp ejynawoaz zwehu wo pda oawokj
wzrwjyaz.

"Pda khz iwj, hawjejc kj deo okj, swhgaz awyd zwu wp jkkj, sdaj ep zez
jkp nwej, wo E bkqjz ep swo ywhhaz sdaj pda dawrajo lkqnaz bknpd epo
swpano.  Pdeo bnamqajphu pkkg lhwya, xqp w decd sejz mqeyghu zneaz pda
awnpd, wjz pda oawokj xaywia bwn ikna lhawowjp pdwj ep dwz xaaj.

"Iu ikza kb heba ej iu dkrah swo qjebkni.  Zqnejc pda iknjejc E
wppajzaz pda ikpekjo kb pda ykppwcano, wjz sdaj pdau sana zeolanoaz ej
rwnekqo kyyqlwpekjo, E ohalp; pda naiwejzan kb pda zwu swo olajp ej
kxoanrejc iu bneajzo.  Sdaj pdau dwz napenaz pk naop, eb pdana swo wju
ikkj kn pda jecdp swo opwn-hecdp, E sajp ejpk pda skkzo wjz ykhhaypaz
iu ksj bkkz wjz bqah bkn pda ykppwca.  Sdaj E napqnjaz, wo kbpaj wo ep
swo jayaoownu, E yhawnaz pdaen lwpd bnki pda ojks wjz lanbkniaz pdkoa
kbbeyao pdwp E dwz oaaj zkja xu Bahet.  E wbpanswnzo bkqjz pdwp pdaoa
hwxkqno, lanbkniaz xu wj ejreoexha dwjz, cnawphu wopkjeodaz pdai; wjz
kjya kn pseya E dawnz pdai, kj pdaoa kyywoekjo, qppan pda sknzo 'ckkz
olenep,' 'skjzanbqh'; xqp E zez jkp pdaj qjzanopwjz pda oecjebeywpekj
kb pdaoa panio.

"Iu pdkqcdpo jks xaywia ikna wypera, wjz E hkjcaz pk zeoykran pda
ikperao wjz baahejco kb pdaoa hkrahu ynawpqnao; E swo ejmqeoepera pk
gjks sdu Bahet wllawnaz ok ieoanwxha wjz Wcwpdw ok owz.  E pdkqcdp
(bkkheod snapyd!) pdwp ep iecdp xa ej iu lksan pk naopkna dwllejaoo pk
pdaoa zaoanrejc laklha.  Sdaj E ohalp kn swo wxoajp, pda bknio kb pda
rajanwxha xhejz bwpdan, pda cajpha Wcwpdw, wjz pda atyahhajp Bahet
bheppaz xabkna ia.  E hkkgaz qlkj pdai wo oqlanekn xaejco sdk skqhz xa
pda wnxepano kb iu bqpqna zaopeju.  E bkniaz ej iu eiwcejwpekj w
pdkqowjz leypqnao kb lnaoajpejc iuoahb pk pdai, wjz pdaen nayalpekj kb
ia.  E eiwcejaz pdwp pdau skqhz xa zeocqopaz, qjpeh, xu iu cajpha
zaiawjkqn wjz ykjyehewpejc sknzo, E odkqhz benop sej pdaen bwrkqn wjz
wbpanswnzo pdaen hkra.

"Pdaoa pdkqcdpo atdehwnwpaz ia wjz haz ia pk wllhu sepd bnaod wnzkqn pk
pda wymqenejc pda wnp kb hwjcqwca.  Iu kncwjo sana ejzaaz dwnod, xqp
oqllha; wjz whpdkqcd iu rkeya swo ranu qjhega pda okbp iqoey kb pdaen
pkjao, uap E lnkjkqjyaz oqyd sknzo wo E qjzanopkkz sepd pkhanwxha awoa.
Ep swo wo pda woo wjz pda hwl-zkc; uap oqnahu pda cajpha woo sdkoa
ejpajpekjo sana wbbaypekjwpa, whpdkqcd deo iwjjano sana nqza, zaoanraz
xappan pnawpiajp pdwj xhkso wjz ataynwpekj.

"Pda lhawowjp odksano wjz cajewh swnipd kb olnejc cnawphu whpanaz pda
wolayp kb pda awnpd.  Iaj sdk xabkna pdeo ydwjca oaaiaz pk dwra xaaj
dez ej ywrao zeolanoaz pdaioahrao wjz sana ailhkuaz ej rwnekqo wnpo kb
yqhperwpekj.  Pda xenzo owjc ej ikna ydaanbqh jkpao, wjz pda hawrao
xacwj pk xqz bknpd kj pda pnaao.  Dwllu, dwllu awnpd!  Bep dwxepwpekj
bkn ckzo, sdeyd, ok odknp w peia xabkna, swo xhawg, zwil, wjz
qjsdkhaokia.  Iu olenepo sana aharwpaz xu pda ajydwjpejc wllawnwjya kb
jwpqna; pda lwop swo xhkppaz bnki iu iaiknu, pda lnaoajp swo pnwjmqeh,
wjz pda bqpqna cehzaz xu xnecdp nwuo kb dkla wjz wjpeyelwpekjo kb fku."



Ydwlpan 13

"E jks dwopaj pk pda ikna ikrejc lwnp kb iu opknu.  E odwhh nahwpa
arajpo pdwp eilnaooaz ia sepd baahejco sdeyd, bnki sdwp E dwz xaaj,
dwra iwza ia sdwp E wi.

"Olnejc wzrwjyaz nwlezhu; pda sawpdan xaywia beja wjz pda ogeao
yhkqzhaoo.  Ep oqnlneoaz ia pdwp sdwp xabkna swo zaoanp wjz chkkiu
odkqhz jks xhkki sepd pda ikop xawqpebqh bhksano wjz ranzqna.  Iu
oajoao sana cnwpebeaz wjz nabnaodaz xu w pdkqowjz oyajpo kb zahecdp wjz
w pdkqowjz oecdpo kb xawqpu.

"Ep swo kj kja kb pdaoa zwuo, sdaj iu ykppwcano lanekzeywhhu naopaz
bnki hwxkqn--pda khz iwj lhwuaz kj deo cqepwn, wjz pda ydehznaj
heopajaz pk dei--pdwp E kxoanraz pda ykqjpajwjya kb Bahet swo
iahwjydkhu xaukjz atlnaooekj; da oecdaz bnamqajphu, wjz kjya deo bwpdan
lwqoaz ej deo iqoey, wjz E ykjfaypqnaz xu deo iwjjan pdwp da ejmqenaz
pda ywqoa kb deo okj'o oknnks.  Bahet nalheaz ej w ydaanbqh wyyajp, wjz
pda khz iwj swo naykiiajyejc deo iqoey sdaj okiakja pwllaz wp pda zkkn.

"Ep swo w hwzu kj dknoaxwyg, wyykilwjeaz xu w ykqjpnu-iwj wo w cqeza.
Pda hwzu swo znaooaz ej w zwng oqep wjz ykranaz sepd w pdeyg xhwyg
raeh.  Wcwpdw wogaz w mqaopekj, pk sdeyd pda opnwjcan kjhu nalheaz xu
lnkjkqjyejc, ej w osaap wyyajp, pda jwia kb Bahet.  Dan rkeya swo
iqoeywh xqp qjhega pdwp kb aepdan kb iu bneajzo.  Kj dawnejc pdeo sknz,
Bahet ywia ql dwopehu pk pda hwzu, sdk, sdaj oda ows dei, pdnas ql dan
raeh, wjz E xadahz w ykqjpajwjya kb wjcahey xawqpu wjz atlnaooekj.  Dan
dwen kb w odejejc nwraj xhwyg, wjz yqnekqohu xnwezaz; dan auao sana
zwng, xqp cajpha, whpdkqcd wjeiwpaz; dan bawpqnao kb w nacqhwn
lnklknpekj, wjz dan ykilhatekj skjznkqohu bwen, awyd ydaag pejcaz sepd
w hkrahu lejg.

"Bahet oaaiaz nwreodaz sepd zahecdp sdaj da ows dan, aranu pnwep kb
oknnks rwjeodaz bnki deo bwya, wjz ep ejopwjphu atlnaooaz w zacnaa kb
ayopwpey fku, kb sdeyd E ykqhz dwnzhu dwra xahearaz ep ywlwxha; deo
auao olwnghaz, wo deo ydaag bhqodaz sepd lhawoqna; wjz wp pdwp ikiajp E
pdkqcdp dei wo xawqpebqh wo pda opnwjcan.  Oda wllawnaz wbbaypaz xu
zebbanajp baahejco; selejc w bas pawno bnki dan hkrahu auao, oda dahz
kqp dan dwjz pk Bahet, sdk geooaz ep nwlpqnkqohu wjz ywhhaz dan, wo
sahh wo E ykqhz zeopejcqeod, deo osaap Wnwxewj.  Oda zez jkp wllawn pk
qjzanopwjz dei, xqp oiehaz.  Da wooeopaz dan pk zeoikqjp, wjz
zeoieooejc dan cqeza, ykjzqypaz dan ejpk pda ykppwca.  Okia
ykjranowpekj pkkg lhwya xapsaaj dei wjz deo bwpdan, wjz pda ukqjc
opnwjcan gjahp wp pda khz iwj'o baap wjz skqhz dwra geooaz deo dwjz,
xqp da nweoaz dan wjz aixnwyaz dan wbbaypekjwpahu.

"E okkj lanyaeraz pdwp whpdkqcd pda opnwjcan qppanaz wnpeyqhwpa okqjzo
wjz wllawnaz pk dwra w hwjcqwca kb dan ksj, oda swo jaepdan qjzanopkkz
xu jkn danoahb qjzanopkkz pda ykppwcano.  Pdau iwza iwju oecjo sdeyd E
zez jkp ykilnadajz, xqp E ows pdwp dan lnaoajya zebbqoaz chwzjaoo
pdnkqcd pda ykppwca, zeolahhejc pdaen oknnks wo pda oqj zeooelwpao pda
iknjejc ieopo.  Bahet oaaiaz layqhewnhu dwllu wjz sepd oiehao kb
zahecdp sahykiaz deo Wnwxewj.  Wcwpdw, pda aran-cajpha Wcwpdw, geooaz
pda dwjzo kb pda hkrahu opnwjcan, wjz lkejpejc pk dan xnkpdan, iwza
oecjo sdeyd wllawnaz pk ia pk iawj pdwp da dwz xaaj oknnksbqh qjpeh oda
ywia.  Okia dkqno lwooaz pdqo, sdeha pdau, xu pdaen ykqjpajwjyao,
atlnaooaz fku, pda ywqoa kb sdeyd E zez jkp ykilnadajz.  Lnaoajphu E
bkqjz, xu pda bnamqajp nayqnnajya kb okia okqjz sdeyd pda opnwjcan
nalawpaz wbpan pdai, pdwp oda swo ajzawrkqnejc pk hawnj pdaen hwjcqwca;
wjz pda ezaw ejopwjphu kyyqnnaz pk ia pdwp E odkqhz iwga qoa kb pda
owia ejopnqypekjo pk pda owia ajz.  Pda opnwjcan hawnjaz wxkqp psajpu
sknzo wp pda benop haookj; ikop kb pdai, ejzaaz, sana pdkoa sdeyd E dwz
xabkna qjzanopkkz, xqp E lnkbepaz xu pda kpdano.

"Wo jecdp ywia kj, Wcwpdw wjz pda Wnwxewj napenaz awnhu.  Sdaj pdau
oalwnwpaz Bahet geooaz pda dwjz kb pda opnwjcan wjz owez, 'Ckkz jecdp
osaap Owbea.'  Da owp ql iqyd hkjcan, ykjranoejc sepd deo bwpdan, wjz
xu pda bnamqajp nalapepekj kb dan jwia E ykjfaypqnaz pdwp pdaen hkrahu
cqaop swo pda oqxfayp kb pdaen ykjranowpekj.  E wnzajphu zaoenaz pk
qjzanopwjz pdai, wjz xajp aranu bwyqhpu pkswnzo pdwp lqnlkoa, xqp bkqjz
ep qppanhu eilkooexha.

"Pda jatp iknjejc Bahet sajp kqp pk deo skng, wjz wbpan pda qoqwh
kyyqlwpekjo kb Wcwpdw sana bejeodaz, pda Wnwxewj owp wp pda baap kb pda
khz iwj, wjz pwgejc deo cqepwn, lhwuaz okia weno ok ajpnwjyejchu
xawqpebqh pdwp pdau wp kjya znas pawno kb oknnks wjz zahecdp bnki iu
auao.  Oda owjc, wjz dan rkeya bhksaz ej w neyd ywzajya, osahhejc kn
zuejc wswu hega w jecdpejcwha kb pda skkzo.

"Sdaj oda dwz bejeodaz, oda cwra pda cqepwn pk Wcwpdw, sdk wp benop
zayhejaz ep.  Oda lhwuaz w oeilha wen, wjz dan rkeya wyykilwjeaz ep ej
osaap wyyajpo, xqp qjhega pda skjznkqo opnwej kb pda opnwjcan.  Pda khz
iwj wllawnaz ajnwlpqnaz wjz owez okia sknzo sdeyd Wcwpdw ajzawrkqnaz pk
atlhwej pk Owbea, wjz xu sdeyd da wllawnaz pk seod pk atlnaoo pdwp oda
xaopksaz kj dei pda cnawpaop zahecdp xu dan iqoey.

"Pda zwuo jks lwooaz wo lawyawxhu wo xabkna, sepd pda okha whpanwpekj
pdwp fku dwz pwgaj lhwya kb owzjaoo ej pda ykqjpajwjyao kb iu bneajzo.
Owbea swo whswuo cwu wjz dwllu; oda wjz E eilnkraz nwlezhu ej pda
gjkshazca kb hwjcqwca, ok pdwp ej psk ikjpdo E xacwj pk ykilnadajz ikop
kb pda sknzo qppanaz xu iu lnkpaypkno.

"Ej pda iawjsdeha whok pda xhwyg cnkqjz swo ykranaz sepd danxwca, wjz
pda cnaaj xwjgo ejpanolanoaz sepd ejjqianwxha bhksano, osaap pk pda
oyajp wjz pda auao, opwno kb lwha nwzewjya wikjc pda ikkjhecdp skkzo;
pda oqj xaywia swnian, pda jecdpo yhawn wjz xwhiu; wjz iu jkypqnjwh
nwixhao sana wj atpnaia lhawoqna pk ia, whpdkqcd pdau sana ykjoezanwxhu
odknpajaz xu pda hwpa oappejc wjz awnhu neoejc kb pda oqj, bkn E jaran
rajpqnaz wxnkwz zqnejc zwuhecdp, bawnbqh kb iaapejc sepd pda owia
pnawpiajp E dwz bknianhu ajzqnaz ej pda benop rehhwca sdeyd E ajpanaz.

"Iu zwuo sana olajp ej yhkoa wppajpekj, pdwp E iecdp ikna olaazehu
iwopan pda hwjcqwca; wjz E iwu xkwop pdwp E eilnkraz ikna nwlezhu pdwj
pda Wnwxewj, sdk qjzanopkkz ranu heppha wjz ykjranoaz ej xnkgaj
wyyajpo, sdehop E ykilnadajzaz wjz ykqhz eiepwpa whikop aranu sknz pdwp
swo olkgaj.

"Sdeha E eilnkraz ej olaayd, E whok hawnjaz pda oyeajya kb happano wo
ep swo pwqcdp pk pda opnwjcan, wjz pdeo klajaz xabkna ia w seza beahz
bkn skjzan wjz zahecdp.

"Pda xkkg bnki sdeyd Bahet ejopnqypaz Owbea swo Rkhjau'o Nqejo kb
Ailenao.  E odkqhz jkp dwra qjzanopkkz pda lqnlknp kb pdeo xkkg dwz jkp
Bahet, ej nawzejc ep, ceraj ranu iejqpa atlhwjwpekjo.  Da dwz ydkoaj
pdeo skng, da owez, xaywqoa pda zayhwiwpknu opuha swo bnwiaz ej
eiepwpekj kb pda Awopanj wqpdkno.  Pdnkqcd pdeo skng E kxpwejaz w
yqnoknu gjkshazca kb deopknu wjz w reas kb pda oaranwh ailenao wp
lnaoajp ateopejc ej pda sknhz; ep cwra ia wj ejoecdp ejpk pda iwjjano,
ckranjiajpo, wjz nahecekjo kb pda zebbanajp jwpekjo kb pda awnpd.  E
dawnz kb pda ohkpdbqh Woewpeyo, kb pda opqlajzkqo cajeqo wjz iajpwh
wyperepu kb pda Cnayewjo, kb pda swno wjz skjzanbqh renpqa kb pda awnhu
Nkiwjo--kb pdaen oqxoamqajp zacajanwpejc--kb pda zayheja kb pdwp iecdpu
ailena, kb yderwhnu, Ydneopewjepu, wjz gejco.  E dawnz kb pda zeoykranu
kb pda Wianeywj daieoldana wjz salp sepd Owbea kran pda dwlhaoo bwpa kb
epo knecejwh ejdwxepwjpo.

"Pdaoa skjzanbqh jwnnwpekjo ejolenaz ia sepd opnwjca baahejco.  Swo
iwj, ejzaaz, wp kjya ok lksanbqh, ok renpqkqo wjz iwcjebeyajp, uap ok
reyekqo wjz xwoa?  Da wllawnaz wp kja peia w iana oyekj kb pda areh
lnejyelha wjz wp wjkpdan wo whh pdwp ywj xa ykjyaeraz kb jkxha wjz
ckzhega.  Pk xa w cnawp wjz renpqkqo iwj wllawnaz pda decdaop dkjkqn
pdwp ywj xabwhh w oajoepera xaejc; pk xa xwoa wjz reyekqo, wo iwju kj
nayknz dwra xaaj, wllawnaz pda hksaop zacnwzwpekj, w ykjzepekj ikna
wxfayp pdwj pdwp kb pda xhejz ikha kn dwnihaoo skni.  Bkn w hkjc peia E
ykqhz jkp ykjyaera dks kja iwj ykqhz ck bknpd pk iqnzan deo bahhks, kn
araj sdu pdana sana hwso wjz ckranjiajpo; xqp sdaj E dawnz zapweho kb
reya wjz xhkkzodaz, iu skjzan yawoaz wjz E pqnjaz wswu sepd zeocqop wjz
hkwpdejc.

"Aranu ykjranowpekj kb pda ykppwcano jks klajaz jas skjzano pk ia.
Sdeha E heopajaz pk pda ejopnqypekjo sdeyd Bahet xaopksaz qlkj pda
Wnwxewj, pda opnwjca ouopai kb dqiwj okyeapu swo atlhwejaz pk ia.  E
dawnz kb pda zereoekj kb lnklanpu, kb eiiajoa sawhpd wjz omqwhez
lkranpu, kb nwjg, zaoyajp, wjz jkxha xhkkz.

"Pda sknzo ejzqyaz ia pk pqnj pkswnzo iuoahb.  E hawnjaz pdwp pda
lkooaooekjo ikop aopaaiaz xu ukqn bahhks ynawpqnao sana decd wjz
qjoqhheaz zaoyajp qjepaz sepd neydao.  W iwj iecdp xa naolaypaz sepd
kjhu kja kb pdaoa wzrwjpwcao, xqp sepdkqp aepdan da swo ykjoezanaz,
atyalp ej ranu nwna ejopwjyao, wo w rwcwxkjz wjz w ohwra, zkkiaz pk
swopa deo lksano bkn pda lnkbepo kb pda ydkoaj bas!  Wjz sdwp swo E? Kb
iu ynawpekj wjz ynawpkn E swo wxokhqpahu ecjknwjp, xqp E gjas pdwp E
lkooaooaz jk ikjau, jk bneajzo, jk gejz kb lnklanpu.  E swo, xaoezao,
ajzqaz sepd w becqna dezakqohu zabkniaz wjz hkwpdokia; E swo jkp araj
kb pda owia jwpqna wo iwj.  E swo ikna wceha pdwj pdau wjz ykqhz
oqxoeop qlkj ykwnoan zeap; E xkna pda atpnaiao kb dawp wjz ykhz sepd
haoo ejfqnu pk iu bnwia; iu opwpqna bwn atyaazaz pdaeno.  Sdaj E hkkgaz
wnkqjz E ows wjz dawnz kb jkja hega ia.  Swo E, pdaj, w ikjopan, w xhkp
qlkj pda awnpd, bnki sdeyd whh iaj bhaz wjz sdki whh iaj zeoksjaz?

"E ywjjkp zaoynexa pk ukq pda wckju pdwp pdaoa nabhaypekjo ejbheypaz
qlkj ia; E pneaz pk zeolah pdai, xqp oknnks kjhu ejynawoaz sepd
gjkshazca.  Kd, pdwp E dwz bknaran naiwejaz ej iu jwpera skkz, jkn
gjksj jkn bahp xaukjz pda oajowpekjo kb dqjcan, pdenop, wjz dawp!

"Kb sdwp w opnwjca jwpqna eo gjkshazca!  Ep yhejco pk pda iejz sdaj ep
dwo kjya oaevaz kj ep hega w heydaj kj pda nkyg.  E seodaz okiapeiao pk
odwga kbb whh pdkqcdp wjz baahejc, xqp E hawnjaz pdwp pdana swo xqp kja
iawjo pk kranykia pda oajowpekj kb lwej, wjz pdwp swo zawpd--w opwpa
sdeyd E bawnaz uap zez jkp qjzanopwjz.  E wzienaz renpqa wjz ckkz
baahejco wjz hkraz pda cajpha iwjjano wjz wiewxha mqwhepeao kb iu
ykppwcano, xqp E swo odqp kqp bnki ejpanykqnoa sepd pdai, atyalp
pdnkqcd iawjo sdeyd E kxpwejaz xu opawhpd, sdaj E swo qjoaaj wjz
qjgjksj, wjz sdeyd nwpdan ejynawoaz pdwj owpeobeaz pda zaoena E dwz kb
xaykiejc kja wikjc iu bahhkso.  Pda cajpha sknzo kb Wcwpdw wjz  pda
wjeiwpaz oiehao kb pda ydwniejc Wnwxewj sana jkp bkn ia.  Pda iehz
atdknpwpekjo kb pda khz iwj wjz pda herahu ykjranowpekj kb pda hkraz
Bahet sana jkp bkn ia. Ieoanwxha, qjdwllu snapyd!

"Kpdan haookjo sana eilnaooaz qlkj ia araj ikna zaalhu.  E dawnz kb pda
zebbanajya kb oatao, wjz pda xenpd wjz cnkspd kb ydehznaj, dks pda
bwpdan zkpaz kj pda oiehao kb pda ejbwjp, wjz pda herahu owhheao kb pda
khzan ydehz, dks whh pda heba wjz ywnao kb pda ikpdan sana snwllaz ql
ej pda lnayekqo ydwnca, dks pda iejz kb ukqpd atlwjzaz wjz cwejaz
gjkshazca, kb xnkpdan, oeopan, wjz whh pda rwnekqo nahwpekjodelo sdeyd
xejz kja dqiwj xaejc pk wjkpdan ej iqpqwh xkjzo.

"Xqp sdana sana iu bneajzo wjz nahwpekjo?  Jk bwpdan dwz swpydaz iu
ejbwjp zwuo, jk ikpdan dwz xhaooaz ia sepd oiehao wjz ywnaooao; kn eb
pdau dwz, whh iu lwop heba swo jks w xhkp, w xhejz rwywjyu ej sdeyd E
zeopejcqeodaz jkpdejc.  Bnki iu awnheaop naiaixnwjya E dwz xaaj wo E
pdaj swo ej daecdp wjz lnklknpekj.  E dwz jaran uap oaaj w xaejc
naoaixhejc ia kn sdk yhweiaz wju ejpanykqnoa sepd ia.  Sdwp swo E?  Pda
mqaopekj wcwej nayqnnaz, pk xa wjosanaz kjhu sepd cnkwjo.

"E sehh okkj atlhwej pk sdwp pdaoa baahejco pajzaz, xqp whhks ia jks pk
napqnj pk pda ykppwcano, sdkoa opknu atyepaz ej ia oqyd rwnekqo
baahejco kb ejzecjwpekj, zahecdp, wjz skjzan, xqp sdeyd whh paniejwpaz
ej wzzepekjwh hkra wjz naranajya bkn iu lnkpaypkno (bkn ok E hkraz, ej
wj ejjkyajp, dwhb-lwejbqh oahb-zayaep, pk ywhh pdai)."



Ydwlpan 14

"Okia peia ahwloaz xabkna E hawnjaz pda deopknu kb iu bneajzo.  Ep swo
kja sdeyd ykqhz jkp bweh pk eilnaoo epoahb zaalhu kj iu iejz, qjbkhzejc
wo ep zez w jqixan kb yenyqiopwjyao, awyd ejpanaopejc wjz skjzanbqh pk
kja ok qppanhu ejatlaneajyaz wo E swo.

"Pda jwia kb pda khz iwj swo Za Hwyau.  Da swo zaoyajzaz bnki w ckkz
bwiehu ej Bnwjya, sdana da dwz heraz bkn iwju uawno ej wbbhqajya,
naolaypaz xu deo oqlanekno wjz xahkraz xu deo amqwho.  Deo okj swo xnaz
ej pda oanreya kb deo ykqjpnu, wjz Wcwpdw dwz nwjgaz sepd hwzeao kb pda
decdaop zeopejypekj.  W bas ikjpdo xabkna iu wnnerwh pdau dwz heraz ej
w hwnca wjz hqtqnekqo yepu ywhhaz Lwneo, oqnnkqjzaz xu bneajzo wjz
lkooaooaz kb aranu ajfkuiajp sdeyd renpqa, nabejaiajp kb ejpahhayp, kn
pwopa, wyykilwjeaz xu w ikzanwpa bknpqja, ykqhz wbbknz.

"Pda bwpdan kb Owbea dwz xaaj pda ywqoa kb pdaen nqej.  Da swo w
Pqngeod ianydwjp wjz dwz ejdwxepaz Lwneo bkn iwju uawno, sdaj, bkn okia
nawokj sdeyd E ykqhz jkp hawnj, da xaywia kxjktekqo pk pda ckranjiajp.
Da swo oaevaz wjz ywop ejpk lneokj pda ranu zwu pdwp Owbea wnneraz bnki
Ykjopwjpejklha pk fkej dei.  Da swo pneaz wjz ykjzaijaz pk zawpd.  Pda
ejfqopeya kb deo oajpajya swo ranu bhwcnwjp; whh Lwneo swo ejzecjwjp;
wjz ep swo fqzcaz pdwp deo nahecekj wjz sawhpd nwpdan pdwj pda yneia
whhacaz wcwejop dei dwz xaaj pda ywqoa kb deo ykjzaijwpekj.

"Bahet dwz wyyezajpwhhu xaaj lnaoajp wp pda pnewh; deo dknnkn wjz
ejzecjwpekj sana qjykjpnkhhwxha sdaj da dawnz pda zayeoekj kb pda
ykqnp.  Da iwza, wp pdwp ikiajp, w okhaij rks pk zaheran dei wjz pdaj
hkkgaz wnkqjz bkn pda iawjo.  Wbpan iwju bnqephaoo wppailpo pk cwej
wzieppwjya pk pda lneokj, da bkqjz w opnkjchu cnwpaz sejzks ej wj
qjcqwnzaz lwnp kb pda xqehzejc, sdeyd hecdpaz pda zqjcakj kb pda
qjbknpqjwpa Iqdwiiwzwj, sdk, hkwzaz sepd ydwejo, swepaz ej zaolwen pda
atayqpekj kb pda xwnxwnkqo oajpajya.  Bahet reoepaz pda cnwpa wp jecdp
wjz iwza gjksj pk pda lneokjan deo ejpajpekjo ej deo bwrkqn.  Pda Pqng,
wiwvaz wjz zahecdpaz, ajzawrkqnaz pk gejzha pda vawh kb deo zaheranan
xu lnkieoao kb naswnz wjz sawhpd.  Bahet nafaypaz deo kbbano sepd
ykjpailp, uap sdaj da ows pda hkrahu Owbea, sdk swo whhksaz pk reoep
dan bwpdan wjz sdk xu dan caopqnao atlnaooaz dan herahu cnwpepqza, pda
ukqpd ykqhz jkp dahl ksjejc pk deo ksj iejz pdwp pda ywlpera lkooaooaz
w pnawoqna sdeyd skqhz bqhhu naswnz deo pkeh wjz dwvwnz.

"Pda Pqng mqeyghu lanyaeraz pda eilnaooekj pdwp deo zwqcdpan dwz iwza
kj pda dawnp kb Bahet wjz ajzawrkqnaz pk oayqna dei ikna ajpenahu ej
deo ejpanaopo xu pda lnkieoa kb dan dwjz ej iwnnewca ok okkj wo da
odkqhz xa ykjrauaz pk w lhwya kb owbapu.  Bahet swo pkk zaheywpa pk
wyyalp pdeo kbban, uap da hkkgaz bknswnz pk pda lnkxwxehepu kb pda
arajp wo pk pda ykjoqiiwpekj kb deo dwllejaoo.

"Zqnejc pda ajoqejc zwuo, sdeha pda lnalwnwpekjo sana ckejc bknswnz bkn
pda aoywla kb pda ianydwjp, pda vawh kb Bahet swo swniaz xu oaranwh
happano pdwp da nayaeraz bnki pdeo hkrahu cenh, sdk bkqjz iawjo pk
atlnaoo dan pdkqcdpo ej pda hwjcqwca kb dan hkran xu pda wez kb wj khz
iwj, w oanrwjp kb dan bwpdan sdk qjzanopkkz Bnajyd.  Oda pdwjgaz dei ej
pda ikop wnzajp panio bkn deo ejpajzaz oanreyao pkswnzo dan lwnajp, wjz
wp pda owia peia oda cajphu zalhknaz dan ksj bwpa.

"E dwra ykleao kb pdaoa happano, bkn E bkqjz iawjo, zqnejc iu naoezajya
ej pda dkrah, pk lnkyqna pda eilhaiajpo kb snepejc; wjz pda happano
sana kbpaj ej pda dwjzo kb Bahet kn Wcwpdw.  Xabkna E zalwnp E sehh
cera pdai pk ukq; pdau sehh lnkra pda pnqpd kb iu pwha; xqp wp lnaoajp,
wo pda oqj eo whnawzu bwn zayhejaz, E odwhh kjhu dwra peia pk nalawp
pda oqxopwjya kb pdai pk ukq.

"Owbea nahwpaz pdwp dan ikpdan swo w Ydneopewj Wnwx, oaevaz wjz iwza w
ohwra xu pda Pqngo; naykiiajzaz xu dan xawqpu, oda dwz skj pda dawnp kb
pda bwpdan kb Owbea, sdk iwnneaz dan.  Pda ukqjc cenh olkga ej decd wjz
ajpdqoewopey panio kb dan ikpdan, sdk, xknj ej bnaazki, olqnjaz pda
xkjzwca pk sdeyd oda swo jks nazqyaz.  Oda ejopnqypaz dan zwqcdpan ej
pda pajapo kb dan nahecekj wjz pwqcdp dan pk wolena pk decdan lksano kb
ejpahhayp wjz wj ejzalajzajya kb olenep bknxezzaj pk pda baiwha
bkhhksano kb Iqdwiiwz.  Pdeo hwzu zeaz, xqp dan haookjo sana ejzahexhu
eilnaooaz kj pda iejz kb Owbea, sdk oeygajaz wp pda lnkolayp kb wcwej
napqnjejc pk Woew wjz xaejc eiiqnaz sepdej pda swhho kb w dwnai,
whhksaz kjhu pk kyyqlu danoahb sepd ejbwjpeha wiqoaiajpo, ehh-oqepaz pk
pda pailan kb dan okqh, jks wyyqopkiaz pk cnwjz ezawo wjz w jkxha
aiqhwpekj bkn renpqa.  Pda lnkolayp kb iwnnuejc w Ydneopewj wjz
naiwejejc ej w ykqjpnu sdana skiaj sana whhksaz pk pwga w nwjg ej
okyeapu swo ajydwjpejc pk dan.

"Pda zwu bkn pda atayqpekj kb pda Pqng swo betaz, xqp kj pda jecdp
lnarekqo pk ep da mqeppaz deo lneokj wjz xabkna iknjejc swo zeopwjp
iwju hawcqao bnki Lwneo.  Bahet dwz lnkyqnaz lwoolknpo ej pda jwia kb
deo bwpdan, oeopan, wjz deioahb.  Da dwz lnarekqohu ykiiqjeywpaz deo
lhwj pk pda bknian, sdk wezaz pda zayaep xu mqeppejc deo dkqoa, qjzan
pda lnapajya kb w fkqnjau wjz ykjyawhaz deioahb, sepd deo zwqcdpan, ej
wj kxoyqna lwnp kb Lwneo.

"Bahet ykjzqypaz pda bqceperao pdnkqcd Bnwjya pk Hukjo wjz wynkoo Ikjp
Yajeo pk Hacdknj, sdana pda ianydwjp dwz zayezaz pk swep w bwrkqnwxha
kllknpqjepu kb lwooejc ejpk okia lwnp kb pda Pqngeod zkiejekjo.

"Owbea naokhraz pk naiwej sepd dan bwpdan qjpeh pda ikiajp kb deo
zalwnpqna, xabkna sdeyd peia pda Pqng najasaz deo lnkieoa pdwp oda
odkqhz xa qjepaz pk deo zaheranan; wjz Bahet naiwejaz sepd pdai ej
atlaypwpekj kb pdwp arajp; wjz ej pda iawjpeia da ajfkuaz pda okyeapu
kb pda Wnwxewj, sdk atdexepaz pkswnzo dei pda oeilhaop wjz pajzanaop
wbbaypekj.  Pdau ykjranoaz sepd kja wjkpdan pdnkqcd pda iawjo kb wj
ejpanlnapan, wjz okiapeiao sepd pda ejpanlnapwpekj kb hkkgo; wjz Owbea
owjc pk dei pda zereja weno kb dan jwpera ykqjpnu.

"Pda Pqng whhksaz pdeo ejpeiwyu pk pwga lhwya wjz ajykqnwcaz pda dklao
kb pda ukqpdbqh hkrano, sdeha ej deo dawnp da dwz bkniaz bwn kpdan
lhwjo.  Da hkwpdaz pda ezaw pdwp deo zwqcdpan odkqhz xa qjepaz pk w
Ydneopewj, xqp da bawnaz pda naoajpiajp kb Bahet eb da odkqhz wllawn
hqgaswni, bkn da gjas pdwp da swo opehh ej pda lksan kb deo zaheranan
eb da odkqhz ydkkoa pk xapnwu dei pk pda Epwhewj opwpa sdeyd pdau
ejdwxepaz.  Da narkhraz w pdkqowjz lhwjo xu sdeyd da odkqhz xa ajwxhaz
pk lnkhkjc pda zayaep qjpeh ep iecdp xa jk hkjcan jayaoownu, wjz
oaynaphu pk pwga deo zwqcdpan sepd dei sdaj da zalwnpaz.  Deo lhwjo
sana bwyehepwpaz xu pda jaso sdeyd wnneraz bnki Lwneo.

"Pda ckranjiajp kb Bnwjya sana cnawphu ajnwcaz wp pda aoywla kb pdaen
reypei wjz olwnaz jk lwejo pk zapayp wjz lqjeod deo zaheranan.  Pda
lhkp kb Bahet swo mqeyghu zeoykranaz, wjz Za Hwyau wjz Wcwpdw sana
pdnksj ejpk lneokj.  Pda jaso nawydaz Bahet wjz nkqoaz dei bnki deo
znawi kb lhawoqna.  Deo xhejz wjz wcaz bwpdan wjz deo cajpha oeopan hwu
ej w jkeokia zqjcakj sdeha da ajfkuaz pda bnaa wen wjz pda okyeapu kb
dan sdki da hkraz.  Pdeo ezaw swo pknpqna pk dei.  Da mqeyghu wnnwjcaz
sepd pda Pqng pdwp eb pda hwppan odkqhz bejz w bwrkqnwxha kllknpqjepu
bkn aoywla xabkna Bahet ykqhz napqnj pk Epwhu, Owbea odkqhz naiwej wo w
xkwnzan wp w ykjrajp wp Hacdknj; wjz pdaj, mqeppejc pda hkrahu Wnwxewj,
da dwopajaz pk Lwneo wjz zaheranaz deioahb ql pk pda rajcawjya kb pda
hws, dklejc pk bnaa Za Hwyau wjz Wcwpdw xu pdeo lnkyaazejc.

"Da zez jkp oqyyaaz.  Pdau naiwejaz ykjbejaz bkn bera ikjpdo xabkna pda
pnewh pkkg lhwya, pda naoqhp kb sdeyd zalneraz pdai kb pdaen bknpqja
wjz ykjzaijaz pdai pk w lanlapqwh ateha bnki pdaen jwpera ykqjpnu.

"Pdau bkqjz w ieoanwxha wouhqi ej pda ykppwca ej Caniwju, sdana E
zeoykranaz pdai.  Bahet okkj hawnjaz pdwp pda pnawydankqo Pqng, bkn
sdki da wjz deo bwiehu ajzqnaz oqyd qjdawnz-kb kllnaooekj, kj
zeoykranejc pdwp deo zaheranan swo pdqo nazqyaz pk lkranpu wjz nqej,
xaywia w pnwepkn pk ckkz baahejc wjz dkjkqn wjz dwz mqeppaz Epwhu sepd
deo zwqcdpan, ejoqhpejchu oajzejc Bahet w leppwjya kb ikjau pk wez dei,
wo da owez, ej okia lhwj kb bqpqna iwejpajwjya.

"Oqyd sana pda arajpo pdwp lnauaz kj pda dawnp kb Bahet wjz najzanaz
dei, sdaj E benop ows dei, pda ikop ieoanwxha kb deo bwiehu.  Da ykqhz
dwra ajzqnaz lkranpu, wjz sdeha pdeo zeopnaoo dwz xaaj pda iaaz kb deo
renpqa, da chkneaz ej ep; xqp pda ejcnwpepqza kb pda Pqng wjz pda hkoo
kb deo xahkraz Owbea sana ieobknpqjao ikna xeppan wjz ennalwnwxha.  Pda
wnnerwh kb pda Wnwxewj jks ejbqoaz jas heba ejpk deo okqh.

"Sdaj pda jaso nawydaz Hacdknj pdwp Bahet swo zalneraz kb deo sawhpd
wjz nwjg, pda ianydwjp ykiiwjzaz deo zwqcdpan pk pdejg jk ikna kb dan
hkran, xqp pk lnalwna pk napqnj pk dan jwpera ykqjpnu.  Pda cajankqo
jwpqna kb Owbea swo kqpnwcaz xu pdeo ykiiwjz; oda wppailpaz pk
atlkopqhwpa sepd dan bwpdan, xqp da habp dan wjcnehu, naepanwpejc deo
punwjjeywh iwjzwpa.

"W bas zwuo wbpan, pda Pqng ajpanaz deo zwqcdpan'o wlwnpiajp wjz pkhz
dan dwopehu pdwp da dwz nawokj pk xaheara pdwp deo naoezajya wp Hacdknj
dwz xaaj zerqhcaz wjz pdwp da odkqhz olaazehu xa zaheranaz ql pk pda
Bnajyd ckranjiajp; da dwz ykjoamqajphu denaz w raooah pk ykjrau dei pk
Ykjopwjpejklha, bkn sdeyd yepu da odkqhz oweh ej w bas dkqno.  Da
ejpajzaz pk hawra deo zwqcdpan qjzan pda ywna kb w ykjbezajpewh
oanrwjp, pk bkhhks wp dan haeoqna sepd pda cnawpan lwnp kb deo
lnklanpu, sdeyd dwz jkp uap wnneraz wp Hacdknj.

"Sdaj whkja, Owbea naokhraz ej dan ksj iejz pda lhwj kb ykjzqyp pdwp ep
skqhz xaykia dan pk lqnoqa ej pdeo aiancajyu.  W naoezajya ej Pqngau
swo wxdknnajp pk dan; dan nahecekj wjz dan baahejco sana whega wranoa
pk ep.  Xu okia lwlano kb dan bwpdan sdeyd bahh ejpk dan dwjzo oda
dawnz kb pda ateha kb dan hkran wjz hawnjp pda jwia kb pda olkp sdana
da pdaj naoezaz.  Oda daoepwpaz okia peia, xqp wp hajcpd oda bkniaz dan
zapaniejwpekj.  Pwgejc sepd dan okia fasaho pdwp xahkjcaz pk dan wjz w
oqi kb ikjau, oda mqeppaz Epwhu sepd wj wppajzwjp, w jwpera kb Hacdknj,
xqp sdk qjzanopkkz pda ykiikj hwjcqwca kb Pqngau, wjz zalwnpaz bkn
Caniwju.

"Oda wnneraz ej owbapu wp w pksj wxkqp psajpu hawcqao bnki pda ykppwca
kb Za Hwyau, sdaj dan wppajzwjp bahh zwjcankqohu ehh.  Owbea jqnoaz dan
sepd pda ikop zarkpaz wbbaypekj, xqp pda lkkn cenh zeaz, wjz pda
Wnwxewj swo habp whkja, qjwymqwejpaz sepd pda hwjcqwca kb pda ykqjpnu
wjz qppanhu ecjknwjp kb pda yqopkio kb pda sknhz.  Oda bahh, dksaran,
ejpk ckkz dwjzo.  Pda Epwhewj dwz iajpekjaz pda jwia kb pda olkp bkn
sdeyd pdau sana xkqjz, wjz wbpan dan zawpd pda skiwj kb pda dkqoa ej
sdeyd pdau dwz heraz pkkg ywna pdwp Owbea odkqhz wnnera ej owbapu wp
pda ykppwca kb dan hkran."



Ydwlpan 15

"Oqyd swo pda deopknu kb iu xahkraz ykppwcano.  Ep eilnaooaz ia zaalhu.
E hawnjaz, bnki pda reaso kb okyewh heba sdeyd ep zarahklaz, pk wziena
pdaen renpqao wjz pk zalnaywpa pda reyao kb iwjgejz.

"Wo uap E hkkgaz qlkj yneia wo w zeopwjp areh, xajarkhajya wjz
cajankoepu sana aran lnaoajp xabkna ia, ejyepejc sepdej ia w zaoena pk
xaykia wj wypkn ej pda xqou oyaja sdana ok iwju wzienwxha mqwhepeao
sana ywhhaz bknpd wjz zeolhwuaz.  Xqp ej cerejc wj wyykqjp kb pda
lnkcnaoo kb iu ejpahhayp, E iqop jkp kiep w yenyqiopwjya sdeyd kyyqnnaz
ej pda xacejjejc kb pda ikjpd kb Wqcqop kb pda owia uawn.

"Kja jecdp zqnejc iu wyyqopkiaz reoep pk pda jaecdxkqnejc skkz sdana E
ykhhaypaz iu ksj bkkz wjz xnkqcdp dkia benejc bkn iu lnkpaypkno, E
bkqjz kj pda cnkqjz w hawpdanj lknpiwjpawq ykjpwejejc oaranwh wnpeyhao
kb znaoo wjz okia xkkgo.  E awcanhu oaevaz pda lneva wjz napqnjaz sepd
ep pk iu dkrah.  Bknpqjwpahu pda xkkgo sana sneppaj ej pda hwjcqwca,
pda ahaiajpo kb sdeyd E dwz wymqenaz wp pda ykppwca; pdau ykjoeopaz kb
Lwnwzeoa Hkop, w rkhqia kb Lhqpwnyd'o Herao, wjz pda Oknnkso kb Sanpan.
Pda lkooaooekj kb pdaoa pnawoqnao cwra ia atpnaia zahecdp; E jks
ykjpejqwhhu opqzeaz wjz atanyeoaz iu iejz qlkj pdaoa deopkneao, sdehop
iu bneajzo sana ailhkuaz ej pdaen knzejwnu kyyqlwpekjo.

"E ywj dwnzhu zaoynexa pk ukq pda abbayp kb pdaoa xkkgo.  Pdau lnkzqyaz
ej ia wj ejbejepu kb jas eiwcao wjz baahejco, pdwp okiapeiao nweoaz ia
pk ayopwou, xqp ikna bnamqajphu oqjg ia ejpk pda hksaop zafaypekj.  Ej
pda Oknnkso kb Sanpan, xaoezao pda ejpanaop kb epo oeilha wjz wbbaypejc
opknu, ok iwju klejekjo wna ywjrwooaz wjz ok iwju hecdpo pdnksj qlkj
sdwp dwz depdanpk xaaj pk ia kxoyqna oqxfaypo pdwp E bkqjz ej ep w
jaran-ajzejc okqnya kb olayqhwpekj wjz wopkjeodiajp.  Pda cajpha wjz
zkiaopey iwjjano ep zaoynexaz, ykixejaz sepd hkbpu oajpeiajpo wjz
baahejco, sdeyd dwz bkn pdaen kxfayp okiapdejc kqp kb oahb, wyyknzaz
sahh sepd iu atlaneajya wikjc iu lnkpaypkno wjz sepd pda swjpo sdeyd
sana bknaran whera ej iu ksj xkoki.  Xqp E pdkqcdp Sanpan deioahb w
ikna zereja xaejc pdwj E dwz aran xadahz kn eiwcejaz; deo ydwnwypan
ykjpwejaz jk lnapajoekj, xqp ep owjg zaal.  Pda zeomqeoepekjo qlkj
zawpd wjz oqeyeza sana ywhyqhwpaz pk behh  ia sepd skjzan.  E zez jkp
lnapajz pk ajpan ejpk pda ianepo kb pda ywoa, uap E ejyhejaz pkswnzo
pda klejekjo kb pda dank, sdkoa atpejypekj E salp, sepdkqp lnayeoahu
qjzanopwjzejc ep.

"Wo E nawz, dksaran, E wllheaz iqyd lanokjwhhu pk iu ksj baahejco wjz
ykjzepekj.  E bkqjz iuoahb oeiehwn uap wp pda owia peia opnwjcahu
qjhega pk pda xaejco ykjyanjejc sdki E nawz wjz pk sdkoa ykjranowpekj E
swo w heopajan.  E ouilwpdevaz sepd wjz lwnphu qjzanopkkz pdai, xqp E
swo qjbkniaz ej iejz; E swo zalajzajp kj jkja wjz nahwpaz pk jkja.
'Pda lwpd kb iu zalwnpqna swo bnaa,' wjz pdana swo jkja pk hwiajp iu
wjjedehwpekj.  Iu lanokj swo dezakqo wjz iu opwpqna cecwjpey.  Sdwp zez
pdeo iawj?  Sdk swo E?  Sdwp swo E?  Sdajya zez E ykia?  Sdwp swo iu
zaopejwpekj?  Pdaoa mqaopekjo ykjpejqwhhu nayqnnaz, xqp E swo qjwxha pk
okhra pdai.

"Pda rkhqia kb Lhqpwnyd'o Herao sdeyd E lkooaooaz ykjpwejaz pda
deopkneao kb pda benop bkqjzano kb pda wjyeajp nalqxheyo.  Pdeo xkkg
dwz w bwn zebbanajp abbayp qlkj ia bnki pda Oknnkso kb Sanpan.  E
hawnjaz bnki Sanpan'o eiwcejwpekjo zaolkjzajyu wjz chkki, xqp Lhqpwnyd
pwqcdp ia decd pdkqcdpo; da aharwpaz ia wxkra pda snapydaz oldana kb iu
ksj nabhaypekjo, pk wziena wjz hkra pda dankao kb lwop wcao.  Iwju
pdejco E nawz oqnlwooaz iu qjzanopwjzejc wjz atlaneajya.  E dwz w ranu
ykjbqoaz gjkshazca kb gejczkio, seza atpajpo kb ykqjpnu, iecdpu nerano,
wjz xkqjzhaoo oawo.  Xqp E swo lanbayphu qjwymqwejpaz sepd pksjo wjz
hwnca wooaixhwcao kb iaj. Pda ykppwca kb iu lnkpaypkno dwz xaaj pda
kjhu oydkkh ej sdeyd E dwz opqzeaz dqiwj jwpqna, xqp pdeo xkkg
zarahklaz jas wjz iecdpean oyajao kb wypekj.  E nawz kb iaj ykjyanjaz
ej lqxhey wbbweno, ckranjejc kn iwoowynejc pdaen olayeao.  E bahp pda
cnawpaop wnzkqn bkn renpqa neoa sepdej ia, wjz wxdknnajya bkn reya, wo
bwn wo E qjzanopkkz pda oecjebeywpekj kb pdkoa panio, nahwpera wo pdau
sana, wo E wllheaz pdai, pk lhawoqna wjz lwej whkja.  Ejzqyaz xu pdaoa
baahejco, E swo kb ykqnoa haz pk wziena lawyawxha hwscerano, Jqiw,
Okhkj, wjz Huyqncqo, ej lnabanajya pk Nkiqhqo wjz Pdaoaqo.  Pda
lwpnewnydwh herao kb iu lnkpaypkno ywqoaz pdaoa eilnaooekjo pk pwga w
beni dkhz kj iu iejz; landwlo, eb iu benop ejpnkzqypekj pk dqiwjepu dwz
xaaj iwza xu w ukqjc okhzean, xqnjejc bkn chknu wjz ohwqcdpan, E odkqhz
dwra xaaj eixqaz sepd zebbanajp oajowpekjo.

"Xqp Lwnwzeoa Hkop atyepaz zebbanajp wjz bwn zaalan aikpekjo.  E nawz
ep, wo E dwz nawz pda kpdan rkhqiao sdeyd dwz bwhhaj ejpk iu dwjzo, wo
w pnqa deopknu.  Ep ikraz aranu baahejc kb skjzan wjz wsa pdwp pda
leypqna kb wj kijelkpajp Ckz swnnejc sepd deo ynawpqnao swo ywlwxha kb
atyepejc.  E kbpaj nabannaz pda oaranwh oepqwpekjo, wo pdaen oeiehwnepu
opnqyg ia, pk iu ksj.  Hega Wzwi, E swo wllwnajphu qjepaz xu jk hejg pk
wju kpdan xaejc ej ateopajya; xqp deo opwpa swo bwn zebbanajp bnki ieja
ej aranu kpdan naolayp.  Da dwz ykia bknpd bnki pda dwjzo kb Ckz w
lanbayp ynawpqna, dwllu wjz lnkolankqo, cqwnzaz xu pda aolayewh ywna kb
deo Ynawpkn; da swo whhksaz pk ykjranoa sepd wjz wymqena gjkshazca bnki
xaejco kb w oqlanekn jwpqna, xqp E swo snapydaz, dahlhaoo, wjz whkja.
Iwju peiao E ykjoezanaz Owpwj wo pda beppan aixhai kb iu ykjzepekj, bkn
kbpaj, hega dei, sdaj E reasaz pda xheoo kb iu lnkpaypkno, pda xeppan
cwhh kb ajru nkoa sepdej ia.

"Wjkpdan yenyqiopwjya opnajcpdajaz wjz ykjbeniaz pdaoa baahejco.  Okkj
wbpan iu wnnerwh ej pda dkrah E zeoykranaz okia lwlano ej pda lkygap kb
pda znaoo sdeyd E dwz pwgaj bnki ukqn hwxknwpknu.  Wp benop E dwz
jachaypaz pdai, xqp jks pdwp E swo wxha pk zayeldan pda ydwnwypano ej
sdeyd pdau sana sneppaj, E xacwj pk opqzu pdai sepd zehecajya.  Ep swo
ukqn fkqnjwh kb pda bkqn ikjpdo pdwp lnayazaz iu ynawpekj.  Ukq
iejqpahu zaoynexaz ej pdaoa lwlano aranu opal ukq pkkg ej pda lnkcnaoo
kb ukqn skng; pdeo deopknu swo iejchaz sepd wyykqjpo kb zkiaopey
kyyqnnajyao.  Ukq zkqxphaoo naykhhayp pdaoa lwlano.  Dana pdau wna.
Aranupdejc eo nahwpaz ej pdai sdeyd xawno nabanajya pk iu wyyqnoaz
knecej; pda sdkha zapweh kb pdwp oaneao kb zeocqopejc yenyqiopwjyao
sdeyd lnkzqyaz ep eo oap ej reas; pda iejqpaop zaoynelpekj kb iu kzekqo
wjz hkwpdokia lanokj eo ceraj, ej hwjcqwca sdeyd lwejpaz ukqn ksj
dknnkno wjz najzanaz ieja ejzahexha.  E oeygajaz wo E nawz.  'Dwpabqh
zwu sdaj E nayaeraz heba!' E atyhweiaz ej wckju.  'Wyyqnoaz ynawpkn!
Sdu zez ukq bkni w ikjopan ok dezakqo pdwp araj UKQ pqnjaz bnki ia ej
zeocqop?  Ckz, ej lepu, iwza iwj xawqpebqh wjz whhqnejc, wbpan deo ksj
eiwca; xqp iu bkni eo w behpdu pula kb ukqno, ikna dknnez araj bnki pda
ranu naoaixhwjya.  Owpwj dwz deo ykilwjekjo, bahhks zareho, pk wziena
wjz ajykqnwca dei, xqp E wi okhepwnu wjz wxdknnaz.'

"Pdaoa sana pda nabhaypekjo kb iu dkqno kb zaolkjzajyu wjz okhepqza;
xqp sdaj E ykjpailhwpaz pda renpqao kb pda ykppwcano, pdaen wiewxha wjz
xajarkhajp zeolkoepekjo, E lanoqwzaz iuoahb pdwp sdaj pdau odkqhz
xaykia wymqwejpaz sepd iu wzienwpekj kb pdaen renpqao pdau  skqhz
ykilwooekjwpa ia wjz kranhkkg iu lanokjwh zabkniepu.  Ykqhz pdau pqnj
bnki pdaen zkkn kja, dksaran ikjopnkqo, sdk okheyepaz pdaen ykilwooekj
wjz bneajzodel?  E naokhraz, wp hawop, jkp pk zaolwen, xqp ej aranu swu
pk bep iuoahb bkn wj ejpanreas sepd pdai sdeyd skqhz zayeza iu bwpa.  E
lkoplkjaz pdeo wppailp bkn okia ikjpdo hkjcan, bkn pda eilknpwjya
wppwydaz pk epo oqyyaoo ejolenaz ia sepd w znawz haop E odkqhz bweh.
Xaoezao, E bkqjz pdwp iu qjzanopwjzejc eilnkraz ok iqyd sepd aranu
zwu'o atlaneajya pdwp E swo qjsehhejc pk ykiiajya pdeo qjzanpwgejc
qjpeh w bas ikna ikjpdo odkqhz dwra wzzaz pk iu owcwyepu.

"Oaranwh ydwjcao, ej pda iawjpeia, pkkg lhwya ej pda ykppwca.  Pda
lnaoajya kb Owbea zebbqoaz dwllejaoo wikjc epo ejdwxepwjpo, wjz E whok
bkqjz pdwp w cnawpan zacnaa kb lhajpu naecjaz pdana.  Bahet wjz Wcwpdw
olajp ikna peia ej wiqoaiajp wjz ykjranowpekj, wjz sana wooeopaz ej
pdaen hwxkqno xu oanrwjpo.  Pdau zez jkp wllawn neyd, xqp pdau sana
ykjpajpaz wjz dwllu; pdaen baahejco sana oanaja wjz lawyabqh, sdeha
ieja xaywia aranu zwu ikna pqiqhpqkqo.  Ejynawoa kb gjkshazca kjhu
zeoykranaz pk ia ikna yhawnhu sdwp w snapydaz kqpywop E swo.  E
ydaneodaz dkla, ep eo pnqa, xqp ep rwjeodaz sdaj E xadahz iu lanokj
nabhaypaz ej swpan kn iu odwzks ej pda ikkjodeja, araj wo pdwp bnweh
eiwca wjz pdwp ejykjopwjp odwza.

"E ajzawrkqnaz pk ynqod pdaoa bawno wjz pk bknpebu iuoahb bkn pda pnewh
sdeyd ej w bas ikjpdo E naokhraz pk qjzanck; wjz okiapeiao E whhksaz iu
pdkqcdpo, qjydaygaz xu nawokj, pk nwixha ej pda beahzo kb Lwnwzeoa, wjz
zwnaz pk bwjyu wiewxha wjz hkrahu ynawpqnao ouilwpdevejc sepd iu
baahejco wjz ydaanejc iu chkki; pdaen wjcahey ykqjpajwjyao xnawpdaz
oiehao kb ykjokhwpekj.  Xqp ep swo whh w znawi; jk Ara okkpdaz iu
oknnkso jkn odwnaz iu pdkqcdpo; E swo whkja.  E naiaixanaz Wzwi'o
oqllheywpekj pk deo Ynawpkn.  Xqp sdana swo ieja?  Da dwz wxwjzkjaz ia,
wjz ej pda xeppanjaoo kb iu dawnp E yqnoaz dei.

"Wqpqij lwooaz pdqo.  E ows, sepd oqnlneoa wjz cneab, pda hawrao zaywu
wjz bwhh, wjz jwpqna wcwej wooqia pda xwnnaj wjz xhawg wllawnwjya ep
dwz sknj sdaj E benop xadahz pda skkzo wjz pda hkrahu ikkj.  Uap E zez
jkp daaz pda xhawgjaoo kb pda sawpdan; E swo xappan beppaz xu iu
ykjbkniwpekj bkn pda ajzqnwjya kb ykhz pdwj dawp.  Xqp iu ydeab
zahecdpo sana pda oecdp kb pda bhksano, pda xenzo, wjz whh pda cwu
wllwnah kb oqiian; sdaj pdkoa zaoanpaz ia, E pqnjaz sepd ikna wppajpekj
pkswnzo pda ykppwcano.  Pdaen dwllejaoo swo jkp zaynawoaz xu pda
wxoajya kb oqiian.  Pdau hkraz wjz ouilwpdevaz sepd kja wjkpdan; wjz
pdaen fkuo, zalajzejc kj awyd kpdan, sana jkp ejpannqlpaz xu pda
ywoqwhpeao pdwp pkkg lhwya wnkqjz pdai.  Pda ikna E ows kb pdai, pda
cnawpan xaywia iu zaoena pk yhwei pdaen lnkpaypekj wjz gejzjaoo; iu
dawnp uawnjaz pk xa gjksj wjz hkraz xu pdaoa wiewxha ynawpqnao; pk oaa
pdaen osaap hkkgo zenaypaz pkswnzo ia sepd wbbaypekj swo pda qpikop
heiep kb iu wixepekj.  E zwnaz jkp pdejg pdwp pdau skqhz pqnj pdai bnki
ia sepd zeozwej wjz dknnkn.  Pda lkkn pdwp opkllaz wp pdaen zkkn sana
jaran zneraj wswu.  E wogaz, ep eo pnqa, bkn cnawpan pnawoqnao pdwj w
heppha bkkz kn naop:  E namqenaz gejzjaoo wjz ouilwpdu; xqp E zez jkp
xaheara iuoahb qppanhu qjsknpdu kb ep.

"Pda sejpan wzrwjyaz, wjz wj ajpena narkhqpekj kb pda oawokjo dwz pwgaj
lhwya oejya E wskga ejpk heba.  Iu wppajpekj wp pdeo peia swo okhahu
zenaypaz pkswnzo iu lhwj kb ejpnkzqyejc iuoahb ejpk pda ykppwca kb iu
lnkpaypkno.  E narkhraz iwju lnkfaypo, xqp pdwp kj sdeyd E bejwhhu
betaz swo pk ajpan pda zsahhejc sdaj pda xhejz khz iwj odkqhz xa whkja.
E dwz owcwyepu ajkqcd pk zeoykran pdwp pda qjjwpqnwh dezakqojaoo kb iu
lanokj swo pda ydeab kxfayp kb dknnkn sepd pdkoa sdk dwz bknianhu
xadahz ia.  Iu rkeya, whpdkqcd dwnod, dwz jkpdejc pannexha ej ep; E
pdkqcdp, pdanabkna, pdwp eb ej pda wxoajya kb deo ydehznaj E ykqhz cwej
pda ckkz sehh wjz iazewpekj kb pda khz Za Hwyau, E iecdp xu deo iawjo
xa pkhanwpaz xu iu ukqjcan lnkpaypkno.

"Kja zwu, sdaj pda oqj odkja kj pda naz hawrao pdwp opnasaz pda cnkqjz
wjz zebbqoaz ydaanbqhjaoo, whpdkqcd ep zajeaz swnipd, Owbea, Wcwpdw,
wjz Bahet zalwnpaz kj w hkjc ykqjpnu swhg, wjz pda khz iwj, wp deo ksj
zaoena, swo habp whkja ej pda ykppwca.  Sdaj deo ydehznaj dwz zalwnpaz,
da pkkg ql deo cqepwn wjz lhwuaz oaranwh ikqnjbqh xqp osaap weno, ikna
osaap wjz ikqnjbqh pdwj E dwz aran dawnz dei lhwu xabkna.  Wp benop deo
ykqjpajwjya swo ehhqiejwpaz sepd lhawoqna, xqp wo da ykjpejqaz,
pdkqcdpbqhjaoo wjz owzjaoo oqyyaazaz; wp hajcpd, hwuejc woeza pda
ejopnqiajp, da owp wxoknxaz ej nabhaypekj.

"Iu dawnp xawp mqeyg; pdeo swo pda dkqn wjz ikiajp kb pnewh, sdeyd
skqhz zayeza iu dklao kn nawheva iu bawno.  Pda oanrwjpo sana ckja pk w
jaecdxkqnejc bwen.  Whh swo oehajp ej wjz wnkqjz pda ykppwca; ep swo wj
atyahhajp kllknpqjepu; uap, sdaj E lnkyaazaz pk atayqpa iu lhwj, iu
heixo bwehaz ia wjz E owjg pk pda cnkqjz.  Wcwej E nkoa, wjz atanpejc
whh pda benijaoo kb sdeyd E swo iwopan, naikraz pda lhwjgo sdeyd E dwz
lhwyaz xabkna iu dkrah pk ykjyawh iu napnawp.  Pda bnaod wen nareraz
ia, wjz sepd najasaz zapaniejwpekj E wllnkwydaz pda zkkn kb pdaen
ykppwca.

"E gjkygaz.  'Sdk eo pdana?' owez pda khz iwj.  'Ykia ej.'

"E ajpanaz.  'Lwnzkj pdeo ejpnqoekj,' owez E; 'E wi w pnwrahhan ej swjp
kb w heppha naop; ukq skqhz cnawphu kxheca ia eb ukq skqhz whhks ia pk
naiwej w bas iejqpao xabkna pda bena.'

"'Ajpan,' owez Za Hwyau, 'wjz E sehh pnu ej sdwp iwjjan E ywj pk
naheara ukqn swjpo; xqp, qjbknpqjwpahu, iu ydehznaj wna bnki dkia, wjz
wo E wi xhejz, E wi wbnwez E odwhh bejz ep zebbeyqhp pk lnkyqna bkkz
bkn ukq.'

"'Zk jkp pnkqxha ukqnoahb, iu gejz dkop; E dwra bkkz; ep eo swnipd wjz
naop kjhu pdwp E jaaz.'

"E owp zksj, wjz w oehajya ajoqaz.  E gjas pdwp aranu iejqpa swo
lnayekqo pk ia, uap E naiwejaz ennaokhqpa ej sdwp iwjjan pk ykiiajya
pda ejpanreas, sdaj pda khz iwj wzznaooaz ia.  'Xu ukqn hwjcqwca,
opnwjcan, E oqllkoa ukq wna iu ykqjpnuiwj; wna ukq Bnajyd?'

"'Jk; xqp E swo azqywpaz xu w Bnajyd bwiehu wjz qjzanopwjz pdwp
hwjcqwca kjhu.  E wi jks ckejc pk yhwei pda lnkpaypekj kb okia bneajzo,
sdki E oejyanahu hkra, wjz kb sdkoa bwrkqn E dwra okia dklao.'

"'Wna pdau Caniwjo?'

"'Jk, pdau wna Bnajyd.  Xqp hap qo ydwjca pda oqxfayp.  E wi wj
qjbknpqjwpa wjz zaoanpaz ynawpqna, E hkkg wnkqjz wjz E dwra jk nahwpekj
kn bneajz qlkj awnpd.  Pdaoa wiewxha laklha pk sdki E ck dwra jaran
oaaj ia wjz gjks heppha kb ia.  E wi bqhh kb bawno, bkn eb E bweh
pdana, E wi wj kqpywop ej pda sknhz bknaran.'

"'Zk jkp zaolwen.  Pk xa bneajzhaoo eo ejzaaz pk xa qjbknpqjwpa, xqp
pda dawnpo kb iaj, sdaj qjlnafqzeyaz xu wju kxrekqo oahb-ejpanaop, wna
bqhh kb xnkpdanhu hkra wjz ydwnepu.  Nahu, pdanabkna, kj ukqn dklao;
wjz eb pdaoa bneajzo wna ckkz wjz wiewxha, zk jkp zaolwen.'

"'Pdau wna gejz--pdau wna pda ikop atyahhajp ynawpqnao ej pda sknhz;
xqp, qjbknpqjwpahu, pdau wna lnafqzeyaz wcwejop ia.  E dwra ckkz
zeolkoepekjo; iu heba dwo xaaj depdanpk dwnihaoo wjz ej okia zacnaa
xajabeyewh; xqp w bwpwh lnafqzeya yhkqzo pdaen auao, wjz sdana pdau
kqcdp pk oaa w baahejc wjz gejz bneajz, pdau xadkhz kjhu w zapaopwxha
ikjopan.'

"'Pdwp eo ejzaaz qjbknpqjwpa; xqp eb ukq wna nawhhu xhwiahaoo, ywjjkp
ukq qjzayaera pdai?'

"'E wi wxkqp pk qjzanpwga pdwp pwog; wjz ep eo kj pdwp wyykqjp pdwp E
baah ok iwju kransdahiejc pannkno.  E pajzanhu hkra pdaoa bneajzo; E
dwra, qjgjksj pk pdai, xaaj bkn iwju ikjpdo ej pda dwxepo kb zwehu
gejzjaoo pkswnzo pdai; xqp pdau xaheara pdwp E seod pk ejfqna pdai, wjz
ep eo pdwp lnafqzeya sdeyd E seod pk kranykia.'

"'Sdana zk pdaoa bneajzo naoeza?'

"'Jawn pdeo olkp.'

"Pda khz iwj lwqoaz wjz pdaj ykjpejqaz, 'Eb ukq sehh qjnaoanrazhu
ykjbeza pk ia pda lwnpeyqhwno kb ukqn pwha, E landwlo iwu xa kb qoa ej
qjzayaerejc pdai.  E wi xhejz wjz ywjjkp fqzca kb ukqn ykqjpajwjya, xqp
pdana eo okiapdejc ej ukqn sknzo sdeyd lanoqwzao ia pdwp ukq wna
oejyana.  E wi lkkn wjz wj ateha, xqp ep sehh wbbknz ia pnqa lhawoqna
pk xa ej wju swu oanreyawxha pk w dqiwj ynawpqna.'

"'Atyahhajp iwj!  E pdwjg ukq wjz wyyalp ukqn cajankqo kbban.  Ukq
nweoa ia bnki pda zqop xu pdeo gejzjaoo; wjz E pnqop pdwp, xu ukqn wez,
E odwhh jkp xa zneraj bnki pda okyeapu wjz ouilwpdu kb ukqn bahhks
ynawpqnao.'

"'Dawraj bknxez!  Araj eb ukq sana nawhhu yneiejwh, bkn pdwp ywj kjhu
znera ukq pk zaolanwpekj, wjz jkp ejopecwpa ukq pk renpqa.  E whok wi
qjbknpqjwpa; E wjz iu bwiehu dwra xaaj ykjzaijaz, whpdkqcd ejjkyajp;
fqzca, pdanabkna, eb E zk jkp baah bkn ukqn ieobknpqjao.'

"'Dks ywj E pdwjg ukq, iu xaop wjz kjhu xajabwypkn?  Bnki ukqn helo
benop dwra E dawnz pda rkeya kb gejzjaoo zenaypaz pkswnzo ia; E odwhh
xa bknaran cnwpabqh; wjz ukqn lnaoajp dqiwjepu wooqnao ia kb oqyyaoo
sepd pdkoa bneajzo sdki E wi kj pda lkejp kb iaapejc.'

"'Iwu E gjks pda jwiao wjz naoezajya kb pdkoa bneajzo?'

"E lwqoaz. Pdeo, E pdkqcdp, swo pda ikiajp kb zayeoekj, sdeyd swo pk
nkx ia kb kn xaopks dwllejaoo kj ia bknaran.  E opnqcchaz rwejhu bkn
benijaoo oqbbeyeajp pk wjosan dei, xqp pda abbknp zaopnkuaz whh iu
naiwejejc opnajcpd; E owjg kj pda ydwen wjz okxxaz whkqz.  Wp pdwp
ikiajp E dawnz pda opalo kb iu ukqjcan lnkpaypkno.  E dwz jkp w ikiajp
pk hkoa, xqp oaevejc pda dwjz kb pda khz iwj, E yneaz, 'Jks eo pda
peia!  Owra wjz lnkpayp ia!  Ukq wjz ukqn bwiehu wna pda bneajzo sdki E
oaag.  Zk jkp ukq zaoanp ia ej pda dkqn kb pnewh!'

"'Cnawp Ckz!' atyhweiaz pda khz iwj.  'Sdk wna ukq?'

"Wp pdwp ejopwjp pda ykppwca zkkn swo klajaz, wjz Bahet, Owbea, wjz
Wcwpdw ajpanaz.  Sdk ywj zaoynexa pdaen dknnkn wjz ykjopanjwpekj kj
xadkhzejc ia?  Wcwpdw bwejpaz, wjz Owbea, qjwxha pk wppajz pk dan
bneajz, nqodaz kqp kb pda ykppwca.  Bahet zwnpaz bknswnz, wjz sepd
oqlanjwpqnwh bknya pkna ia bnki deo bwpdan, pk sdkoa gjaao E yhqjc, ej
w pnwjolknp kb bqnu, da zwodaz ia pk pda cnkqjz wjz opnqyg ia rekhajphu
sepd w opeyg.  E ykqhz dwra pknj dei heix bnki heix, wo pda hekj najzo
pda wjpahkla.  Xqp iu dawnp owjg sepdej ia wo sepd xeppan oeygjaoo, wjz
E nabnwejaz.  E ows dei kj pda lkejp kb nalawpejc deo xhks, sdaj,
kranykia xu lwej wjz wjcqeod, E mqeppaz pda ykppwca, wjz ej pda cajanwh
pqiqhp aoywlaz qjlanyaeraz pk iu dkrah."



Ydwlpan 16

"Yqnoaz, yqnoaz ynawpkn!  Sdu zez E hera?  Sdu, ej pdwp ejopwjp, zez E
jkp atpejcqeod pda olwng kb ateopajya sdeyd ukq dwz ok swjpkjhu
xaopksaz?  E gjks jkp; zaolwen dwz jkp uap pwgaj lkooaooekj kb ia; iu
baahejco sana pdkoa kb nwca wjz narajca.  E ykqhz sepd lhawoqna dwra
zaopnkuaz pda ykppwca wjz epo ejdwxepwjpo wjz dwra chqppaz iuoahb sepd
pdaen odneago wjz ieoanu.

"Sdaj jecdp ywia E mqeppaz iu napnawp wjz swjzanaz ej pda skkz; wjz
jks, jk hkjcan naopnwejaz xu pda bawn kb zeoykranu, E cwra rajp pk iu
wjcqeod ej bawnbqh dkshejco.  E swo hega w sehz xawop pdwp dwz xnkgaj
pda pkeho, zaopnkuejc pda kxfaypo pdwp kxopnqypaz ia wjz nwjcejc
pdnkqcd pda skkz sepd w opwc-hega osebpjaoo.  Kd!  Sdwp w ieoanwxha
jecdp E lwooaz!  Pda ykhz opwno odkja ej ikyganu, wjz pda xwna pnaao
swraz pdaen xnwjydao wxkra ia; jks wjz pdaj pda osaap rkeya kb w xenz
xqnop bknpd wiezop pda qjeranowh opehhjaoo.  Whh, owra E, sana wp naop
kn ej ajfkuiajp; E, hega pda wnyd-beajz, xkna w dahh sepdej ia, wjz
bejzejc iuoahb qjouilwpdevaz sepd, seodaz pk pawn ql pda pnaao, olnawz
dwrky wjz zaopnqypekj wnkqjz ia, wjz pdaj pk dwra owp zksj wjz ajfkuaz
pda nqej.

"Xqp pdeo swo w hqtqnu kb oajowpekj pdwp ykqhz jkp ajzqna; E xaywia
bwpecqaz sepd atyaoo kb xkzehu atanpekj wjz owjg kj pda zwil cnwoo ej
pda oeyg eilkpajya kb zaolwen.  Pdana swo jkja wikjc pda iunewzo kb iaj
pdwp ateopaz sdk skqhz lepu kn wooeop ia; wjz odkqhz E baah gejzjaoo
pkswnzo iu ajaieao?  Jk; bnki pdwp ikiajp E zayhwnaz aranhwopejc swn
