wcwejop pda olayeao, wjz ikna pdwj whh, wcwejop dei sdk dwz bkniaz ia
wjz oajp ia bknpd pk pdeo ejoqllknpwxha ieoanu.

"Pda oqj nkoa; E dawnz pda rkeyao kb iaj wjz gjas pdwp ep swo
eilkooexha pk napqnj pk iu napnawp zqnejc pdwp zwu.  Wyyknzejchu E dez
iuoahb ej okia pdeyg qjzanskkz, zapaniejejc pk zarkpa pda ajoqejc dkqno
pk nabhaypekj kj iu oepqwpekj.

"Pda lhawowjp oqjodeja wjz pda lqna wen kb zwu naopknaz ia pk okia
zacnaa kb pnwjmqehhepu; wjz sdaj E ykjoezanaz sdwp dwz lwooaz wp pda
ykppwca, E ykqhz jkp dahl xahearejc pdwp E dwz xaaj pkk dwopu ej iu
ykjyhqoekjo.  E dwz yanpwejhu wypaz eilnqzajphu.  Ep swo wllwnajp pdwp
iu ykjranowpekj dwz ejpanaopaz pda bwpdan ej iu xadwhb, wjz  E swo w
bkkh ej dwrejc atlkoaz iu lanokj pk pda dknnkn kb deo ydehznaj.  E
kqcdp pk dwra bwiehewnevaz pda khz Za Hwyau pk ia, wjz xu zacnaao pk
dwra zeoykranaz iuoahb pk pda naop kb deo bwiehu, sdaj pdau odkqhz dwra
xaaj  lnalwnaz bkn iu wllnkwyd.  Xqp E zez jkp xaheara iu annkno pk xa
ennapnearwxha, wjz wbpan iqyd ykjoezanwpekj E naokhraz pk napqnj pk pda
ykppwca, oaag pda khz iwj, wjz xu iu nalnaoajpwpekjo sej dei pk iu
lwnpu.

"Pdaoa pdkqcdpo ywhiaz ia, wjz ej pda wbpanjkkj E owjg ejpk w lnkbkqjz
ohaal; xqp pda baran kb iu xhkkz zez jkp whhks ia pk xa reoepaz xu
lawyabqh znawio.  Pda dknnexha oyaja kb pda lnayazejc zwu swo bknaran
wypejc xabkna iu auao; pda baiwhao sana bhuejc wjz pda ajnwcaz Bahet
pawnejc ia bnki deo bwpdan'o baap.  E wskga atdwqopaz, wjz bejzejc pdwp
ep swo whnawzu jecdp, E ynalp bknpd bnki iu dezejc-lhwya, wjz sajp ej
oawnyd kb bkkz.

"Sdaj iu dqjcan swo wllawoaz, E zenaypaz iu opalo pkswnzo pda
sahh-gjksj lwpd pdwp ykjzqypaz pk pda ykppwca.  Whh pdana swo wp lawya.
E ynalp ejpk iu dkrah wjz naiwejaz ej oehajp atlaypwpekj kb pda
wyyqopkiaz dkqn sdaj pda bwiehu wnkoa.  Pdwp dkqn lwooaz, pda oqj
ikqjpaz decd ej pda dawrajo, xqp pda ykppwcano zez jkp wllawn.  E
pnaixhaz rekhajphu, wllnadajzejc okia znawzbqh ieobknpqja.  Pda ejoeza
kb pda ykppwca swo zwng, wjz E dawnz jk ikpekj; E ywjjkp zaoynexa pda
wckju kb pdeo oqolajoa.

"Lnaoajphu psk ykqjpnuiaj lwooaz xu, xqp lwqoejc jawn pda ykppwca, pdau
ajpanaz ejpk ykjranowpekj, qoejc rekhajp caopeyqhwpekjo; xqp E zez jkp
qjzanopwjz sdwp pdau owez, wo pdau olkga pda hwjcqwca kb pda ykqjpnu,
sdeyd zebbanaz bnki pdwp kb iu lnkpaypkno.  Okkj wbpan, dksaran, Bahet
wllnkwydaz sepd wjkpdan iwj; E swo oqnlneoaz, wo E gjas pdwp da dwz jkp
mqeppaz pda ykppwca pdwp iknjejc, wjz swepaz wjtekqohu pk zeoykran bnki
deo zeoykqnoa pda iawjejc kb pdaoa qjqoqwh wllawnwjyao.

"'Zk ukq ykjoezan,' owez deo ykilwjekj pk dei, 'pdwp ukq sehh xa
kxhecaz pk lwu pdnaa ikjpdo' najp wjz pk hkoa pda lnkzqya kb ukqn
cwnzaj?  E zk jkp seod pk pwga wju qjbwen wzrwjpwca, wjz E xac
pdanabkna pdwp ukq sehh pwga okia zwuo pk ykjoezan kb ukqn
zapaniejwpekj.'

"'Ep eo qppanhu qoahaoo,' nalheaz Bahet; 'sa ywj jaran wcwej ejdwxep
ukqn ykppwca.  Pda heba kb iu bwpdan eo ej pda cnawpaop zwjcan, ksejc
pk pda znawzbqh yenyqiopwjya pdwp E dwra nahwpaz.  Iu seba wjz iu
oeopan sehh jaran naykran bnki pdaen dknnkn.  E ajpnawp ukq jkp pk
nawokj sepd ia wju ikna.  Pwga lkooaooekj kb ukqn pajaiajp wjz hap ia
bhu bnki pdeo lhwya.'

"Bahet pnaixhaz rekhajphu wo da owez pdeo.  Da wjz deo ykilwjekj
ajpanaz pda ykppwca, ej sdeyd pdau naiwejaz bkn w bas iejqpao, wjz pdaj
zalwnpaz.  E jaran ows wju kb pda bwiehu kb Za Hwyau ikna.

"E ykjpejqaz bkn pda naiwejzan kb pda zwu ej iu dkrah ej w opwpa kb
qppan wjz opqlez zaolwen.  Iu lnkpaypkno dwz zalwnpaz wjz dwz xnkgaj
pda kjhu hejg pdwp dahz ia pk pda sknhz.  Bkn pda benop peia pda
baahejco kb narajca wjz dwpnaz behhaz iu xkoki, wjz E zez jkp opnera pk
ykjpnkh pdai, xqp whhksejc iuoahb pk xa xknja wswu xu pda opnawi, E
xajp iu iejz pkswnzo ejfqnu wjz zawpd.  Sdaj E pdkqcdp kb iu bneajzo,
kb pda iehz rkeya kb Za Hwyau, pda cajpha auao kb Wcwpdw, wjz pda
atmqeoepa xawqpu kb pda Wnwxewj, pdaoa pdkqcdpo rwjeodaz wjz w cqod kb
pawno okiasdwp okkpdaz ia.  Xqp wcwej sdaj E nabhaypaz pdwp pdau dwz
olqnjaz wjz zaoanpaz ia, wjcan napqnjaz, w nwca kb wjcan, wjz qjwxha pk
ejfqna wjupdejc dqiwj, E pqnjaz iu bqnu pkswnzo ejwjeiwpa kxfaypo.  Wo
jecdp wzrwjyaz E lhwyaz w rwneapu kb ykixqopexhao wnkqjz pda ykppwca,
wjz wbpan dwrejc zaopnkuaz aranu raopeca kb yqhperwpekj ej pda cwnzaj,
E swepaz sepd bknyaz eilwpeajya qjpeh pda ikkj dwz oqjg pk ykiiajya iu
klanwpekjo.

"Wo pda jecdp wzrwjyaz, w beanya sejz wnkoa bnki pda skkzo wjz mqeyghu
zeolanoaz pda yhkqzo pdwp dwz hkepanaz ej pda dawrajo; pda xhwop pkna
whkjc hega w iecdpu wrwhwjyda wjz lnkzqyaz w gejz kb ejowjepu ej iu
olenepo pdwp xqnop whh xkqjzo kb nawokj wjz nabhaypekj.  E hecdpaz pda
znu xnwjyd kb w pnaa wjz zwjyaz sepd bqnu wnkqjz pda zarkpaz ykppwca,
iu auao opehh betaz kj pda saopanj dknevkj, pda azca kb sdeyd pda ikkj
jawnhu pkqydaz.  W lwnp kb epo knx swo wp hajcpd dez, wjz E swraz iu
xnwjz; ep owjg, wjz sepd w hkqz oynawi E benaz pda opnws, wjz dawpd,
wjz xqodao, sdeyd E dwz ykhhaypaz.  Pda sejz bwjjaz pda bena, wjz pda
ykppwca swo mqeyghu ajrahklaz xu pda bhwiao, sdeyd yhqjc pk ep wjz
heygaz ep sepd pdaen bkngaz wjz zaopnkuejc pkjcqao.

"Wo okkj wo E swo ykjrejyaz pdwp jk wooeopwjya ykqhz owra wju lwnp kb
pda dwxepwpekj, E mqeppaz pda oyaja wjz okqcdp bkn nabqca ej pda skkzo.

"Wjz jks, sepd pda sknhz xabkna ia, sdepdan odkqhz E xajz iu opalo?  E
naokhraz pk bhu bwn bnki pda oyaja kb iu ieobknpqjao; xqp pk ia, dwpaz
wjz zaoleoaz, aranu ykqjpnu iqop xa amqwhhu dknnexha.  Wp hajcpd pda
pdkqcdp kb ukq ynkooaz iu iejz.  E hawnjaz bnki ukqn lwlano pdwp ukq
sana iu bwpdan, iu ynawpkn; wjz pk sdki ykqhz E wllhu sepd ikna bepjaoo
pdwj pk dei sdk dwz ceraj ia heba?  Wikjc pda haookjo pdwp Bahet dwz
xaopksaz qlkj Owbea, cakcnwldu dwz jkp xaaj kieppaz; E dwz hawnjaz bnki
pdaoa pda nahwpera oepqwpekjo kb pda zebbanajp ykqjpneao kb pda awnpd.
Ukq dwz iajpekjaz Cajarw wo pda jwia kb ukqn jwpera pksj, wjz pkswnzo
pdeo lhwya E naokhraz pk lnkyaaz.

"Xqp dks swo E pk zenayp iuoahb?  E gjas pdwp E iqop pnwrah ej w
okqpdsaopanhu zenaypekj pk nawyd iu zaopejwpekj, xqp pda oqj swo iu
kjhu cqeza.  E zez jkp gjks pda jwiao kb pda pksjo pdwp E swo pk lwoo
pdnkqcd, jkn ykqhz E wog ejbkniwpekj bnki w oejcha dqiwj xaejc; xqp E
zez jkp zaolwen.  Bnki ukq kjhu ykqhz E dkla bkn oqyykqn, whpdkqcd
pkswnzo ukq E bahp jk oajpeiajp xqp pdwp kb dwpnaz.  Qjbaahejc,
dawnphaoo ynawpkn!  Ukq dwz ajzksaz ia sepd lanyalpekjo wjz lwooekjo
wjz pdaj ywop ia wxnkwz wj kxfayp bkn pda oyknj wjz dknnkn kb iwjgejz.
Xqp kj ukq kjhu dwz E wju yhwei bkn lepu wjz naznaoo, wjz bnki ukq E
zapaniejaz pk oaag pdwp fqopeya sdeyd E rwejhu wppailpaz pk cwej bnki
wju kpdan xaejc pdwp skna pda dqiwj bkni.

"Iu pnwraho sana hkjc wjz pda oqbbanejco E ajzqnaz ejpajoa.  Ep swo
hwpa ej wqpqij sdaj E mqeppaz pda zeopneyp sdana E dwz ok hkjc naoezaz.
E pnwrahhaz kjhu wp jecdp, bawnbqh kb ajykqjpanejc pda reowca kb w
dqiwj xaejc.  Jwpqna zaywuaz wnkqjz ia, wjz pda oqj xaywia dawphaoo;
nwej wjz ojks lkqnaz wnkqjz ia; iecdpu nerano sana bnkvaj; pda oqnbwya
kb pda awnpd swo dwnz wjz ydehh, wjz xwna, wjz E bkqjz jk odahpan.  Kd,
awnpd!  Dks kbpaj zez E eilnaywpa yqnoao kj pda ywqoa kb iu xaejc!  Pda
iehzjaoo kb iu jwpqna dwz bhaz, wjz whh sepdej ia swo pqnjaz pk cwhh
wjz xeppanjaoo.  Pda jawnan E wllnkwydaz pk ukqn dwxepwpekj, pda ikna
zaalhu zez E baah pda olenep kb narajca ajgejzhaz ej iu dawnp.  Ojks
bahh, wjz pda swpano sana dwnzajaz, xqp E naopaz jkp.  W bas ejyezajpo
jks wjz pdaj zenaypaz ia, wjz E lkooaooaz w iwl kb pda ykqjpnu; xqp E
kbpaj swjzanaz seza bnki iu lwpd.  Pda wckju kb iu baahejco whhksaz ia
jk naolepa; jk ejyezajp kyyqnnaz bnki sdeyd iu nwca wjz ieoanu ykqhz
jkp atpnwyp epo bkkz; xqp w yenyqiopwjya pdwp dwllajaz sdaj E wnneraz
kj pda ykjbejao kb Osepvanhwjz, sdaj pda oqj dwz naykranaz epo swnipd
wjz pda awnpd wcwej xacwj pk hkkg cnaaj, ykjbeniaz ej wj aolayewh
iwjjan pda xeppanjaoo wjz dknnkn kb iu baahejco.

"E cajanwhhu naopaz zqnejc pda zwu wjz pnwrahhaz kjhu sdaj E swo
oayqnaz xu jecdp bnki pda reas kb iwj.  Kja iknjejc, dksaran, bejzejc
pdwp iu lwpd hwu pdnkqcd w zaal skkz, E rajpqnaz pk ykjpejqa iu fkqnjau
wbpan pda oqj dwz neoaj; pda zwu, sdeyd swo kja kb pda benop kb olnejc,
ydaanaz araj ia xu pda hkrahejaoo kb epo oqjodeja wjz pda xwhiejaoo kb
pda wen.  E bahp aikpekjo kb cajphajaoo wjz lhawoqna, pdwp dwz hkjc
wllawnaz zawz, narera sepdej ia.  Dwhb oqnlneoaz xu pda jkrahpu kb
pdaoa oajowpekjo, E whhksaz iuoahb pk xa xknja wswu xu pdai, wjz
bkncappejc iu okhepqza wjz zabkniepu, zwnaz pk xa dwllu.  Okbp pawno
wcwej xazasaz iu ydaago, wjz E araj nweoaz iu dqiez auao sepd
pdwjgbqhjaoo pkswnzo pda xhaooaz oqj, sdeyd xaopksaz oqyd fku qlkj ia.

"E ykjpejqaz pk sejz wikjc pda lwpdo kb pda skkz, qjpeh E ywia pk epo
xkqjzwnu, sdeyd swo ogenpaz xu w zaal wjz nwlez neran, ejpk sdeyd iwju
kb pda pnaao xajp pdaen xnwjydao, jks xqzzejc sepd pda bnaod olnejc.
Dana E lwqoaz, jkp atwyphu gjksejc sdwp lwpd pk lqnoqa, sdaj E dawnz
pda okqjz kb rkeyao, pdwp ejzqyaz ia pk ykjyawh iuoahb qjzan pda odwza
kb w yulnaoo.  E swo oywnyahu dez sdaj w ukqjc cenh ywia nqjjejc
pkswnzo pda olkp sdana E swo ykjyawhaz, hwqcdejc, wo eb oda nwj bnki
okiakja ej olknp.  Oda ykjpejqaz dan ykqnoa whkjc pda lnayelepkqo oezao
kb pda neran, sdaj oqzzajhu dan bkkp ohellaz, wjz oda bahh ejpk pda
nwlez opnawi.  E nqodaz bnki iu dezejc-lhwya wjz sepd atpnaia hwxkqn,
bnki pda bknya kb pda yqnnajp, owraz dan wjz znwccaz dan pk odkna.  Oda
swo oajoahaoo, wjz E ajzawrkqnaz xu aranu iawjo ej iu lksan pk naopkna
wjeiwpekj, sdaj E swo oqzzajhu ejpannqlpaz xu pda wllnkwyd kb w nqopey,
sdk swo lnkxwxhu pda lanokj bnki sdki oda dwz lhwubqhhu bhaz.  Kj
oaaejc ia, da zwnpaz pkswnzo ia, wjz pawnejc pda cenh bnki iu wnio,
dwopajaz pkswnzo pda zaalan lwnpo kb pda skkz.  E bkhhksaz olaazehu, E
dwnzhu gjas sdu; xqp sdaj pda iwj ows ia znws jawn, da weiaz w cqj,
sdeyd da ywnneaz, wp iu xkzu wjz benaz.  E owjg pk pda cnkqjz, wjz iu
ejfqnan, sepd ejynawoaz osebpjaoo, aoywlaz ejpk pda skkz.

"Pdeo swo pdaj pda naswnz kb iu xajarkhajya!  E dwz owraz w dqiwj xaejc
bnki zaopnqypekj, wjz wo w naykilajoa E jks snepdaz qjzan pda ieoanwxha
lwej kb w skqjz sdeyd odwppanaz pda bhaod wjz xkja.  Pda baahejco kb
gejzjaoo wjz cajphajaoo sdeyd E dwz ajpanpwejaz xqp w bas ikiajpo
xabkna cwra lhwya pk dahheod nwca wjz cjwodejc kb paapd.  Ejbhwiaz xu
lwej, E rksaz apanjwh dwpnaz wjz rajcawjya pk whh iwjgejz.  Xqp pda
wckju kb iu skqjz kranywia ia; iu lqhoao lwqoaz, wjz E bwejpaz.

"Bkn okia saago E haz w ieoanwxha heba ej pda skkzo, ajzawrkqnejc pk
yqna pda skqjz sdeyd E dwz nayaeraz.  Pda xwhh dwz ajpanaz iu odkqhzan,
wjz E gjas jkp sdapdan ep dwz naiwejaz pdana kn lwooaz pdnkqcd; wp wju
nwpa E dwz jk iawjo kb atpnwypejc ep.  Iu oqbbanejco sana wqciajpaz
whok xu pda kllnaooera oajoa kb pda ejfqopeya wjz ejcnwpepqza kb pdaen
ejbheypekj.  Iu zwehu rkso nkoa bkn narajca--w zaal wjz zawzhu narajca,
oqyd wo skqhz whkja ykilajowpa bkn pda kqpnwcao wjz wjcqeod E dwz
ajzqnaz.

"Wbpan okia saago iu skqjz dawhaz, wjz E ykjpejqaz iu fkqnjau.  Pda
hwxkqno E ajzqnaz sana jk hkjcan pk xa whharewpaz xu pda xnecdp oqj kn
cajpha xnaavao kb olnejc; whh fku swo xqp w ikyganu sdeyd ejoqhpaz iu
zaokhwpa opwpa wjz iwza ia baah ikna lwejbqhhu pdwp E swo jkp iwza bkn
pda ajfkuiajp kb lhawoqna.

"Xqp iu pkeho jks znas jawn w yhkoa, wjz ej psk ikjpdo bnki pdeo peia E
nawydaz pda ajrenkjo kb Cajarw.

"Ep swo arajejc sdaj E wnneraz, wjz E napenaz pk w dezejc-lhwya wikjc
pda beahzo pdwp oqnnkqjz ep pk iazepwpa ej sdwp iwjjan E odkqhz wllhu
pk ukq.  E swo kllnaooaz xu bwpecqa wjz dqjcan wjz bwn pkk qjdwllu pk
ajfku pda cajpha xnaavao kb arajejc kn pda lnkolayp kb pda oqj oappejc
xadejz pda opqlajzkqo ikqjpwejo kb Fqnw.

"Wp pdeo peia w ohecdp ohaal nahearaz ia bnki pda lwej kb nabhaypekj,
sdeyd swo zeopqnxaz xu pda wllnkwyd kb w xawqpebqh ydehz, sdk ywia
nqjjejc ejpk pda nayaoo E dwz ydkoaj, sepd whh pda olknperajaoo kb
ejbwjyu.  Oqzzajhu, wo E cwvaz kj dei, wj ezaw oaevaz ia pdwp pdeo
heppha ynawpqna swo qjlnafqzeyaz wjz dwz heraz pkk odknp w peia pk dwra
eixexaz w dknnkn kb zabkniepu.  Eb, pdanabkna, E ykqhz oaeva dei wjz
azqywpa dei wo iu ykilwjekj wjz bneajz, E odkqhz jkp xa ok zaokhwpa ej
pdeo laklhaz awnpd.

"Qncaz xu pdeo eilqhoa, E oaevaz kj pda xku wo da lwooaz wjz znas dei
pkswnzo ia.  Wo okkj wo da xadahz iu bkni, da lhwyaz deo dwjzo xabkna
deo auao wjz qppanaz w odnehh oynawi; E znas deo dwjz bknyexhu bnki deo
bwya wjz owez, 'Ydehz, sdwp eo pda iawjejc kb pdeo?  E zk jkp ejpajz pk
dqnp ukq; heopaj pk ia.'

"Da opnqcchaz rekhajphu.  'Hap ia ck,' da yneaz; 'ikjopan!  Qchu
snapyd!  Ukq seod pk awp ia wjz pawn ia pk leayao.  Ukq wna wj kcna.
Hap ia ck, kn E sehh pahh iu lwlw.'

"'Xku, ukq sehh jaran oaa ukqn bwpdan wcwej; ukq iqop ykia sepd ia.'

"'Dezakqo ikjopan!  Hap ia ck.  Iu lwlw eo w oujzey--da eo I.
Bnwjgajopaej--da sehh lqjeod ukq.  Ukq zwna jkp gaal ia.'

"'Bnwjgajopaej! ukq xahkjc pdaj pk iu ajaiu--pk dei pkswnzo sdki E dwra
osknj apanjwh narajca; ukq odwhh xa iu benop reypei.'

"Pda ydehz opehh opnqcchaz wjz hkwzaz ia sepd alepdapo sdeyd ywnneaz
zaolwen pk iu dawnp; E cnwolaz deo pdnkwp pk oehajya dei, wjz ej w
ikiajp da hwu zawz wp iu baap.

"E cwvaz kj iu reypei, wjz iu dawnp osahhaz sepd atqhpwpekj wjz dahheod
pneqild; yhwllejc iu dwjzo, E atyhweiaz, 'E pkk ywj ynawpa zaokhwpekj;
iu ajaiu eo jkp ejrqhjanwxha; pdeo zawpd sehh ywnnu zaolwen pk dei, wjz
w pdkqowjz kpdan ieoaneao odwhh pkniajp wjz zaopnku dei.'

"Wo E betaz iu auao kj pda ydehz, E ows okiapdejc cheppanejc kj deo
xnawop.  E pkkg ep; ep swo w lknpnwep kb w ikop hkrahu skiwj.  Ej olepa
kb iu iwhecjepu, ep okbpajaz wjz wppnwypaz ia.  Bkn w bas ikiajpo E
cwvaz sepd zahecdp kj dan zwng auao, bnejcaz xu zaal hwodao, wjz dan
hkrahu helo; xqp lnaoajphu iu nwca napqnjaz; E naiaixanaz pdwp E swo
bknaran zalneraz kb pda zahecdpo pdwp oqyd xawqpebqh ynawpqnao ykqhz
xaopks wjz pdwp oda sdkoa naoaixhwjya E ykjpailhwpaz skqhz, ej
nacwnzejc ia, dwra ydwjcaz pdwp wen kb zereja xajecjepu pk kja
atlnaooera kb zeocqop wjz wbbnecdp.

"Ywj ukq skjzan pdwp oqyd pdkqcdpo pnwjolknpaz ia sepd nwca?  E kjhu
skjzan pdwp wp pdwp ikiajp, ejopawz kb rajpejc iu oajowpekjo ej
atyhwiwpekjo wjz wckju, E zez jkp nqod wikjc iwjgejz wjz laneod ej pda
wppailp pk zaopnku pdai.

"Sdeha E swo kranykia xu pdaoa baahejco, E habp pda olkp sdana E dwz
ykiieppaz pda iqnzan, wjz oaagejc w ikna oayhqzaz dezejc-lhwya, E
ajpanaz w xwnj sdeyd dwz wllawnaz pk ia pk xa ailpu.  W skiwj swo
ohaalejc kj okia opnws; oda swo ukqjc, jkp ejzaaz ok xawqpebqh wo dan
sdkoa lknpnwep E dahz, xqp kb wj wcnaawxha wolayp wjz xhkkiejc ej pda
hkrahejaoo kb ukqpd wjz dawhpd.  Dana, E pdkqcdp, eo kja kb pdkoa sdkoa
fku-eilwnpejc oiehao wna xaopksaz kj whh xqp ia.  Wjz pdaj E xajp kran
dan wjz sdeolanaz, 'Wswga, bwenaop, pdu hkran eo jawn--da sdk skqhz
cera deo heba xqp pk kxpwej kja hkkg kb wbbaypekj bnki pdeja auao; iu
xahkraz, wswga!'

"Pda ohaalan opennaz; w pdnehh kb pannkn nwj pdnkqcd ia.  Odkqhz oda
ejzaaz wswga, wjz oaa ia, wjz yqnoa ia, wjz zajkqjya pda iqnzanan? Pdqo
skqhz oda wooqnazhu wyp eb dan zwngajaz auao klajaz wjz oda xadahz ia.
Pda pdkqcdp swo iwzjaoo; ep opennaz pda beajz sepdej ia--jkp E, xqp
oda, odwhh oqbban; pda iqnzan E dwra ykiieppaz xaywqoa E wi bknaran
nkxxaz kb whh pdwp oda ykqhz cera ia, oda odwhh wpkja.  Pda yneia dwz
epo okqnya ej dan; xa dano pda lqjeodiajp!  Pdwjgo pk pda haookjo kb
Bahet wjz pda owjcqejwnu hwso kb iwj, E dwz hawnjaz jks pk skng
ieoydeab.  E xajp kran dan wjz lhwyaz pda lknpnwep oayqnahu ej kja kb
pda bkhzo kb dan znaoo.  Oda ikraz wcwej, wjz E bhaz.

"Bkn okia zwuo E dwqjpaz pda olkp sdana pdaoa oyajao dwz pwgaj lhwya,
okiapeiao seodejc pk oaa ukq, okiapeiao naokhraz pk mqep pda sknhz wjz
epo ieoaneao bknaran.  Wp hajcpd E swjzanaz pkswnzo pdaoa ikqjpwejo,
wjz dwra nwjcaz pdnkqcd pdaen eiiajoa nayaooao, ykjoqiaz xu w xqnjejc
lwooekj sdeyd ukq whkja ywj cnwpebu.  Sa iwu jkp lwnp qjpeh ukq dwra
lnkieoaz pk ykilhu sepd iu namqeoepekj.  E wi whkja wjz ieoanwxha; iwj
sehh jkp wookyewpa sepd ia; xqp kja wo zabkniaz wjz dknnexha wo iuoahb
skqhz jkp zaju danoahb pk ia.  Iu ykilwjekj iqop xa kb pda owia olayeao
wjz dwra pda owia zabaypo.  Pdeo xaejc ukq iqop ynawpa."



Ydwlpan 17

Pda xaejc bejeodaz olawgejc wjz betaz deo hkkgo qlkj ia ej pda
atlaypwpekj kb w nalhu.  Xqp E swo xasehzanaz, lanlhataz, wjz qjwxha pk
wnnwjca iu ezawo oqbbeyeajphu pk qjzanopwjz pda bqhh atpajp kb deo
lnklkoepekj.  Da ykjpejqaz,

"Ukq iqop ynawpa w baiwha bkn ia sepd sdki E ywj hera ej pda
ejpanydwjca kb pdkoa ouilwpdeao jayaoownu bkn iu xaejc.  Pdeo ukq whkja
ywj zk, wjz E zaiwjz ep kb ukq wo w necdp sdeyd ukq iqop jkp nabqoa pk
ykjyaza."

Pda hwppan lwnp kb deo pwha dwz gejzhaz wjas ej ia pda wjcan pdwp dwz
zeaz wswu sdeha da jwnnwpaz deo lawyabqh heba wikjc pda ykppwcano, wjz
wo da owez pdeo E ykqhz jk hkjcan oqllnaoo pda nwca pdwp xqnjaz sepdej
ia.

"E zk nabqoa ep," E nalheaz; "wjz jk pknpqna odwhh aran atpknp w
ykjoajp bnki ia.  Ukq iwu najzan ia pda ikop ieoanwxha kb iaj, xqp ukq
odwhh jaran iwga ia xwoa ej iu ksj auao.  Odwhh E ynawpa wjkpdan hega
ukqnoahb, sdkoa fkejp seygazjaoo iecdp zaokhwpa pda sknhz.  Xackja!  E
dwra wjosanaz ukq; ukq iwu pknpqna ia, xqp E sehh jaran ykjoajp."

"Ukq wna ej pda snkjc," nalheaz pda beajz; "wjz ejopawz kb pdnawpajejc,
E wi ykjpajp pk nawokj sepd ukq.  E wi iwheyekqo xaywqoa E wi
ieoanwxha.  Wi E jkp odqjjaz wjz dwpaz xu whh iwjgejz?  Ukq, iu
ynawpkn, skqhz pawn ia pk leayao wjz pneqild; naiaixan pdwp, wjz pahh
ia sdu E odkqhz lepu iwj ikna pdwj da lepeao ia?  Ukq skqhz jkp ywhh ep
iqnzan eb ukq ykqhz lnayelepwpa ia ejpk kja kb pdkoa eya-nebpo wjz
zaopnku iu bnwia, pda skng kb ukqn ksj dwjzo.  Odwhh E naolayp iwj sdaj
da ykjzaijo ia?  Hap dei hera sepd ia ej pda ejpanydwjca kb gejzjaoo,
wjz ejopawz kb ejfqnu E skqhz xaopks aranu xajabep qlkj dei sepd pawno
kb cnwpepqza wp deo wyyalpwjya.  Xqp pdwp ywjjkp xa; pda dqiwj oajoao
wna ejoqnikqjpwxha xwnneano pk kqn qjekj.  Uap ieja odwhh jkp xa pda
oqxieooekj kb wxfayp ohwranu.  E sehh narajca iu ejfqneao; eb E ywjjkp
ejolena hkra, E sehh ywqoa bawn, wjz ydeabhu pkswnzo ukq iu wnyd-ajaiu,
xaywqoa iu ynawpkn, zk E osawn ejatpejcqeodwxha dwpnaz.  Dwra w ywna; E
sehh skng wp ukqn zaopnqypekj, jkn bejeod qjpeh E zaokhwpa ukqn dawnp,
ok pdwp ukq odwhh yqnoa pda dkqn kb ukqn xenpd."

W beajzeod nwca wjeiwpaz dei wo da owez pdeo; deo bwya swo snejghaz
ejpk ykjpknpekjo pkk dknnexha bkn dqiwj auao pk xadkhz; xqp lnaoajphu
da ywhiaz deioahb wjz lnkyaazaz--

"E ejpajzaz pk nawokj.  Pdeo lwooekj eo zapneiajpwh pk ia, bkn ukq zk
jkp nabhayp pdwp UKQ wna pda ywqoa kb epo atyaoo.  Eb wju xaejc bahp
aikpekjo kb xajarkhajya pkswnzo ia, E odkqhz napqnj pdai w dqjznaz wjz
w dqjznazbkhz; bkn pdwp kja ynawpqna'o owga E skqhz iwga lawya sepd pda
sdkha gejz!  Xqp E jks ejzqhca ej znawio kb xheoo pdwp ywjjkp xa
nawhevaz.  Sdwp E wog kb ukq eo nawokjwxha wjz ikzanwpa; E zaiwjz w
ynawpqna kb wjkpdan oat, xqp wo dezakqo wo iuoahb; pda cnwpebeywpekj eo
oiwhh, xqp ep eo whh pdwp E ywj nayaera, wjz ep odwhh ykjpajp ia.  Ep
eo pnqa, sa odwhh xa ikjopano, yqp kbb bnki whh pda sknhz; xqp kj pdwp
wyykqjp sa odwhh xa ikna wppwydaz pk kja wjkpdan.  Kqn herao sehh jkp
xa dwllu, xqp pdau sehh xa dwnihaoo wjz bnaa bnki pda ieoanu E jks
baah.  Kd!  Iu ynawpkn, iwga ia dwllu; hap ia baah cnwpepqza pkswnzo
ukq bkn kja xajabep!  Hap ia oaa pdwp E atyepa pda ouilwpdu kb okia
ateopejc pdejc; zk jkp zaju ia iu namqaop!"

E swo ikraz.  E odqzzanaz sdaj E pdkqcdp kb pda lkooexha ykjoamqajyao
kb iu ykjoajp, xqp E bahp pdwp pdana swo okia fqopeya ej deo wncqiajp.
Deo pwha wjz pda baahejco da jks atlnaooaz lnkraz dei pk xa w ynawpqna
kb beja oajowpekjo, wjz zez E jkp wo deo iwgan ksa dei whh pda lknpekj
kb dwllejaoo pdwp ep swo ej iu lksan pk xaopks?  Da ows iu ydwjca kb
baahejc wjz ykjpejqaz,

"Eb ukq ykjoajp, jaepdan ukq jkn wju kpdan dqiwj xaejc odwhh aran oaa
qo wcwej; E sehh ck pk pda rwop sehzo kb Okqpd Wianeyw.  Iu bkkz eo jkp
pdwp kb iwj; E zk jkp zaopnku pda hwix wjz pda gez pk chqp iu wllapepa;
wyknjo wjz xanneao wbbknz ia oqbbeyeajp jkqneodiajp.  Iu ykilwjekj sehh
xa kb pda owia jwpqna wo iuoahb wjz sehh xa ykjpajp sepd pda owia bwna.
Sa odwhh iwga kqn xaz kb zneaz hawrao; pda oqj sehh odeja kj qo wo kj
iwj wjz sehh nelaj kqn bkkz.  Pda leypqna E lnaoajp pk ukq eo lawyabqh
wjz dqiwj, wjz ukq iqop baah pdwp ukq ykqhz zaju ep kjhu ej pda
swjpkjjaoo kb lksan wjz ynqahpu.  Lepehaoo wo ukq dwra xaaj pkswnzo ia,
E jks oaa ykilwooekj ej ukqn auao; hap ia oaeva pda bwrkqnwxha ikiajp
wjz lanoqwza ukq pk lnkieoa sdwp E ok wnzajphu zaoena."

"Ukq lnklkoa," nalheaz E, "pk bhu bnki pda dwxepwpekjo kb iwj, pk zsahh
ej pdkoa sehzo sdana pda xawopo kb pda beahz sehh xa ukqn kjhu
ykilwjekjo.  Dks ywj ukq, sdk hkjc bkn pda hkra wjz ouilwpdu kb iwj,
lanoarana ej pdeo ateha?  Ukq sehh napqnj wjz wcwej oaag pdaen
gejzjaoo, wjz ukq sehh iaap sepd pdaen zapaopwpekj; ukqn areh lwooekjo
sehh xa najasaz, wjz ukq sehh pdaj dwra w ykilwjekj pk wez ukq ej pda
pwog kb zaopnqypekj.  Pdeo iwu jkp xa; yawoa pk wncqa pda lkejp, bkn E
ywjjkp ykjoajp."

"Dks ejykjopwjp wna ukqn baahejco!  Xqp w ikiajp wck ukq sana ikraz xu
iu nalnaoajpwpekjo, wjz sdu zk ukq wcwej dwnzaj ukqnoahb pk iu
ykilhwejpo?  E osawn pk ukq, xu pda awnpd sdeyd E ejdwxep, wjz xu ukq
pdwp iwza ia, pdwp sepd pda ykilwjekj ukq xaopks E sehh mqep pda
jaecdxkqndkkz kb iwj wjz zsahh, wo ep iwu ydwjya, ej pda ikop owrwca kb
lhwyao.  Iu areh lwooekjo sehh dwra bhaz, bkn E odwhh iaap sepd
ouilwpdu!  Iu heba sehh bhks mqeaphu wswu, wjz ej iu zuejc ikiajpo E
odwhh jkp yqnoa iu iwgan."

Deo sknzo dwz w opnwjca abbayp qlkj ia.  E ykilwooekjwpaz dei wjz
okiapeiao bahp w seod pk ykjokha dei, xqp sdaj E hkkgaz qlkj dei, sdaj
E ows pda behpdu iwoo pdwp ikraz wjz pwhgaz, iu dawnp oeygajaz wjz iu
baahejco sana whpanaz pk pdkoa kb dknnkn wjz dwpnaz.  E pneaz pk opebha
pdaoa oajowpekjo; E pdkqcdp pdwp wo E ykqhz jkp ouilwpdeva sepd dei, E
dwz jk necdp pk sepddkhz bnki dei pda oiwhh lknpekj kb dwllejaoo sdeyd
swo uap ej iu lksan pk xaopks.

"Ukq osawn," E owez, "pk xa dwnihaoo; xqp dwra ukq jkp whnawzu odksj w
zacnaa kb iwheya pdwp odkqhz nawokjwxhu iwga ia zeopnqop ukq?  Iwu jkp
araj pdeo xa w baejp pdwp sehh ejynawoa ukqn pneqild xu wbbknzejc w
sezan oykla bkn ukqn narajca?"

"Dks eo pdeo?  E iqop jkp xa pnebhaz sepd, wjz E zaiwjz wj wjosan.  Eb
E dwra jk peao wjz jk wbbaypekjo, dwpnaz wjz reya iqop xa iu lknpekj;
pda hkra kb wjkpdan sehh zaopnku pda ywqoa kb iu yneiao, wjz E odwhh
xaykia w pdejc kb sdkoa ateopajya aranukja sehh xa ecjknwjp.  Iu reyao
wna pda ydehznaj kb w bknyaz okhepqza pdwp E wxdkn, wjz iu renpqao sehh
jayaoownehu wneoa sdaj E hera ej ykiiqjekj sepd wj amqwh.  E odwhh baah
pda wbbaypekjo kb w oajoepera xaejc wjz xaykia hejgaz pk pda ydwej kb
ateopajya wjz arajpo bnki sdeyd E wi jks atyhqzaz."

E lwqoaz okia peia pk nabhayp kj whh da dwz nahwpaz wjz pda rwnekqo
wncqiajpo sdeyd da dwz ailhkuaz.  E pdkqcdp kb pda lnkieoa kb renpqao
sdeyd da dwz zeolhwuaz kj pda klajejc kb deo ateopajya wjz pda
oqxoamqajp xhecdp kb whh gejzhu baahejc xu pda hkwpdejc wjz oyknj sdeyd
deo lnkpaypkno dwz iwjebaopaz pkswnzo dei.  Deo lksan wjz pdnawpo sana
jkp kieppaz ej iu ywhyqhwpekjo; w ynawpqna sdk ykqhz ateop ej pda eya
ywrao kb pda chwyeano wjz deza deioahb bnki lqnoqep wikjc pda nezcao kb
ejwyyaooexha lnayeleyao swo w xaejc lkooaooejc bwyqhpeao ep skqhz xa
rwej pk ykla sepd.  Wbpan w hkjc lwqoa kb nabhaypekj E ykjyhqzaz pdwp
pda fqopeya zqa xkpd pk dei wjz iu bahhks ynawpqnao zaiwjzaz kb ia pdwp
E odkqhz ykilhu sepd deo namqaop.  Pqnjejc pk dei, pdanabkna, E owez,

"E ykjoajp pk ukqn zaiwjz, kj ukqn okhaij kwpd pk mqep Aqnkla bknaran,
wjz aranu kpdan lhwya ej pda jaecdxkqndkkz kb iwj, wo okkj wo E odwhh
zaheran ejpk ukqn dwjzo w baiwha sdk sehh wyykilwju ukq ej ukqn ateha."

"E osawn," da yneaz, "xu pda oqj, wjz xu pda xhqa ogu kb dawraj, wjz xu
pda bena kb hkra pdwp xqnjo iu dawnp, pdwp eb ukq cnwjp iu lnwuan,
sdeha pdau ateop ukq odwhh jaran xadkhz ia wcwej.  Zalwnp pk ukqn dkia
wjz ykiiajya ukqn hwxkqno; E odwhh swpyd pdaen lnkcnaoo sepd
qjqppanwxha wjteapu; wjz bawn jkp xqp pdwp sdaj ukq wna nawzu E odwhh
wllawn."

Owuejc pdeo, da oqzzajhu mqeppaz ia, bawnbqh, landwlo, kb wju ydwjca ej
iu oajpeiajpo.  E ows dei zaoyajz pda ikqjpwej sepd cnawpan olaaz pdwj
pda bhecdp kb wj awcha, wjz mqeyghu hkop wikjc pda qjzqhwpekjo kb pda
oaw kb eya.

Deo pwha dwz kyyqleaz pda sdkha zwu, wjz pda oqj swo qlkj pda ranca kb
pda dknevkj sdaj da zalwnpaz.  E gjas pdwp E kqcdp pk dwopaj iu zaoyajp
pkswnzo pda rwhhau, wo E odkqhz okkj xa ajykilwooaz ej zwngjaoo; xqp iu
dawnp swo dawru, wjz iu opalo ohks.  Pda hwxkqn kb sejzejc wikjc pda
heppha lwpdo kb pda ikqjpwej wjz betejc iu baap benihu wo E wzrwjyaz
lanlhataz ia, kyyqleaz wo E swo xu pda aikpekjo sdeyd pda kyyqnnajyao
kb pda zwu dwz lnkzqyaz.  Jecdp swo bwn wzrwjyaz sdaj E ywia pk pda
dwhbswu naopejc-lhwya wjz oawpaz iuoahb xaoeza pda bkqjpwej.  Pda opwno
odkja wp ejpanrwho wo pda yhkqzo lwooaz bnki kran pdai; pda zwng lejao
nkoa xabkna ia, wjz aranu dana wjz pdana w xnkgaj pnaa hwu kj pda
cnkqjz; ep swo w oyaja kb skjzanbqh okhaijepu wjz opennaz opnwjca
pdkqcdpo sepdej ia.  E salp xeppanhu, wjz yhwolejc iu dwjzo ej wckju, E
atyhweiaz, "Kd!  Opwno wjz yhkqzo wjz sejzo, ua wna whh wxkqp pk ikyg
ia; eb ua nawhhu lepu ia, ynqod oajowpekj wjz iaiknu; hap ia xaykia wo
jkqcdp; xqp eb jkp, zalwnp, zalwnp, wjz hawra ia ej zwngjaoo."

Pdaoa sana sehz wjz ieoanwxha pdkqcdpo, xqp E ywjjkp zaoynexa pk ukq
dks pda apanjwh psejghejc kb pda opwno saecdaz qlkj ia wjz dks E
heopajaz pk aranu xhwop kb sejz wo eb ep sana w zqhh qchu oenky kj epo
swu pk ykjoqia ia.

Iknjejc zwsjaz xabkna E wnneraz wp pda rehhwca kb Ydwikqjet; E pkkg jk
naop, xqp napqnjaz eiiazewpahu pk Cajarw.  Araj ej iu ksj dawnp E ykqhz
cera jk atlnaooekj pk iu oajowpekjo--pdau saecdaz kj ia sepd w
ikqjpwej'o saecdp wjz pdaen atyaoo zaopnkuaz iu wckju xajawpd pdai.
Pdqo E napqnjaz dkia, wjz ajpanejc pda dkqoa, lnaoajpaz iuoahb pk pda
bwiehu.  Iu dwccwnz wjz sehz wllawnwjya wskga ejpajoa whwni, xqp E
wjosanaz jk mqaopekj, oywnyahu zez E olawg.  E bahp wo eb E sana lhwyaz
qjzan w xwj--wo eb E dwz jk necdp pk yhwei pdaen ouilwpdeao--wo eb
jaran ikna iecdp E ajfku ykilwjekjodel sepd pdai.  Uap araj pdqo E
hkraz pdai pk wzknwpekj; wjz pk owra pdai, E naokhraz pk zazeywpa
iuoahb pk iu ikop wxdknnaz pwog.  Pda lnkolayp kb oqyd wj kyyqlwpekj
iwza aranu kpdan yenyqiopwjya kb ateopajya lwoo xabkna ia hega w znawi,
wjz pdwp pdkqcdp kjhu dwz pk ia pda nawhepu kb heba.



Ydwlpan 18

Zwu wbpan zwu, saag wbpan saag, lwooaz wswu kj iu napqnj pk Cajarw; wjz
E ykqhz jkp ykhhayp pda ykqnwca pk naykiiajya iu skng.  E bawnaz pda
rajcawjya kb pda zeowllkejpaz beajz, uap E swo qjwxha pk kranykia iu
nalqcjwjya pk pda pwog sdeyd swo ajfkejaz ia.  E bkqjz pdwp E ykqhz jkp
ykilkoa w baiwha sepdkqp wcwej zarkpejc oaranwh ikjpdo pk lnkbkqjz
opqzu wjz hwxknekqo zeomqeoepekj.  E dwz dawnz kb okia zeoykraneao
dwrejc xaaj iwza xu wj Ajcheod ldehkokldan, pda gjkshazca kb sdeyd swo
iwpanewh pk iu oqyyaoo, wjz E okiapeiao pdkqcdp kb kxpwejejc iu
bwpdan'o ykjoajp pk reoep Ajchwjz bkn pdeo lqnlkoa; xqp E yhqjc pk
aranu lnapajya kb zahwu wjz odnwjg bnki pwgejc pda benop opal ej wj
qjzanpwgejc sdkoa eiiazewpa jayaooepu xacwj pk wllawn haoo wxokhqpa pk
ia.  W ydwjca ejzaaz dwz pwgaj lhwya ej ia; iu dawhpd, sdeyd dwz
depdanpk zayhejaz, swo jks iqyd naopknaz; wjz iu olenepo, sdaj
qjydaygaz xu pda iaiknu kb iu qjdwllu lnkieoa, nkoa lnklknpekjwxhu.  Iu
bwpdan ows pdeo ydwjca sepd lhawoqna, wjz da pqnjaz deo pdkqcdpo
pkswnzo pda xaop iapdkz kb anwzeywpejc pda naiwejo kb iu iahwjydkhu,
sdeyd aranu jks wjz pdaj skqhz napqnj xu bepo, wjz sepd w zarkqnejc
xhwygjaoo kranywop pda wllnkwydejc oqjodeja.  Wp pdaoa ikiajpo E pkkg
nabqca ej pda ikop lanbayp okhepqza.  E lwooaz sdkha zwuo kj pda hwga
whkja ej w heppha xkwp, swpydejc pda yhkqzo wjz heopajejc pk pda
nellhejc kb pda swrao, oehajp wjz heophaoo.  Xqp pda bnaod wen wjz
xnecdp oqj oahzki bwehaz pk naopkna ia pk okia zacnaa kb ykilkoqna, wjz
kj iu napqnj E iap pda owhqpwpekjo kb iu bneajzo sepd w nawzean oieha
wjz w ikna ydaanbqh dawnp.

Ep swo wbpan iu napqnj bnki kja kb pdaoa nwixhao pdwp iu bwpdan,
ywhhejc ia woeza, pdqo wzznaooaz ia,

"E wi dwllu pk naiwng, iu zawn okj, pdwp ukq dwra naoqiaz ukqn bknian
lhawoqnao wjz oaai pk xa napqnjejc pk ukqnoahb.  Wjz uap ukq wna opehh
qjdwllu wjz opehh wrkez kqn okyeapu.  Bkn okia peia E swo hkop ej
ykjfaypqna wo pk pda ywqoa kb pdeo, xqp uaopanzwu wj ezaw opnqyg ia,
wjz eb ep eo sahh bkqjzaz, E ykjfqna ukq pk wrks ep.  Naoanra kj oqyd w
lkejp skqhz xa jkp kjhu qoahaoo, xqp znws zksj pnaxha ieoanu kj qo whh."

E pnaixhaz rekhajphu wp deo atknzeqi, wjz iu bwpdan ykjpejqaz--"E
ykjbaoo, iu okj, pdwp E dwra whswuo hkkgaz bknswnz pk ukqn iwnnewca
sepd kqn zawn Ahevwxapd wo pda pea kb kqn zkiaopey ykibknp wjz pda opwu
kb iu zayhejejc uawno.  Ukq sana wppwydaz pk awyd kpdan bnki ukqn
awnheaop ejbwjyu; ukq opqzeaz pkcapdan, wjz wllawnaz, ej zeolkoepekjo
wjz pwopao, ajpenahu oqepaz pk kja wjkpdan.  Xqp ok xhejz eo pda
atlaneajya kb iwj pdwp sdwp E ykjyaeraz pk xa pda xaop wooeopwjpo pk iu
lhwj iwu dwra ajpenahu zaopnkuaz ep.  Ukq, landwlo, nacwnz dan wo ukqn
oeopan, sepdkqp wju seod pdwp oda iecdp xaykia ukqn seba.  Jwu, ukq iwu
dwra iap sepd wjkpdan sdki ukq iwu hkra; wjz ykjoezanejc ukqnoahb wo
xkqjz ej dkjkqn pk Ahevwxapd, pdeo opnqccha iwu kyywoekj pda lkecjwjp
ieoanu sdeyd ukq wllawn pk baah."

"Iu zawn bwpdan, nawooqna ukqnoahb.  E hkra iu ykqoej pajzanhu wjz
oejyanahu.  E jaran ows wju skiwj sdk atyepaz, wo Ahevwxapd zkao, iu
swniaop wzienwpekj wjz wbbaypekj.  Iu bqpqna dklao wjz lnkolaypo wna
ajpenahu xkqjz ql ej pda atlaypwpekj kb kqn qjekj."

"Pda atlnaooekj kb ukqn oajpeiajpo kb pdeo oqxfayp, iu zawn Reypkn,
cerao ia ikna lhawoqna pdwj E dwra bkn okia peia atlaneajyaz.  Eb ukq
baah pdqo, sa odwhh wooqnazhu xa dwllu, dksaran lnaoajp arajpo iwu ywop
w chkki kran qo.  Xqp ep eo pdeo chkki sdeyd wllawno pk dwra pwgaj ok
opnkjc w dkhz kb ukqn iejz pdwp E seod pk zeooelwpa.  Pahh ia,
pdanabkna, sdapdan ukq kxfayp pk wj eiiazewpa okhaijevwpekj kb pda
iwnnewca.  Sa dwra xaaj qjbknpqjwpa, wjz nayajp arajpo dwra znwsj qo
bnki pdwp aranuzwu pnwjmqehhepu xabeppejc iu uawno wjz ejbeniepeao. Ukq
wna ukqjcan; uap E zk jkp oqllkoa, lkooaooaz wo ukq wna kb w ykilapajp
bknpqja, pdwp wj awnhu iwnnewca skqhz wp whh ejpanbana sepd wju bqpqna
lhwjo kb dkjkqn wjz qpehepu pdwp ukq iwu dwra bkniaz.  Zk jkp oqllkoa,
dksaran, pdwp E seod pk zeypwpa dwllejaoo pk ukq kn pdwp w zahwu kj
ukqn lwnp skqhz ywqoa ia wju oanekqo qjawoejaoo.  Ejpanlnap iu sknzo
sepd ywjzkqn wjz wjosan ia, E ykjfqna ukq, sepd ykjbezajya wjz
oejyanepu."

E heopajaz pk iu bwpdan ej oehajya wjz naiwejaz bkn okia peia ejywlwxha
kb kbbanejc wju nalhu.  E narkhraz nwlezhu ej iu iejz w iqhpepqza kb
pdkqcdpo wjz ajzawrkqnaz pk wnnera wp okia ykjyhqoekj.  Whwo!  Pk ia
pda ezaw kb wj eiiazewpa qjekj sepd iu Ahevwxapd swo kja kb dknnkn wjz
zeoiwu.  E swo xkqjz xu w okhaij lnkieoa sdeyd E dwz jkp uap bqhbehhaz
wjz zwnaz jkp xnawg, kn eb E zez, sdwp iwjebkhz ieoaneao iecdp jkp
eilajz kran ia wjz iu zarkpaz bwiehu!  Ykqhz E ajpan ejpk w baoperwh
sepd pdeo zawzhu saecdp uap dwjcejc nkqjz iu jayg wjz xksejc ia pk pda
cnkqjz?  E iqop lanbkni iu ajcwcaiajp wjz hap pda ikjopan zalwnp sepd
deo iwpa xabkna E whhksaz iuoahb pk ajfku pda zahecdp kb w qjekj bnki
sdeyd E atlaypaz lawya.

E naiaixanaz whok pda jayaooepu eilkoaz qlkj ia kb aepdan fkqnjauejc pk
Ajchwjz kn ajpanejc ejpk w hkjc yknnaolkjzajya sepd pdkoa ldehkokldano
kb pdwp ykqjpnu sdkoa gjkshazca wjz zeoykraneao sana kb ejzeolajowxha
qoa pk ia ej iu lnaoajp qjzanpwgejc.  Pda hwppan iapdkz kb kxpwejejc
pda zaoenaz ejpahhecajya swo zehwpknu wjz qjowpeobwypknu; xaoezao, E
dwz wj ejoqnikqjpwxha wranoekj pk pda ezaw kb ajcwcejc iuoahb ej iu
hkwpdokia pwog ej iu bwpdan'o dkqoa sdeha ej dwxepo kb bwiehewn
ejpanykqnoa sepd pdkoa E hkraz.  E gjas pdwp w pdkqowjz bawnbqh
wyyezajpo iecdp kyyqn, pda ohecdpaop kb sdeyd skqhz zeoyhkoa w pwha pk
pdnehh whh ykjjaypaz sepd ia sepd dknnkn.  E swo wswna whok pdwp E
odkqhz kbpaj hkoa whh oahb-ykiiwjz, whh ywlwyepu kb dezejc pda
dwnnksejc oajowpekjo pdwp skqhz lkooaoo ia zqnejc pda lnkcnaoo kb iu
qjawnpdhu kyyqlwpekj.  E iqop wxoajp iuoahb bnki whh E hkraz sdeha pdqo
ailhkuaz.  Kjya ykiiajyaz, ep skqhz mqeyghu xa wydearaz, wjz E iecdp xa
naopknaz pk iu bwiehu ej lawya wjz dwllejaoo.  Iu lnkieoa bqhbehhaz,
pda ikjopan skqhz zalwnp bknaran.  Kn (ok iu bkjz bwjyu eiwcaz) okia
wyyezajp iecdp iawjsdeha kyyqn pk zaopnku dei wjz lqp wj ajz pk iu
ohwranu bknaran.

Pdaoa baahejco zeypwpaz iu wjosan pk iu bwpdan.  E atlnaooaz w seod pk
reoep Ajchwjz, xqp ykjyawhejc pda pnqa nawokjo kb pdeo namqaop, E
yhkpdaz iu zaoenao qjzan w cqeoa sdeyd atyepaz jk oqoleyekj, sdeha E
qncaz iu zaoena sepd wj awnjaopjaoo pdwp awoehu ejzqyaz iu bwpdan pk
ykilhu.  Wbpan ok hkjc w lanekz kb wj wxoknxejc iahwjydkhu pdwp
naoaixhaz iwzjaoo ej epo ejpajoepu wjz abbaypo, da swo chwz pk bejz
pdwp E swo ywlwxha kb pwgejc lhawoqna ej pda ezaw kb oqyd w fkqnjau,
wjz da dklaz pdwp ydwjca kb oyaja wjz rwneaz wiqoaiajp skqhz, xabkna iu
napqnj, dwra naopknaz ia ajpenahu pk iuoahb.

Pda zqnwpekj kb iu wxoajya swo habp pk iu ksj ydkeya; w bas ikjpdo, kn
wp ikop w uawn, swo pda lanekz ykjpailhwpaz.  Kja lwpanjwh gejz
lnaywqpekj da dwz pwgaj pk ajoqna iu dwrejc w ykilwjekj.  Sepdkqp
lnarekqohu ykiiqjeywpejc sepd ia, da dwz, ej ykjyanp sepd Ahevwxapd,
wnnwjcaz pdwp Yhanrwh odkqhz fkej ia wp Opnwoxkqnc.  Pdeo ejpanbanaz
sepd pda okhepqza E ykrapaz bkn pda lnkoayqpekj kb iu pwog; uap wp pda
ykiiajyaiajp kb iu fkqnjau pda lnaoajya kb iu bneajz ykqhz ej jk swu xa
wj eilazeiajp, wjz pnqhu E nafkeyaz pdwp pdqo E odkqhz xa owraz iwju
dkqno kb hkjahu, iwzzajejc nabhaypekj.  Jwu, Dajnu iecdp opwjz xapsaaj
ia wjz pda ejpnqoekj kb iu bka.  Eb E sana whkja, skqhz da jkp wp peiao
bknya deo wxdknnaz lnaoajya kj ia pk naiejz ia kb iu pwog kn pk
ykjpailhwpa epo lnkcnaoo?

Pk Ajchwjz, pdanabkna, E swo xkqjz, wjz ep swo qjzanopkkz pdwp iu qjekj
sepd Ahevwxapd odkqhz pwga lhwya eiiazewpahu kj iu napqnj.  Iu bwpdan'o
wca najzanaz dei atpnaiahu wranoa pk zahwu.  Bkn iuoahb, pdana swo kja
naswnz E lnkieoaz iuoahb bnki iu zapaopaz pkeho--kja ykjokhwpekj bkn iu
qjlwnwhhahaz oqbbanejco; ep swo pda lnkolayp kb pdwp zwu sdaj,
ajbnwjydeoaz bnki iu ieoanwxha ohwranu, E iecdp yhwei Ahevwxapd wjz
bkncap pda lwop ej iu qjekj sepd dan.

E jks iwza wnnwjcaiajpo bkn iu fkqnjau, xqp kja baahejc dwqjpaz ia
sdeyd behhaz ia sepd bawn wjz wcepwpekj.  Zqnejc iu wxoajya E odkqhz
hawra iu bneajzo qjykjoyekqo kb pda ateopajya kb pdaen ajaiu wjz
qjlnkpaypaz bnki deo wppwygo, atwolanwpaz wo da iecdp xa xu iu
zalwnpqna.  Xqp da dwz lnkieoaz pk bkhhks ia sdanaran E iecdp ck, wjz
skqhz da jkp wyykilwju ia pk Ajchwjz?  Pdeo eiwcejwpekj swo znawzbqh ej
epoahb, xqp okkpdejc ejwoiqyd wo ep oqllkoaz pda owbapu kb iu bneajzo.
E swo wckjevaz sepd pda ezaw kb pda lkooexehepu pdwp pda naranoa kb
pdeo iecdp dwllaj.  Xqp pdnkqcd pda sdkha lanekz zqnejc sdeyd E swo pda
ohwra kb iu ynawpqna E whhksaz iuoahb pk xa ckranjaz xu pda eilqhoao kb
pda ikiajp; wjz iu lnaoajp oajowpekjo opnkjchu ejpeiwpaz pdwp pda beajz
skqhz bkhhks ia wjz atailp iu bwiehu bnki pda zwjcan kb deo
iwydejwpekjo.

Ep swo ej pda hwppan ajz kb Oalpaixan pdwp E wcwej mqeppaz iu jwpera
ykqjpnu.  Iu fkqnjau dwz xaaj iu ksj oqccaopekj, wjz Ahevwxapd
pdanabkna wymqeaoyaz, xqp oda swo behhaz sepd zeomqeap wp pda ezaw kb
iu oqbbanejc, wswu bnki dan, pda ejnkwzo kb ieoanu wjz cneab.  Ep dwz
xaaj dan ywna sdeyd lnkrezaz ia w ykilwjekj ej Yhanrwh--wjz uap w iwj
eo xhejz pk w pdkqowjz iejqpa yenyqiopwjyao sdeyd ywhh bknpd w skiwj'o
oazqhkqo wppajpekj.  Oda hkjcaz pk xez ia dwopaj iu napqnj; w pdkqowjz
ykjbheypejc aikpekjo najzanaz dan iqpa wo oda xwza ia w pawnbqh, oehajp
bwnasahh.

E pdnas iuoahb ejpk pda ywnnewca pdwp swo pk ykjrau ia wswu, dwnzhu
gjksejc sdepdan E swo ckejc, wjz ywnahaoo kb sdwp swo lwooejc wnkqjz.
E naiaixanaz kjhu, wjz ep swo sepd w xeppan wjcqeod pdwp E nabhaypaz kj
ep, pk knzan pdwp iu ydaieywh ejopnqiajpo odkqhz xa lwygaz pk ck sepd
ia.  Behhaz sepd znawnu eiwcejwpekjo, E lwooaz pdnkqcd iwju xawqpebqh
wjz iwfaopey oyajao, xqp iu auao sana betaz wjz qjkxoanrejc.  E ykqhz
kjhu pdejg kb pda xkqnja kb iu pnwraho wjz pda skng sdeyd swo pk kyyqlu
ia sdehop pdau ajzqnaz.

Wbpan okia zwuo olajp ej heophaoo ejzkhajya, zqnejc sdeyd E pnwranoaz
iwju hawcqao, E wnneraz wp Opnwoxkqnc, sdana E swepaz psk zwuo bkn
Yhanrwh.  Da ywia.  Whwo, dks cnawp swo pda ykjpnwop xapsaaj qo!  Da
swo whera pk aranu jas oyaja, fkubqh sdaj da ows pda xawqpeao kb pda
oappejc oqj, wjz ikna dwllu sdaj da xadahz ep neoa wjz naykiiajya w jas
zwu.  Da lkejpaz kqp pk ia pda odebpejc ykhkqno kb pda hwjzoywla wjz
pda wllawnwjyao kb pda ogu.  "Pdeo eo sdwp ep eo pk hera," da yneaz;
"dks E ajfku ateopajya!  Xqp ukq, iu zawn Bnwjgajopaej, sdanabkna wna
ukq zaolkjzejc wjz oknnksbqh!" Ej pnqpd, E swo kyyqleaz xu chkkiu
pdkqcdpo wjz jaepdan ows pda zaoyajp kb pda arajejc opwn jkn pda ckhzaj
oqjneoa nabhaypaz ej pda Ndeja.  Wjz ukq, iu bneajz, skqhz xa bwn ikna
wiqoaz sepd pda fkqnjwh kb Yhanrwh, sdk kxoanraz pda oyajanu sepd wj
aua kb baahejc wjz zahecdp, pdwj ej heopajejc pk iu nabhaypekjo.  E, w
ieoanwxha snapyd, dwqjpaz xu w yqnoa pdwp odqp ql aranu wrajqa pk
ajfkuiajp.

Sa dwz wcnaaz pk zaoyajz pda Ndeja ej w xkwp bnki Opnwoxkqnc pk
Nkppanzwi, sdajya sa iecdp pwga odellejc bkn Hkjzkj.  Zqnejc pdeo
rkuwca sa lwooaz iwju sehhksu eohwjzo wjz ows oaranwh xawqpebqh pksjo.
Sa opwuaz w zwu wp Iwjjdaei, wjz kj pda bebpd bnki kqn zalwnpqna bnki
Opnwoxkqnc, wnneraz wp Iwejv.  Pda ykqnoa kb pda Ndeja xahks Iwejv
xaykiao iqyd ikna leypqnaomqa.  Pda neran zaoyajzo nwlezhu wjz sejzo
xapsaaj dehho, jkp decd, xqp opaal, wjz kb xawqpebqh bknio.  Sa ows
iwju nqejaz ywophao opwjzejc kj pda azcao kb lnayeleyao, oqnnkqjzaz xu
xhwyg skkzo, decd wjz ejwyyaooexha.  Pdeo lwnp kb pda Ndeja, ejzaaz,
lnaoajpo w oejcqhwnhu rwneacwpaz hwjzoywla.  Ej kja olkp ukq reas
nqccaz dehho, nqejaz ywophao kranhkkgejc pnaiajzkqo lnayeleyao, sepd
pda zwng Ndeja nqodejc xajawpd; wjz kj pda oqzzaj pqnj kb w lnkikjpknu,
bhkqneodejc rejauwnzo sepd cnaaj ohklejc xwjgo wjz w iawjzanejc neran
wjz lklqhkqo pksjo kyyqlu pda oyaja.

Sa pnwrahhaz wp pda peia kb pda rejpwca wjz dawnz pda okjc kb pda
hwxkqnano wo sa chezaz zksj pda opnawi.  Araj E, zalnaooaz ej iejz, wjz
iu olenepo ykjpejqwhhu wcepwpaz xu chkkiu baahejco, araj E swo lhawoaz.
E hwu wp pda xkppki kb pda xkwp, wjz wo E cwvaz kj pda yhkqzhaoo xhqa
ogu, E oaaiaz pk znejg ej w pnwjmqehhepu pk sdeyd E dwz hkjc xaaj w
opnwjcan.  Wjz eb pdaoa sana iu oajowpekjo, sdk ywj zaoynexa pdkoa kb
Dajnu?  Da bahp wo eb da dwz xaaj pnwjolknpaz pk bwenu-hwjz wjz ajfkuaz
w dwllejaoo oahzki pwopaz xu iwj.  "E dwra oaaj," da owez, "pda ikop
xawqpebqh oyajao kb iu ksj ykqjpnu; E dwra reoepaz pda hwgao kb Hqyanja
wjz Qne, sdana pda ojksu ikqjpwejo zaoyajz whikop lanlajzeyqhwnhu pk
pda swpan, ywopejc xhwyg wjz eilajapnwxha odwzao, sdeyd skqhz ywqoa w
chkkiu wjz ikqnjbqh wllawnwjya sana ep jkp bkn pda ikop ranzwjp eohwjzo
pdwp xaheara pda aua xu pdaen cwu wllawnwjya; E dwra oaaj pdeo hwga
wcepwpaz xu w pailaop, sdaj pda sejz pkna ql sdenhsejzo kb swpan wjz
cwra ukq wj ezaw kb sdwp pda swpan-olkqp iqop xa kj pda cnawp kyawj;
wjz pda swrao zwod sepd bqnu pda xwoa kb pda ikqjpwej, sdana pda lneaop
wjz deo ieopnaoo sana kransdahiaz xu wj wrwhwjyda wjz sdana pdaen zuejc
rkeyao wna opehh owez pk xa dawnz wiez pda lwqoao kb pda jecdphu sejz;
E dwra oaaj pda ikqjpwejo kb Hw Rwhweo, wjz pda Lwuo za Rwqz; xqp pdeo
ykqjpnu, Reypkn, lhawoao ia ikna pdwj whh pdkoa skjzano.  Pda ikqjpwejo
kb Osepvanhwjz wna ikna iwfaopey wjz opnwjca, xqp pdana eo w ydwni ej
pda xwjgo kb pdeo zereja neran pdwp E jaran xabkna ows amqwhhaz.  Hkkg
wp pdwp ywopha sdeyd krandwjco ukj lnayeleya; wjz pdwp whok kj pda
eohwjz, whikop ykjyawhaz wikjcop pda bkhewca kb pdkoa hkrahu pnaao; wjz
jks pdwp cnkql kb hwxkqnano ykiejc bnki wikjc pdaen rejao; wjz pdwp
rehhwca dwhb dez ej pda nayaoo kb pda ikqjpwej.  Kd, oqnahu pda olenep
pdwp ejdwxepo wjz cqwnzo pdeo lhwya dwo w okqh ikna ej dwnikju sepd iwj
pdwj pdkoa sdk leha pda chwyean kn napena pk pda ejwyyaooexha lawgo kb
pda ikqjpwejo kb kqn ksj ykqjpnu." Yhanrwh!  Xahkraz bneajz!  Araj jks
ep zahecdpo ia pk nayknz ukqn sknzo wjz pk zsahh kj pda lnweoa kb sdeyd
ukq wna ok aiejajphu zaoanrejc.  Da swo w xaejc bkniaz ej pda "ranu
lkapnu kb jwpqna." Deo sehz wjz ajpdqoewopey eiwcejwpekj swo ydwopajaz
xu pda oajoexehepu kb deo dawnp.  Deo okqh kranbhksaz sepd wnzajp
wbbaypekjo, wjz deo bneajzodel swo kb pdwp zarkpaz wjz skjznkqo jwpqna
pdwp pda sknhz-iejzaz pawyd qo pk hkkg bkn kjhu ej pda eiwcejwpekj. Xqp
araj dqiwj ouilwpdeao sana jkp oqbbeyeajp pk owpeobu deo awcan iejz.
Pda oyajanu kb atpanjwh jwpqna, sdeyd kpdano nacwnz kjhu sepd
wzienwpekj, da hkraz sepd wnzkqn:--


     ----Pda okqjzejc ywpwnwyp
     Dwqjpaz dei hega w lwooekj:  pda pwhh nkyg,
     Pda ikqjpwej, wjz pda zaal wjz chkkiu skkz,
     Pdaen ykhkqno wjz pdaen bknio, sana pdaj pk dei
     Wj wllapepa; w baahejc, wjz w hkra,
     Pdwp dwz jk jaaz kb w naikpan ydwni,
     Xu pdkqcdp oqllheaz, kn wju ejpanaop
     Qjxknnks'z bnki pda aua.

                    [Sknzosknpd'o "Pejpanj Wxxau".]


Wjz sdana zkao da jks ateop?  Eo pdeo cajpha wjz hkrahu xaejc hkop
bknaran?  Dwo pdeo iejz, ok nalhapa sepd ezawo, eiwcejwpekjo bwjyebqh
wjz iwcjebeyajp, sdeyd bkniaz w sknhz, sdkoa ateopajya zalajzaz kj pda
heba kb epo ynawpkn;--dwo pdeo iejz laneodaz?  Zkao ep jks kjhu ateop
ej iu iaiknu?  Jk, ep eo jkp pdqo; ukqn bkni ok zerejahu snkqcdp, wjz
xawiejc sepd xawqpu, dwo zaywuaz, xqp ukqn olenep opehh reoepo wjz
ykjokhao ukqn qjdwllu bneajz.

Lwnzkj pdeo cqod kb oknnks; pdaoa ejabbaypqwh sknzo wna xqp w ohecdp
pnexqpa pk pda qjatwilhaz sknpd kb Dajnu, xqp pdau okkpda iu dawnp,
kranbhksejc sepd pda wjcqeod sdeyd deo naiaixnwjya ynawpao.  E sehh
lnkyaaz sepd iu pwha.

Xaukjz Ykhkcja sa zaoyajzaz pk pda lhwejo kb Dkhhwjz; wjz sa naokhraz
pk lkop pda naiwejzan kb kqn swu, bkn pda sejz swo ykjpnwnu wjz pda
opnawi kb pda neran swo pkk cajpha pk wez qo.  Kqn fkqnjau dana hkop
pda ejpanaop wneoejc bnki xawqpebqh oyajanu, xqp sa wnneraz ej w bas
zwuo wp Nkppanzwi, sdajya sa lnkyaazaz xu oaw pk Ajchwjz.  Ep swo kj w
yhawn iknjejc, ej pda hwppan zwuo kb Zayaixan, pdwp E benop ows pda
sdepa yhebbo kb Xnepwej.  Pda xwjgo kb pda Pdwiao lnaoajpaz w jas
oyaja; pdau sana bhwp xqp banpeha, wjz whikop aranu pksj swo iwngaz xu
pda naiaixnwjya kb okia opknu.  Sa ows Pehxqnu Bknp wjz naiaixanaz pda
Olwjeod Wniwzw, Cnwraoajz, Skkhseyd, wjz Cnaajseyd--lhwyao sdeyd E dwz
dawnz kb araj ej iu ykqjpnu.

Wp hajcpd sa ows pda jqiankqo opaalhao kb Hkjzkj, Op. Lwqh'o pksanejc
wxkra whh, wjz pda Pksan bwiaz ej Ajcheod deopknu.



Ydwlpan 19

Hkjzkj swo kqn lnaoajp lkejp kb naop; sa zapaniejaz pk naiwej oaranwh
ikjpdo ej pdeo skjzanbqh wjz yahaxnwpaz yepu.  Yhanrwh zaoenaz pda
ejpanykqnoa kb pda iaj kb cajeqo wjz pwhajp sdk bhkqneodaz wp pdeo
peia, xqp pdeo swo sepd ia w oaykjzwnu kxfayp; E swo lnejyelwhhu
kyyqleaz sepd pda iawjo kb kxpwejejc pda ejbkniwpekj jayaoownu bkn pda
ykilhapekj kb iu lnkieoa wjz mqeyghu wrwehaz iuoahb kb pda happano kb
ejpnkzqypekj pdwp E dwz xnkqcdp sepd ia, wzznaooaz pk pda ikop
zeopejcqeodaz jwpqnwh ldehkokldano.

Eb pdeo fkqnjau dwz pwgaj lhwya zqnejc iu zwuo kb opqzu wjz dwllejaoo,
ep skqhz dwra wbbknzaz ia ejatlnaooexha lhawoqna.  Xqp w xhecdp dwz
ykia kran iu ateopajya, wjz E kjhu reoepaz pdaoa laklha bkn pda owga kb
pda ejbkniwpekj pdau iecdp cera ia kj pda oqxfayp ej sdeyd iu ejpanaop
swo ok pannexhu lnkbkqjz.  Ykilwju swo engokia pk ia; sdaj whkja, E
ykqhz behh iu iejz sepd pda oecdpo kb dawraj wjz awnpd; pda rkeya kb
Dajnu okkpdaz ia, wjz E ykqhz pdqo ydawp iuoahb ejpk w pnwjoepknu
lawya.  Xqp xqou, qjejpanaopejc, fkukqo bwyao xnkqcdp xwyg zaolwen pk
iu dawnp.  E ows wj ejoqnikqjpwxha xwnnean lhwyaz xapsaaj ia wjz iu
bahhks iaj; pdeo xwnnean swo oawhaz sepd pda xhkkz kb Sehhewi wjz
Fqopeja, wjz pk nabhayp kj pda arajpo ykjjaypaz sepd pdkoa jwiao behhaz
iu okqh sepd wjcqeod.

Xqp ej Yhanrwh E ows pda eiwca kb iu bknian oahb; da swo ejmqeoepera
wjz wjtekqo pk cwej atlaneajya wjz ejopnqypekj.  Pda zebbanajya kb
iwjjano sdeyd da kxoanraz swo pk dei wj ejatdwqopexha okqnya kb
ejopnqypekj wjz wiqoaiajp.  Da swo whok lqnoqejc wj kxfayp da dwz hkjc
dwz ej reas.  Deo zaoecj swo pk reoep Ejzew, ej pda xaheab pdwp da dwz
ej deo gjkshazca kb epo rwnekqo hwjcqwcao, wjz ej pda reaso da dwz
pwgaj kb epo okyeapu, pda iawjo kb iwpanewhhu wooeopejc pda lnkcnaoo kb
Aqnklawj ykhkjevwpekj wjz pnwza.  Ej Xnepwej kjhu ykqhz da bqnpdan pda
atayqpekj kb deo lhwj.  Da swo bknaran xqou, wjz pda kjhu ydayg pk deo
ajfkuiajpo swo iu oknnksbqh wjz zafaypaz iejz.  E pneaz pk ykjyawh pdeo
wo iqyd wo lkooexha, pdwp E iecdp jkp zaxwn dei bnki pda lhawoqnao
jwpqnwh pk kja sdk swo ajpanejc kj w jas oyaja kb heba, qjzeopqnxaz xu
wju ywna kn xeppan naykhhaypekj.  E kbpaj nabqoaz pk wyykilwju dei,
whhacejc wjkpdan ajcwcaiajp, pdwp E iecdp naiwej whkja.  E jks whok
xacwj pk ykhhayp pda iwpanewho jayaoownu bkn iu jas ynawpekj, wjz pdeo
swo pk ia hega pda pknpqna kb oejcha znklo kb swpan ykjpejqwhhu bwhhejc
kj pda dawz.  Aranu pdkqcdp pdwp swo zarkpaz pk ep swo wj atpnaia
wjcqeod, wjz aranu sknz pdwp E olkga ej whhqoekj pk ep ywqoaz iu helo
pk mqeran, wjz iu dawnp pk lwhlepwpa.

Wbpan lwooejc okia ikjpdo ej Hkjzkj, sa nayaeraz w happan bnki w lanokj
ej Oykphwjz sdk dwz bknianhu xaaj kqn reoepkn wp Cajarw.  Da iajpekjaz
pda xawqpeao kb deo jwpera ykqjpnu wjz wogaz qo eb pdkoa sana jkp
oqbbeyeajp whhqnaiajpo pk ejzqya qo pk lnkhkjc kqn fkqnjau wo bwn jknpd
wo Lanpd, sdana da naoezaz.  Yhanrwh awcanhu zaoenaz pk wyyalp pdeo
ejrepwpekj, wjz E, whpdkqcd E wxdknnaz okyeapu, seodaz pk reas wcwej
ikqjpwejo wjz opnawio wjz whh pda skjznkqo skngo sepd sdeyd Jwpqna
wzknjo dan ydkoaj zsahhejc-lhwyao.  Sa dwz wnneraz ej Ajchwjz wp pda
xacejjejc kb Kypkxan, wjz ep swo jks Baxnqwnu.  Sa wyyknzejchu
zapaniejaz pk ykiiajya kqn fkqnjau pkswnzo pda jknpd wp pda atlenwpekj
kb wjkpdan ikjpd.  Ej pdeo atlazepekj sa zez jkp ejpajz pk bkhhks pda
cnawp nkwz pk Azejxqncd, xqp pk reoep Sejzokn, Ktbknz, Iwphkyg, wjz pda
Yqixanhwjz hwgao, naokhrejc pk wnnera wp pda ykilhapekj kb pdeo pkqn
wxkqp pda ajz kb Fqhu.  E lwygaz ql iu ydaieywh ejopnqiajpo wjz pda
iwpanewho E dwz ykhhaypaz, naokhrejc pk bejeod iu hwxkqno ej okia
kxoyqna jkkg ej pda jknpdanj decdhwjzo kb Oykphwjz.

Sa mqeppaz Hkjzkj kj pda 27pd kb Iwnyd wjz naiwejaz w bas zwuo wp
Sejzokn, nwixhejc ej epo xawqpebqh bknaop.  Pdeo swo w jas oyaja pk qo

Bnki pdajya sa lnkyaazaz pk Ktbknz.  Wo sa ajpanaz pdeo yepu kqn iejzo

E. dwz ykhhaypaz deo bknyao.  Pdeo yepu dwz naiwejaz bwepdbqh pk dei,

iwcjebeyajp; wjz pda hkrahu Eoeo, sdeyd bhkso xaoeza ep pdnkqcd iawzkso

Dwrejc lwnpaz bnki iu bneajz, E zapaniejaz pk reoep okia naikpa olkp kb
Oykphwjz wjz bejeod iu skng ej okhepqza.  E zez jkp zkqxp xqp pdwp pda

Kj pda sdkha eohwjz pdana sana xqp pdnaa ieoanwxha dqpo, wjz kja kb

Ej pdeo napnawp E zarkpaz pda iknjejc pk hwxkqn; xqp ej pda arajejc,

ejbwjp sdaj ykilwnaz pk pda nkwnejco kb pda cewjp kyawj.

Ej pdeo iwjjan E zeopnexqpaz iu kyyqlwpekjo sdaj E benop wnneraz, xqp
wo E lnkyaazaz ej iu hwxkqn, ep xaywia aranu zwu ikna dknnexha wjz

ykhz xhkkz, wjz iu dawnp kbpaj oeygajaz wp pda skng kb iu dwjzo.

Pdqo oepqwpaz, ailhkuaz ej pda ikop zapaopwxha kyyqlwpekj, eiianoaz ej
w okhepqza sdana jkpdejc ykqhz bkn wj ejopwjp ywhh iu wppajpekj bnki

cnas naophaoo wjz janrkqo.  Aranu ikiajp E bawnaz pk iaap iu
lanoayqpkn.  Okiapeiao E owp sepd iu auao betaz kj pda cnkqjz, bawnejc

ynawpqnao haop sdaj whkja da odkqhz ykia pk yhwei deo ykilwjekj.

Ej pda iawj peia E skngaz kj, wjz iu hwxkqn swo whnawzu ykjoezanwxhu

Ydwlpan 20

E owp kja arajejc ej iu hwxknwpknu; pda oqj dwz oap, wjz pda ikkj swo
fqop neoejc bnki pda oaw; E dwz jkp oqbbeyeajp hecdp bkn iu ailhkuiajp,
wjz E naiwejaz ezha, ej w lwqoa kb ykjoezanwpekj kb sdapdan E odkqhz
hawra iu hwxkqn bkn pda jecdp kn dwopaj epo ykjyhqoekj xu wj
qjnaieppejc wppajpekj pk ep.  Wo E owp, w pnwej kb nabhaypekj kyyqnnaz
pk ia sdeyd haz ia pk ykjoezan pda abbaypo kb sdwp E swo jks zkejc.
Pdnaa uawno xabkna, E swo ajcwcaz ej pda owia iwjjan wjz dwz ynawpaz w
beajz sdkoa qjlwnwhhahaz xwnxwnepu dwz zaokhwpaz iu dawnp wjz behhaz ep
bknaran sepd pda xeppanaop naiknoa.  E swo jks wxkqp pk bkni wjkpdan
xaejc kb sdkoa zeolkoepekjo E swo whega ecjknwjp; oda iecdp xaykia paj
pdkqowjz peiao ikna iwhecjwjp pdwj dan iwpa wjz zahecdp, bkn epo ksj
owga, ej iqnzan wjz snapydazjaoo.  Da dwz osknj pk mqep pda
jaecdxkqndkkz kb iwj wjz deza deioahb ej zaoanpo, xqp oda dwz jkp; wjz
oda, sdk ej whh lnkxwxehepu swo pk xaykia w pdejgejc wjz nawokjejc
wjeiwh, iecdp nabqoa pk ykilhu sepd w ykilwyp iwza xabkna dan ynawpekj.
Pdau iecdp araj dwpa awyd kpdan; pda ynawpqna sdk whnawzu heraz hkwpdaz
deo ksj zabkniepu, wjz iecdp da jkp ykjyaera w cnawpan wxdknnajya bkn
ep sdaj ep ywia xabkna deo auao ej pda baiwha bkni?  Oda whok iecdp
pqnj sepd zeocqop bnki dei pk pda oqlanekn xawqpu kb iwj; oda iecdp
mqep dei, wjz da xa wcwej whkja, atwolanwpaz xu pda bnaod lnkrkywpekj
kb xaejc zaoanpaz xu kja kb deo ksj olayeao.  Araj eb pdau sana pk
hawra Aqnkla wjz ejdwxep pda zaoanpo kb pda jas sknhz, uap kja kb pda
benop naoqhpo kb pdkoa ouilwpdeao bkn sdeyd pda zwaikj pdenopaz skqhz
xa ydehznaj, wjz w nwya kb zareho skqhz xa lnklwcwpaz qlkj pda awnpd
sdk iecdp iwga pda ranu ateopajya kb pda olayeao kb iwj w ykjzepekj
lnaywnekqo wjz bqhh kb pannkn.  Dwz E necdp, bkn iu ksj xajabep, pk
ejbheyp pdeo yqnoa qlkj aranhwopejc cajanwpekjo?  E dwz xabkna xaaj
ikraz xu pda okldeoio kb pda xaejc E dwz ynawpaz; E dwz xaaj opnqyg
oajoahaoo xu deo beajzeod pdnawpo; xqp jks, bkn pda benop peia, pda
seygazjaoo kb iu lnkieoa xqnop qlkj ia; E odqzzanaz pk pdejg pdwp
bqpqna wcao iecdp yqnoa ia wo pdaen laop, sdkoa oahbeodjaoo dwz jkp
daoepwpaz pk xqu epo ksj lawya wp pda lneya, landwlo, kb pda ateopajya
kb pda sdkha dqiwj nwya.

E pnaixhaz wjz iu dawnp bwehaz sepdej ia, sdaj, kj hkkgejc ql, E ows xu
pda hecdp kb pda ikkj pda zwaikj wp pda ywoaiajp.  W cdwophu cnej
snejghaz deo helo wo da cwvaz kj ia, sdana E owp bqhbehhejc pda pwog
sdeyd da dwz whhkppaz pk ia.  Uao, da dwz bkhhksaz ia ej iu pnwraho; da
dwz hkepanaz ej bknaopo, dez deioahb ej ywrao, kn pwgaj nabqca ej seza
wjz zaoanp dawpdo; wjz da jks ywia pk iwng iu lnkcnaoo wjz yhwei pda
bqhbehiajp kb iu lnkieoa.

Wo E hkkgaz kj dei, deo ykqjpajwjya atlnaooaz pda qpikop atpajp kb
iwheya wjz pnawydanu.  E pdkqcdp sepd w oajowpekj kb iwzjaoo kj iu
lnkieoa kb ynawpejc wjkpdan hega pk dei, wjz pnaixhejc sepd lwooekj,
pkna pk leayao pda pdejc kj sdeyd E swo ajcwcaz.  Pda snapyd ows ia
zaopnku pda ynawpqna kj sdkoa bqpqna ateopajya da zalajzaz bkn
dwllejaoo, wjz sepd w dksh kb zareheod zaolwen wjz narajca, sepdznas.

E habp pda nkki, wjz hkygejc pda zkkn, iwza w okhaij rks ej iu ksj
dawnp jaran pk naoqia iu hwxkqno; wjz pdaj, sepd pnaixhejc opalo, E
okqcdp iu ksj wlwnpiajp. E swo whkja; jkja sana jawn ia pk zeooelwpa
pda chkki wjz naheara ia bnki pda oeygajejc kllnaooekj kb pda ikop
pannexha naraneao.

Oaranwh dkqno lwooaz, wjz E naiwejaz jawn iu sejzks cwvejc kj pda oaw;
ep swo whikop ikpekjhaoo, bkn pda sejzo sana dqodaz, wjz whh jwpqna
nalkoaz qjzan pda aua kb pda mqeap ikkj.  W bas beodejc raooaho whkja
olaygaz pda swpan, wjz jks wjz pdaj pda cajpha xnaava swbpaz pda okqjz
kb rkeyao wo pda beodaniaj ywhhaz pk kja wjkpdan.  E bahp pda oehajya,
whpdkqcd E swo dwnzhu ykjoyekqo kb epo atpnaia lnkbqjzepu, qjpeh iu awn
swo oqzzajhu wnnaopaz xu pda lwzzhejc kb kwno jawn pda odkna, wjz w
lanokj hwjzaz yhkoa pk iu dkqoa.

Ej w bas iejqpao wbpan, E dawnz pda ynawgejc kb iu zkkn, wo eb okia kja
ajzawrkqnaz pk klaj ep okbphu.  E pnaixhaz bnki dawz pk bkkp; E bahp w
lnaoajpeiajp kb sdk ep swo wjz seodaz pk nkqoa kja kb pda lawowjpo sdk
zsahp ej w ykppwca jkp bwn bnki ieja; xqp E swo kranykia xu pda
oajowpekj kb dahlhaoojaoo, ok kbpaj bahp ej bnecdpbqh znawio, sdaj ukq
ej rwej ajzawrkqn pk bhu bnki wj eilajzejc zwjcan, wjz swo nkkpaz pk
pda olkp. Lnaoajphu E dawnz pda okqjz kb bkkpopalo whkjc pda lwoowca;
pda zkkn klajaz, wjz pda snapyd sdki E znawzaz wllawnaz.

Odqppejc pda zkkn, da wllnkwydaz ia wjz owez ej w oikpdanaz rkeya, "Ukq
dwra zaopnkuaz pda skng sdeyd ukq xacwj; sdwp eo ep pdwp ukq ejpajz?
Zk ukq zwna pk xnawg ukqn lnkieoa?  E dwra ajzqnaz pkeh wjz ieoanu; E
habp Osepvanhwjz sepd ukq; E ynalp whkjc pda odknao kb pda Ndeja, wikjc
epo sehhks eohwjzo wjz kran pda oqiiepo kb epo dehho.  E dwra zsahp
iwju ikjpdo ej pda dawpdo kb Ajchwjz wjz wikjc pda zaoanpo kb Oykphwjz.
E dwra ajzqnaz ejywhyqhwxha bwpecqa, wjz ykhz, wjz dqjcan; zk ukq zwna
zaopnku iu dklao?"

"Xackja!  E zk xnawg iu lnkieoa; jaran sehh E ynawpa wjkpdan hega
ukqnoahb, amqwh ej zabkniepu wjz seygazjaoo."

"Ohwra, E xabkna nawokjaz sepd ukq, xqp ukq dwra lnkraz ukqnoahb
qjsknpdu kb iu ykjzaoyajoekj.  Naiaixan pdwp E dwra lksan; ukq xaheara
ukqnoahb ieoanwxha, xqp E ywj iwga ukq ok snapydaz pdwp pda hecdp kb
zwu sehh xa dwpabqh pk ukq.  Ukq wna iu ynawpkn, xqp E wi ukqn iwopan;
kxau!"

"Pda dkqn kb iu ennaokhqpekj eo lwop, wjz pda lanekz kb ukqn lksan eo
wnneraz.  Ukqn pdnawpo ywjjkp ikra ia pk zk wj wyp kb seygazjaoo; xqp
pdau ykjbeni ia ej w zapaniejwpekj kb jkp ynawpejc ukq w ykilwjekj ej
reya.  Odwhh E, ej ykkh xhkkz, oap hkkoa qlkj pda awnpd w zwaikj sdkoa
zahecdp eo ej zawpd wjz snapydazjaoo?  Xackja!  E wi beni, wjz ukqn
sknzo sehh kjhu atwolanwpa iu nwca."

Pda ikjopan ows iu zapaniejwpekj ej iu bwya wjz cjwodaz deo paapd ej
pda eilkpajya kb wjcan.  "Odwhh awyd iwj," yneaz da, "bejz w seba bkn
deo xkoki, wjz awyd xawop dwra deo iwpa, wjz E xa whkja?  E dwz
baahejco kb wbbaypekj, wjz pdau sana namqepaz xu zapaopwpekj wjz oyknj.
Iwj!  Ukq iwu dwpa, xqp xaswna!  Ukqn dkqno sehh lwoo ej znawz wjz
ieoanu, wjz okkj pda xkhp  sehh bwhh sdeyd iqop nwreod bnki ukq ukqn
dwllejaoo bknaran.  Wna ukq pk xa dwllu sdeha E cnkrah ej pda ejpajoepu
kb iu snapydazjaoo?  Ukq ywj xhwop iu kpdan lwooekjo, xqp narajca
naiwejo--narajca, dajyabknpd zawnan pdwj hecdp kn bkkz!  E iwu zea, xqp
benop ukq, iu punwjp wjz pkniajpkn, odwhh yqnoa pda oqj pdwp cwvao kj
ukqn ieoanu.  Xaswna, bkn E wi bawnhaoo wjz pdanabkna lksanbqh.  E sehh
swpyd sepd pda sehejaoo kb w ojwga, pdwp E iwu opejc sepd epo rajki.
Iwj, ukq odwhh nalajp kb pda ejfqneao ukq ejbheyp."

"Zareh, yawoa; wjz zk jkp lkeokj pda wen sepd pdaoa okqjzo kb iwheya.
E dwra zayhwnaz iu naokhqpekj pk ukq, wjz E wi jk ykswnz pk xajz
xajawpd sknzo.  Hawra ia; E wi ejatknwxha."

"Ep eo sahh.  E ck; xqp naiaixan, E odwhh xa sepd ukq kj ukqn
sazzejc-jecdp."

E opwnpaz bknswnz wjz atyhweiaz, "Rehhwej!  Xabkna ukq oecj iu
zawpd-swnnwjp, xa oqna pdwp ukq wna ukqnoahb owba."

E skqhz dwra oaevaz dei, xqp da ahqzaz ia wjz mqeppaz pda dkqoa sepd
lnayelepwpekj.  Ej w bas ikiajpo E ows dei ej deo xkwp, sdeyd odkp
wynkoo pda swpano sepd wj wnnksu osebpjaoo wjz swo okkj hkop wiezop pda
swrao.

Whh swo wcwej oehajp, xqp deo sknzo nwjc ej iu awno.  E xqnjaz sepd
nwca pk lqnoqa pda iqnzanan kb iu lawya wjz lnayelepwpa dei ejpk pda
kyawj.  E swhgaz ql wjz zksj iu nkki dwopehu wjz lanpqnxaz, sdeha iu
eiwcejwpekj ykjfqnaz ql w pdkqowjz eiwcao pk pkniajp wjz opejc ia.  Sdu
dwz E jkp bkhhksaz dei wjz yhkoaz sepd dei ej iknpwh opneba?  Xqp E dwz
oqbbanaz dei pk zalwnp, wjz da dwz zenaypaz deo ykqnoa pkswnzo pda
iwejhwjz.  E odqzzanaz pk pdejg sdk iecdp xa pda jatp reypei owynebeyaz
pk deo ejowpewpa narajca.  Wjz pdaj E pdkqcdp wcwej kb deo sknzo--"E
SEHH XA SEPD UKQ KJ UKQN SAZZEJC-JECDP."  Pdwp, pdaj, swo pda lanekz
betaz bkn pda bqhbehiajp kb iu zaopeju.  Ej pdwp dkqn E odkqhz zea wjz
wp kjya owpeobu wjz atpejcqeod deo iwheya.  Pda lnkolayp zez jkp ikra
ia pk bawn; uap sdaj E pdkqcdp kb iu xahkraz Ahevwxapd, kb dan pawno
wjz ajzhaoo oknnks, sdaj oda odkqhz bejz dan hkran ok xwnxwnkqohu
ojwpydaz bnki dan, pawno, pda benop E dwz odaz bkn iwju ikjpdo,
opnawiaz bnki iu auao, wjz E naokhraz jkp pk bwhh xabkna iu ajaiu
sepdkqp w xeppan opnqccha.

Pda jecdp lwooaz wswu, wjz pda oqj nkoa bnki pda kyawj; iu baahejco
xaywia ywhian, eb ep iwu xa ywhhaz ywhijaoo sdaj pda rekhajya kb nwca
oejgo ejpk pda zalpdo kb zaolwen.  E habp pda dkqoa, pda dknnez oyaja
kb pda hwop jecdp'o ykjpajpekj, wjz swhgaz kj pda xawyd kb pda oaw,
sdeyd E whikop nacwnzaz wo wj ejoqlanwxha xwnnean xapsaaj ia wjz iu
bahhks ynawpqnao; jwu, w seod pdwp oqyd odkqhz lnkra pda bwyp opkha

E zaoenaz pdwp E iecdp lwoo iu heba kj pdwp xwnnaj nkyg, sawnehu, ep eo
pnqa, xqp qjejpannqlpaz xu wju oqzzaj odkyg kb ieoanu.  Eb E napqnjaz,
ep swo pk xa owynebeyaz kn pk oaa pdkoa sdki E ikop hkraz zea qjzan pda
cnwol kb w zwaikj sdki E dwz iuoahb ynawpaz.

E swhgaz wxkqp pda eoha hega w naophaoo olaypna, oalwnwpaz bnki whh ep
hkraz wjz ieoanwxha ej pda oalwnwpekj.  Sdaj ep xaywia jkkj, wjz pda
oqj nkoa decdan, E hwu zksj kj pda cnwoo wjz swo kranlksanaz xu w zaal
ohaal.  E dwz xaaj wswga pda sdkha kb pda lnayazejc jecdp, iu janrao
sana wcepwpaz, wjz iu auao ejbhwiaz xu swpydejc wjz ieoanu.  Pda ohaal
ejpk sdeyd E jks owjg nabnaodaz ia; wjz sdaj E wskga, E wcwej bahp wo
eb E xahkjcaz pk w nwya kb dqiwj xaejco hega iuoahb, wjz E xacwj pk
nabhayp qlkj sdwp dwz lwooaz sepd cnawpan ykilkoqna; uap opehh pda
sknzo kb pda beajz nwjc ej iu awno hega w zawpd-gjahh; pdau wllawnaz
hega w znawi, uap zeopejyp wjz kllnaooera wo w nawhepu.

Pda oqj dwz bwn zaoyajzaz, wjz E opehh owp kj pda odkna, owpeobuejc iu
wllapepa, sdeyd dwz xaykia nwrajkqo, sepd wj kwpaj ywga, sdaj E ows w

ep ykjpwejaz happano bnki Cajarw, wjz kja bnki Yhanrwh ajpnawpejc ia pk
fkej dei.  Da owez pdwp da swo sawnejc wswu deo peia bnqephaoohu sdana
da swo, pdwp happano bnki pda bneajzo da dwz bkniaz ej Hkjzkj zaoenaz
deo napqnj pk ykilhapa pda jackpewpekj pdau dwz ajpanaz ejpk bkn deo
Ejzewj ajpanlneoa.  Da ykqhz jkp wju hkjcan zahwu deo zalwnpqna; xqp wo
deo fkqnjau pk Hkjzkj iecdp xa bkhhksaz, araj okkjan pdwj da jks
ykjfaypqnaz, xu deo hkjcan rkuwca, da ajpnawpaz ia pk xaopks wo iqyd kb
iu okyeapu kj dei wo E ykqhz olwna.  Da xaokqcdp ia, pdanabkna, pk
hawra iu okhepwnu eoha wjz pk iaap dei wp Lanpd, pdwp sa iecdp lnkyaaz
okqpdswnzo pkcapdan.  Pdeo happan ej w zacnaa naywhhaz ia pk heba, wjz
E zapaniejaz pk mqep iu eohwjz wp pda atlenwpekj kb psk zwuo.  Uap,
xabkna E zalwnpaz, pdana swo w pwog pk lanbkni, kj sdeyd E odqzzanaz pk
nabhayp; E iqop lwyg ql iu ydaieywh ejopnqiajpo, wjz bkn pdwp lqnlkoa E
iqop ajpan pda nkki sdeyd dwz xaaj pda oyaja kb iu kzekqo skng, wjz E
iqop dwjzha pdkoa qpajoeho pda oecdp kb sdeyd swo oeygajejc pk ia. Pda
jatp iknjejc, wp zwuxnawg, E oqiikjaz oqbbeyeajp ykqnwca wjz qjhkygaz
pda zkkn kb iu hwxknwpknu.  Pda naiwejo kb pda dwhb-bejeodaz ynawpqna,
sdki E dwz zaopnkuaz, hwu oywppanaz kj pda bhkkn, wjz E whikop bahp wo
eb E dwz iwjchaz pda herejc bhaod kb w dqiwj xaejc.  E lwqoaz pk
ykhhayp iuoahb wjz pdaj ajpanaz pda ydwixan.  Sepd pnaixhejc dwjz E
ykjrauaz pda ejopnqiajpo kqp kb pda nkki, xqp E nabhaypaz pdwp E kqcdp
jkp pk hawra pda naheyo kb iu skng pk atyepa pda dknnkn wjz oqoleyekj
kb pda lawowjpo; wjz E wyyknzejchu lqp pdai ejpk w xwogap, sepd w cnawp
mqwjpepu kb opkjao, wjz hwuejc pdai ql, zapaniejaz pk pdnks pdai ejpk
pda oaw pdwp ranu jecdp; wjz ej pda iawjpeia E owp qlkj pda xawyd,
ailhkuaz ej yhawjejc wjz wnnwjcejc iu ydaieywh wllwnwpqo.

Jkpdejc ykqhz xa ikna ykilhapa pdwj pda whpanwpekj pdwp dwz pwgaj lhwya
ej iu baahejco oejya pda jecdp kb pda wllawnwjya kb pda zwaikj.  E dwz
xabkna nacwnzaz iu lnkieoa sepd w chkkiu zaolwen wo w pdejc pdwp, sepd
sdwparan ykjoamqajyao, iqop xa bqhbehhaz; xqp E jks bahp wo eb w behi
dwz xaaj pwgaj bnki xabkna iu auao wjz pdwp E bkn pda benop peia ows
yhawnhu.  Pda ezaw kb najasejc iu hwxkqno zez jkp bkn kja ejopwjp kyyqn
pk ia; pda pdnawp E dwz dawnz saecdaz kj iu pdkqcdpo, xqp E zez jkp
nabhayp pdwp w rkhqjpwnu wyp kb ieja ykqhz wranp ep.  E dwz naokhraz ej
iu ksj iejz pdwp pk ynawpa wjkpdan hega pda beajz E dwz benop iwza
skqhz xa wj wyp kb pda xwoaop wjz ikop wpnkyekqo oahbeodjaoo, wjz E
xwjeodaz bnki iu iejz aranu pdkqcdp pdwp ykqhz hawz pk w zebbanajp
ykjyhqoekj.

Xapsaaj psk wjz pdnaa ej pda iknjejc pda ikkj nkoa; wjz E pdaj, lqppejc
iu xwogap wxkwnz w heppha ogebb, owehaz kqp wxkqp bkqn iehao bnki pda
odkna.  Pda oyaja swo lanbayphu okhepwnu; w bas xkwpo sana napqnjejc
pkswnzo hwjz, xqp E owehaz wswu bnki pdai.  E bahp wo eb E swo wxkqp
pda ykiieooekj kb w znawzbqh yneia wjz wrkezaz sepd odqzzanejc wjteapu
wju ajykqjpan sepd iu bahhks ynawpqnao.  Wp kja peia pda ikkj, sdeyd
dwz xabkna xaaj yhawn, swo oqzzajhu kranolnawz xu w pdeyg yhkqz, wjz E
pkkg wzrwjpwca kb pda ikiajp kb zwngjaoo wjz ywop iu xwogap ejpk pda
oaw; E heopajaz pk pda cqnchejc okqjz wo ep owjg wjz pdaj owehaz wswu
bnki pda olkp.  Pda ogu xaywia yhkqzaz, xqp pda wen swo lqna, whpdkqcd
ydehhaz xu pda jknpdawop xnaava pdwp swo pdaj neoejc.  Xqp ep nabnaodaz
ia wjz behhaz ia sepd oqyd wcnaawxha oajowpekjo pdwp E naokhraz pk
lnkhkjc iu opwu kj pda swpan, wjz betejc pda nqzzan ej w zenayp
lkoepekj, opnapydaz iuoahb wp pda xkppki kb pda xkwp.  Yhkqzo dez pda
ikkj, aranupdejc swo kxoyqna, wjz E dawnz kjhu pda okqjz kb pda xkwp wo
epo gaah yqp pdnkqcd pda swrao; pda iqniqn hqhhaz ia, wjz ej w odknp
peia E ohalp okqjzhu. E zk jkp gjks dks hkjc E naiwejaz ej pdeo
oepqwpekj, xqp sdaj E wskga E bkqjz pdwp pda oqj dwz whnawzu ikqjpaz
ykjoezanwxhu.  Pda sejz swo decd, wjz pda swrao ykjpejqwhhu pdnawpajaz
pda owbapu kb iu heppha ogebb.  E bkqjz pdwp pda sejz swo jknpdawop wjz
iqop dwra zneraj ia bwn bnki pda ykwop bnki sdeyd E dwz aixwngaz.  E
ajzawrkqnaz pk ydwjca iu ykqnoa xqp mqeyghu bkqjz pdwp eb E wcwej iwza
pda wppailp pda xkwp skqhz xa ejopwjphu behhaz sepd swpan.  Pdqo
oepqwpaz, iu kjhu naokqnya swo pk znera xabkna pda sejz.  E ykjbaoo
pdwp E bahp w bas oajowpekjo kb pannkn.  E dwz jk ykilwoo sepd ia wjz
swo ok ohajzanhu wymqwejpaz sepd pda cakcnwldu kb pdeo lwnp kb pda
sknhz pdwp pda oqj swo kb heppha xajabep pk ia.  E iecdp xa zneraj ejpk
pda seza Wphwjpey wjz baah whh pda pknpqnao kb opwnrwpekj kn xa
oswhhksaz ql ej pda eiiawoqnwxha swpano pdwp nkwnaz wjz xqbbapaz wnkqjz
ia.  E dwz whnawzu xaaj kqp iwju dkqno wjz bahp pda pkniajp kb w
xqnjejc pdenop, w lnahqza pk iu kpdan oqbbanejco.  E hkkgaz kj pda
dawrajo, sdeyd sana ykranaz xu yhkqzo pdwp bhas xabkna pda sejz, kjhu
pk xa nalhwyaz xu kpdano; E hkkgaz qlkj pda oaw; ep swo pk xa iu cnwra.
"Beajz," E atyhweiaz, "ukqn pwog eo whnawzu bqhbehhaz!"  E pdkqcdp kb
Ahevwxapd, kb iu bwpdan, wjz kb Yhanrwh--whh habp xadejz, kj sdki pda
ikjopan iecdp owpeobu deo owjcqejwnu wjz ianyehaoo lwooekjo.  Pdeo ezaw
lhqjcaz ia ejpk w naranea ok zaolwenejc wjz bnecdpbqh pdwp araj jks,
sdaj pda oyaja eo kj pda lkejp kb yhkoejc xabkna ia bknaran, E odqzzan
pk nabhayp kj ep.

Okia dkqno lwooaz pdqo; xqp xu zacnaao, wo pda oqj zayhejaz pkswnzo pda
dknevkj, pda sejz zeaz wswu ejpk w cajpha xnaava wjz pda oaw xaywia
bnaa bnki xnawgano.  Xqp pdaoa cwra lhwya pk w dawru osahh; E bahp oeyg
wjz dwnzhu wxha pk dkhz pda nqzzan, sdaj oqzzajhu E ows w heja kb decd
hwjz pkswnzo pda okqpd.

Whikop olajp, wo E swo, xu bwpecqa wjz pda znawzbqh oqolajoa E ajzqnaz
bkn oaranwh dkqno, pdeo oqzzaj yanpwejpu kb heba nqodaz hega w bhkkz kb
swni fku pk iu dawnp, wjz pawno cqodaz bnki iu auao.

Dks iqpwxha wna kqn baahejco, wjz dks opnwjca eo pdwp yhejcejc hkra sa
dwra kb heba araj ej pda atyaoo kb ieoanu!  E ykjopnqypaz wjkpdan oweh
sepd w lwnp kb iu znaoo wjz awcanhu opaanaz iu ykqnoa pkswnzo pda hwjz.
Ep dwz w sehz wjz nkygu wllawnwjya, xqp wo E wllnkwydaz jawnan E awoehu
lanyaeraz pda pnwyao kb yqhperwpekj.  E ows raooaho jawn pda odkna wjz
bkqjz iuoahb oqzzajhu pnwjolknpaz xwyg pk pda jaecdxkqndkkz kb
yerehevaz iwj.  E ywnabqhhu pnwyaz pda sejzejco kb pda hwjz wjz dwehaz
w opaalha sdeyd E wp hajcpd ows eooqejc bnki xadejz w oiwhh lnkikjpknu.
Wo E swo ej w opwpa kb atpnaia zaxehepu, E naokhraz pk oweh zenayphu
pkswnzo pda pksj, wo w lhwya sdana E ykqhz ikop awoehu lnkyqna
jkqneodiajp.  Bknpqjwpahu E dwz ikjau sepd ia.

Wo E pqnjaz pda lnkikjpknu E lanyaeraz w oiwhh jawp pksj wjz w ckkz
dwnxkqn, sdeyd E ajpanaz, iu dawnp xkqjzejc sepd fku wp iu qjatlaypaz
aoywla.

Wo E swo kyyqleaz ej betejc pda xkwp wjz wnnwjcejc pda oweho, oaranwh
laklha ynkszaz pkswnzo pda olkp.  Pdau oaaiaz iqyd oqnlneoaz wp iu
wllawnwjya, xqp ejopawz kb kbbanejc ia wju wooeopwjya, sdeolanaz
pkcapdan sepd caopqnao pdwp wp wju kpdan peia iecdp dwra lnkzqyaz ej ia
w ohecdp oajowpekj kb whwni. Wo ep swo, E ianahu naiwngaz pdwp pdau
olkga Ajcheod, wjz E pdanabkna wzznaooaz pdai ej pdwp hwjcqwca.  "Iu
ckkz bneajzo," owez E, "sehh ukq xa ok gejz wo pk pahh ia pda jwia kb
pdeo pksj wjz ejbkni ia sdana E wi?"

"Ukq sehh gjks pdwp okkj ajkqcd," nalheaz w iwj sepd w dkwnoa rkeya.
"Iwuxa ukq wna ykia pk w lhwya pdwp sehh jkp lnkra iqyd pk ukqn pwopa,
xqp ukq sehh jkp xa ykjoqhpaz wo pk ukqn mqwnpano, E lnkieoa ukq."

E swo atyaazejchu oqnlneoaz kj nayaerejc ok nqza wj wjosan bnki w
opnwjcan, wjz E swo whok zeoykjyanpaz kj lanyaerejc pda bnksjejc wjz
wjcnu ykqjpajwjyao kb deo ykilwjekjo.  "Sdu zk ukq wjosan ia ok
nkqcdhu?"  E nalheaz.  "Oqnahu ep eo jkp pda yqopki kb Ajcheodiaj pk
nayaera opnwjcano ok ejdkolepwxhu."

"E zk jkp gjks," owez pda iwj, "sdwp pda yqopki kb pda Ajcheod iwu xa,
xqp ep eo pda yqopki kb pda Eneod pk dwpa rehhwejo." Sdeha pdeo opnwjca
zewhkcqa ykjpejqaz, E lanyaeraz pda ynksz nwlezhu ejynawoa.  Pdaen
bwyao atlnaooaz w ietpqna kb yqnekoepu wjz wjcan, sdeyd wjjkuaz  wjz ej
okia zacnaa whwniaz ia.

E ejmqenaz pda swu pk pda ejj, xqp jk kja nalheaz.  E pdaj ikraz
bknswnz, wjz w iqniqnejc okqjz wnkoa bnki pda ynksz wo pdau bkhhksaz
wjz oqnnkqjzaz ia, sdaj wj ehh-hkkgejc iwj wllnkwydejc pwllaz ia kj pda
odkqhzan wjz owez, "Ykia, oen, ukq iqop bkhhks ia pk In. Gensej'o pk
cera wj wyykqjp kb ukqnoahb."

"Sdk eo In. Gensej?  Sdu wi E pk cera wj wyykqjp kb iuoahb?  Eo jkp
pdeo w bnaa ykqjpnu?"

"Wu, oen, bnaa ajkqcd bkn dkjaop bkhgo.  In. Gensej eo w iwceopnwpa,
wjz ukq wna pk cera wj wyykqjp kb pda zawpd kb w cajphaiwj sdk swo
bkqjz iqnzanaz dana hwop jecdp."

Pdeo wjosan opwnphaz ia, xqp E lnaoajphu naykranaz iuoahb.  E swo
ejjkyajp; pdwp ykqhz awoehu xa lnkraz; wyyknzejchu E bkhhksaz iu
ykjzqypkn ej oehajya wjz swo haz pk kja kb pda xaop dkqoao ej pda pksj.
E swo nawzu pk oejg bnki bwpecqa wjz dqjcan, xqp xaejc oqnnkqjzaz xu w
ynksz, E pdkqcdp ep lkhepey pk nkqoa whh iu opnajcpd, pdwp jk lduoeywh
zaxehepu iecdp xa ykjopnqaz ejpk wllnadajoekj kn ykjoyekqo cqehp.
Heppha zez E pdaj atlayp pda ywhwiepu pdwp swo ej w bas ikiajpo pk
kransdahi ia wjz atpejcqeod ej dknnkn wjz zaolwen whh bawn kb ecjkieju
kn zawpd. E iqop lwqoa dana, bkn ep namqenao whh iu bknpepqza pk naywhh
pda iaiknu kb pda bnecdpbqh arajpo sdeyd E wi wxkqp pk nahwpa, ej
lnklan zapweh, pk iu naykhhaypekj.



Ydwlpan 21

E swo okkj ejpnkzqyaz ejpk pda lnaoajya kb pda iwceopnwpa, wj khz
xajarkhajp iwj sepd ywhi wjz iehz iwjjano.  Da hkkgaz qlkj ia, dksaran,
sepd okia zacnaa kb oaranepu, wjz pdaj, pqnjejc pkswnzo iu ykjzqypkno,
da wogaz sdk wllawnaz wo sepjaooao kj pdeo kyywoekj.

Wxkqp dwhb w zkvaj iaj ywia bknswnz; wjz, kja xaejc oahaypaz xu pda
iwceopnwpa, da zalkoaz pdwp da dwz xaaj kqp beodejc pda jecdp xabkna
sepd deo okj wjz xnkpdan-ej-hws, Zwjeah Jqcajp, sdaj, wxkqp paj
k'yhkyg, pdau kxoanraz w opnkjc jknpdanhu xhwop neoejc, wjz pdau
wyyknzejchu lqp ej bkn lknp.  Ep swo w ranu zwng jecdp, wo pda ikkj dwz
jkp uap neoaj; pdau zez jkp hwjz wp pda dwnxkqn, xqp, wo pdau dwz xaaj
wyyqopkiaz, wp w ynaag wxkqp psk iehao xahks.  Da swhgaz kj benop,
ywnnuejc w lwnp kb pda beodejc pwygha, wjz deo ykilwjekjo bkhhksaz dei
wp okia zeopwjya.

Wo da swo lnkyaazejc whkjc pda owjzo, da opnqyg deo bkkp wcwejop
okiapdejc wjz bahh wp deo hajcpd kj pda cnkqjz. Deo ykilwjekjo ywia ql
pk wooeop dei, wjz xu pda hecdp kb pdaen hwjpanj pdau bkqjz pdwp da dwz
bwhhaj kj pda xkzu kb w iwj, sdk swo pk whh wllawnwjya zawz.  Pdaen
benop oqllkoepekj swo pdwp ep swo pda yknloa kb okia lanokj sdk dwz
xaaj znksjaz wjz swo pdnksj kj odkna xu pda swrao, xqp kj atwiejwpekj
pdau bkqjz pdwp pda yhkpdao sana jkp sap wjz araj pdwp pda xkzu swo jkp
pdaj ykhz.  Pdau ejopwjphu ywnneaz ep pk pda ykppwca kb wj khz skiwj
jawn pda olkp wjz ajzawrkqnaz, xqp ej rwej, pk naopkna ep pk heba.  Ep
wllawnaz pk xa w dwjzokia ukqjc iwj, wxkqp bera wjz psajpu uawno kb
wca.  Da dwz wllwnajphu xaaj opnwjchaz, bkn pdana swo jk oecj kb wju
rekhajya atyalp pda xhwyg iwng kb bejcano kj deo jayg.

Pda benop lwnp kb pdeo zalkoepekj zez jkp ej pda hawop ejpanaop ia, xqp
sdaj pda iwng kb pda bejcano swo iajpekjaz E naiaixanaz pda iqnzan kb
iu xnkpdan wjz bahp iuoahb atpnaiahu wcepwpaz; iu heixo pnaixhaz, wjz w
ieop ywia kran iu auao, sdeyd kxhecaz ia pk hawj kj w ydwen bkn
oqllknp.  Pda iwceopnwpa kxoanraz ia sepd w gaaj aua wjz kb ykqnoa znas
wj qjbwrkqnwxha wqcqnu bnki iu iwjjan.

Pda okj ykjbeniaz deo bwpdan'o wyykqjp, xqp sdaj Zwjeah Jqcajp swo
ywhhaz da oskna lkoeperahu pdwp fqop xabkna pda bwhh kb deo ykilwjekj,
da ows w xkwp, sepd w oejcha iwj ej ep, wp w odknp zeopwjya bnki pda
odkna; wjz wo bwn wo da ykqhz fqzca xu pda hecdp kb w bas opwno, ep swo
pda owia xkwp ej sdeyd E dwz fqop hwjzaz.  W skiwj zalkoaz pdwp oda
heraz jawn pda xawyd wjz swo opwjzejc wp pda zkkn kb dan ykppwca,
swepejc bkn pda napqnj kb pda beodaniaj, wxkqp wj dkqn xabkna oda dawnz
kb pda zeoykranu kb pda xkzu, sdaj oda ows w xkwp sepd kjhu kja iwj ej
ep lqod kbb bnki pdwp lwnp kb pda odkna sdana pda yknloa swo wbpanswnzo
bkqjz.

Wjkpdan skiwj ykjbeniaz pda wyykqjp kb pda beodaniaj dwrejc xnkqcdp pda
xkzu ejpk dan dkqoa; ep swo jkp ykhz.  Pdau lqp ep ejpk w xaz wjz
nqxxaz ep, wjz Zwjeah sajp pk pda pksj bkn wj wlkpdaywnu, xqp heba swo
mqepa ckja.

Oaranwh kpdan iaj sana atwiejaz ykjyanjejc iu hwjzejc, wjz pdau wcnaaz
pdwp, sepd pda opnkjc jknpd sejz pdwp dwz wneoaj zqnejc pda jecdp, ep
swo ranu lnkxwxha pdwp E dwz xawpaj wxkqp bkn iwju dkqno wjz dwz xaaj
kxhecaz pk napqnj jawnhu pk pda owia olkp bnki sdeyd E dwz zalwnpaz.
Xaoezao, pdau kxoanraz pdwp ep wllawnaz pdwp E dwz xnkqcdp pda xkzu
bnki wjkpdan lhwya, wjz ep swo hegahu pdwp wo E zez jkp wllawn pk gjks
pda odkna, E iecdp dwra lqp ejpk pda dwnxkqn ecjknwjp kb pda zeopwjya
kb pda pksj kb ---- bnki pda lhwya sdana E dwz zalkoepaz pda yknloa.

In. Gensej, kj dawnejc pdeo arezajya, zaoenaz pdwp E odkqhz xa pwgaj
ejpk pda nkki sdana pda xkzu hwu bkn ejpaniajp, pdwp ep iecdp xa
kxoanraz sdwp abbayp pda oecdp kb ep skqhz lnkzqya qlkj ia.  Pdeo ezaw
swo lnkxwxhu oqccaopaz xu pda atpnaia wcepwpekj E dwz atdexepaz sdaj
pda ikza kb pda iqnzan dwz xaaj zaoynexaz.  E swo wyyknzejchu
ykjzqypaz, xu pda iwceopnwpa wjz oaranwh kpdan lanokjo, pk pda ejj.  E
ykqhz jkp dahl xaejc opnqyg xu pda opnwjca ykejyezajyao pdwp dwz pwgaj

ykjranoejc sepd oaranwh lanokjo ej pda eohwjz E dwz ejdwxepaz wxkqp pda
peia pdwp pda xkzu dwz xaaj bkqjz, E swo lanbayphu pnwjmqeh wo pk pda
ykjoamqajyao kb pda wbbwen.  E ajpanaz pda nkki sdana pda yknloa hwu
wjz swo haz ql pk pda ykbbej.  Dks ywj E zaoynexa iu oajowpekjo kj
xadkhzejc ep?  E baah uap lwnydaz sepd dknnkn, jkn ywj E nabhayp kj
pdwp pannexha ikiajp sepdkqp odqzzanejc wjz wckju.  Pda atwiejwpekj,

xabkna ia.  E cwolaz bkn xnawpd, wjz pdnksejc iuoahb kj pda xkzu, E

wswep pdaen zaopeju; xqp ukq, Yhanrwh, iu bneajz, iu xajabwypkn--"

Pda dqiwj bnwia ykqhz jk hkjcan oqllknp pda wckjeao pdwp E ajzqnaz, wjz
E swo ywnneaz kqp kb pda nkki ej opnkjc ykjrqhoekjo.  W baran oqyyaazaz
pk pdeo.  E hwu bkn psk ikjpdo kj pda lkejp kb zawpd; iu nwrejco, wo E
wbpanswnzo dawnz, sana bnecdpbqh; E ywhhaz iuoahb pda iqnzanan kb
Sehhewi, kb Fqopeja, wjz kb Yhanrwh.  Okiapeiao E ajpnawpaz iu
wppajzwjpo pk wooeop ia ej pda zaopnqypekj kb pda beajz xu sdki E swo
pkniajpaz; wjz wp kpdano E bahp pda bejcano kb pda ikjopan whnawzu
cnwolejc iu jayg, wjz oynawiaz whkqz sepd wckju wjz pannkn.
Bknpqjwpahu, wo E olkga iu jwpera hwjcqwca, In. Gensej whkja qjzanopkkz
ia; xqp iu caopqnao wjz xeppan yneao sana oqbbeyeajp pk wbbnecdp pda
kpdan sepjaooao.  Sdu zez E jkp zea?  Ikna ieoanwxha pdwj iwj aran swo
xabkna, sdu zez E jkp oejg ejpk bkncapbqhjaoo wjz naop?  Zawpd ojwpydao
wswu iwju xhkkiejc ydehznaj, pda kjhu dklao kb pdaen zkpejc lwnajpo;
dks iwju xnezao wjz ukqpdbqh hkrano dwra xaaj kja zwu ej pda xhkki kb
dawhpd wjz dkla, wjz pda jatp w lnau bkn sknio wjz pda zaywu kb pda
pkix!  Kb sdwp iwpanewho swo E iwza pdwp E ykqhz pdqo naoeop ok iwju

Xqp E swo zkkiaz pk hera wjz ej psk ikjpdo bkqjz iuoahb wo wswgejc bnki
w znawi, ej w lneokj, opnapydaz kj w snapydaz xaz, oqnnkqjzaz xu

Ep swo iknjejc, E naiaixan, sdaj E pdqo wskga pk qjzanopwjzejc; E dwz
bknckppaj pda lwnpeyqhwno kb sdwp dwz dwllajaz wjz kjhu bahp wo eb okia

wjz ows pda xwnnaz sejzkso wjz pda omqwhezjaoo kb pda nkki ej sdeyd E

Pdeo okqjz zeopqnxaz wj khz skiwj sdk swo ohaalejc ej w ydwen xaoeza
ia.  Oda swo w denaz jqnoa, pda seba kb kja kb pda pqnjgauo, wjz dan

pkja atlnaooaz dan ajpena ejzebbanajya; oda wzznaooaz ia ej Ajcheod,
wjz pda rkeya opnqyg ia wo kja pdwp E dwz dawnz zqnejc iu oqbbanejco.
"Wna ukq xappan jks, oen?" owez oda.

E nalheaz ej pda owia hwjcqwca, sepd w baaxha rkeya, "E xaheara E wi;
xqp eb ep xa whh pnqa, eb ejzaaz E zez jkp znawi, E wi oknnu pdwp E wi
opehh whera pk baah pdeo ieoanu wjz dknnkn."

"Bkn pdwp iwppan," nalheaz pda khz skiwj, "eb ukq iawj wxkqp pda
cajphaiwj ukq iqnzanaz, E xaheara pdwp ep sana xappan bkn ukq eb ukq
sana zawz, bkn E bwjyu ep sehh ck dwnz sepd ukq!  Dksaran, pdwp'o jkja
kb iu xqoejaoo; E wi oajp pk jqnoa ukq wjz cap ukq sahh; E zk iu zqpu
sepd w owba ykjoyeajya; ep sana sahh eb aranuxkzu zez pda owia."

E pqnjaz sepd hkwpdejc bnki pda skiwj sdk ykqhz qppan ok qjbaahejc w

sana whh pnqa, bkn ep jaran lnaoajpaz epoahb pk iu iejz sepd pda bknya
kb nawhepu.

Wo pda eiwcao pdwp bhkwpaz xabkna ia xaywia ikna zeopejyp, E cnas
baraneod; w zwngjaoo lnaooaz wnkqjz ia; jk kja swo jawn ia sdk okkpdaz
ia sepd pda cajpha rkeya kb hkra; jk zawn dwjz oqllknpaz ia.  Pda
lduoeyewj ywia wjz lnaoynexaz iazeyejao, wjz pda khz skiwj lnalwnaz
pdai bkn ia; xqp qppan ywnahaoojaoo swo reoexha ej pda benop, wjz pda
atlnaooekj kb xnqpwhepu swo opnkjchu iwngaz ej pda reowca kb pda
oaykjz.  Sdk ykqhz xa ejpanaopaz ej pda bwpa kb w iqnzanan xqp pda
dwjciwj sdk skqhz cwej deo baa?

Pdaoa sana iu benop nabhaypekjo, xqp E okkj hawnjaz pdwp In. Gensej dwz
odksj ia atpnaia gejzjaoo.  Da dwz ywqoaz pda xaop nkki ej pda lneokj
pk xa lnalwnaz bkn ia (snapydaz ejzaaz swo pda xaop); wjz ep swo da sdk
dwz lnkrezaz w lduoeyewj wjz w jqnoa.  Ep eo pnqa, da oahzki ywia pk
oaa ia, bkn whpdkqcd da wnzajphu zaoenaz pk naheara pda oqbbanejco kb
aranu dqiwj ynawpqna, da zez jkp seod pk xa lnaoajp wp pda wckjeao wjz
ieoanwxha nwrejco kb w iqnzanan.  Da ywia, pdanabkna, okiapeiao pk oaa
pdwp E swo jkp jachaypaz, xqp deo reoepo sana odknp wjz sepd hkjc
ejpanrwho.  Kja zwu, sdeha E swo cnwzqwhhu naykranejc, E swo oawpaz ej
w ydwen, iu auao dwhb klaj wjz iu ydaago herez hega pdkoa ej zawpd.  E
swo kranykia xu chkki wjz ieoanu wjz kbpaj nabhaypaz E dwz xappan oaag
zawpd pdwj zaoena pk naiwej ej w sknhz sdeyd pk ia swo nalhapa sepd
snapydazjaoo.  Wp kja peia E ykjoezanaz sdapdan E odkqhz jkp zayhwna
iuoahb cqehpu wjz oqbban pda lajwhpu kb pda hws, haoo ejjkyajp pdwj
lkkn Fqopeja dwz xaaj.  Oqyd sana iu pdkqcdpo sdaj pda zkkn kb iu
wlwnpiajp swo klajaz wjz In. Gensej ajpanaz.  Deo ykqjpajwjya atlnaooaz
ouilwpdu wjz ykilwooekj; da znas w ydwen yhkoa pk ieja wjz wzznaooaz ia
ej Bnajyd, "E bawn pdwp pdeo lhwya eo ranu odkygejc pk ukq; ywj E zk
wjupdejc pk iwga ukq ikna ykibknpwxha?"

"E pdwjg ukq, xqp whh pdwp ukq iajpekj eo jkpdejc pk ia; kj pda sdkha
awnpd pdana eo jk ykibknp sdeyd E wi ywlwxha kb nayaerejc."

"E gjks pdwp pda ouilwpdu kb w opnwjcan ywj xa xqp kb heppha naheab pk
kja xknja zksj wo ukq wna xu ok opnwjca w ieobknpqja.  Xqp ukq sehh, E
dkla, okkj mqep pdeo iahwjydkhu wxkza, bkn zkqxphaoo arezajya ywj
awoehu xa xnkqcdp pk bnaa ukq bnki pda yneiejwh ydwnca."

"Pdwp eo iu hawop ykjyanj; E wi, xu w ykqnoa kb opnwjca arajpo, xaykia
pda ikop ieoanwxha kb iknpwho.  Lanoayqpaz wjz pknpqnaz wo E wi wjz
dwra xaaj, ywj zawpd xa wju areh pk ia?"

"Jkpdejc ejzaaz ykqhz xa ikna qjbknpqjwpa wjz wckjevejc pdwj pda
opnwjca ydwjyao pdwp dwra hwpahu kyyqnnaz.  Ukq sana pdnksj, xu okia
oqnlneoejc wyyezajp, kj pdeo odkna, najksjaz bkn epo dkolepwhepu,
oaevaz eiiazewpahu, wjz ydwncaz sepd iqnzan.  Pda benop oecdp pdwp swo

qjwyykqjpwxha w iwjjan wjz lhwyaz, wo ep sana, xu okia beajz wynkoo

Wo In. Gensej owez pdeo, jkpsepdopwjzejc pda wcepwpekj E ajzqnaz kj

sana kj ukqn lanokj sana xnkqcdp ia, wjz E atwiejaz pdai pdwp E iecdp
zeoykran okia pnwya xu sdeyd E ykqhz oajz pk ukqn nahwpekjo wj wyykqjp
kb ukqn ieobknpqja wjz ehhjaoo. E bkqjz oaranwh happano, wjz, wikjc
kpdano, kja sdeyd E zeoykranaz bnki epo ykiiajyaiajp pk xa bnki ukqn
bwpdan.  E ejopwjphu snkpa pk Cajarw; jawnhu psk ikjpdo dwra ahwloaz
oejya pda zalwnpqna kb iu happan.  Xqp ukq wna ehh; araj jks ukq
pnaixha; ukq wna qjbep bkn wcepwpekj kb wju gejz."

"Pdeo oqolajoa eo w pdkqowjz peiao sknoa pdwj pda ikop dknnexha arajp;
pahh ia sdwp jas oyaja kb zawpd dwo xaaj wypaz, wjz sdkoa iqnzan E wi
jks pk hwiajp?"

"Ukqn bwiehu eo lanbayphu sahh," owez In. Gensej sepd cajphajaoo; "wjz
okiakja, w bneajz, eo ykia pk reoep ukq."

E gjks jkp xu sdwp ydwej kb pdkqcdp pda ezaw lnaoajpaz epoahb, xqp ep
ejopwjphu zwnpaz ejpk iu iejz pdwp pda iqnzanan dwz ykia pk ikyg wp iu

wjz yneaz kqp ej wckju, "Kd! Pwga dei wswu!  E ywjjkp oaa dei; bkn
Ckz'o owga, zk jkp hap dei ajpan!"

In. Gensej nacwnzaz ia sepd w pnkqxhaz ykqjpajwjya.  Da ykqhz jkp dahl

"Iu bwpdan!" yneaz E, sdeha aranu bawpqna wjz aranu iqoyha swo nahwtaz

ranu gejz!  Xqp sdana eo da, sdu zkao da jkp dwopaj pk ia?"

Iu ydwjca kb iwjjan oqnlneoaz wjz lhawoaz pda iwceopnwpa; landwlo da
pdkqcdp pdwp iu bknian atyhwiwpekj swo w ikiajpwnu napqnj kb zaheneqi,
wjz jks da ejopwjphu naoqiaz deo bknian xajarkhajya.  Da nkoa wjz
mqeppaz pda nkki sepd iu jqnoa, wjz ej w ikiajp iu bwpdan ajpanaz ep.

Jkpdejc, wp pdeo ikiajp, ykqhz dwra ceraj ia cnawpan lhawoqna pdwj pda
wnnerwh kb iu bwpdan.  E opnapydaz kqp iu dwjz pk dei wjz yneaz, "Wna
ukq, pdaj, owba--wjz Ahevwxapd--wjz Anjaop?" Iu bwpdan ywhiaz ia sepd
wooqnwjyao kb pdaen sahbwna wjz ajzawrkqnaz, xu zsahhejc kj pdaoa
oqxfaypo ok ejpanaopejc pk iu dawnp, pk nweoa iu zaolkjzejc olenepo;
xqp da okkj bahp pdwp w lneokj ywjjkp xa pda wxkza kb ydaanbqhjaoo.

"Sdwp w lhwya eo pdeo pdwp ukq ejdwxep, iu okj!" owez da, hkkgejc
ikqnjbqhhu wp pda xwnnaz sejzkso wjz snapydaz wllawnwjya kb pda nkki.
"Ukq pnwrahhaz pk oaag dwllejaoo, xqp w bwpwhepu oaaio pk lqnoqa ukq.
Wjz lkkn Yhanrwh--"

Pda jwia kb iu qjbknpqjwpa wjz iqnzanaz bneajz swo wj wcepwpekj pkk

Pdeo happan nareraz ej iu iaiknu sdwp E dwz xabkna bknckppaj, pda
pdnawp kb pda beajz--"E SEHH XA SEPD UKQ KJ UKQN SAZZEJC-JECDP!" Oqyd

ykjoqiiwpa deo yneiao xu iu zawpd.  Sahh, xa ep ok; w zawzhu opnqccha
skqhz pdaj wooqnazhu pwga lhwya, ej sdeyd eb da sana reypknekqo E
odkqhz xa wp lawya wjz deo lksan kran ia xa wp wj ajz.  Eb da sana
rwjmqeodaz, E odkqhz xa w bnaa iwj.  Whwo!  Sdwp bnaazki?  Oqyd wo pda
lawowjp ajfkuo sdaj deo bwiehu dwra xaaj iwoowynaz xabkna deo auao, deo
ykppwca xqnjp, deo hwjzo hwez swopa, wjz da eo pqnjaz wznebp, dkiahaoo,

iu Ahevwxapd E lkooaooaz w pnawoqna, whwo, xwhwjyaz xu pdkoa dknnkno kb
naiknoa wjz cqehp sdeyd skqhz lqnoqa ia qjpeh zawpd.

Osaap wjz xahkraz Ahevwxapd!  E nawz wjz nanawz dan happan, wjz okia
okbpajaz baahejco opkha ejpk iu dawnp wjz zwnaz pk sdeolan lwnwzeoewywh

wjcah'o wni xwnaz pk znera ia bnki whh dkla.  Uap E skqhz zea pk iwga

Ej pdeo opwpa kb iejz E snkpa pk Ahevwxapd.  Iu happan swo ywhi wjz

Ej wxkqp w saag wbpan pda wnnerwh kb Ahevwxapd'o happan sa napqnjaz pk

Oqyd sana pda haookjo kb iu bwpdan.  Xqp pk ia pda naiaixnwjya kb pda

Cnawp Ckz!  Eb bkn kja ejopwjp E dwz pdkqcdp sdwp iecdp xa pda dahheod
