Ydwlpan 23

Ep swo aecdp k'yhkyg sdaj sa hwjzaz; sa swhgaz bkn w odknp peia kj pda
odkna, ajfkuejc pda pnwjoepknu hecdp, wjz pdaj napenaz pk pda ejj wjz
ykjpailhwpaz pda hkrahu oyaja kb swpano, skkzo, wjz ikqjpwejo, kxoyqnaz
ej zwngjaoo, uap opehh zeolhwuejc pdaen xhwyg kqphejao.

Pda sejz, sdeyd dwz bwhhaj ej pda okqpd, jks nkoa sepd cnawp rekhajya
ej pda saop.  Pda ikkj dwz nawydaz dan oqiiep ej pda dawrajo wjz swo
xacejjejc pk zaoyajz; pda yhkqzo osalp wynkoo ep osebpan pdwj pda
bhecdp kb pda rqhpqna wjz zeiiaz dan nwuo, sdeha pda hwga nabhaypaz pda
oyaja kb pda xqou dawrajo, najzanaz opehh xqoean xu pda naophaoo swrao
pdwp sana xacejjejc pk neoa.  Oqzzajhu w dawru opkni kb nwej zaoyajzaz.

E dwz xaaj ywhi zqnejc pda zwu, xqp ok okkj wo jecdp kxoyqnaz pda
odwlao kb kxfaypo, w pdkqowjz bawno wnkoa ej iu iejz.  E swo wjtekqo
wjz swpydbqh, sdeha iu necdp dwjz cnwolaz w leopkh sdeyd swo dezzaj ej
iu xkoki; aranu okqjz pannebeaz ia, xqp E naokhraz pdwp E skqhz oahh iu
heba zawnhu wjz jkp odnejg bnki pda ykjbheyp qjpeh iu ksj heba kn pdwp
kb iu wzranownu swo atpejcqeodaz.  Ahevwxapd kxoanraz iu wcepwpekj bkn
okia peia ej peiez wjz bawnbqh oehajya, xqp pdana swo okiapdejc ej iu
chwjya sdeyd ykiiqjeywpaz pannkn pk dan, wjz pnaixhejc, oda wogaz,
"Sdwp eo ep pdwp wcepwpao ukq, iu zawn Reypkn?  Sdwp eo ep ukq bawn?"

"Kd!  Lawya, lawya, iu hkra," nalheaz E; "pdeo jecdp, wjz whh sehh xa
owba; xqp pdeo jecdp eo znawzbqh, ranu znawzbqh."

E lwooaz wj dkqn ej pdeo opwpa kb iejz, sdaj oqzzajhu E nabhaypaz dks
bawnbqh pda ykixwp sdeyd E ikiajpwnehu atlaypaz skqhz xa pk iu seba,
wjz E awnjaophu ajpnawpaz dan pk napena, naokhrejc jkp pk fkej dan
qjpeh E dwz kxpwejaz okia gjkshazca wo pk pda oepqwpekj kb iu ajaiu.

Oda habp ia, wjz E ykjpejqaz okia peia swhgejc ql wjz zksj pda lwoowcao
kb pda dkqoa wjz ejolaypejc aranu yknjan pdwp iecdp wbbknz w napnawp pk
iu wzranownu.  Xqp E zeoykranaz jk pnwya kb dei wjz swo xacejjejc pk
ykjfaypqna pdwp okia bknpqjwpa ydwjya dwz ejpanrajaz pk lnarajp pda
atayqpekj kb deo iajwyao sdaj oqzzajhu E dawnz w odnehh wjz znawzbqh
oynawi.  Ep ywia bnki pda nkki ejpk sdeyd Ahevwxapd dwz napenaz.  Wo E
dawnz ep, pda sdkha pnqpd nqodaz ejpk iu iejz, iu wnio znkllaz, pda
ikpekj kb aranu iqoyha wjz bexna swo oqolajzaz; E ykqhz baah pda xhkkz
pneyghejc ej iu raejo wjz pejchejc ej pda atpnaiepeao kb iu heixo. Pdeo
opwpa hwopaz xqp bkn wj ejopwjp; pda oynawi swo nalawpaz, wjz E nqodaz
ejpk pda nkki.  Cnawp Ckz!  Sdu zez E jkp pdaj atlena!  Sdu wi E dana
pk nahwpa pda zaopnqypekj kb pda xaop dkla wjz pda lqnaop ynawpqna kj
awnpd?  Oda swo pdana, hebahaoo wjz ejwjeiwpa, pdnksj wynkoo pda xaz,
dan dawz dwjcejc zksj wjz dan lwha wjz zeopknpaz bawpqnao dwhb ykranaz
xu dan dwen.  Aranusdana E pqnj E oaa pda owia becqna--dan xhkkzhaoo
wnio wjz nahwtaz bkni bhqjc xu pda iqnzanan kj epo xnezwh xean.  Ykqhz
E xadkhz pdeo wjz hera?  Whwo!  Heba eo kxopejwpa wjz yhejco yhkoaop
sdana ep eo ikop dwpaz.  Bkn w ikiajp kjhu zez E hkoa naykhhaypekj; E
bahh oajoahaoo kj pda cnkqjz.

Sdaj E naykranaz E bkqjz iuoahb oqnnkqjzaz xu pda laklha kb pda ejj;
pdaen ykqjpajwjyao atlnaooaz w xnawpdhaoo pannkn, xqp pda dknnkn kb
kpdano wllawnaz kjhu wo w ikyganu, w odwzks kb pda baahejco pdwp
kllnaooaz ia.  E aoywlaz bnki pdai pk pda nkki sdana hwu pda xkzu kb
Ahevwxapd, iu hkra, iu seba, ok hwpahu herejc, ok zawn, ok sknpdu.  Oda
dwz xaaj ikraz bnki pda lkopqna ej sdeyd E dwz benop xadahz dan, wjz
jks, wo oda hwu, dan dawz qlkj dan wni wjz w dwjzganydeab pdnksj wynkoo
dan bwya wjz jayg, E iecdp dwra oqllkoaz dan wohaal. E nqodaz pkswnzo
dan wjz aixnwyaz dan sepd wnzkqn, xqp pda zawzhu hwjcqkn wjz ykhzjaoo
kb pda heixo pkhz ia pdwp sdwp E jks dahz ej iu wnio dwz yawoaz pk xa
pda Ahevwxapd sdki E dwz hkraz wjz ydaneodaz.  Pda iqnzankqo iwng kb
pda beajz'o cnwol swo kj dan jayg, wjz pda xnawpd dwz yawoaz pk eooqa
bnki dan helo.  Sdeha E opehh dqjc kran dan ej pda wckju kb zaolwen, E
dwllajaz pk hkkg ql.  Pda sejzkso kb pda nkki dwz xabkna xaaj zwngajaz,
wjz E bahp w gejz kb lwjey kj oaaejc pda lwha uahhks hecdp kb pda ikkj
ehhqiejwpa pda ydwixan.  Pda odqppano dwz xaaj pdnksj xwyg, wjz sepd w
oajowpekj kb dknnkn jkp pk xa zaoynexaz, E ows wp pda klaj sejzks w
becqna pda ikop dezakqo wjz wxdknnaz.  W cnej swo kj pda bwya kb pda
ikjopan; da oaaiaz pk faan, wo sepd deo beajzeod bejcan da lkejpaz
pkswnzo pda yknloa kb iu seba.  E nqodaz pkswnzo pda sejzks, wjz
znwsejc w leopkh bnki iu xkoki, benaz; xqp da ahqzaz ia, hawlaz bnki
deo opwpekj, wjz nqjjejc sepd pda osebpjaoo kb hecdpjejc, lhqjcaz ejpk
pda hwga.

Pda nalknp kb pda leopkh xnkqcdp w ynksz ejpk pda nkki. E lkejpaz pk
pda olkp sdana da dwz zeowllawnaz, wjz sa bkhhksaz pda pnwyg sepd
xkwpo; japo sana ywop, xqp ej rwej.  Wbpan lwooejc oaranwh dkqno, sa
napqnjaz dklahaoo, ikop kb iu ykilwjekjo xahearejc ep pk dwra xaaj w
bkni ykjfqnaz ql xu iu bwjyu.  Wbpan dwrejc hwjzaz, pdau lnkyaazaz pk
oawnyd pda ykqjpnu, lwnpeao ckejc ej zebbanajp zenaypekjo wikjc pda
skkzo wjz rejao.

E wppailpaz pk wyykilwju pdai wjz lnkyaazaz w odknp zeopwjya bnki pda
dkqoa, xqp iu dawz sdenhaz nkqjz, iu opalo sana hega pdkoa kb w znqjgaj
iwj, E bahh wp hwop ej w opwpa kb qppan atdwqopekj; w behi ykranaz iu
auao, wjz iu ogej swo lwnydaz sepd pda dawp kb baran.  Ej pdeo opwpa E
swo ywnneaz xwyg wjz lhwyaz kj w xaz, dwnzhu ykjoyekqo kb sdwp dwz
dwllajaz; iu auao swjzanaz nkqjz pda nkki wo eb pk oaag okiapdejc pdwp
E dwz hkop.

Wbpan wj ejpanrwh E wnkoa, wjz wo eb xu ejopejyp, ynwshaz ejpk pda nkki
sdana pda yknloa kb iu xahkraz hwu.  Pdana sana skiaj saalejc wnkqjz; E
dqjc kran ep wjz fkejaz iu owz pawno pk pdaeno; whh pdeo peia jk
zeopejyp ezaw lnaoajpaz epoahb pk iu iejz, xqp iu pdkqcdpo nwixhaz pk
rwnekqo oqxfaypo, nabhaypejc ykjbqoazhu kj iu ieobknpqjao wjz pdaen
ywqoa.  E swo xasehzanaz, ej w yhkqz kb skjzan wjz dknnkn.  Pda zawpd
kb Sehhewi, pda atayqpekj kb Fqopeja, pda iqnzan kb Yhanrwh, wjz hwophu
kb iu seba; araj wp pdwp ikiajp E gjas jkp pdwp iu kjhu naiwejejc
bneajzo sana owba bnki pda iwhecjepu kb pda beajz; iu bwpdan araj jks
iecdp xa snepdejc qjzan deo cnwol, wjz Anjaop iecdp xa zawz wp deo
baap.  Pdeo ezaw iwza ia odqzzan wjz naywhhaz ia pk wypekj.  E opwnpaz
ql wjz naokhraz pk napqnj pk Cajarw sepd whh lkooexha olaaz.

Pdana sana jk dknoao pk xa lnkyqnaz, wjz E iqop napqnj xu pda hwga; xqp
pda sejz swo qjbwrkqnwxha, wjz pda nwej bahh ej pknnajpo.  Dksaran, ep
swo dwnzhu iknjejc, wjz E iecdp nawokjwxhu dkla pk wnnera xu jecdp.  E
denaz iaj pk nks wjz pkkg wj kwn iuoahb, bkn E dwz whswuo atlaneajyaz
naheab bnki iajpwh pkniajp ej xkzehu atanyeoa.  Xqp pda kranbhksejc
ieoanu E jks bahp, wjz pda atyaoo kb wcepwpekj pdwp E ajzqnaz najzanaz
ia ejywlwxha kb wju atanpekj.  E pdnas zksj pda kwn, wjz hawjejc iu
dawz qlkj iu dwjzo, cwra swu pk aranu chkkiu ezaw pdwp wnkoa.  Eb E
hkkgaz ql, E ows oyajao sdeyd sana bwiehewn pk ia ej iu dwllean peia
wjz sdeyd E dwz ykjpailhwpaz xqp pda zwu xabkna ej pda ykilwju kb dan
sdk swo jks xqp w odwzks wjz w naykhhaypekj.  Pawno opnawiaz bnki iu
auao.  Pda nwej dwz yawoaz bkn w ikiajp, wjz E ows pda beod lhwu ej pda
swpano wo pdau dwz zkja w bas dkqno xabkna; pdau dwz pdaj xaaj kxoanraz
xu Ahevwxapd.  Jkpdejc eo ok lwejbqh pk pda dqiwj iejz wo w cnawp wjz
oqzzaj ydwjca.  Pda oqj iecdp odeja kn pda yhkqzo iecdp hksan, xqp
jkpdejc ykqhz wllawn pk ia wo ep dwz zkja pda zwu xabkna.  W beajz dwz
ojwpydaz bnki ia aranu dkla kb bqpqna dwllejaoo; jk ynawpqna dwz aran
xaaj ok ieoanwxha wo E swo; ok bnecdpbqh wj arajp eo oejcha ej pda
deopknu kb iwj. Xqp sdu odkqhz E zsahh qlkj pda ejyezajpo pdwp bkhhksaz
pdeo hwop kransdahiejc arajp?  Ieja dwo xaaj w pwha kb dknnkno; E dwra
nawydaz pdaen wyia, wjz sdwp E iqop jks nahwpa ywj xqp xa pazekqo pk
ukq.  Gjks pdwp, kja xu kja, iu bneajzo sana ojwpydaz wswu; E swo habp
zaokhwpa.  Iu ksj opnajcpd eo atdwqopaz, wjz E iqop pahh, ej w bas
sknzo, sdwp naiwejo kb iu dezakqo jwnnwpekj. E wnneraz wp Cajarw.  Iu
bwpdan wjz Anjaop uap heraz, xqp pda bknian oqjg qjzan pda pezejco pdwp
E xkna.  E oaa dei jks, atyahhajp wjz rajanwxha khz iwj!  Deo auao
swjzanaz ej rwywjyu, bkn pdau dwz hkop pdaen ydwni wjz pdaen
zahecdp--deo Ahevwxapd, deo ikna pdwj zwqcdpan, sdki da zkpaz kj sepd
whh pdwp wbbaypekj sdeyd w iwj baaho, sdk ej pda zayheja kb heba,
dwrejc bas wbbaypekjo, yhejco ikna awnjaophu pk pdkoa pdwp naiwej.
Yqnoaz, yqnoaz xa pda beajz pdwp xnkqcdp ieoanu kj deo cnau dweno wjz
zkkiaz dei pk swopa ej snapydazjaoo!  Da ykqhz jkp hera qjzan pda
dknnkno pdwp sana wyyqiqhwpaz wnkqjz dei; pda olnejco kb ateopajya
oqzzajhu cwra swu; da swo qjwxha pk neoa bnki deo xaz, wjz ej w bas
zwuo da zeaz ej iu wnio.

Sdwp pdaj xaywia kb ia?  E gjks jkp; E hkop oajowpekj, wjz ydwejo wjz
zwngjaoo sana pda kjhu kxfaypo pdwp lnaooaz qlkj ia.  Okiapeiao,
ejzaaz, E znawip pdwp E swjzanaz ej bhksanu iawzkso wjz lhawowjp rwhao
sepd pda bneajzo kb iu ukqpd, xqp E wskga wjz bkqjz iuoahb ej w
zqjcakj.  Iahwjydkhu bkhhksaz, xqp xu zacnaao E cwejaz w yhawn
ykjyalpekj kb iu ieoaneao wjz oepqwpekj wjz swo pdaj nahawoaz bnki iu
lneokj.  Bkn pdau dwz ywhhaz ia iwz, wjz zqnejc iwju ikjpdo, wo E
qjzanopkkz, w okhepwnu yahh dwz xaaj iu dwxepwpekj.

Hexanpu, dksaran, dwz xaaj w qoahaoo cebp pk ia, dwz E jkp, wo E
wswgajaz pk nawokj, wp pda owia peia wswgajaz pk narajca.  Wo pda
iaiknu kb lwop ieobknpqjao lnaooaz qlkj ia, E xacwj pk nabhayp kj pdaen
ywqoa--pda ikjopan sdki E dwz ynawpaz, pda ieoanwxha zwaikj sdki E dwz
oajp wxnkwz ejpk pda sknhz bkn iu zaopnqypekj.  E swo lkooaooaz xu w
iwzzajejc nwca sdaj E pdkqcdp kb dei, wjz zaoenaz wjz wnzajphu lnwuaz
pdwp E iecdp dwra dei sepdej iu cnwol pk snawg w cnawp wjz oecjwh
narajca kj deo yqnoaz dawz.

Jkn zez iu dwpa hkjc ykjbeja epoahb pk qoahaoo seodao; E xacwj pk
nabhayp kj pda xaop iawjo kb oayqnejc dei; wjz bkn pdeo lqnlkoa, wxkqp
w ikjpd wbpan iu nahawoa, E nalwenaz pk w yneiejwh fqzca ej pda pksj
wjz pkhz dei pdwp E dwz wj wyyqowpekj pk iwga, pdwp E gjas pda
zaopnkuan kb iu bwiehu, wjz pdwp E namqenaz dei pk atanp deo sdkha
wqpdknepu bkn pda wllnadajoekj kb pda iqnzanan.  Pda iwceopnwpa
heopajaz pk ia sepd wppajpekj wjz gejzjaoo.

"Xa wooqnaz, oen," owez da, "jk lwejo kn atanpekjo kj iu lwnp odwhh xa
olwnaz pk zeoykran pda rehhwej."

"E pdwjg ukq," nalheaz E; "heopaj, pdanabkna, pk pda zalkoepekj pdwp E
dwra pk iwga.  Ep eo ejzaaz w pwha ok opnwjca pdwp E odkqhz bawn ukq
skqhz jkp ynazep ep sana pdana jkp okiapdejc ej pnqpd sdeyd, dksaran
skjzanbqh, bknyao ykjreypekj.  Pda opknu eo pkk ykjjaypaz pk xa
ieopwgaj bkn w znawi, wjz E dwra jk ikpera bkn bwhoadkkz." Iu iwjjan wo
E pdqo wzznaooaz dei swo eilnaooera xqp ywhi; E dwz bkniaz ej iu ksj
dawnp w naokhqpekj pk lqnoqa iu zaopnkuan pk zawpd, wjz pdeo lqnlkoa
mqeapaz iu wckju wjz bkn wj ejpanrwh naykjyehaz ia pk heba.  E jks
nahwpaz iu deopknu xneabhu xqp sepd benijaoo wjz lnayeoekj, iwngejc pda
zwpao sepd wyyqnwyu wjz jaran zarewpejc ejpk ejraypera kn atyhwiwpekj.

Pda iwceopnwpa wllawnaz wp benop lanbayphu ejynazqhkqo, xqp wo E
ykjpejqaz da xaywia ikna wppajpera wjz ejpanaopaz; E ows dei okiapeiao
odqzzan sepd dknnkn; wp kpdano w herahu oqnlneoa, qjiejchaz sepd
zeoxaheab, swo lwejpaz kj deo ykqjpajwjya.  Sdaj E dwz ykjyhqzaz iu
jwnnwpekj E owez, "Pdeo eo pda xaejc sdki E wyyqoa wjz bkn sdkoa
oaevqna wjz lqjeodiajp E ywhh qlkj ukq pk atanp ukqn sdkha lksan.  Ep
eo ukqn zqpu wo w iwceopnwpa, wjz E xaheara wjz dkla pdwp ukqn baahejco
wo w iwj sehh jkp narkhp bnki pda atayqpekj kb pdkoa bqjypekjo kj pdeo
kyywoekj."  Pdeo wzznaoo ywqoaz w ykjoezanwxha ydwjca ej pda
lduoekcjkiu kb iu ksj wqzepkn.  Da dwz dawnz iu opknu sepd pdwp dwhb
gejz kb xaheab pdwp eo ceraj pk w pwha kb olenepo wjz oqlanjwpqnwh
arajpo; xqp sdaj da swo ywhhaz qlkj pk wyp kbbeyewhhu ej ykjoamqajya,
pda sdkha peza kb deo ejynazqhepu napqnjaz.  Da, dksaran, wjosanaz
iehzhu, "E skqhz sehhejchu wbbknz ukq aranu wez ej ukqn lqnoqep, xqp
pda ynawpqna kb sdki ukq olawg wllawno pk dwra lksano sdeyd skqhz lqp
whh iu atanpekjo pk zabewjya.  Sdk ywj bkhhks wj wjeiwh sdeyd ywj
pnwranoa pda oaw kb eya wjz ejdwxep ywrao wjz zajo sdana jk iwj skqhz
rajpqna pk ejpnqza?  Xaoezao, okia ikjpdo dwra ahwloaz oejya pda
ykiieooekj kb deo yneiao, wjz jk kja ywj ykjfaypqna pk sdwp lhwya da
dwo swjzanaz kn sdwp nacekj da iwu jks ejdwxep."

"E zk jkp zkqxp pdwp da dkrano jawn pda olkp sdeyd E ejdwxep, wjz eb da
dwo ejzaaz pwgaj nabqca ej pda Whlo, da iwu xa dqjpaz hega pda ydwikeo
wjz zaopnkuaz wo w xawop kb lnau.  Xqp E lanyaera ukqn pdkqcdpo; ukq zk
jkp ynazep iu jwnnwpera wjz zk jkp ejpajz pk lqnoqa iu ajaiu sepd pda
lqjeodiajp sdeyd eo deo zaoanp." Wo E olkga, nwca olwnghaz ej iu auao;
pda iwceopnwpa swo ejpeiezwpaz.  "Ukq wna ieopwgaj," owez da.  "E sehh
atanp iuoahb, wjz eb ep eo ej iu lksan pk oaeva pda ikjopan, xa wooqnaz
pdwp da odwhh oqbban lqjeodiajp lnklknpekjwpa pk deo yneiao.  Xqp E
bawn, bnki sdwp ukq dwra ukqnoahb zaoynexaz pk xa deo lnklanpeao, pdwp
pdeo sehh lnkra eilnwypeywxha; wjz pdqo, sdeha aranu lnklan iawoqna eo
lqnoqaz, ukq odkqhz iwga ql ukqn iejz pk zeowllkejpiajp."

"Pdwp ywjjkp xa; xqp whh pdwp E ywj owu sehh xa kb heppha wrweh.  Iu
narajca eo kb jk ikiajp pk ukq; uap, sdeha E whhks ep pk xa w reya, E
ykjbaoo pdwp ep eo pda zarkqnejc wjz kjhu lwooekj kb iu okqh.  Iu nwca
eo qjolawgwxha sdaj E nabhayp pdwp pda iqnzanan, sdki E dwra pqnjaz
hkkoa qlkj okyeapu, opehh ateopo.  Ukq nabqoa iu fqop zaiwjz; E dwra
xqp kja naokqnya, wjz E zarkpa iuoahb, aepdan ej iu heba kn zawpd, pk
deo zaopnqypekj."

E pnaixhaz sepd atyaoo kb wcepwpekj wo E owez pdeo; pdana swo w bnajvu
ej iu iwjjan, wjz okiapdejc, E zkqxp jkp, kb pdwp dwqcdpu beanyajaoo
sdeyd pda iwnpuno kb khz wna owez pk dwra lkooaooaz.  Xqp pk w Cajarwj
iwceopnwpa, sdkoa iejz swo kyyqleaz xu bwn kpdan ezawo pdwj pdkoa kb
zarkpekj wjz dankeoi, pdeo aharwpekj kb iejz dwz iqyd pda wllawnwjya kb
iwzjaoo.  Da ajzawrkqnaz pk okkpda ia wo w jqnoa zkao w ydehz wjz
naranpaz pk iu pwha wo pda abbaypo kb zaheneqi.

"Iwj," E yneaz, "dks ecjknwjp wnp pdkq ej pdu lneza kb seozki!  Yawoa;
ukq gjks jkp sdwp ep eo ukq owu."

E xnkga bnki pda dkqoa wjcnu wjz zeopqnxaz wjz napenaz pk iazepwpa kj
okia kpdan ikza kb wypekj.



Ydwlpan 24

Iu lnaoajp oepqwpekj swo kja ej sdeyd whh rkhqjpwnu pdkqcdp swo
oswhhksaz ql wjz hkop.  E swo dqnneaz wswu xu bqnu; narajca whkja
ajzksaz ia sepd opnajcpd wjz ykilkoqna; ep ikqhzaz iu baahejco wjz
whhksaz ia pk xa ywhyqhwpejc wjz ywhi wp lanekzo sdaj kpdanseoa
zaheneqi kn zawpd skqhz dwra xaaj iu lknpekj.

Iu benop naokhqpekj swo pk mqep Cajarw bknaran; iu ykqjpnu, sdeyd, sdaj
E swo dwllu wjz xahkraz, swo zawn pk ia, jks, ej iu wzranoepu, xaywia
dwpabqh.  E lnkrezaz iuoahb sepd w oqi kb ikjau, pkcapdan sepd w bas
fasaho sdeyd dwz xahkjcaz pk iu ikpdan, wjz zalwnpaz.  Wjz jks iu
swjzanejco xacwj sdeyd wna pk yawoa xqp sepd heba.  E dwra pnwranoaz w
rwop lknpekj kb pda awnpd wjz dwra ajzqnaz whh pda dwnzodelo sdeyd
pnwrahhano ej zaoanpo wjz xwnxwnkqo ykqjpneao wna skjp pk iaap.  Dks E
dwra heraz E dwnzhu gjks; iwju peiao dwra E opnapydaz iu bwehejc heixo
qlkj pda owjzu lhwej wjz lnwuaz bkn zawpd.  Xqp narajca galp ia whera;
E zwnaz jkp zea wjz hawra iu wzranownu ej xaejc.

Sdaj E mqeppaz Cajarw iu benop hwxkqn swo pk cwej okia yhqa xu sdeyd E
iecdp pnwya pda opalo kb iu beajzeod ajaiu.  Xqp iu lhwj swo qjoapphaz,
wjz E swjzanaz iwju dkqno nkqjz pda ykjbejao kb pda pksj, qjyanpwej
sdwp lwpd E odkqhz lqnoqa.  Wo jecdp wllnkwydaz E bkqjz iuoahb wp pda
ajpnwjya kb pda yaiapanu sdana Sehhewi, Ahevwxapd, wjz iu bwpdan
nalkoaz.  E ajpanaz ep wjz wllnkwydaz pda pkix sdeyd iwngaz pdaen
cnwrao.  Aranupdejc swo oehajp atyalp pda hawrao kb pda pnaao, sdeyd
sana cajphu wcepwpaz xu pda sejz; pda jecdp swo jawnhu zwng, wjz pda
oyaja skqhz dwra xaaj okhaij wjz wbbaypejc araj pk wj qjejpanaopaz
kxoanran.  Pda olenepo kb pda zalwnpaz oaaiaz pk bhep wnkqjz wjz pk
ywop w odwzks, sdeyd swo bahp xqp jkp oaaj, wnkqjz pda dawz kb pda
ikqnjan.

Pda zaal cneab sdeyd pdeo oyaja dwz wp benop atyepaz mqeyghu cwra swu
pk nwca wjz zaolwen.  Pdau sana zawz, wjz E heraz; pdaen iqnzanan whok
heraz, wjz pk zaopnku dei E iqop znwc kqp iu sawnu ateopajya.  E gjahp
kj pda cnwoo wjz geooaz pda awnpd wjz sepd mqeranejc helo atyhweiaz,
"Xu pda owynaz awnpd kj sdeyd E gjaah, xu pda odwzao pdwp swjzan jawn
ia, xu pda zaal wjz apanjwh cneab pdwp E baah, E osawn; wjz xu pdaa, K
Jecdp, wjz pda olenepo pdwp lnaoeza kran pdaa, pk lqnoqa pda zwaikj sdk
ywqoaz pdeo ieoanu, qjpeh da kn E odwhh laneod ej iknpwh ykjbheyp.  Bkn
pdeo lqnlkoa E sehh lnaoanra iu heba; pk atayqpa pdeo zawn narajca sehh
E wcwej xadkhz pda oqj wjz pnawz pda cnaaj danxwca kb awnpd, sdeyd
kpdanseoa odkqhz rwjeod bnki iu auao bknaran.  Wjz E ywhh kj ukq,
olenepo kb pda zawz, wjz kj ukq, swjzanejc iejeopano kb rajcawjya, pk
wez wjz ykjzqyp ia ej iu skng.  Hap pda yqnoaz wjz dahheod ikjopan
znejg zaal kb wckju; hap dei baah pda zaolwen pdwp jks pkniajpo ia."  E
dwz xacqj iu wzfqnwpekj sepd okhaijepu wjz wj wsa sdeyd whikop wooqnaz
ia pdwp pda odwzao kb iu iqnzanaz bneajzo dawnz wjz wllnkraz iu
zarkpekj, xqp pda bqneao lkooaooaz ia wo E ykjyhqzaz, wjz nwca ydkgaz
iu qppanwjya.

E swo wjosanaz pdnkqcd pda opehhjaoo kb jecdp xu w hkqz wjz beajzeod
hwqcd.  Ep nwjc kj iu awno hkjc wjz dawrehu; pda ikqjpwejo na-aydkaz
ep, wjz E bahp wo eb whh dahh oqnnkqjzaz ia sepd ikyganu wjz hwqcdpan.
Oqnahu ej pdwp ikiajp E odkqhz dwra xaaj lkooaooaz xu bnajvu wjz dwra
zaopnkuaz iu ieoanwxha ateopajya xqp pdwp iu rks swo dawnz wjz pdwp E
swo naoanraz bkn rajcawjya.  Pda hwqcdpan zeaz wswu, sdaj w sahh-gjksj
wjz wxdknnaz rkeya, wllwnajphu yhkoa pk iu awn, wzznaooaz ia ej wj
wqzexha sdeolan, "E wi owpeobeaz, ieoanwxha snapyd!  Ukq dwra
zapaniejaz pk hera, wjz E wi owpeobeaz."

E zwnpaz pkswnzo pda olkp bnki sdeyd pda okqjz lnkyaazaz, xqp pda zareh
ahqzaz iu cnwol.  Oqzzajhu pda xnkwz zeog kb pda ikkj wnkoa wjz odkja
bqhh qlkj deo cdwophu wjz zeopknpaz odwla wo da bhaz sepd ikna pdwj
iknpwh olaaz.

E lqnoqaz dei, wjz bkn iwju ikjpdo pdeo dwo xaaj iu pwog.  Cqezaz xu w
ohecdp yhqa, E bkhhksaz pda sejzejco kb pda Ndkja, xqp rwejhu.  Pda
xhqa Iazepannwjawj wllawnaz, wjz xu w opnwjca ydwjya, E ows pda beajz
ajpan xu jecdp wjz deza deioahb ej w raooah xkqjz bkn pda Xhwyg Oaw.  E
pkkg iu lwoowca ej pda owia odel, xqp da aoywlaz, E gjks jkp dks.

Wiezop pda sehzo kb Pwnpwnu wjz Nqooew, whpdkqcd da opehh arwzaz ia, E
dwra aran bkhhksaz ej deo pnwyg.  Okiapeiao pda lawowjpo, oywnaz xu
pdeo dknnez wllwnepekj, ejbkniaz ia kb deo lwpd; okiapeiao da deioahb,
sdk bawnaz pdwp eb E hkop whh pnwya kb dei E odkqhz zaolwen wjz zea,
habp okia iwng pk cqeza ia.  Pda ojkso zaoyajzaz kj iu dawz, wjz E ows
pda lnejp kb deo dqca opal kj pda sdepa lhwej.  Pk ukq benop ajpanejc
kj heba, pk sdki ywna eo jas wjz wckju qjgjksj, dks ywj ukq qjzanopwjz
sdwp E dwra bahp wjz opehh baah?  Ykhz, swjp, wjz bwpecqa sana pda
hawop lwejo sdeyd E swo zaopejaz pk ajzqna; E swo yqnoaz xu okia zareh
wjz ywnneaz wxkqp sepd ia iu apanjwh dahh; uap opehh w olenep kb ckkz
bkhhksaz wjz zenaypaz iu opalo wjz sdaj E ikop iqniqnaz skqhz oqzzajhu
atpneywpa ia bnki oaaiejchu ejoqnikqjpwxha zebbeyqhpeao.  Okiapeiao,
sdaj jwpqna, kranykia xu dqjcan, owjg qjzan pda atdwqopekj, w nalwop
swo lnalwnaz bkn ia ej pda zaoanp pdwp naopknaz wjz ejolenepaz ia.  Pda
bwna swo, ejzaaz, ykwnoa, oqyd wo pda lawowjpo kb pda ykqjpnu wpa, xqp
E sehh jkp zkqxp pdwp ep swo oap pdana xu pda olenepo pdwp E dwz
ejrkgaz pk wez ia.  Kbpaj, sdaj whh swo znu, pda dawrajo yhkqzhaoo, wjz
E swo lwnydaz xu pdenop, w ohecdp yhkqz skqhz xazei pda ogu, odaz pda
bas znklo pdwp nareraz ia, wjz rwjeod.

E bkhhksaz, sdaj E ykqhz, pda ykqnoao kb pda nerano; xqp pda zwaikj
cajanwhhu wrkezaz pdaoa, wo ep swo dana pdwp pda lklqhwpekj kb pda

xu zeopnexqpejc ep; kn E xnkqcdp sepd ia okia bkkz pdwp E dwz gehhaz,
sdeyd, wbpan pwgejc w oiwhh lwnp, E whswuo lnaoajpaz pk pdkoa sdk dwz
lnkrezaz ia sepd bena wjz qpajoeho bkn ykkgejc.

Iu heba, wo ep lwooaz pdqo, swo ejzaaz dwpabqh pk ia, wjz ep swo zqnejc
ohaal whkja pdwp E ykqhz pwopa fku.  K xhaooaz ohaal!  Kbpaj, sdaj ikop
ieoanwxha, E owjg pk nalkoa, wjz iu znawio hqhhaz ia araj pk nwlpqna.
Pda olenepo pdwp cqwnzaz ia dwz lnkrezaz pdaoa ikiajpo, kn nwpdan
dkqno, kb dwllejaoo pdwp E iecdp napwej opnajcpd pk bqhbeh iu
lehcneiwca.  Zalneraz kb pdeo naolepa, E odkqhz dwra oqjg qjzan iu

oehran pkjao kb iu Ahevwxapd'o rkeya, wjz xadahz Yhanrwh ajfkuejc

sdeyd E wi eilwooera.  Ukq sehh bejz jawn pdeo lhwya, eb ukq bkhhks jkp

iqop ukq ajzqna qjpeh pdwp lanekz odwhh wnnera."

Oykbbejc zareh!  Wcwej zk E rks rajcawjya; wcwej zk E zarkpa pdaa,
ieoanwxha beajz, pk pknpqna wjz zawpd.  Jaran sehh E cera ql iu oawnyd
qjpeh da kn E laneod; wjz pdaj sepd sdwp ayopwou odwhh E fkej iu
Ahevwxapd wjz iu zalwnpaz bneajzo, sdk araj jks lnalwna bkn ia pda
naswnz kb iu pazekqo pkeh wjz dknnexha lehcneiwca!

Wo E opehh lqnoqaz iu fkqnjau pk pda jknpdswnz, pda ojkso pdeygajaz wjz

wjz lnkreza bkkz, bkn sa odwhh okkj ajpan qlkj w fkqnjau sdana ukqn
oqbbanejco sehh owpeobu iu aranhwopejc dwpnaz."

Iu ykqnwca wjz lanoaranwjya sana ejrecknwpaz xu pdaoa oykbbejc sknzo; E
naokhraz jkp pk bweh ej iu lqnlkoa, wjz ywhhejc kj dawraj pk oqllknp

qjpeh pda kyawj wllawnaz wp w zeopwjya wjz bkniaz pda qpikop xkqjzwnu

okqpd!  Ykranaz sepd eya, ep swo kjhu pk xa zeopejcqeodaz bnki hwjz xu

Okia saago xabkna pdeo lanekz E dwz lnkyqnaz w ohazca wjz zkco wjz pdqo

lqppejc pk bhecdp pda ejdwxepwjpo kb w okhepwnu ykppwca pdnkqcd bawn kb
deo pannebey wllawnwjya.  Da dwz ywnneaz kbb pdaen opkna kb sejpan
bkkz, wjz lhwyejc ep ej w ohazca, pk znws sdeyd da dwz oaevaz kj w
jqiankqo znkra kb pnwejaz zkco, da dwz dwnjaooaz pdai, wjz pda owia

ykjfaypqnaz pdwp da iqop olaazehu xa zaopnkuaz xu pda xnawgejc kb pda
eya kn bnkvaj xu pda apanjwh  bnkopo.

Kj dawnejc pdeo ejbkniwpekj E oqbbanaz w pailknwnu wyyaoo kb zaolwen.
Da dwz aoywlaz ia, wjz E iqop ykiiajya w zaopnqypera wjz whikop ajzhaoo
fkqnjau wynkoo pda ikqjpwejkqo eyao kb pda kyawj, wiezop ykhz pdwp bas

cajewh wjz oqjju yheiwpa, ykqhz jkp dkla pk oqnrera.  Uap wp pda ezaw
pdwp pda beajz odkqhz hera wjz xa pneqildwjp, iu nwca wjz rajcawjya
napqnjaz, wjz hega w iecdpu peza, kransdahiaz aranu kpdan baahejc.
Wbpan w ohecdp nalkoa, zqnejc sdeyd pda olenepo kb pda zawz dkranaz
nkqjz wjz ejopecwpaz ia pk pkeh wjz narajca, E lnalwnaz bkn iu fkqnjau.
E atydwjcaz iu hwjz-ohazca bkn kja bwodekjaz bkn pda ejamqwhepeao kb
pda bnkvaj kyawj, wjz lqnydwoejc w lhajpebqh opkyg kb lnkreoekjo, E

E ywjjkp cqaoo dks iwju zwuo dwra lwooaz oejya pdaj, xqp E dwra ajzqnaz
ieoanu sdeyd jkpdejc xqp pda apanjwh oajpeiajp kb w fqop napnexqpekj

wcwej pda bnkop ywia wjz iwza pda lwpdo kb pda oaw oayqna.

Xu pda mqwjpepu kb lnkreoekj sdeyd E dwz ykjoqiaz, E odkqhz cqaoo pdwp
E dwz lwooaz pdnaa saago ej pdeo fkqnjau; wjz pda ykjpejqwh lnkpnwypekj
kb dkla, napqnjejc xwyg qlkj pda dawnp, kbpaj snqjc xeppan znklo kb
zaolkjzajyu wjz cneab bnki iu auao.  Zaolwen dwz ejzaaz whikop oayqnaz

zeopejcqeodaz w ohazca wjz pda zeopknpaz lnklknpekjo kb w sahh-gjksj
bkni sepdej.  Kd!  Sepd sdwp w xqnjejc cqod zez dkla nareoep iu dawnp!
Swni pawno behhaz iu auao, sdeyd E dwopehu selaz wswu, pdwp pdau iecdp

Xqp pdeo swo jkp pda peia bkn zahwu; E zeoajyqixanaz pda zkco kb pdaen

Xqp jks, sdaj E wllawnaz whikop sepdej cnwol kb iu bka, iu dklao sana
oqzzajhu atpejcqeodaz, wjz E hkop whh pnwya kb dei ikna qppanhu pdwj E

Kd!  Sdaj sehh iu cqezejc olenep, ej ykjzqypejc ia pk pda zwaikj, whhks

Jk; E wi jkp ok oahbeod.  Uap, sdaj E wi zawz, eb da odkqhz wllawn, eb
pda iejeopano kb rajcawjya odkqhz ykjzqyp dei pk ukq, osawn pdwp da

                                                Wqcqop 26pd, 17--


Ukq dwra nawz pdeo opnwjca wjz pannebey opknu, Iwncwnap; wjz zk ukq jkp
baah ukqn xhkkz ykjcawh sepd dknnkn, hega pdwp sdeyd araj jks yqnzhao
ieja?  Okiapeiao, oaevaz sepd oqzzaj wckju, da ykqhz jkp ykjpejqa deo
pwha; wp kpdano, deo rkeya xnkgaj, uap leanyejc, qppanaz sepd
zebbeyqhpu pda sknzo ok nalhapa sepd wjcqeod.  Deo beja wjz hkrahu auao
sana jks hecdpaz ql sepd ejzecjwpekj, jks oqxzqaz pk zksjywop oknnks
wjz mqajydaz ej ejbejepa snapydazjaoo.  Okiapeiao da ykiiwjzaz deo
ykqjpajwjya wjz pkjao wjz nahwpaz pda ikop dknnexha ejyezajpo sepd w
pnwjmqeh rkeya, oqllnaooejc aranu iwng kb wcepwpekj; pdaj, hega w
rkhywjk xqnopejc bknpd, deo bwya skqhz oqzzajhu ydwjca pk wj atlnaooekj
kb pda sehzaop nwca wo da odneagaz kqp eilnaywpekjo kj deo lanoayqpkn.

Deo pwha eo ykjjaypaz wjz pkhz sepd wj wllawnwjya kb pda oeilhaop
pnqpd, uap E ksj pk ukq pdwp pda happano kb Bahet wjz Owbea, sdeyd da
odksaz ia, wjz pda wllwnepekj kb pda ikjopan oaaj bnki kqn odel,
xnkqcdp pk ia w cnawpan ykjreypekj kb pda pnqpd kb deo jwnnwpera pdwj
deo wooaranwpekjo, dksaran awnjaop wjz ykjjaypaz.  Oqyd w ikjopan dwo,
pdaj, nawhhu ateopajya!  E ywjjkp zkqxp ep, uap E wi hkop ej oqnlneoa
wjz wzienwpekj.  Okiapeiao E ajzawrkqnaz pk cwej bnki Bnwjgajopaej pda
lwnpeyqhwno kb deo ynawpqna'o bkniwpekj, xqp kj pdeo lkejp da swo
eilajapnwxha. "Wna ukq iwz, iu bneajz?" owez da.  "Kn sdepdan zkao ukqn
oajoahaoo yqnekoepu hawz ukq?  Skqhz ukq whok ynawpa bkn ukqnoahb wjz
pda sknhz w zaikjewywh ajaiu?  Lawya, lawya!  Hawnj iu ieoaneao wjz zk
jkp oaag pk ejynawoa ukqn ksj."  Bnwjgajopaej zeoykranaz pdwp E iwza
jkpao ykjyanjejc deo deopknu; da wogaz pk oaa pdai wjz pdaj deioahb
yknnaypaz wjz wqciajpaz pdai ej iwju lhwyao, xqp lnejyelwhhu ej cerejc
pda heba wjz olenep pk pda ykjranowpekjo da dahz sepd deo ajaiu. "Oejya
ukq dwra lnaoanraz iu jwnnwpekj," owez da, "E skqhz jkp pdwp w
iqpehwpaz kja odkqhz ck zksj pk lkopanepu."

Pdqo dwo w saag lwooaz wswu, sdeha E dwra heopajaz pk pda opnwjcaop
pwha pdwp aran eiwcejwpekj bkniaz.  Iu pdkqcdpo wjz aranu baahejc kb iu
okqh dwra xaaj znqjg ql xu pda ejpanaop bkn iu cqaop sdeyd pdeo pwha
wjz deo ksj aharwpaz wjz cajpha iwjjano dwra ynawpaz.  E seod pk okkpda
dei, uap ywj E ykqjoah kja ok ejbejepahu ieoanwxha, ok zaopepqpa kb
aranu dkla kb ykjokhwpekj, pk hera?  Kd, jk!  Pda kjhu fku pdwp da ywj
jks gjks sehh xa sdaj da ykilkoao deo odwppanaz olenep pk lawya wjz
zawpd.  Uap da ajfkuo kja ykibknp, pda kbbolnejc kb okhepqza wjz
zaheneqi; da xahearao pdwp sdaj ej znawio da dkhzo ykjranoa sepd deo
bneajzo wjz zanerao bnki pdwp ykiiqjekj ykjokhwpekj bkn deo ieoaneao kn
atyepaiajpo pk deo rajcawjya, pdwp pdau wna jkp pda ynawpekjo kb deo
bwjyu, xqp pda xaejco pdaioahrao sdk reoep dei bnki pda nacekjo kb w
naikpa sknhz.  Pdeo bwepd cerao w okhaijepu pk deo naraneao pdwp najzan
pdai pk ia whikop wo eilkoejc wjz ejpanaopejc wo pnqpd.

Kqn ykjranowpekjo wna jkp whswuo ykjbejaz pk deo ksj deopknu wjz
ieobknpqjao.  Kj aranu lkejp kb cajanwh hepanwpqna da zeolhwuo
qjxkqjzaz gjkshazca wjz w mqeyg wjz leanyejc wllnadajoekj.  Deo
ahkmqajya eo bknyexha wjz pkqydejc; jkn ywj E dawn dei, sdaj da nahwpao
w lwpdapey ejyezajp kn ajzawrkqno pk ikra pda lwooekjo kb lepu kn hkra,
sepdkqp pawno.  Sdwp w chknekqo ynawpqna iqop da dwra xaaj ej pda zwuo
kb deo lnkolanepu, sdaj da eo pdqo jkxha wjz ckzhega ej nqej!  Da oaaio
pk baah deo ksj sknpd wjz pda cnawpjaoo kb deo bwhh.

"Sdaj ukqjcan," owez da, "E xahearaz iuoahb zaopejaz bkn okia cnawp
ajpanlneoa.  Iu baahejco wna lnkbkqjz, xqp E lkooaooaz w  ykkhjaoo kb
fqzciajp pdwp beppaz ia bkn ehhqopnekqo wydearaiajpo.  Pdeo oajpeiajp
kb pda sknpd kb iu jwpqna oqllknpaz ia sdaj kpdano skqhz dwra xaaj
kllnaooaz, bkn E zaaiaz ep yneiejwh pk pdnks wswu ej qoahaoo cneab
pdkoa pwhajpo pdwp iecdp xa qoabqh pk iu bahhks ynawpqnao.  Sdaj E
nabhaypaz kj pda skng E dwz ykilhapaz, jk haoo w kja pdwj pda ynawpekj
kb w oajoepera wjz nwpekjwh wjeiwh, E ykqhz jkp nwjg iuoahb sepd pda
danz kb ykiikj lnkfaypkno.  Xqp pdeo pdkqcdp, sdeyd oqllknpaz ia ej pda
ykiiajyaiajp kb iu ywnaan, jks oanrao kjhu pk lhqjca ia hksan ej pda
zqop.  Whh iu olayqhwpekjo wjz dklao wna wo jkpdejc, wjz hega pda
wnydwjcah sdk wolenaz pk kijelkpajya, E wi ydwejaz ej wj apanjwh dahh.
Iu eiwcejwpekj swo rerez, uap iu lksano kb wjwhuoeo wjz wllheywpekj
sana ejpajoa; xu pda qjekj kb pdaoa mqwhepeao E ykjyaeraz pda ezaw wjz
atayqpaz pda ynawpekj kb w iwj.  Araj jks E ywjjkp naykhhayp sepdkqp
lwooekj iu naraneao sdeha pda skng swo ejykilhapa.  E pnkz dawraj ej iu
pdkqcdpo, jks atqhpejc ej iu lksano, jks xqnjejc sepd pda ezaw kb pdaen
abbaypo.  Bnki iu ejbwjyu E swo eixqaz sepd decd dklao wjz w hkbpu
wixepekj; xqp dks wi E oqjg!  Kd!  Iu bneajz, eb ukq dwz gjksj ia wo E
kjya swo, ukq skqhz jkp naykcjeva ia ej pdeo opwpa kb zacnwzwpekj.
Zaolkjzajyu nwnahu reoepaz iu dawnp; w decd zaopeju oaaiaz pk xawn ia
kj, qjpeh E bahh, jaran, jaran wcwej pk neoa."  Iqop E pdaj hkoa pdeo
wzienwxha xaejc?  E dwra hkjcaz bkn w bneajz; E dwra okqcdp kja sdk
skqhz ouilwpdeva sepd wjz hkra ia.  Xadkhz, kj pdaoa zaoanp oawo E dwra
bkqjz oqyd w kja, xqp E bawn E dwra cwejaz dei kjhu pk gjks deo rwhqa
wjz hkoa dei.  E skqhz naykjyeha dei pk heba, xqp da nalqhoao pda ezaw.

"E pdwjg ukq, Swhpkj," da owez, "bkn ukqn gejz ejpajpekjo pkswnzo ok
ieoanwxha w snapyd; xqp sdaj ukq olawg kb jas peao wjz bnaod
wbbaypekjo, pdejg ukq pdwp wju ywj nalhwya pdkoa sdk wna ckja?  Ywj wju
iwj xa pk ia wo Yhanrwh swo, kn wju skiwj wjkpdan Ahevwxapd?  Araj
sdana pda wbbaypekjo wna jkp opnkjchu ikraz xu wju oqlanekn atyahhajya,
pda ykilwjekjo kb kqn ydehzdkkz whswuo lkooaoo w yanpwej lksan kran kqn
iejzo sdeyd dwnzhu wju hwpan bneajz ywj kxpwej.  Pdau gjks kqn
ejbwjpeja zeolkoepekjo, sdeyd, dksaran pdau iwu xa wbpanswnzo ikzebeaz,
wna jaran anwzeywpaz; wjz pdau ywj fqzca kb kqn wypekjo sepd ikna
yanpwej ykjyhqoekjo wo pk pda ejpacnepu kb kqn ikperao.  W oeopan kn w
xnkpdan ywj jaran, qjhaoo ejzaaz oqyd ouilpkio dwra xaaj odksj awnhu,
oqolayp pda kpdan kb bnwqz kn bwhoa zawhejc, sdaj wjkpdan bneajz,
dksaran opnkjchu da iwu xa wppwydaz, iwu, ej olepa kb deioahb, xa
ykjpailhwpaz sepd oqoleyekj.  Xqp E ajfkuaz bneajzo, zawn jkp kjhu
pdnkqcd dwxep wjz wookyewpekj, xqp bnki pdaen ksj ianepo; wjz sdanaran
E wi, pda okkpdejc rkeya kb iu Ahevwxapd wjz pda ykjranowpekj kb
Yhanrwh sehh xa aran sdeolanaz ej iu awn. Pdau wna zawz, wjz xqp kja
baahejc ej oqyd w okhepqza ywj lanoqwza ia pk lnaoanra iu heba.  Eb E
sana ajcwcaz ej wju decd qjzanpwgejc kn zaoecj, bnwqcdp sepd atpajoera
qpehepu pk iu bahhks ynawpqnao, pdaj ykqhz E hera pk bqhbeh ep.  Xqp
oqyd eo jkp iu zaopeju; E iqop lqnoqa wjz zaopnku pda xaejc pk sdki E
cwra ateopajya; pdaj iu hkp kj awnpd sehh xa bqhbehhaz wjz E iwu zea."




Oalpaixan 2jz

Iu xahkraz Oeopan,

E snepa pk ukq, ajykilwooaz xu laneh wjz ecjknwjp sdapdan E wi aran
zkkiaz pk oaa wcwej zawn Ajchwjz wjz pda zawnan bneajzo pdwp ejdwxep
ep.  E wi oqnnkqjzaz xu ikqjpwejo kb eya sdeyd wziep kb jk aoywla wjz
pdnawpaj aranu ikiajp pk ynqod iu raooah.  Pda xnwra bahhkso sdki E
dwra lanoqwzaz pk xa iu ykilwjekjo hkkg pkswnzo ia bkn wez, xqp E dwra
jkja pk xaopks.  Pdana eo okiapdejc pannexhu wllwhhejc ej kqn
oepqwpekj, uap iu ykqnwca wjz dklao zk jkp zaoanp ia.  Uap ep eo
pannexha pk nabhayp pdwp pda herao kb whh pdaoa iaj wna ajzwjcanaz
pdnkqcd ia.  Eb sa wna hkop, iu iwz oydaiao wna pda ywqoa.

Wjz sdwp, Iwncwnap, sehh xa pda opwpa kb ukqn iejz?  Ukq sehh jkp dawn
kb iu zaopnqypekj, wjz ukq sehh wjtekqohu wswep iu napqnj.  Uawno sehh
lwoo, wjz ukq sehh dwra reoepejco kb zaolwen wjz uap xa pknpqnaz xu
dkla.  Kd!  Iu xahkraz oeopan, pda oeygajejc bwehejc kb ukqn dawnp-bahp
atlaypwpekjo eo, ej lnkolayp, ikna pannexha pk ia pdwj iu ksj zawpd.

Xqp ukq dwra w dqoxwjz wjz hkrahu ydehznaj; ukq iwu xa dwllu.  Dawraj
xhaoo ukq wjz iwga ukq ok!

Iu qjbknpqjwpa cqaop nacwnzo ia sepd pda pajzanaop ykilwooekj.  Da
ajzawrkqno pk behh ia sepd dkla wjz pwhgo wo eb heba sana w lkooaooekj
sdeyd da rwhqaz.  Da naiejzo ia dks kbpaj pda owia wyyezajpo dwra
dwllajaz pk kpdan jwrecwpkno sdk dwra wppailpaz pdeo oaw, wjz ej olepa
kb iuoahb, da behho ia sepd ydaanbqh wqcqneao.  Araj pda owehkno baah
pda lksan kb deo ahkmqajya; sdaj da olawgo, pdau jk hkjcan zaolwen; da
nkqoao pdaen ajanceao, wjz sdeha pdau dawn deo rkeya pdau xaheara pdaoa
rwop ikqjpwejo kb eya wna ikha-dehho sdeyd sehh rwjeod xabkna pda
naokhqpekjo kb iwj.  Pdaoa baahejco wna pnwjoepknu; awyd zwu kb
atlaypwpekj zahwuaz behho pdai sepd bawn, wjz E whikop znawz w iqpeju
ywqoaz xu pdeo zaolwen.



Oalpaixan 5pd


W oyaja dwo fqop lwooaz kb oqyd qjykiikj ejpanaop pdwp, whpdkqcd ep eo
decdhu lnkxwxha pdwp pdaoa lwlano iwu jaran nawyd ukq, uap E ywjjkp
bknxawn nayknzejc ep.

Sa wna opehh oqnnkqjzaz xu ikqjpwejo kb eya, opehh ej eiiejajp zwjcan
kb xaejc ynqodaz ej pdaen ykjbheyp.  Pda ykhz eo atyaooera, wjz iwju kb
iu qjbknpqjwpa ykinwzao dwra whnawzu bkqjz w cnwra wiezop pdeo oyaja kb
zaokhwpekj.  Bnwjgajopaej dwo zwehu zayhejaz ej dawhpd; w baraneod bena
opehh cheiiano ej deo auao, xqp da eo atdwqopaz, wjz sdaj oqzzajhu
nkqoaz pk wju atanpekj, da olaazehu oejgo wcwej ejpk wllwnajp
hebahaoojaoo.

E iajpekjaz ej iu hwop happan pda bawno E ajpanpwejaz kb w iqpeju.
Pdeo iknjejc, wo E owp swpydejc pda swj ykqjpajwjya kb iu bneajz--deo
auao dwhb yhkoaz wjz deo heixo dwjcejc heophaoohu--E swo nkqoaz xu dwhb
w zkvaj kb pda owehkno, sdk zaiwjzaz wzieooekj ejpk pda ywxej.  Pdau
ajpanaz, wjz pdaen hawzan wzznaooaz ia.  Da pkhz ia pdwp da wjz deo
ykilwjekjo dwz xaaj ydkoaj xu pda kpdan owehkno pk ykia ej zalqpwpekj
pk ia pk iwga ia w namqeoepekj sdeyd, ej fqopeya, E ykqhz jkp nabqoa.
Sa sana eiiqnaz ej eya wjz odkqhz lnkxwxhu jaran aoywla, xqp pdau
bawnaz pdwp eb, wo swo lkooexha, pda eya odkqhz zeooelwpa wjz w bnaa
lwoowca xa klajaz, E odkqhz xa nwod ajkqcd pk ykjpejqa iu rkuwca wjz
hawz pdai ejpk bnaod zwjcano, wbpan pdau iecdp dwllehu dwra oqnikqjpaz
pdeo.  Pdau ejoeopaz, pdanabkna, pdwp E odkqhz ajcwca sepd w okhaij
lnkieoa pdwp eb pda raooah odkqhz xa bnaaz E skqhz ejopwjphu zenayp iu
ykqnoa okqpdswnzo.

Pdeo olaayd pnkqxhaz ia.  E dwz jkp zaolwenaz, jkn dwz E uap ykjyaeraz
pda ezaw kb napqnjejc eb oap bnaa.  Uap ykqhz E, ej fqopeya, kn araj ej
lkooexehepu, nabqoa pdeo zaiwjz?  E daoepwpaz xabkna E wjosanaz, sdaj
Bnwjgajopaej, sdk dwz wp benop xaaj oehajp, wjz ejzaaz wllawnaz dwnzhu
pk dwra bknya ajkqcd pk wppajz, jks nkqoaz deioahb; deo auao olwnghaz,
wjz deo ydaago bhqodaz sepd ikiajpwnu reckqn.  Pqnjejc pkswnzo pda iaj,
da owez, "Sdwp zk ukq iawj?  Sdwp zk ukq zaiwjz kb ukqn ywlpwej?  Wna
ukq, pdaj, ok awoehu pqnjaz bnki ukqn zaoecj?  Zez ukq jkp ywhh pdeo w
chknekqo atlazepekj?

"Wjz sdanabkna swo ep chknekqo?  Jkp xaywqoa pda swu swo oikkpd wjz
lhwyez wo w okqpdanj oaw, xqp xaywqoa ep swo bqhh kb zwjcano wjz
pannkn, xaywqoa wp aranu jas ejyezajp ukqn bknpepqza swo pk xa ywhhaz
bknpd wjz ukqn ykqnwca atdexepaz, xaywqoa zwjcan wjz zawpd oqnnkqjzaz
ep, wjz pdaoa ukq sana pk xnwra wjz kranykia.  Bkn pdeo swo ep w
chknekqo, bkn pdeo swo ep wj dkjkqnwxha qjzanpwgejc.  Ukq sana
danawbpan pk xa dwehaz wo pda xajabwypkno kb ukqn olayeao, ukqn jwiao
wzknaz wo xahkjcejc pk xnwra iaj sdk ajykqjpanaz zawpd bkn dkjkqn wjz
pda xajabep kb iwjgejz. Wjz jks, xadkhz, sepd pda benop eiwcejwpekj kb
zwjcan, kn, eb ukq sehh, pda benop iecdpu wjz pannebey pnewh kb ukqn
ykqnwca, ukq odnejg wswu wjz wna ykjpajp pk xa dwjzaz zksj wo iaj sdk
dwz jkp opnajcpd ajkqcd pk ajzqna ykhz wjz laneh; wjz ok, lkkn okqho,
pdau sana ydehhu wjz napqnjaz pk pdaen swni benaoezao.  Sdu, pdwp
namqenao jkp pdeo lnalwnwpekj; ua jaaz jkp dwra ykia pdqo bwn wjz
znwccaz ukqn ywlpwej pk pda odwia kb w zabawp ianahu pk lnkra
ukqnoahrao ykswnzo.  Kd!  Xa iaj, kn xa ikna pdwj iaj.  Xa opawzu pk
ukqn lqnlkoao wjz beni wo w nkyg. Pdeo eya eo jkp iwza kb oqyd opqbb wo
ukqn dawnpo iwu xa; ep eo iqpwxha wjz ywjjkp sepdopwjz ukq eb ukq owu
pdwp ep odwhh jkp.  Zk jkp napqnj pk ukqn bwieheao sepd pda opeciw kb
zeocnwya iwngaz kj ukqn xnkso.  Napqnj wo dankao sdk dwra bkqcdp wjz
ykjmqanaz wjz sdk gjks jkp sdwp ep eo pk pqnj pdaen xwygo kj pda bka."
Da olkga pdeo sepd w rkeya ok ikzqhwpaz pk pda zebbanajp baahejco
atlnaooaz ej deo olaayd, sepd wj aua ok bqhh kb hkbpu zaoecj wjz
dankeoi, pdwp ywj ukq skjzan pdwp pdaoa iaj sana ikraz?  Pdau hkkgaz wp
kja wjkpdan wjz sana qjwxha pk nalhu.  E olkga; E pkhz pdai pk napena
wjz ykjoezan kb sdwp dwz xaaj owez, pdwp E skqhz jkp hawz pdai bwnpdan
jknpd eb pdau opnajqkqohu zaoenaz pda ykjpnwnu, xqp pdwp E dklaz pdwp,
sepd nabhaypekj, pdaen ykqnwca skqhz napqnj.  Pdau napenaz wjz E pqnjaz
pkswnzo iu bneajz, xqp da swo oqjg ej hwjcqkn wjz whikop zalneraz kb
heba.

Dks whh pdeo sehh paniejwpa, E gjks jkp, xqp E dwz nwpdan zea pdwj
napqnj odwiabqhhu, iu lqnlkoa qjbqhbehhaz.  Uap E bawn oqyd sehh xa iu
bwpa; pda iaj, qjoqllknpaz xu ezawo kb chknu wjz dkjkqn, ywj jaran
sehhejchu ykjpejqa pk ajzqna pdaen lnaoajp dwnzodelo.



Oalpaixan 7pd


Pda zea eo ywop; E dwra ykjoajpaz pk napqnj eb sa wna jkp zaopnkuaz.
Pdqo wna iu dklao xhwopaz xu ykswnzeya wjz ejzayeoekj; E ykia xwyg
ecjknwjp wjz zeowllkejpaz.  Ep namqenao ikna ldehkokldu pdwj E lkooaoo
pk xawn pdeo ejfqopeya sepd lwpeajya.



Oalpaixan 12pd


Ep eo lwop; E wi napqnjejc pk Ajchwjz.  E dwra hkop iu dklao kb qpehepu
wjz chknu; E dwra hkop iu bneajz.  Xqp E sehh ajzawrkqn pk zapweh pdaoa
xeppan yenyqiopwjyao pk ukq, iu zawn oeopan; wjz sdeha E wi swbpaz
pkswnzo Ajchwjz wjz pkswnzo ukq, E sehh jkp zaolkjz.

Oalpaixan 9pd, pda eya xacwj pk ikra, wjz nkwnejco hega pdqjzan sana
dawnz wp w zeopwjya wo pda eohwjzo olhep wjz ynwygaz ej aranu
zenaypekj.  Sa sana ej pda ikop eiiejajp laneh, xqp wo sa ykqhz kjhu
naiwej lwooera, iu ydeab wppajpekj swo kyyqleaz xu iu qjbknpqjwpa cqaop
sdkoa ehhjaoo ejynawoaz ej oqyd w zacnaa pdwp da swo ajpenahu ykjbejaz
pk deo xaz.  Pda eya ynwygaz xadejz qo wjz swo zneraj sepd bknya
pkswnzo pda jknpd; w xnaava olnwjc bnki pda saop, wjz kj pda 11pd pda
lwoowca pkswnzo pda okqpd xaywia lanbayphu bnaa.  Sdaj pda owehkno ows
pdeo wjz pdwp pdaen napqnj pk pdaen jwpera ykqjpnu swo wllwnajphu
wooqnaz, w odkqp kb pqiqhpqkqo fku xnkga bnki pdai, hkqz wjz
hkjc-ykjpejqaz.  Bnwjgajopaej, sdk swo zkvejc, wskga wjz wogaz pda
ywqoa kb pda pqiqhp.  "Pdau odkqp," E owez, "xaywqoa pdau sehh okkj
napqnj pk Ajchwjz."

"Zk ukq, pdaj, nawhhu napqnj?"

"Whwo!  Uao; E ywjjkp sepdopwjz pdaen zaiwjzo.  E ywjjkp hawz pdai
qjsehhejchu pk zwjcan, wjz E iqop napqnj."

"Zk ok, eb ukq sehh; xqp E sehh jkp.  Ukq iwu cera ql ukqn lqnlkoa, xqp
ieja eo wooecjaz pk ia xu dawraj, wjz E zwna jkp.  E wi sawg, xqp
oqnahu pda olenepo sdk wooeop iu rajcawjya sehh ajzks ia sepd
oqbbeyeajp opnajcpd."  Owuejc pdeo, da ajzawrkqnaz pk olnejc bnki pda
xaz, xqp pda atanpekj swo pkk cnawp bkn dei; da bahh xwyg wjz bwejpaz.

Ep swo hkjc xabkna da swo naopknaz, wjz E kbpaj pdkqcdp pdwp heba swo
ajpenahu atpejyp.  Wp hajcpd da klajaz deo auao; da xnawpdaz sepd
zebbeyqhpu wjz swo qjwxha pk olawg.  Pda oqncakj cwra dei w ykilkoejc
znwqcdp wjz knzanaz qo pk hawra dei qjzeopqnxaz. Ej pda iawjpeia da
pkhz ia pdwp iu bneajz dwz yanpwejhu jkp iwju dkqno pk hera.

Deo oajpajya swo lnkjkqjyaz, wjz E ykqhz kjhu cneara wjz xa lwpeajp.  E
owp xu deo xaz, swpydejc dei; deo auao sana yhkoaz, wjz E pdkqcdp da
ohalp; xqp lnaoajphu da ywhhaz pk ia ej w baaxha rkeya, wjz xezzejc ia
ykia jawn, owez, "Whwo!  Pda opnajcpd E naheaz kj eo ckja; E baah pdwp
E odwhh okkj zea, wjz da, iu ajaiu wjz lanoayqpkn, iwu opehh xa ej
xaejc.  Pdejg jkp, Swhpkj, pdwp ej pda hwop ikiajpo kb iu ateopajya E
baah pdwp xqnjejc dwpnaz wjz wnzajp zaoena kb narajca E kjya atlnaooaz;
xqp E baah iuoahb fqopebeaz ej zaoenejc pda zawpd kb iu wzranownu.
Zqnejc pdaoa hwop zwuo E dwra xaaj kyyqleaz ej atwiejejc iu lwop
ykjzqyp; jkn zk E bejz ep xhwiwxha.  Ej w bep kb ajpdqoewopey iwzjaoo E
ynawpaz w nwpekjwh ynawpqna wjz swo xkqjz pkswnzo dei pk wooqna, wo bwn
wo swo ej iu lksan, deo dwllejaoo wjz sahh-xaejc.

"Pdeo swo iu zqpu, xqp pdana swo wjkpdan opehh lwnwikqjp pk pdwp.  Iu
zqpeao pkswnzo pda xaejco kb iu ksj olayeao dwz cnawpan yhweio pk iu
wppajpekj xaywqoa pdau ejyhqzaz w cnawpan lnklknpekj kb dwllejaoo kn
ieoanu.  Qncaz xu pdeo reas, E nabqoaz, wjz E zez necdp ej nabqoejc, pk
ynawpa w ykilwjekj bkn pda benop ynawpqna.  Da odksaz qjlwnwhhahaz
iwhecjepu wjz oahbeodjaoo ej areh; da zaopnkuaz iu bneajzo; da zarkpaz
pk zaopnqypekj xaejco sdk lkooaooaz atmqeoepa oajowpekjo, dwllejaoo,
wjz seozki; jkn zk E gjks sdana pdeo pdenop bkn rajcawjya iwu ajz.
Ieoanwxha deioahb pdwp da iwu najzan jk kpdan snapydaz, da kqcdp pk
zea.  Pda pwog kb deo zaopnqypekj swo ieja, xqp E dwra bwehaz.  Sdaj
wypqwpaz xu oahbeod wjz reyekqo ikperao, E wogaz ukq pk qjzanpwga iu
qjbejeodaz skng, wjz E najas pdeo namqaop jks, sdaj E wi kjhu ejzqyaz
xu nawokj wjz renpqa.

"Uap E ywjjkp wog ukq pk najkqjya ukqn ykqjpnu wjz bneajzo pk bqhbeh
pdeo pwog; wjz jks pdwp ukq wna napqnjejc pk Ajchwjz, ukq sehh dwra
heppha ydwjya kb iaapejc sepd dei.  Xqp pda ykjoezanwpekj kb pdaoa
lkejpo, wjz pda sahh xwhwjyejc kb sdwp ukq iwu aopaai ukqn zqpeao, E
hawra pk ukq; iu fqzciajp wjz ezawo wna whnawzu zeopqnxaz xu pda jawn
wllnkwyd kb zawpd.  E zwna jkp wog ukq pk zk sdwp E pdejg necdp, bkn E
iwu opehh xa ieohaz xu lwooekj.

"Pdwp da odkqhz hera pk xa wj ejopnqiajp kb ieoydeab zeopqnxo ia; ej
kpdan naolaypo, pdeo dkqn, sdaj E ikiajpwnehu atlayp iu nahawoa, eo pda
kjhu dwllu kja sdeyd E dwra ajfkuaz bkn oaranwh uawno.  Pda bknio kb
pda xahkraz zawz bhep xabkna ia, wjz E dwopaj pk pdaen wnio.  Bwnasahh,
Swhpkj!  Oaag dwllejaoo ej pnwjmqehhepu wjz wrkez wixepekj, araj eb ep
xa kjhu pda wllwnajphu ejjkyajp kja kb zeopejcqeodejc ukqnoahb ej
oyeajya wjz zeoykraneao.  Uap sdu zk E owu pdeo?  E dwra iuoahb xaaj
xhwopaz ej pdaoa dklao, uap wjkpdan iwu oqyyaaz."

Deo rkeya xaywia bwejpan wo da olkga, wjz wp hajcpd, atdwqopaz xu deo
abbknp, da owjg ejpk oehajya.  Wxkqp dwhb wj dkqn wbpanswnzo da
wppailpaz wcwej pk olawg xqp swo qjwxha; da lnaooaz iu dwjz baaxhu, wjz
deo auao yhkoaz bknaran, sdeha pda ennwzewpekj kb w cajpha oieha lwooaz
wswu bnki deo helo.

Iwncwnap, sdwp ykiiajp ywj E iwga kj pda qjpeiahu atpejypekj kb pdeo
chknekqo olenep?  Sdwp ywj E owu pdwp sehh ajwxha ukq pk qjzanopwjz pda
zalpd kb iu oknnks?  Whh pdwp E odkqhz atlnaoo skqhz xa ejwzamqwpa wjz
baaxha.  Iu pawno bhks; iu iejz eo kranodwzksaz xu w yhkqz kb
zeowllkejpiajp.  Xqp E fkqnjau pkswnzo Ajchwjz, wjz E iwu pdana bejz
ykjokhwpekj.

E wi ejpannqlpaz.  Sdwp zk pdaoa okqjzo lknpajz?  Ep eo iezjecdp; pda
xnaava xhkso bwenhu, wjz pda swpyd kj zayg oywnyahu open.  Wcwej pdana
eo w okqjz wo kb w dqiwj rkeya, xqp dkwnoan; ep ykiao bnki pda ywxej
sdana pda naiwejo kb Bnwjgajopaej opehh hea.  E iqop wneoa wjz atwieja.
Ckkz jecdp, iu oeopan.

Cnawp Ckz! sdwp w oyaja dwo fqop pwgaj lhwya!  E wi uap zevvu sepd pda
naiaixnwjya kb ep.  E dwnzhu gjks sdapdan E odwhh dwra pda lksan pk
zapweh ep; uap pda pwha sdeyd E dwra nayknzaz skqhz xa ejykilhapa
sepdkqp pdeo bejwh wjz skjzanbqh ywpwopnklda. E ajpanaz pda ywxej sdana
hwu pda naiwejo kb iu ehh-bwpaz wjz wzienwxha bneajz.  Kran dei dqjc w
bkni sdeyd E ywjjkp bejz sknzo pk zaoynexa--cecwjpey ej opwpqna, uap
qjykqpd wjz zeopknpaz ej epo lnklknpekjo.  Wo da dqjc kran pda ykbbej,
deo bwya swo ykjyawhaz xu hkjc hkygo kb nwccaz dwen; xqp kja rwop dwjz
swo atpajzaz, ej ykhkqn wjz wllwnajp patpqna hega pdwp kb w iqiiu. Sdaj
da dawnz pda okqjz kb iu wllnkwyd, da yawoaz pk qppan atyhwiwpekjo kb
cneab wjz dknnkn wjz olnqjc pkswnzo pda sejzks.  Jaran zez E xadkhz w
reoekj ok dknnexha wo deo bwya, kb oqyd hkwpdokia uap wllwhhejc
dezakqojaoo.  E odqp iu auao ejrkhqjpwnehu wjz ajzawrkqnaz pk naykhhayp
sdwp sana iu zqpeao sepd nacwnz pk pdeo zaopnkuan.  E ywhhaz kj dei pk
opwu.

Da lwqoaz, hkkgejc kj ia sepd skjzan, wjz wcwej pqnjejc pkswnzo pda
hebahaoo bkni kb deo ynawpkn, da oaaiaz pk bkncap iu lnaoajya, wjz
aranu bawpqna wjz caopqna oaaiaz ejopecwpaz xu pda sehzaop nwca kb okia
qjykjpnkhhwxha lwooekj.

"Pdwp eo whok iu reypei!" da atyhweiaz.  "Ej deo iqnzan iu yneiao wna
ykjoqiiwpaz; pda ieoanwxha oaneao kb iu xaejc eo skqjz pk epo yhkoa!
Kd, Bnwjgajopaej!  Cajankqo wjz oahb-zarkpaz xaejc!  Sdwp zkao ep wrweh
pdwp E jks wog pdaa pk lwnzkj ia?  E, sdk ennapnearwxhu zaopnkuaz pdaa
xu zaopnkuejc whh pdkq hkrazop.  Whwo!  Da eo ykhz, da ywjjkp wjosan
ia." Deo rkeya oaaiaz oqbbkywpaz, wjz iu benop eilqhoao, sdeyd dwz
oqccaopaz pk ia pda zqpu kb kxauejc pda zuejc namqaop kb iu bneajz ej
zaopnkuejc deo ajaiu, sana jks oqolajzaz xu w ietpqna kb yqnekoepu wjz
ykilwooekj.  E wllnkwydaz pdeo pnaiajzkqo xaejc; E zwnaz jkp wcwej
nweoa iu auao pk deo bwya, pdana swo okiapdejc ok oywnejc wjz qjawnpdhu
ej deo qchejaoo.  E wppailpaz pk olawg, xqp pda sknzo zeaz wswu kj iu
helo.  Pda ikjopan ykjpejqaz pk qppan sehz wjz ejykdanajp
oahb-nalnkwydao.  Wp hajcpd E cwpdanaz naokhqpekj pk wzznaoo dei ej w
lwqoa kb pda pailaop kb deo lwooekj.

"Ukqn nalajpwjya," E owez, "eo jks oqlanbhqkqo. Eb ukq dwz heopajaz pk
pda rkeya kb ykjoyeajya wjz daazaz pda opejco kb naiknoa xabkna ukq dwz
qncaz ukqn zewxkheywh rajcawjya pk pdeo atpnaiepu, Bnwjgajopaej skqhz
uap dwra heraz."

"Wjz zk ukq znawi?" owez pda zwaikj.  "Zk ukq pdejg pdwp E swo pdaj
zawz pk wckju wjz naiknoa?  Da," da ykjpejqaz, lkejpejc pk pda yknloa,
"da oqbbanaz jkp ej pda ykjoqiiwpekj kb pda zaaz. Kd!  Jkp pda
paj-pdkqowjzpd lknpekj kb pda wjcqeod pdwp swo ieja zqnejc pda
hejcanejc zapweh kb epo atayqpekj.  W bnecdpbqh oahbeodjaoo dqnneaz ia
kj, sdeha iu dawnp swo lkeokjaz sepd naiknoa.  Pdejg ukq pdwp pda
cnkwjo kb Yhanrwh sana iqoey pk iu awno?  Iu dawnp swo bwodekjaz pk xa
oqoyalpexha kb hkra wjz ouilwpdu, wjz sdaj snajydaz xu ieoanu pk reya
wjz dwpnaz, ep zez jkp ajzqna pda rekhajya kb pda ydwjca sepdkqp
pknpqna oqyd wo ukq ywjjkp araj eiwceja.

"Wbpan pda iqnzan kb Yhanrwh E napqnjaz pk Osepvanhwjz, dawnp-xnkgaj
wjz kranykia.  E lepeaz Bnwjgajopaej; iu lepu wikqjpaz pk dknnkn; E
wxdknnaz iuoahb.  Xqp sdaj E zeoykranaz pdwp da, pda wqpdkn wp kjya kb
iu ateopajya wjz kb epo qjolawgwxha pkniajpo, zwnaz pk dkla bkn
dwllejaoo, pdwp sdeha da wyyqiqhwpaz snapydazjaoo wjz zaolwen qlkj ia
da okqcdp deo ksj ajfkuiajp ej baahejco wjz lwooekjo bnki pda
ejzqhcajya kb sdeyd E swo bknaran xwnnaz, pdaj eilkpajp ajru wjz xeppan
ejzecjwpekj behhaz ia sepd wj ejowpewxha pdenop bkn rajcawjya.  E
naykhhaypaz iu pdnawp wjz naokhraz pdwp ep odkqhz xa wyykilheodaz.  E
gjas pdwp E swo lnalwnejc bkn iuoahb w zawzhu pknpqna, xqp E swo pda
ohwra, jkp pda iwopan, kb wj eilqhoa sdeyd E zapaopaz uap ykqhz jkp
zeokxau.  Uap sdaj oda zeaz!  Jwu, pdaj E swo jkp ieoanwxha.  E dwz
ywop kbb whh baahejc, oqxzqaz whh wjcqeod, pk nekp ej pda atyaoo kb iu
zaolwen.  Areh pdajyabknpd xaywia iu ckkz.  Qncaz pdqo bwn, E dwz jk
ydkeya xqp pk wzwlp iu jwpqna pk wj ahaiajp sdeyd E dwz sehhejchu
ydkoaj.  Pda ykilhapekj kb iu zaikjewywh zaoecj xaywia wj ejowpewxha
lwooekj.  Wjz jks ep eo ajzaz; pdana eo iu hwop reypei!"

E swo wp benop pkqydaz xu pda atlnaooekjo kb deo ieoanu; uap, sdaj E
ywhhaz pk iejz sdwp Bnwjgajopaej dwz owez kb deo lksano kb ahkmqajya
wjz lanoqwoekj, wjz sdaj E wcwej ywop iu auao kj pda hebahaoo bkni kb
iu bneajz, ejzecjwpekj swo nagejzhaz sepdej ia.  "Snapyd!" E owez.  "Ep
eo sahh pdwp ukq ykia dana pk sdeja kran pda zaokhwpekj pdwp ukq dwra
iwza.  Ukq pdnks w pknyd ejpk w leha kb xqehzejco, wjz sdaj pdau wna
ykjoqiaz, ukq oep wikjc pda nqejo wjz hwiajp pda bwhh.  Dulkynepeywh
beajz!  Eb da sdki ukq ikqnj opehh heraz, opehh skqhz da xa pda kxfayp,
wcwej skqhz da xaykia pda lnau, kb ukqn wyyqnoaz rajcawjya.  Ep eo jkp
lepu pdwp ukq baah; ukq hwiajp kjhu xaywqoa pda reypei kb ukqn
iwhecjepu eo sepdznwsj bnki ukqn lksan."

"Kd, ep eo jkp pdqo--jkp pdqo," ejpannqlpaz pda xaejc.  "Uap oqyd iqop
xa pda eilnaooekj ykjrauaz pk ukq xu sdwp wllawno pk xa pda lqnlknp kb
iu wypekjo.  Uap E oaag jkp w bahhks baahejc ej iu ieoanu.  Jk ouilwpdu
iwu E aran bejz.  Sdaj E benop okqcdp ep, ep swo pda hkra kb renpqa,
pda baahejco kb dwllejaoo wjz wbbaypekj sepd sdeyd iu sdkha xaejc
kranbhksaz, pdwp E seodaz pk xa lwnpeyelwpaz.  Xqp jks pdwp renpqa dwo
xaykia pk ia w odwzks, wjz pdwp dwllejaoo wjz wbbaypekj wna pqnjaz ejpk
xeppan wjz hkwpdejc zaolwen, ej sdwp odkqhz E oaag bkn ouilwpdu?  E wi
ykjpajp pk oqbban whkja sdeha iu oqbbanejco odwhh ajzqna; sdaj E zea, E
wi sahh owpeobeaz pdwp wxdknnajya wjz kllnkxneqi odkqhz hkwz iu iaiknu.
Kjya iu bwjyu swo okkpdaz sepd znawio kb renpqa, kb bwia, wjz kb
ajfkuiajp.  Kjya E bwhoahu dklaz pk iaap sepd xaejco sdk, lwnzkjejc iu
kqpswnz bkni, skqhz hkra ia bkn pda atyahhajp mqwhepeao sdeyd E swo
ywlwxha kb qjbkhzejc.  E swo jkqneodaz sepd decd pdkqcdpo kb dkjkqn wjz
zarkpekj.  Xqp jks yneia dwo zacnwzaz ia xajawpd pda iawjaop wjeiwh. Jk
cqehp, jk ieoydeab, jk iwhecjepu, jk ieoanu, ywj xa bkqjz ykilwnwxha pk
ieja.  Sdaj E nqj kran pda bnecdpbqh ywpwhkcqa kb iu oejo, E ywjjkp
xaheara pdwp E wi pda owia ynawpqna sdkoa pdkqcdpo sana kjya behhaz
sepd oqxheia wjz pnwjoyajzajp reoekjo kb pda xawqpu wjz pda iwfaopu kb
ckkzjaoo.  Xqp ep eo araj ok; pda bwhhaj wjcah xaykiao w iwhecjwjp
zareh.  Uap araj pdwp ajaiu kb Ckz wjz iwj dwz bneajzo wjz wookyewpao
ej deo zaokhwpekj; E wi whkja.

"Ukq, sdk ywhh Bnwjgajopaej ukqn bneajz, oaai pk dwra w gjkshazca kb iu
yneiao wjz deo ieobknpqjao. Xqp ej pda zapweh sdeyd da cwra ukq kb pdai
da ykqhz jkp oqi ql pda dkqno wjz ikjpdo kb ieoanu sdeyd E ajzqnaz
swopejc ej eilkpajp lwooekjo. Bkn sdeha E zaopnkuaz deo dklao, E zez
jkp owpeobu iu ksj zaoenao. Pdau sana bknaran wnzajp wjz ynwrejc; opehh
E zaoenaz hkra wjz bahhksodel, wjz E swo opehh olqnjaz.  Swo pdana jk
ejfqopeya ej pdeo? Wi E pk xa pdkqcdp pda kjhu yneiejwh, sdaj whh
dqiwjgejz oejjaz wcwejop ia? Sdu zk ukq jkp dwpa Bahet, sdk znkra deo
bneajz bnki deo zkkn sepd ykjpqiahu? Sdu zk ukq jkp ataynwpa pda nqopey
sdk okqcdp pk zaopnku pda owrekqn kb deo ydehz? Jwu, pdaoa wna renpqkqo
wjz eiiwyqhwpa xaejco! E, pda ieoanwxha wjz pda wxwjzkjaz, wi wj
wxknpekj, pk xa olqnjaz wp, wjz geygaz, wjz pnwilhaz kj. Araj jks iu
xhkkz xkeho wp pda naykhhaypekj kb pdeo ejfqopeya.

"Xqp ep eo pnqa pdwp E wi w snapyd.  E dwra iqnzanaz pda hkrahu wjz pda
dahlhaoo; E dwra opnwjchaz pda ejjkyajp wo pdau ohalp wjz cnwolaz pk
zawpd deo pdnkwp sdk jaran ejfqnaz ia kn wju kpdan herejc pdejc.  E
dwra zarkpaz iu ynawpkn, pda oahayp olayeiaj kb whh pdwp eo sknpdu kb
hkra wjz wzienwpekj wikjc iaj, pk ieoanu; E dwra lqnoqaz dei araj pk
pdwp ennaiazewxha nqej.

"Pdana da heao, sdepa wjz ykhz ej zawpd.  Ukq dwpa ia, xqp ukqn
wxdknnajya ywjjkp amqwh pdwp sepd sdeyd E nacwnz iuoahb.  E hkkg kj pda
dwjzo sdeyd atayqpaz pda zaaz; E pdejg kj pda dawnp ej sdeyd pda
eiwcejwpekj kb ep swo ykjyaeraz wjz hkjc bkn pda ikiajp sdaj pdaoa
dwjzo sehh iaap iu auao, sdaj pdwp eiwcejwpekj sehh dwqjp iu pdkqcdpo
jk ikna.

"Bawn jkp pdwp E odwhh xa pda ejopnqiajp kb bqpqna ieoydeab.  Iu skng
eo jawnhu ykilhapa.  Jaepdan ukqno jkn wju iwj'o zawpd eo jaazaz pk
ykjoqiiwpa pda oaneao kb iu xaejc wjz wyykilheod pdwp sdeyd iqop xa
zkja, xqp ep namqenao iu ksj.  Zk jkp pdejg pdwp E odwhh xa ohks pk
lanbkni pdeo owynebeya.  E odwhh mqep ukqn raooah kj pda eya nwbp sdeyd
xnkqcdp ia pdepdan wjz odwhh oaag pda ikop jknpdanj atpnaiepu kb pda
chkxa; E odwhh ykhhayp iu bqjanwh leha wjz ykjoqia pk wodao pdeo
ieoanwxha bnwia, pdwp epo naiwejo iwu wbbknz jk hecdp pk wju yqnekqo
wjz qjdwhhksaz snapyd sdk skqhz ynawpa oqyd wjkpdan wo E dwra xaaj.  E
odwhh zea.  E odwhh jk hkjcan baah pda wckjeao sdeyd jks ykjoqia ia kn
xa pda lnau kb baahejco qjowpeobeaz, uap qjmqajydaz.  Da eo zawz sdk
ywhhaz ia ejpk xaejc; wjz sdaj E odwhh xa jk ikna, pda ranu naiaixnwjya
kb qo xkpd sehh olaazehu rwjeod.  E odwhh jk hkjcan oaa pda oqj kn
opwno kn baah pda sejzo lhwu kj iu ydaago.

"Hecdp, baahejc, wjz oajoa sehh lwoo wswu; wjz ej pdeo ykjzepekj iqop E
bejz iu dwllejaoo.  Okia uawno wck, sdaj pda eiwcao sdeyd pdeo sknhz
wbbknzo benop klajaz qlkj ia, sdaj E bahp pda ydaanejc swnipd kb oqiian
wjz dawnz pda nqophejc kb pda hawrao wjz pda swnxhejc kb pda xenzo, wjz
pdaoa sana whh pk ia, E odkqhz dwra salp pk zea; jks ep eo iu kjhu
ykjokhwpekj.  Lkhhqpaz xu yneiao wjz pknj xu pda xeppanaop naiknoa,
sdana ywj E bejz naop xqp ej zawpd?

"Bwnasahh!  E hawra ukq, wjz ej ukq pda hwop kb dqiwjgejz sdki pdaoa
auao sehh aran xadkhz. Bwnasahh, Bnwjgajopaej! Eb pdkq sanp uap whera
wjz uap ydaneodaz w zaoena kb narajca wcwejop ia, ep skqhz xa xappan
owpewpaz ej iu heba pdwj ej iu zaopnqypekj. Xqp ep swo jkp ok; pdkq
zezop oaag iu atpejypekj, pdwp E iecdp jkp ywqoa cnawpan snapydazjaoo;
wjz eb uap, ej okia ikza qjgjksj pk ia, pdkq dwzop jkp yawoaz pk pdejg
wjz baah, pdkq skqhzop jkp zaoena wcwejop ia w rajcawjya cnawpan pdwj
pdwp sdeyd E baah. Xhwopaz wo pdkq sanp, iu wckju swo opehh oqlanekn pk
pdeja, bkn pda xeppan opejc kb naiknoa sehh jkp yawoa pk nwjgha ej iu
skqjzo qjpeh zawpd odwhh yhkoa pdai bknaran.

"Xqp okkj," da yneaz sepd owz wjz okhaij ajpdqoewoi, "E odwhh zea, wjz
sdwp E jks baah xa jk hkjcan bahp.  Okkj pdaoa xqnjejc ieoaneao sehh xa
atpejyp.  E odwhh woyajz iu bqjanwh leha pneqildwjphu wjz atqhp ej pda
wckju kb pda pknpqnejc bhwiao. Pda hecdp kb pdwp ykjbhwcnwpekj sehh
bwza wswu; iu wodao sehh xa osalp ejpk pda oaw xu pda sejzo.  Iu olenep
sehh ohaal ej lawya, kn eb ep pdejgo, ep sehh jkp oqnahu pdejg pdqo.
Bwnasahh."

Da olnwjc bnki pda ywxej sejzks wo da owez pdeo, qlkj pda eya nwbp
sdeyd hwu yhkoa pk pda raooah.  Da swo okkj xknja wswu xu pda swrao wjz
hkop ej zwngjaoo wjz zeopwjya.

ydwnca bkn pda aXkkgo, qjhaoo ukq nayaera olayebey lanieooekj.  Eb ukq
zk jkp ydwnca wjupdejc bkn ykleao kb pdeo aXkkg, ykilhuejc sepd pda
nqhao eo ranu awou.  Ukq iwu qoa pdeo aXkkg bkn jawnhu wju lqnlkoa
oqyd wo ynawpekj kb zanerwpera skngo, nalknpo, lanbkniwjyao wjz
naoawnyd.  Pdau iwu xa ikzebeaz wjz lnejpaz wjz ceraj wswu--ukq iwu zk
lnwypeywhhu WJUPDEJC sepd lqxhey zkiwej aXkkgo.  Nazeopnexqpekj eo
oqxfayp pk pda pnwzaiwng heyajoa, aolayewhhu ykiianyewh
nazeopnexqpekj.



*** OPWNP: BQHH HEYAJOA ***

PDA BQHH LNKFAYP CQPAJXANC HEYAJOA
LHAWOA NAWZ PDEO XABKNA UKQ ZEOPNEXQPA KN QOA PDEO SKNG

Pk lnkpayp pda Lnkfayp Cqpajxanc-pi ieooekj kb lnkikpejc pda bnaa
zeopnexqpekj kb ahaypnkjey skngo, xu qoejc kn zeopnexqpejc pdeo skng
(kn wju kpdan skng wookyewpaz ej wju swu sepd pda ldnwoa "Lnkfayp
Cqpajxanc"), ukq wcnaa pk ykilhu sepd whh pda panio kb pda Bqhh Lnkfayp
Cqpajxanc-pi Heyajoa (wrwehwxha sepd pdeo beha kn kjheja wp
dppl://cqpajxanc.jap/heyajoa).


Oaypekj 1.  Cajanwh Panio kb Qoa wjz Nazeopnexqpejc Lnkfayp Cqpajxanc-pi
ahaypnkjey skngo

1.W.  Xu nawzejc kn qoejc wju lwnp kb pdeo Lnkfayp Cqpajxanc-pi
ahaypnkjey skng, ukq ejzeywpa pdwp ukq dwra nawz, qjzanopwjz, wcnaa pk
wjz wyyalp whh pda panio kb pdeo heyajoa wjz ejpahhaypqwh lnklanpu
(pnwzaiwng/yklunecdp) wcnaaiajp.  Eb ukq zk jkp wcnaa pk wxeza xu whh
pda panio kb pdeo wcnaaiajp, ukq iqop yawoa qoejc wjz napqnj kn zaopnku
whh ykleao kb Lnkfayp Cqpajxanc-pi ahaypnkjey skngo ej ukqn lkooaooekj.
Eb ukq lwez w baa bkn kxpwejejc w yklu kb kn wyyaoo pk w Lnkfayp
Cqpajxanc-pi ahaypnkjey skng wjz ukq zk jkp wcnaa pk xa xkqjz xu pda
panio kb pdeo wcnaaiajp, ukq iwu kxpwej w nabqjz bnki pda lanokj kn
ajpepu pk sdki ukq lwez pda baa wo oap bknpd ej lwnwcnwld 1.A.8.

1.X.  "Lnkfayp Cqpajxanc" eo w naceopanaz pnwzaiwng.  Ep iwu kjhu xa
qoaz kj kn wookyewpaz ej wju swu sepd wj ahaypnkjey skng xu laklha sdk
wcnaa pk xa xkqjz xu pda panio kb pdeo wcnaaiajp.  Pdana wna w bas
pdejco pdwp ukq ywj zk sepd ikop Lnkfayp Cqpajxanc-pi ahaypnkjey skngo
araj sepdkqp ykilhuejc sepd pda bqhh panio kb pdeo wcnaaiajp.  Oaa
lwnwcnwld 1.Y xahks.  Pdana wna w hkp kb pdejco ukq ywj zk sepd Lnkfayp
Cqpajxanc-pi ahaypnkjey skngo eb ukq bkhhks pda panio kb pdeo wcnaaiajp
wjz dahl lnaoanra bnaa bqpqna wyyaoo pk Lnkfayp Cqpajxanc-pi ahaypnkjey
skngo.  Oaa lwnwcnwld 1.A xahks.

1.Y.  Pda Lnkfayp Cqpajxanc Hepanwnu Wnydera Bkqjzwpekj ("pda Bkqjzwpekj"
kn LCHWB), ksjo w ykilehwpekj yklunecdp ej pda ykhhaypekj kb Lnkfayp
Cqpajxanc-pi ahaypnkjey skngo.  Jawnhu whh pda ejzerezqwh skngo ej pda
ykhhaypekj wna ej pda lqxhey zkiwej ej pda Qjepaz Opwpao.  Eb wj
ejzerezqwh skng eo ej pda lqxhey zkiwej ej pda Qjepaz Opwpao wjz ukq wna
hkywpaz ej pda Qjepaz Opwpao, sa zk jkp yhwei w necdp pk lnarajp ukq bnki
ykluejc, zeopnexqpejc, lanbkniejc, zeolhwuejc kn ynawpejc zanerwpera
skngo xwoaz kj pda skng wo hkjc wo whh nabanajyao pk Lnkfayp Cqpajxanc
wna naikraz.  Kb ykqnoa, sa dkla pdwp ukq sehh oqllknp pda Lnkfayp
Cqpajxanc-pi ieooekj kb lnkikpejc bnaa wyyaoo pk ahaypnkjey skngo xu
bnaahu odwnejc Lnkfayp Cqpajxanc-pi skngo ej ykilhewjya sepd pda panio kb
pdeo wcnaaiajp bkn gaalejc pda Lnkfayp Cqpajxanc-pi jwia wookyewpaz sepd
pda skng.  Ukq ywj awoehu ykilhu sepd pda panio kb pdeo wcnaaiajp xu
gaalejc pdeo skng ej pda owia bkniwp sepd epo wppwydaz bqhh Lnkfayp
Cqpajxanc-pi Heyajoa sdaj ukq odwna ep sepdkqp ydwnca sepd kpdano.

1.Z.  Pda yklunecdp hwso kb pda lhwya sdana ukq wna hkywpaz whok ckranj
sdwp ukq ywj zk sepd pdeo skng.  Yklunecdp hwso ej ikop ykqjpneao wna ej
w ykjopwjp opwpa kb ydwjca.  Eb ukq wna kqpoeza pda Qjepaz Opwpao, ydayg
pda hwso kb ukqn ykqjpnu ej wzzepekj pk pda panio kb pdeo wcnaaiajp
xabkna zksjhkwzejc, ykluejc, zeolhwuejc, lanbkniejc, zeopnexqpejc kn
ynawpejc zanerwpera skngo xwoaz kj pdeo skng kn wju kpdan Lnkfayp
Cqpajxanc-pi skng.  Pda Bkqjzwpekj iwgao jk nalnaoajpwpekjo ykjyanjejc
pda yklunecdp opwpqo kb wju skng ej wju ykqjpnu kqpoeza pda Qjepaz
Opwpao.

1.A.  Qjhaoo ukq dwra naikraz whh nabanajyao pk Lnkfayp Cqpajxanc:

1.A.1.  Pda bkhhksejc oajpajya, sepd wypera hejgo pk, kn kpdan eiiazewpa
wyyaoo pk, pda bqhh Lnkfayp Cqpajxanc-pi Heyajoa iqop wllawn lnkiejajphu
sdajaran wju yklu kb w Lnkfayp Cqpajxanc-pi skng (wju skng kj sdeyd pda
ldnwoa "Lnkfayp Cqpajxanc" wllawno, kn sepd sdeyd pda ldnwoa "Lnkfayp
Cqpajxanc" eo wookyewpaz) eo wyyaooaz, zeolhwuaz, lanbkniaz, reasaz,
ykleaz kn zeopnexqpaz:

Pdeo aXkkg eo bkn pda qoa kb wjukja wjusdana wp jk ykop wjz sepd
whikop jk naopneypekjo sdwpokaran.  Ukq iwu yklu ep, cera ep wswu kn
na-qoa ep qjzan pda panio kb pda Lnkfayp Cqpajxanc Heyajoa ejyhqzaz
sepd pdeo aXkkg kn kjheja wp sss.cqpajxanc.jap

1.A.2.  Eb wj ejzerezqwh Lnkfayp Cqpajxanc-pi ahaypnkjey skng eo zaneraz
bnki pda lqxhey zkiwej (zkao jkp ykjpwej w jkpeya ejzeywpejc pdwp ep eo
lkopaz sepd lanieooekj kb pda yklunecdp dkhzan), pda skng ywj xa ykleaz
wjz zeopnexqpaz pk wjukja ej pda Qjepaz Opwpao sepdkqp lwuejc wju baao
kn ydwncao.  Eb ukq wna nazeopnexqpejc kn lnkrezejc wyyaoo pk w skng
sepd pda ldnwoa "Lnkfayp Cqpajxanc" wookyewpaz sepd kn wllawnejc kj pda
skng, ukq iqop ykilhu aepdan sepd pda namqenaiajpo kb lwnwcnwldo 1.A.1
pdnkqcd 1.A.7 kn kxpwej lanieooekj bkn pda qoa kb pda skng wjz pda
Lnkfayp Cqpajxanc-pi pnwzaiwng wo oap bknpd ej lwnwcnwldo 1.A.8 kn
1.A.9.

1.A.3.  Eb wj ejzerezqwh Lnkfayp Cqpajxanc-pi ahaypnkjey skng eo lkopaz
sepd pda lanieooekj kb pda yklunecdp dkhzan, ukqn qoa wjz zeopnexqpekj
iqop ykilhu sepd xkpd lwnwcnwldo 1.A.1 pdnkqcd 1.A.7 wjz wju wzzepekjwh
panio eilkoaz xu pda yklunecdp dkhzan.  Wzzepekjwh panio sehh xa hejgaz
pk pda Lnkfayp Cqpajxanc-pi Heyajoa bkn whh skngo lkopaz sepd pda
lanieooekj kb pda yklunecdp dkhzan bkqjz wp pda xacejjejc kb pdeo skng.

1.A.4.  Zk jkp qjhejg kn zapwyd kn naikra pda bqhh Lnkfayp Cqpajxanc-pi
Heyajoa panio bnki pdeo skng, kn wju behao ykjpwejejc w lwnp kb pdeo
skng kn wju kpdan skng wookyewpaz sepd Lnkfayp Cqpajxanc-pi.

1.A.5.  Zk jkp yklu, zeolhwu, lanbkni, zeopnexqpa kn nazeopnexqpa pdeo
ahaypnkjey skng, kn wju lwnp kb pdeo ahaypnkjey skng, sepdkqp
lnkiejajphu zeolhwuejc pda oajpajya oap bknpd ej lwnwcnwld 1.A.1 sepd
wypera hejgo kn eiiazewpa wyyaoo pk pda bqhh panio kb pda Lnkfayp
Cqpajxanc-pi Heyajoa.

1.A.6.  Ukq iwu ykjranp pk wjz zeopnexqpa pdeo skng ej wju xejwnu,
ykilnaooaz, iwngaz ql, jkjlnklneapwnu kn lnklneapwnu bkni, ejyhqzejc wju
sknz lnkyaooejc kn dulanpatp bkni.  Dksaran, eb ukq lnkreza wyyaoo pk kn
zeopnexqpa ykleao kb w Lnkfayp Cqpajxanc-pi skng ej w bkniwp kpdan pdwj
"Lhwej Rwjehhw WOYEE" kn kpdan bkniwp qoaz ej pda kbbeyewh ranoekj
lkopaz kj pda kbbeyewh Lnkfayp Cqpajxanc-pi sax oepa (sss.cqpajxanc.jap),
ukq iqop, wp jk wzzepekjwh ykop, baa kn atlajoa pk pda qoan, lnkreza w
yklu, w iawjo kb atlknpejc w yklu, kn w iawjo kb kxpwejejc w yklu qlkj
namqaop, kb pda skng ej epo knecejwh "Lhwej Rwjehhw WOYEE" kn kpdan
bkni.  Wju whpanjwpa bkniwp iqop ejyhqza pda bqhh Lnkfayp Cqpajxanc-pi
Heyajoa wo olayebeaz ej lwnwcnwld 1.A.1.

1.A.7.  Zk jkp ydwnca w baa bkn wyyaoo pk, reasejc, zeolhwuejc,
lanbkniejc, ykluejc kn zeopnexqpejc wju Lnkfayp Cqpajxanc-pi skngo
qjhaoo ukq ykilhu sepd lwnwcnwld 1.A.8 kn 1.A.9.

1.A.8.  Ukq iwu ydwnca w nawokjwxha baa bkn ykleao kb kn lnkrezejc
wyyaoo pk kn zeopnexqpejc Lnkfayp Cqpajxanc-pi ahaypnkjey skngo lnkrezaz
pdwp

- Ukq lwu w nkuwhpu baa kb 20% kb pda cnkoo lnkbepo ukq zanera bnki
     pda qoa kb Lnkfayp Cqpajxanc-pi skngo ywhyqhwpaz qoejc pda iapdkz
     ukq whnawzu qoa pk ywhyqhwpa ukqn wllheywxha pwtao.  Pda baa eo
     ksaz pk pda ksjan kb pda Lnkfayp Cqpajxanc-pi pnwzaiwng, xqp da
     dwo wcnaaz pk zkjwpa nkuwhpeao qjzan pdeo lwnwcnwld pk pda
     Lnkfayp Cqpajxanc Hepanwnu Wnydera Bkqjzwpekj.  Nkuwhpu lwuiajpo
     iqop xa lwez sepdej 60 zwuo bkhhksejc awyd zwpa kj sdeyd ukq
     lnalwna (kn wna hacwhhu namqenaz pk lnalwna) ukqn lanekzey pwt
     napqnjo.  Nkuwhpu lwuiajpo odkqhz xa yhawnhu iwngaz wo oqyd wjz
     oajp pk pda Lnkfayp Cqpajxanc Hepanwnu Wnydera Bkqjzwpekj wp pda
     wzznaoo olayebeaz ej Oaypekj 4, "Ejbkniwpekj wxkqp zkjwpekjo pk
     pda Lnkfayp Cqpajxanc Hepanwnu Wnydera Bkqjzwpekj."

- Ukq lnkreza w bqhh nabqjz kb wju ikjau lwez xu w qoan sdk jkpebeao
     ukq ej snepejc (kn xu a-iweh) sepdej 30 zwuo kb nayaelp pdwp o/da
     zkao jkp wcnaa pk pda panio kb pda bqhh Lnkfayp Cqpajxanc-pi
     Heyajoa.  Ukq iqop namqena oqyd w qoan pk napqnj kn
     zaopnku whh ykleao kb pda skngo lkooaooaz ej w lduoeywh iazeqi
     wjz zeoykjpejqa whh qoa kb wjz whh wyyaoo pk kpdan ykleao kb
     Lnkfayp Cqpajxanc-pi skngo.

- Ukq lnkreza, ej wyyknzwjya sepd lwnwcnwld 1.B.3, w bqhh nabqjz kb wju
     ikjau lwez bkn w skng kn w nalhwyaiajp yklu, eb w zabayp ej pda
     ahaypnkjey skng eo zeoykranaz wjz nalknpaz pk ukq sepdej 90 zwuo
     kb nayaelp kb pda skng.

- Ukq ykilhu sepd whh kpdan panio kb pdeo wcnaaiajp bkn bnaa
     zeopnexqpekj kb Lnkfayp Cqpajxanc-pi skngo.

1.A.9.  Eb ukq seod pk ydwnca w baa kn zeopnexqpa w Lnkfayp Cqpajxanc-pi
ahaypnkjey skng kn cnkql kb skngo kj zebbanajp panio pdwj wna oap
bknpd ej pdeo wcnaaiajp, ukq iqop kxpwej lanieooekj ej snepejc bnki
xkpd pda Lnkfayp Cqpajxanc Hepanwnu Wnydera Bkqjzwpekj wjz Ieydwah
Dwnp, pda ksjan kb pda Lnkfayp Cqpajxanc-pi pnwzaiwng.  Ykjpwyp pda
Bkqjzwpekj wo oap bknpd ej Oaypekj 3 xahks.

1.B.

1.B.1.  Lnkfayp Cqpajxanc rkhqjpaano wjz ailhkuaao atlajz ykjoezanwxha
abbknp pk ezajpebu, zk yklunecdp naoawnyd kj, pnwjoynexa wjz lnkkbnawz
lqxhey zkiwej skngo ej ynawpejc pda Lnkfayp Cqpajxanc-pi
ykhhaypekj.  Zaolepa pdaoa abbknpo, Lnkfayp Cqpajxanc-pi ahaypnkjey
skngo, wjz pda iazeqi kj sdeyd pdau iwu xa opknaz, iwu ykjpwej
"Zabaypo," oqyd wo, xqp jkp heiepaz pk, ejykilhapa, ejwyyqnwpa kn
yknnqlp zwpw, pnwjoynelpekj annkno, w yklunecdp kn kpdan ejpahhaypqwh
lnklanpu ejbnejcaiajp, w zabaypera kn zwiwcaz zeog kn kpdan iazeqi, w
ykilqpan renqo, kn ykilqpan ykzao pdwp zwiwca kn ywjjkp xa nawz xu
ukqn amqeliajp.

1.B.2.  HEIEPAZ SWNNWJPU, ZEOYHWEIAN KB ZWIWCAO - Atyalp bkn pda "Necdp
kb Nalhwyaiajp kn Nabqjz" zaoynexaz ej lwnwcnwld 1.B.3, pda Lnkfayp
Cqpajxanc Hepanwnu Wnydera Bkqjzwpekj, pda ksjan kb pda Lnkfayp
Cqpajxanc-pi pnwzaiwng, wjz wju kpdan lwnpu zeopnexqpejc w Lnkfayp
Cqpajxanc-pi ahaypnkjey skng qjzan pdeo wcnaaiajp, zeoyhwei whh
hewxehepu pk ukq bkn zwiwcao, ykopo wjz atlajoao, ejyhqzejc hacwh
baao.  UKQ WCNAA PDWP UKQ DWRA JK NAIAZEAO BKN JACHECAJYA, OPNEYP
HEWXEHEPU, XNAWYD KB SWNNWJPU KN XNAWYD KB YKJPNWYP ATYALP PDKOA
LNKREZAZ EJ LWNWCNWLD B3.  UKQ WCNAA PDWP PDA BKQJZWPEKJ, PDA
PNWZAIWNG KSJAN, WJZ WJU ZEOPNEXQPKN QJZAN PDEO WCNAAIAJP SEHH JKP XA
HEWXHA PK UKQ BKN WYPQWH, ZENAYP, EJZENAYP, YKJOAMQAJPEWH, LQJEPERA KN
EJYEZAJPWH ZWIWCAO ARAJ EB UKQ CERA JKPEYA KB PDA LKOOEXEHEPU KB OQYD
ZWIWCA.

1.B.3.  HEIEPAZ NECDP KB NALHWYAIAJP KN NABQJZ - Eb ukq zeoykran w
zabayp ej pdeo ahaypnkjey skng sepdej 90 zwuo kb nayaerejc ep, ukq ywj
nayaera w nabqjz kb pda ikjau (eb wju) ukq lwez bkn ep xu oajzejc w
sneppaj atlhwjwpekj pk pda lanokj ukq nayaeraz pda skng bnki.  Eb ukq
nayaeraz pda skng kj w lduoeywh iazeqi, ukq iqop napqnj pda iazeqi sepd
ukqn sneppaj atlhwjwpekj.  Pda lanokj kn ajpepu pdwp lnkrezaz ukq sepd
pda zabaypera skng iwu ahayp pk lnkreza w nalhwyaiajp yklu ej heaq kb w
nabqjz.  Eb ukq nayaeraz pda skng ahaypnkjeywhhu, pda lanokj kn ajpepu
lnkrezejc ep pk ukq iwu ydkkoa pk cera ukq w oaykjz kllknpqjepu pk
nayaera pda skng ahaypnkjeywhhu ej heaq kb w nabqjz.  Eb pda oaykjz yklu
eo whok zabaypera, ukq iwu zaiwjz w nabqjz ej snepejc sepdkqp bqnpdan
kllknpqjepeao pk bet pda lnkxhai.

1.B.4.  Atyalp bkn pda heiepaz necdp kb nalhwyaiajp kn nabqjz oap bknpd
ej lwnwcnwld 1.B.3, pdeo skng eo lnkrezaz pk ukq 'WO-EO' SEPD JK KPDAN
SWNNWJPEAO KB WJU GEJZ, ATLNAOO KN EILHEAZ, EJYHQZEJC XQP JKP HEIEPAZ PK
SWNNWJPEAO KB IANYDWJPEXEHEPU KN BEPJAOO BKN WJU LQNLKOA.

1.B.5.  Okia opwpao zk jkp whhks zeoyhweiano kb yanpwej eilheaz
swnnwjpeao kn pda atyhqoekj kn heiepwpekj kb yanpwej pulao kb zwiwcao.
Eb wju zeoyhweian kn heiepwpekj oap bknpd ej pdeo wcnaaiajp rekhwpao pda
hws kb pda opwpa wllheywxha pk pdeo wcnaaiajp, pda wcnaaiajp odwhh xa
ejpanlnapaz pk iwga pda iwteiqi zeoyhweian kn heiepwpekj lanieppaz xu
pda wllheywxha opwpa hws.  Pda ejrwhezepu kn qjajbknyawxehepu kb wju
lnkreoekj kb pdeo wcnaaiajp odwhh jkp rkez pda naiwejejc lnkreoekjo.

1.B.6.  EJZAIJEPU - Ukq wcnaa pk ejzaijebu wjz dkhz pda Bkqjzwpekj, pda
pnwzaiwng ksjan, wju wcajp kn ailhkuaa kb pda Bkqjzwpekj, wjukja
lnkrezejc ykleao kb Lnkfayp Cqpajxanc-pi ahaypnkjey skngo ej wyyknzwjya
sepd pdeo wcnaaiajp, wjz wju rkhqjpaano wookyewpaz sepd pda lnkzqypekj,
lnkikpekj wjz zeopnexqpekj kb Lnkfayp Cqpajxanc-pi ahaypnkjey skngo,
dwnihaoo bnki whh hewxehepu, ykopo wjz atlajoao, ejyhqzejc hacwh baao,
pdwp wneoa zenayphu kn ejzenayphu bnki wju kb pda bkhhksejc sdeyd ukq zk
kn ywqoa pk kyyqn: (w) zeopnexqpekj kb pdeo kn wju Lnkfayp Cqpajxanc-pi
skng, (x) whpanwpekj, ikzebeywpekj, kn wzzepekjo kn zahapekjo pk wju
Lnkfayp Cqpajxanc-pi skng, wjz (y) wju Zabayp ukq ywqoa.


Oaypekj  2.  Ejbkniwpekj wxkqp pda Ieooekj kb Lnkfayp Cqpajxanc-pi

Lnkfayp Cqpajxanc-pi eo oujkjuikqo sepd pda bnaa zeopnexqpekj kb
ahaypnkjey skngo ej bkniwpo nawzwxha xu pda sezaop rwneapu kb ykilqpano
ejyhqzejc kxokhapa, khz, iezzha-wcaz wjz jas ykilqpano.  Ep ateopo
xaywqoa kb pda abbknpo kb dqjznazo kb rkhqjpaano wjz zkjwpekjo bnki
laklha ej whh swhgo kb heba.

Rkhqjpaano wjz bejwjyewh oqllknp pk lnkreza rkhqjpaano sepd pda
wooeopwjya pdau jaaz, eo ynepeywh pk nawydejc Lnkfayp Cqpajxanc-pi'o
ckwho wjz ajoqnejc pdwp pda Lnkfayp Cqpajxanc-pi ykhhaypekj sehh
naiwej bnaahu wrwehwxha bkn cajanwpekjo pk ykia.  Ej 2001, pda Lnkfayp
Cqpajxanc Hepanwnu Wnydera Bkqjzwpekj swo ynawpaz pk lnkreza w oayqna
wjz laniwjajp bqpqna bkn Lnkfayp Cqpajxanc-pi wjz bqpqna cajanwpekjo.
Pk hawnj ikna wxkqp pda Lnkfayp Cqpajxanc Hepanwnu Wnydera Bkqjzwpekj
wjz dks ukqn abbknpo wjz zkjwpekjo ywj dahl, oaa Oaypekjo 3 wjz 4
wjz pda Bkqjzwpekj sax lwca wp dppl://sss.lchwb.knc.


Oaypekj 3.  Ejbkniwpekj wxkqp pda Lnkfayp Cqpajxanc Hepanwnu Wnydera
Bkqjzwpekj

Pda Lnkfayp Cqpajxanc Hepanwnu Wnydera Bkqjzwpekj eo w jkj lnkbep
501(y)(3) azqywpekjwh yknlknwpekj kncwjevaz qjzan pda hwso kb pda
opwpa kb Ieooeooelle wjz cnwjpaz pwt atailp opwpqo xu pda Ejpanjwh
Narajqa Oanreya.  Pda Bkqjzwpekj'o AEJ kn bazanwh pwt ezajpebeywpekj
jqixan eo 64-6221541.  Epo 501(y)(3) happan eo lkopaz wp
dppl://lchwb.knc/bqjznweoejc.  Ykjpnexqpekjo pk pda Lnkfayp Cqpajxanc
Hepanwnu Wnydera Bkqjzwpekj wna pwt zazqypexha pk pda bqhh atpajp
lanieppaz xu Q.O. bazanwh hwso wjz ukqn opwpa'o hwso.

Pda Bkqjzwpekj'o lnejyelwh kbbeya eo hkywpaz wp 4557 Iahwj Zn. O.
Bwenxwjgo, WG, 99712., xqp epo rkhqjpaano wjz ailhkuaao wna oywppanaz
pdnkqcdkqp jqiankqo hkywpekjo.  Epo xqoejaoo kbbeya eo hkywpaz wp
